/ /lce btsun ngag gi dbang phyug gi rtogs brjod shel dkar gyi phreng ba zhes bya ba bzhugs/ /

/ /na maHpradznyA shA sa na dha ra shI bha drA ya/ 'od gsal 'chi med lding khang las 'ongs 'khon rigs gdung gi mngon mtho zhing / /rgya chen mdo rgyud rgya mtsho'i mnga' bdag
gangs khrod mkhas grub kun gyi rje/ /rgol ngan tshar gcod dregs ldan mi bdag bye ba'i rigs kyi cod pan can/ /sa skya'i bla chen gong ma lnga zhes nyi zla ltar grags der
phyag 'tshal/ /ngag gi dbang phyug dus gsum rgyal ba'i mkhyen brtse ma lus gcig bsdus pa/ /rigs brgya'i khyab bdag nor 'dzin 'gro ba blo gsal kun gyi gnyen gcig po/ /mdzad
bzang rgya mtsho'i gos can kun khyab grags pa don gyi thams cad mkhyen/ /lhar bcas skye rgu'i gtsug rgyan khams gsum chos kyi rgyal por spyi bos mchod/ /rgyal bas lung
bstan yongs rdzogs bstan pa'i mnga' bdag e waM pa/ /rdo rje 'chang dbang ngur smrig gos bklubs 'jam dpal rdo rje mkhyen rab

rje/ /snyan brgyud bye ba'i mdzod 'dzin rigs kun bdag po tshar pa zhes/ /mkhas grub nyin byed snang bar bdag blo'i padmo cis mi 'dzum/ /rgyal ba kun gyi mkhyen brtse'i snang
brnyan ni/ /rab 'byams dkyil 'khor gtso bo he ru kaH /zhing 'dir thub bstan 'dzin phyir ngur smrig gar/ /rnam rol 'dren mchog bzang po khu dbon rgyal/ /snyan brgyud zab
don rin chen dbang gi rgyal/ /rgya chen bsod nams mchog gi gru rdzing gis/ /'dren mkhas grub pa'i lam ston drin chen rje/ /snying nas 'dud do byang chub bar du skyongs/
/khams gsum chos kyi rgyal po kun dga'i mtshan/ /de sras mkhyen brtse'i bdag nyid bsod nams dbang / /dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho'i dbang phyug sngags 'chang rje/ /kun dga' bkra
shis 'bral med gtsug na bzhugs/ /'jam mgon thun mtshams gos 'chang byams pa'i mtshan/ /

lnga rig mkhas pa'i gtsug rgyan ngag dbang bstan/ /mkhas dang grub pa'i dbang phyug bstan 'dzin dbang / /yongs 'dzin bka' drin can rnams dang bas bsngags/ /rgya chen mdo rgyud
tshangs pa'i ral klung las/ /legs 'ongs zab rgyas dam chos dza hu'i rgyun/ /'dzam gling rgya mtsho'i gos can khyon 'bebs pa'i/ /'phags bod mkhas grub tshogs rnams phyag
gi gnas/ /mtshan tsam dran pas dus min 'chi ba las/ /rgyal mdzad tshe mtha' yas pa'i mgon po gang / /'bral med bde chen 'khor lo'i cod pan du/ /bzhugs la mi shigs tshe
yi dngos grub stsol/ /rgyal ba'i ye shes gcig bsdus khro chags sku/ /gar dgu'i nyams ldan dgyes mdzad rdo rje dang / /mkha' spyod zhing gi rdo rje btsun mo sogs/ /yi dam
lha yi tshogs la snying nas 'dud/ /tshogs gnyis rta ljang dbang pos nyer drangs pa'i/ /mtshan dpe'i dkyil 'khor rgyas pa'i nyin byed dbang / /'gro 'd-i yid mkhar shar tshe
mi mthun smag /pha mthar mdzad pa'i zas gtsang sras des skyongs/ /yid 'ongs padma rA ga'i lhun po'i spor/ /nyi gzhon 'od kyis lan brgyar byugs 'dra'i sku/ /dran pas khams
gsum dbang sdud lha gsum gyis/ /srid zhi'i dpal 'byor dbyar mtshor 'gran par mdzod/ /bgrang yas bstan srung ded dpon gur gyi mgon/ /bstan dgra tshar gcod stobs 'phrog
gdong bzhi pa/ /srid gsum bdag mo rdo rje rab brtan sogs/ /bstan srung rgya mtsho'i tshogs kyis dge legs stsol/ /rab dkar ke la sha yi mdangs

'phrog pa'i/ /'jigs med glang po'i dgra yi steng bzhugs nas/ /dngos grub mchog stsol ngal bsos rgyal po dang / /rmugs 'dzin dbang pos 'dod dgu'i char chen phob/ /ces mchod
par brjod pas sngon bsus te/ de'ang dam pa gong ma rnams/ bsam bzhin du bstan pa dang 'gro ba'i don du sku skye ba bzhes te mdzad pa'i phrin las ji snyed kyis 'gro ba rnams
smin grol la bkod pa'i tshul gyi rnam par thar pa 'god pa ni dgos pa chen po dang ldan zhing / gzhan ma tshe gang gi bya las gang byas rnams yi ger bri bar 'os pa zhig
yin na 'jig rten pa rnams gzhan las rnam grangs mang zhing byas pa rgya che ba 'ong 'dug cing / rang nyid kyang dam pa gong ma'i gdan sar mi'i lad mo spre'us byed pa ltar
las rtogs brjod sogs 'bri 'os ga la yod gshis 'bri 'dun gtan nas med na'ang / /dpon rin po che ngag dbang mkhyen brtse rab brtan dang / nyan po nas mkhas shing grub pa
chos rje rin po che/ rmor zhabs drung / mdzod pa lhun grub/ gsang sbugs nas tshong dpon/ gzhan yang bla ma grwa rigs sogs nye bar gnas pa tshang mas 'bri dgos tshul gsung
bar dgos pa chung tshul las khas len ma zhus kyang / rjes su sa skya nas gong ma chos kyi rgyal pos rtogs brjod 'bri dgos tshul gnang bar bka' nan gyen zlog ma nus pa bcas
zur tsam 'bri ba'i lugs su byas pa ni/ de'ang 'gro ba thams cad kyi skyabs dang mgon gcig rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi tshogs gnyis yongs su rdzogs nas bdud btul
ba dang / mngon par byang chub nas chos

kyi 'khor lo bskor te 'gro ba rnams sangs rgyas kyi sa la 'god pa'i gnas 'phags yul rdo rje gdan nas dpag tshad brgya bgrod pa na byang chub sems dpa' lag na padma'i zhing
/ byang phyogs kha ba can gyi sa'i lte ba pho brang chen po'i ri bo gru 'dzin dang / /ra sa 'phrul snang gi gtsug lag khang dang zung du 'brel ba dang nye ba'i cha/ sngon
rgyal blon byang chub sems dpa' rnams dang / slob dpon chen po padma badzra dang / dam pa sangs rgyas sogs skyes chen dam pa rnams kyis byin gyis brlabs shing sgrub pa'i
gnas dang / lo tsA ba ka cog zhang gsum sogs skyes chen du ma'i gtsug lag khang dang / kun dga' ra ba du mas gang ba phan bde'i 'byung khungs su gyur pa'i 'phan yul gyi
khrags gsum gyi gong ma chos rgyal srong btsan sgam po dang / rgya bal gyi btsun mo bzhugs pa'i sa rgyal po lung dang btsun mo lung zhes grags pa dang / sngon rdzogs pa'i
sangs rgyas 'od srung gi 'khor dgra bcom pa lnga brgya 'ja' lus su chos skur gyur pa'i gnas deng sang kyang dung dang gaNDi'i sgra thos pa bka' gdams kyi dge ba'i bshes
gnyen rnams kyi bzhugs gnas/ khyad par bdag chen rdo rje 'chang dang / rdo rings pa chen po/ tshar chen gsum gyi sgrub gnas/ rdo rje 'jigs byed dang / rnal 'byor mas byin
gyis brlabs shing chos srung rnams sbrin bzhin du 'du ba'i gnas bya bzang lhun grub bde chen dang mi ring zhing / zhang sna nam gyi gtsug lag khang bzhengs skabs/ gnas der
'gro ba la phan bde 'byung ba'i smon lam mdzad de brag la phyag brdabs pas/ brag

gas nas gser gyi byams pa khru gang pa zhig byon pa thugs kar ting nge 'dzin sems dpar bzhugs su gsol ba'i byams chen dang nye sras 'khor bcas bzhugs pa'i khrags gong ma'i
gnas kyi gtso bo lug lhas gser gyi lha khang dang nye ba na/ rgyal ba 'brom gyi zhabs kyis bcags shing dge ba'i bshes gnyen ri mkhar ba'i gnas bsam 'grub ri mkhar du rigs
rus dge ba zhwa lu dpon chen gyi brgyud pa yin tshul sogs rgyu mtshan cung zad brjod par ni 'di skad du// ! nyer len mngal skyes srid pa'i sgor zhugs phyin/ /rang rang rigs
kyi brjod tshul cung zad tsam/ /mchog dman lus can skye bor yod mod phyir/ /snga rabs rigs kyi gling slong mtshar du ci/ /'on kyang gdong dum phal la dri bsung gis/ /byugs
te bzhi mdo'i tshong 'dus skye bo'i mir/ /bsngags brjod tsandan gyis bskul zol zog gi /che khyad rin thang len 'dod ma lags par/ /'od gsal 'chi med lha yi lding khang
las/ /'ongs pa'i mes pho gnam lha spyi rings nas/ /bdag gi yab rje sbas pa'i rnal 'byor bar/ /ma nyams rigs kyi che ba drang po'i gtam/ /dam pa'i phyag srol la 'dren 'di
skad do/ /'od gsal lha dbang gom rtse rgyal po yi/ /klu bza' khab bsten nyi zer 'phrul rgyal byung / /de sras bdun byung thu bos gnas skas las/ /babs te stag gzig rgyal
po mche phreng grags/ /sras gsum byung ba'i dang po bar lo yi/ /hor yul la gshegs hor gyi rgyal por gyur/ /bar pa nan los rgya nag rgyal srid bzung / /me long gdong zhes
'dzam gling sum gnyis bskyangs/ /gsum pa

da rgan zhang zhung rgyal por gyur/ /'gro rnams bder bkod bod yul yar klung byon/ /'jig rten dbang phyug srong btsan nang blon mdzad/ /de nas lo tsA dznyA na siddhi yis/ /'jam
dbyangs chos rgyal khri srong bka' bzhin du/ /bstan dang 'gro ba'i dpung gnyen mkhan slob gnyis/ /spyan drangs lha srin kun btul zab yangs kyi/ /sa btul gtsug lag khang
bzhengs rab gnas mdzad/ /rgyal po dgyes te gser gyi yi ge thob/ /dam chos sgyur ba'i lo tsA ba yang mdzad/ /mched zla khyi 'brug gis kyang khri srong dang / /rgyal po
sad na legs kyi nang blon mdzad/ /sgra dang tshad ma'i bstan bcos du ma bsgyur/ /dznyA na'i sras la tag ra tag nu dang / /bzang to re nu gnyis byung dang po yi/ /nang blon
mdzad cing phyi ma kha blon gyur/ /gcung sras lha sbyin khri ral nang blon mdzad/ /rgyal po dgyes te ha ho gangs bzang nas/ /phyug po yur ba gdong yan nyang lung gnang
/ /lha khang brgya rtsa bzhengs te bka' chen bzhi'i/ /che ba'i las ka brtsams te nyang stod phyogs/ /rang gi pho brang brtsigs nas bde skyid stsal/ /de yi rigs las zhang
blon sogs drug gis/ /gtsug lag khang bzhengs kha blon mdo blon mdzad/ /zhang blon sras ni dpal lo de yi sras/ /khri bzang de rigs srag sher bstan khri dang / /de rigs khrom
sher ldong khri bya ba byung / /de'i sras stag gi rgyal mtshan 'chang khri gnyis/ /dang por g.yu thog sgra sogs sras bzhi byung / /gnyis par g.yu 'bum la sogs gsum byung
ba'i/ /che sras lce btsun shes rab 'byung gnas te/ /skyes mchog 'di yis lo ston chen po yi/ /nye gnas mdzad

cing rgyan gong gtsug lag khang / /bzhengs te sangs rgyas bstan pa'i me ro gsos/ /rang nyid kyis kyang gtsug lag khang chen dang / /chos grwa bzhengs par dgongs te lo ston
la/ /mda' sbugs gser gyis bkang ste lung bstan zhus/ /babs pa'i gnas der zhwa lu'i chos grwa btab/ /rdo rje gdan nas slob dpon a bha yar/ /bsnyen par rdzogs te 'phags mchog
spyan ras gzigs/ /spyan drangs gandho la yi gtso bor bzhugs/ /sangs rgyas gnyis pa jo bo chen po yi/ /rab gnas mdzad pas rten la phyag nas chags/ /jo bo'i lung bzhin chu
bo siddha nas/ /'jig rten dbang phyug rang byon spyan drangs te/ /rgyal ba'i bstan pa nyi 'od bzhin du gsal/ /shin tu che ba'i las ka bzhi dang ldan/ /g.yu sgra'i sras
la lce 'bum de yi sras/ /'bum ye'i sras la 'bum dar bya ba byung / /mnga' ris khri skor tsam zhig dbang du bsdus/ /de las 'bum rten de sras sang ye byung / /'di la chos
kyi rgyal po 'phags pa yi/ /zhwa lu khri dpon zhes pa'i gser yig gnang / /khri dpon kun las che bar mnga' dbang bskur/ /de sras rnga sgra la sogs lcam sring drug /byung ba'i
ma gcig lha lcam mkha' 'gro 'bum/ /sa skyar 'gro mgon phyag na'i khab tu bzhes/ /sras mchog dharma phA la rakShi ta/ /'khrungs nas sku zhang zhes grags bkur stir mdzad/
/gong ma'i lung las dpal ldan sa skya pa'i/ /sku zhang yin phyin nged kyi zhang po yang / /yin du chug ces mnga' 'bangs 'khor g.yog sogs/ /shes su bcug pa'i 'ja' sa gser
yig gnang / /de sras sku

zhang rdo rje dbang phyug dang / /ma gcig gzhon nu 'bum 'khrungs sku zhang la/ /sngar bzhin gong mas 'ja' sa gser yig gnang / /gzhon nu 'bum nyid dpal ldan sa skya ru/ /bdag
nyid bzang po dpal gyi khab tu bzhes/ /sras ni gu shrI kun dga' nyi ma dang / /'jam dbyangs don rgyal chos rje bla ma gsum/ /bstan pa'i mnga' bdag chos kyi bdag por gyur/
/sku zhang rnga sgra'i sras po grags rgyal gyis/ /srid bskyangs rgya yul byon nas gong ma'i lung / /thob cing bod yul chol ka gsum dbang bsgyur/ /stag mgo nor bu gnyis
pa 'dzin pa yi/ /hu shi du yan sha yi las ka dang / /gser bre brgya dang dngul bre lnga brgya sogs/ /gnang skyes gya nom stsal te bka' bzhin du/ /bod byon zhwa lu'i gtsug
lag khang chen la/ /gser bskyed rgya phibs gser gyi ganydzi ra/ /dus gsum sangs rgyas sku dang bka' 'gyur sogs/ /gser las grub pa'i rten gsum khyad 'phags bzhengs/ /thams
cad mkhyen pa bu ston rin po che/ /mkhan por mnga' gsol dge 'dun dar rgyas spel/ /sangs rgyas bstan pa nyin mor gsal bar mdzad/ /de sras hor gyi yul du sku 'khrungs pa/
/sku zhang kun dga' don grub ces grags pas/ /gtsug lag logs bris gzhal yas khang rnams bkod/ /bstan 'gyur bzhengs dang chos sde dar rgyas dang / /bu ston chen po'i zhabs
'degs bstan pa spel/ /de dang yab gcig sku mched sku zhang ni/ /ye shes kun dgar gong ma rgyal po yis/ /yab mes ji bzhin 'ja' sa gser yig dang / /thong kyi du wan sha yi
lung yang gnang / /de dang yab gcig lcam sring khye 'dren dpal/ /

sa skyar khab bzhes bla chen kun rgyal 'khrungs/ /dharma pA la nas bzung 'di yan du/ /gdung brgyud drug ring sku yi zhang por gyur/ /de nas sku zhang ye shes kun dga'i sras/
/sku zhang legs pa don grub pa la yang / /gong nas thong ji du wan sha'i las ka /khri skor shes sa'i 'ja' sa sngar bzhin gnang / /legs pa don grub sras kyi phyi tshar ni/
/don rgyal ba sogs gsum nas brgyud pa la/ /smad zhang zhes grags che ba don rgyal ba'i/ /sras gsum che ba sangs rgyas pa sogs gsum/ /de la rin chen bzang po la sogs lnga/
/rin bzang sras po gnyer chen pa rnams ni/ /sku zhang rnga sgra phyogs las mched pa'o/ /de yang sku zhang rdo rje dbang phyug sras/ /nam mkha' mchog grub rab tu ma byung
gong / /sku zhang blo gsal ba dang rgyal ba gnyis/ /'khrungs pa'i sras la sku zhang dpal 'byor ba/ /de sras rdo rje 'chang dbang mkhyen rab rje/ /phun tshogs pa dang
rgyal ba rnam sras pa/ /legs pa pa dang bkra shis pa rnams 'khrungs/ /rdo rje 'chang dbang mkhyen rab chos rje ni/ /rgyal ba'i yab gcig 'jam dpal dbyangs nyid las/ /shA ri'i
bu dang rigs ldan chos rgyal dang / /rgya bod mkhas grub du ma'i skur bstan cing / /sku tshe 'dir yang chung ngu'i dus nyid nas/ /gshed dmar la sogs yi dam du ma gzigs/
/rnam thos sras sogs chos srung bran du 'khor/ /dga' ldan gnas nas rgyal ba byams mgon dang / /rgyal ba rab gsal zung gis lung bstan bzhin/ /ljongs 'dir shing rta'i srol
'byed bcu gsum sogs/ /dam pa'i chos kyis 'gro rnams smin par mdzad/ /khyad par thams

cad mkhyen pa rong ston rje'i/ /chos grar pha rol byad kas nyan pa'i tshe/ /rdo rje 'chang dngos blo gros rgyal mtshan gyis/ /bstan pa nyams gsos 'dzin skyong spel ba la/ /dam
pa khyed las lhag pa gzhan na su/ /med ces gdan sar mnga' gsol chos 'khor bskor/ /mi mthun g.yul las rgyal phyir bstan srung gi /sku brnyan tshogs bzhengs bdag chen rdo
rje 'chang / /mkhyen rab chos rje rdo rings kun spangs rje/ /tshar pa rje sogs bstan 'dzin tshogs rnams kyis/ /rab tu gnas shing dam gzhag mdzad pa'i tshe/ /dam can rgya
mtsho sprin bzhin dngos su thim/ /sku las gdug pa'i khrag rgyun babs pa dang / /rkang gling 'bud sogs rnam 'gyur sna tshogs ston/ /rdo rje'i brag rdzong lta bur dngos
su bzhugs/ /bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gis 'od gsal du/ /stobs 'phrog dbang pos gtsor byas chos srung rnams/ /rings pa sprin bzhin 'du bar gzigs pa'i gnas/ /dpal ldan rtser
yang sgrub gnas mgon khang bzhengs/ /rgya gar lho phyogs ri sul rnal 'byor mas/ /gnyen lor bram ze mngag gtad gnang ba'i skabs/ /dpal mgon bram ze'i gzugs su mngon sum du/
/gnyen gyi bran du bka' bsgos g.yog tu btang / /bla rdo gnang ba zhal bzhi rang byon du/ /gyur pa'i sku rten khyad 'phags ngo mtshar can/ /'jam mgon rim brgyud sku srung
mdzad pa'i rten/ /phyogs 'di'i bstan pa bsrung phyir bzhugs su gsol/ /ji ltar gsol bzhin rgyun gyi dbang po yi/ /pha rol byad ka gnam lcags thog gis bsgral/ /da lta'i
bar du lugs gnyis cher 'phel te/ /chos sgra dbyar gyi rnga ltar sgrog pa 'di/ /dam pa yab

sras sku drin kho nar sems/ /gur mgon chos srung sprin bzhin 'du ba'i sa/ /bsam gtan rang bzhin 'phel ba ya mtshan gnas/ /bka' gdams ri ba'i sgom khang ri khrod du/ /dkon mchog
bzang pos spyan drangs zhabs kyis bcags/ /srung mar phrin bcol rab gnas me tog gtor/ /sku yi snag dpon 'jam dbyangs chos kyi rje/ /rgyal tshab mdzad de nges gsang chos
'khor bskor/ /rgya nag gong ma ta ming chos rgyal gyis/ /snyan pa gsan nas gdan 'dren byung ba'i tshe/ /mkhyen rab chos rje'i lung bstan thugs bzhag nas/ /chos kyi 'od
zer gzhan phan cher dgongs nas/ /tshab tu btang bas rgyal pos ti shrIr bkur/ /gser khang nub kyi khrir bzhugs chos 'khor bskor/ /khyad du 'phags pa'i rten gsum du ma dang
/ /las zhwa 'dzam gling rgyan dang las gos la/ /padma stong ldan khyad du 'phags pa'i ber/ /gser srang lnga brgya las grub dam kha dang / /tshe srid la sogs ming 'dzin
bco lnga bskos/ /sa dkar dang mtshungs lung dang 'ja' sa gnang / /dpag par dka' ba'i longs spyod dang bcas te/ /'jam dbyangs chos kyi rgyal po'i drung du phul/ /de mthun
sne'u gdong nas gong ma'i lung / /ji bzhin bkur nas chos gzhis sogs kyang stsal/ /bla brang bco brgyad lcang lo can du grags/ /rdo rje 'chang dbang blo gros rgyal mtshan
dpal/ /mkhyen rab rje dang rje btsun kun spangs pa/ /tshar chen la sogs mkhas grub du ma yis/ /byin brlabs dam can sprin bzhin 'du ba'i gnas/ /kha'u brag rdzong nyid dang
dbyer med pa'i/ /dben gnas

sgom khang du yang gur mgon dang / /yum chen 'dod khams dbang phyug las mgon sogs/ /legs par bzhengs te rgyal ba'i bstan pa dang / /de 'dzin rnams kyi mgon skyabs srungs shig
pa'i/ /dam bsgrags 'og min zhing nas chos srung rnams/ /dngos su spyan drangs bstim par mdzad pa yi/ /las bzhi mtha' dag bsgrub pa'i phrin las bcol/ /sku zhang legs pa
mched la sras gnyis 'khrungs/ /bsod nams lhun grub khrir pheb chos 'khor bskor/ /gcung po lha dbang rdo rjes srid bskyangs shing / /de sras dang po 'dren mchog chos kyi
rje/ /mchog legs rdo rjes mkhas grub du ma bsten/ /gdan sar pheb ste dam chos rgya chen stsal/ /skal ldan 'gro rnams smin grol lam la bkod/ /gnyis pa rin chen dpal 'byor
gdung 'dzin pa'i/ /sras kyi thu bo bdag gi 'dren pa ni/ /mtha' yas shes bya'i chos kun mkhyen brtse'i gter/ /rab 'byams dkyil 'khor kun gtso he ru kaH /ngur smrig bstan pa'i
rgyal mtshan 'dzin mkhas pa/ /dpal 'byor bzang po'i gzi 'od cher 'bar ba/ /'jam dpal dbyangs dngos kun dga'i mtshan can gyis/ /kun mkhyen chen po'i mi 'jigs seng ge'i
khrir/ /mnga' gsol zab dang rgya che'i chos 'khor bskor/ /mtha' yas 'gro rnams sangs rgyas sar bkod de/ /mchog gi go 'phang brnyes nas phan bde stsol/ /byang chub sems rgyud
ldan pa'i rta mgrin dang / /lugs gnyis la mkhas sgyu rtsal ge sar la/ /'gran par nus pa'i dpa' bo tshe dbang dang / /rig sngags 'chang ba 'jam dbyangs pa dang bzhi/
/bar pa'i sras la rje dpon rin po che/ /dkyil 'khor rgya

mtsho'i dbang phyug ngur smrig 'chang / /'dod rgyal rnam sprul ngag gi dbang po mchog /gong ma'i rgyal tshab bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan 'dzin/ /phrin las lhun grub skal ldan rjes
'dzin byon/ /a ho ngo mtshar rigs kyi chu gter las/ /son pa'i mkhas grub yid bzhin nor bu'i phreng / /chos srid rgyal mtshan gtsug na mdzes pa 'di/ /skye rgu'i legs byas
dpal las gzhan du ci/ /mtho mtho'i rigs kyi lha lam yangs pa'i ngos/ /mkhas mkhas dam pa'i snang brnyan tsha zer can/ /mang mang rim par shar ba'i phrin las kyi/ /bzang
bzang mdzad pa'i gzi byin brjod las 'das/ /cha tsam mdzad pa rang rang rnam thar du/ /yod mod bdag 'dra'i blo gros ches rtul bas/ /mi shes ngal dub yi ge'i tshogs ches
pas/ /zur tsam brgyud pa'i nges khungs tsam du bkod/ /rnam dpyod rigs kyi lhun sdug gangs ri las/ /'ongs pa'i mes po'i chu klung dal babs rgyun/ /mi nyams bdag yid lus rten
'dzin ma ru/ /'khyil ba'i gtam rgyud blo ldan rna bar mdzes/ /zhes rigs rus kyi rgyu mtshan 'god rgyun 'dug pa ltar tshigs su bcad de nyung bsdus su bkod pa'i brgyud
pa de las byung ba'i bdag gi yab rje sbas pa'i rnal 'byor/ khu bo chos kyi spyan ldan gyi mched zla tha chung rim gnyis zab mo'i thugs dam gyis dus 'da' zhing / dbang bskur
ba dang 'gro don du gshegs pa na lha rnams kyis dga' ston du me tog gi char dang / 'ja' 'od kyi gur sogs ltas ngo mtshar ba dang / /lha 'dre gdug pa can rnams kyis gtsos
pa'i rigs la bden brdar gyis

thun brdeg cing / drag sngags dang rol mo'i sgra bsgrags pa tsam gyis 'byung po gzhan du yul 'bud nus pa/ sku gsung thugs rten la rab gnas mdzad pa'i tshe phyag nas dngos su
chags pa sogs ya mtshan gyi rtags du ma dang ldan pa'i sku zhang 'jam dbyangs dbang po dang / yum khri dpon phod mdo ba'i blon po'i rigs dpal stag lung pa chen po'i phyag
mdzod kyi brgyud pa dpon chen phreng stag pa'i sras mo/ /dkon mchog la gus shing yid gzhung pa gu ru sgrol ma gnyis kyi khye'ur gyur pa zhig yin 'dug cing / de'ang gang
las 'phos kyang skye ba zhig yin pa las 'os ma 'das kyang / gsung rgyun sogs las/ khu bo chos kyi spyan ldan gyi dbu bla/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po yab sras kyi dngos
slob/ /sngags 'chang sangs rgyas rin chen gzims khang gong du sgrub pa la bzhugs pa'i dus shig /yab rje 'jam dbyangs dbang po nyid kyi byon pas stan las bzhengs te spyan
hur gyis gzigs nas/ mdang rmi lam du bud med smug mo zhig byung nas/ khyod dag pa mkha' spyod du 'gro'am/ bco brgyad kyi dbon brgyud byed dre ba byung bas/ de ring khyod
'dir byon pa 'di rten 'brel legs byung gsung dges dges du ma mdzad cing zhi bar gshegs nas ring por ma lon par yum la khye'u yod pa'i rtags mtshan du gyur/ khog tu yod
pa'i tshe zhang po lags kyis/ gong ma chos kyi spyan ldan la brtag pa zhus par/ da lan brtag pa yang shin tu legs po byung / bstan pa la phan pa zhig 'ong / bar chad mi 'byung
bar 'dug lung bstan gnang zhing / yum la bka' dbang srung 'khor sogs brtse bas bskyangs/

chu bya lo zla ba dang po tshes gcig gi nam langs pa/ res gza' lha'i bla ma dang rgyu skar rgyal 'dzom pa'i 'grub sbyor bzang po'i thog a zhes pa'i sgra dang bcas te kho bo
btsas shing / btsas ma thag gong ma chos kyi spyan ldan gyis byin rlabs bka' bsgo dang / rim gyis tshe dbang / phyag rdor/ rta mgrin sogs kyi bka' dbang byin rlabs mang
du gnang zhing dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa stsal te/ mkhyen rab chos kyi rgyal po'i mtshan gyi thog ma de btags nas legs par 'dug gsungs nas ming ngag dbang rgyal mtshan du 'dogs
pa gnang zhing dgyes dgyes mdzad/ 'di lo chos gzhis dud bzhi bcu skor gyi sar bu bcu bzhi skyes pa dang / lo legs pa/ rdzing gi chu che ba sogs byung 'dug pas tshang
mas sku bsod che ba zhig 'ong 'dra gleng ba byung 'dug cing / byis pa'i dus 'tshe ba nyung zhing skyed che ba/ so rtse gsum du yod pa/ lce la as mtshan pa/ mthong na kun
gyi yid dga' ba zhig yod 'dug cing / cher longs pa na stan thog du bsdad nas thugs dam byed khul dang / rnga rol la dga' ba/ chos dang mthun pa'i spyod lam la 'jug pa zhig
yod 'dug gshis/ grogs rnams kyis 'di dpon slob sangs rgyas rin chen gyi sku skye yin nges su 'dug zer/ yab yum gyi 'phral gyi kun spyod dang / sku bstod kyi rim pa/ smon
lam rnam gsum sogs dang / klog slob pa mdzad/ lo drug lon pa na yab rje sbas pa'i rnal 'byor sku ltem nas bsnyun g.yog dang / bdun lon pa na yab gzhan don du gshegs par
bsngo ba zhu ba sogs mchod 'bul gyi tshul byas/ sa yos lo'i dgun gong ma chos

kyi spyan ldan khu dbon gyis slob gnyer du dgon par 'ong dgos tshul gnang ba bzhin/ byams mgon gnyis pa rong ston thams cad mkhyen pas chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba'i gnas shrI
nA lendra rnam par rgyal ba'i chos grwa 'ongs pas/ la chung nas dgon gnas mthong ba na thub pa'i dbang po'i gzhal med khang mthong ba ltar sa dang po'i dga' ba thob/ rim
gyis bla brang lcang lo can du slebs nas mkhyen rab chos kyi rgyal po'i dus chen dang 'grigs pas gong ma chos kyi spyan ldan khu dbon tshoms chen du bzhugs khrir pheb nas
tshang mar bzhugs gral dang ston mo gnang ba'i gral gyi mgor/ nged rang la stan mtho ba dang ston mo zab rgyas bcas rten 'brel du stsal zhing / de nas bzung gzims chung
steng shod du nyin mtshan khor yug tu bzhag nas/ phyi dro mang ma'i nang du gung song la rib tsam las chos spyod kyi rim pa dkyil chog skong ba sogs kyi dpe cha dang /
phyag bzhes kyi skor la 'jur skag che ba gnang bas/ nyin rer dpe cha mda' tshad lnga drug re rgyug phul zhing / phyis shog bu bcu lhag re zin pa byung bas shes rab che ba'i
grags pa byung / nub mo gnyid du ma song tsam gyi skabs nam mkha' na dur khrod bdag po yab yum gyis gar mdzad pa/ sngas kyi g.yas g.yon du ru 'dren sde bzhis 'cham byed
pa/ dpal ldan lha mo'i drel rta gwa dmar gyis rdul phyur phyur rgyug pa/ dpal mgon gyis mi rkang gi gling bu dgong re bzhin gtang ba zhig byung ba cung zad 'jigs nas rje
dbon rin po cher zhus pas/ nged rang gong ma'i sku zhabs su khrid 'di la gnod pa zhig yin nam/ dgong re mthong snang sogs

'di 'dra byung 'dug pas bka' bsgo byin rlabs gnang dgos tshul zhu ba gnang song bas/ gnod pa rang min nam gsung bka' bsgo dang byin rlabs rgyas pa stsal/ de'i rgyun zla ba
gnyis tsam gyi ring byung ba ni/ nged rang skye ba snga ma'i stobs dgon gnas su bsdad par chos srung rnams dgyes pa'i rnam 'gyur las gnod 'tshe sogs min pa 'dra/ 'di dag
gi bar rnams su gong ma khu dbon gyis dbus gtsang / khams stod smad/ a mdo/ sog yul sogs nas chos don gnyer du byon pa rnams dang lhan du/ dbang / khrid/ lung / rig gtad
sogs rgyun mar stsal ba rnams zhus// ! lcags 'brug lo'i dgun dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho'i dbang phyug gong ma chos kyi rgyal pos rgyun gyi dbang po'i 'du khang chen mor tshogs
chen du rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug 'jigs bral dpal ldan chos skyong gi bzhed gzhung gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i gdams pa/ dbang / khrid/ lung / man
ngag sogs yongs su rdzogs pa dang / lam zab/ bir srung / nA ro mkha' spyod rnams kyi byin rlabs rnams dang / ba ri lugs kyi sgrub thabs brgya rtsa'i rjes gnang / rgya gzhung
gi lung bcas stsal ba zhus// ! lcags sbrul lor tshogs chen du sa skya bka' 'bum gyi ljags lung yongs rdzogs dang / nged rang sku mched sogs kha shas la ngor lugs dkyil
'khor bdun sogs dbang khrid/ lung rjes gnang sogs du ma stsal/ na gzhon pas kun spyod spre'u'i mched zlar 'os pa zhig yod kyang / rje dbon rin po che nas zhi drag gis
'jun mthar brtse 'dzin gnang bas

mi gral du tshud tsam byung / lo 'di'i dgun nged sku mched byang khams sogs kyi don gnyer ba kha shas la zur chos mang du stsal ba zhus// ! chu rta lo'i dbyar tshogs chen du
sgrub thabs rgya mtsho rgya gzhung gi lung / /thig le bcu drug gi byin rlabs/ rje dbon rin po che nas pha chos/ bu chos/ ri chos/ kye rdor rgyud gsum/ brgyad stong / gzungs
bsdus sogs ljags lung mang ba zhig gnang ba zhus/ zla ba bcu pa'i tshes bcu res gza' phur bu dang / rgyu skar rgyal 'dzom pa'i 'chi med grub pa'i 'grub sbyor bzang po'i
nyin phyag mdzod du rgyal po chen po rnam thos sras kyi sgrub pa dgos 'dod 'byung ba'i zhal shes las byung ba bzhin sgrub pa gnang ba'i dbu btsugs te/ de nyin snga dro
nged rang la mkhan po yongs rdzogs bstan pa rin po che'i mnga' bdag gong ma chos kyi spyan ldan mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin dpal bzang po nyid/ las g.yog rje dbon ngag dbang
bstan 'dzin lhun grub dpal bzang pos gnang nas bar ma rab byung stsal te/ ming mkhyen rab ngag dbang lhun grub tu 'degs pa gnang / bco brgyad du 'jam dbyangs chos kyi rgyal
po'i khrir bzhugs pa'i gras su dbang bskur te shis brjod kyi phyag nas dang dga' ston rgyas par stsal/ sangs rgyas kun dngos dam pa khu dbon gyis/ /bstan la phan dgongs
rab tu byung ba stsal/ /dam pa'i khrir bkod 'dod rgu'i char 'bebs pa'i/ /rnam thos bu la phrin bcol shis brjod mdzad/ /dgos med tshe 'di'i bde skyid rmi lam tsam gyi bde
bas ci zhig bya/ /'dod yon la sogs 'khor ba'i phun tshogs dgos med dug gi sdong por mthong / /

shAkya'i sras kyi rjes 'jug ngur smrig rgyal mtshan 'dzin pas bdag yid 'phrogs/ /de phyir tshe 'di'i phun tshogs bzhi mdo'i rtsa bzhin dor nas bstan la zhugs/ /yang yang rnyed
dka'i dal 'byor rten bzang 'di/ /legs legs rgyal ba'i sras kyi rjes 'jug par/ /mdzes mdzes thun mtshams gos kyis bklubs pa 'di/ /bzang bzang sngon bsags legs byas mthu
las grub/ /sgrub pa'i zhabs phyi'ang zla gcig gi ring zhus/ gong ma khu dbon la chos srung gi phrin las dngos su grub pa'i rtags gtor khang gsar bskrun gnang ba'i rgyal
mtshan gyi tog rnam sras kyi sprul pa'i btsun pa gzhon nu zhig gis phul te gar song cha med du song ba dang / gzhan yang dgos 'dod 'byung ba nas bshad pa'i ltas khyad par
can du ma'ang byung song zhing / gtor ma'ang deng sang gi bar ma rnyings par bzhugs pa ni dam pa gong ma'i thugs rjes nged rang la 'dod yon rgya cher 'phel nas bstan pa
la phan pa'i rtags su snang // ! chu lug lo'i dbyar mkhar gdong nas nged rang dang / /zhang po lags bcas par a ma lags gzhis kyi khur ma lcogs shing / /chos gsha' ma zhig
byung na bsams pa gong ma khu dbon la dgongs pa zhu rogs kyis gsung byung ba bzhin/ /gsol ba btab pas thugs dgyes pa'i tshul dang bcas 'dod sbyar gnang zhing / gong ma
rin po che nas bar ma rab byung kyang stsal te rin sdings su btsun ma rnams kyi mgor gzhug pa nas bzung thugs dam 'phel bas ma Ni dung phyed gnyis tsam song 'dug /lo 'di
nang du gzhung sa chen po'i

mtshan jus kyi nyi ma shar bas bstan 'dzin chos kyi rgyal pos bod khri skor bcu gsum phul te lhar bcas 'gro ba'i skyabs mgon/ rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen pa chen po'i bka'i
'khor lo 'dzam gling kun khyab pas lugs gnyis kyi sgo nas skye 'gro rnams bde skyid rdzogs ldan la 'gran bzod pa gnang ba'i legs 'bul dang / dgon ma lag chos gzhis bcas
kyis rigs sngar lugs bzhin 'jags pa'i gtan tshigs rin po che zhu bar gong mar khu dbon pheb skabs nged rang rin sdings la dpe mtshams su a ma lags kyi sar sleb don bzhin
bsdad/ khams gsum 'gro ba'i mgon po'i rigs brgya'i khyab bdag chen po dang mchod yon nas sngar babs la gzigs pa'i lugs gnyis kyi spyan rgyang bdag rkyen dgon ma lag chos
gzhis dang bcas pa 'jags gnas kyi gtan tshigs/ sku ber sogs bla chas rgyas pa/ gser dngul/ ja/ gos dar/ gser sga/ rta sogs kyi gnang sbyin bka' drin bskyangs te phyir pheb
pa dang mjal/ lo 'di'i dgun khams 'grul ba kha shas 'byor ba dang / a ma lags kyis lam 'bras kyi bka' chos bka' drin bskyangs dgos tshul zhus par brten rdzong shar gyi
'du khang du tshogs chen la gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i gdams pa rgyu lam gyi dbang bdag med ma'i byin rlabs/ lam zab dang / bir srung phyi ma/ pod
sngon ma'i lung bcas gnang ba thob cing / snang gsum gyi skabs grang dmyal gyi lo rgyus kyi chos thun stsal skabs dgong mo rmi lam du grang dmyal gyi gnas su slebs

nas sems can du ma sdug bsngal gyis gzer ba rmis pas gnyid sad pa na 'jigs shing / zhag bcu skor gyi ring yid mi bde bas mchi ma 'khrugs pa dang nges 'byung gi snang ba skyes/
rgyu dbang skabs su 'ja' li'i steng du gong ma nyid dgyes mdzad rdo rje he ru ka yab yum du mthong bas dga' bde dang dad gus kyi spu long g.yos shing / de nas bzung bla
ma 'di rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas dngos yin snyam pa las khu bo dang mi phal pa'i snang ba skad cig kyang mi 'char/ lam zab gnang skabs dpal ldan bla ma dam pa de nyid rje
btsun sa skya pa chen po'i sku'i rnam pa bzhugs pa chos thun de ma rdzogs bar mthong zhing / 'di dag gi skabs nam mkha' la 'ja' dang / sum rtsen pa rnams kyis me tog gi
char yang yang 'bebs par 'dug /nged sku mched dang / ra ba smad slob dpon pa sogs kha shas kyis gsol ba btab pa'i ngor lam zab dang / bir srung nang ma/ bla ma rin 'byung
/ tshar gsum khug pa/ sgrub pa lung sbyin/ brda chig brgyud/ lam sbas bshad/ brda don gsal ba/ rnam 'joms bir lugs/ mgon rkyang gi rjes gnang sogs thun mong ma yin pa rnams
dang / pod nag ma'i lung bcas gnang / dpal ldan sa skya pa'i chos srung kun gyi gtso bo dpal rdo rje nag po chen po gur gyi mgon po lha lnga ma dang / brgyad ma/ bcu
gnyis ma rnams kyi dbang dang / phyi nang gi khrid/ me 'bar ma dang snyan brgyud pu sti'i lung / pho rkyang / mo rkyang / sbags sgrub rnams kyi

rjes gnang dang lung sogs stsal zhing / gnyan mgon zhal bzhi pa'i bsnyen dus/ sgrub dus/ gsang sgrub dkar po tshe 'phel rnams kyi rjes gnang / gsang khrid dang be'u bum ha
la nag po kha skong dang bcas pa'i lung sogs sngags 'chang sangs rgyas rin chen dang / mkhas grub snying rje bzang po las gsan pa'i mgon po che chung gi chos skor rnams stsal/
lo 'di nang du gong ma sku mtshams la bzhugs pa'i zhabs phyir nged rang phyag na rdo rje 'byung po 'dul byed kyi bsnyen mtshams la bsdad pa'i tshe/ skabs shig rmi lam
du gong ma chos kyi rgyal po nyid 'byung po 'dul byed du gyur pa'i thugs ka nas/ rigs gsum mgon po byang chub sems dpa'i tshul spros pas/ de dag gi sku las kyang 'od zer
dpag tu med pa spros pas nged rang la re ltos bcas pa'i mdo khams/ rgya bod/ sog po sogs kyi 'gro ba rnams thar pa'i zam par 'dren pa'i tshul zhig byung ba/ nged rang
ltos bcas dpal ldan bla ma dam pas rjes su 'dzin pa'i brdar go zhing / de nas khu dbon gyi slob dpon ltar tshe kun rnam gsum/ tshe dbang / rta mgrin/ phyag rdor sogs 'phral
dgos rnams nged rang nas gyis gsung pa ltar rim par byas/ tshogs chen la sgrub thabs brgya rtsa sogs kyang bshad pas grwa rigs tshang mas dga' mo 'ong 'dra zer mgu ba'i
lugs byed 'dug /lo mjug dpal sa skya pa chen po bdag chen mthu stobs dbang phyug chibs kha bsgyur ba'i chibs bsu ser sbreng sogs gnang song zhing / pheb 'phral bdag chen
bco brgyad du gdan

'dren gnang ba'i tshe nged rang gi mgo thog tu phyag bzhag nas byin rlabs yun ring por gnang zhing dgyes dgyes mdzad/ de nyin tshe dbang grub rgyal ma dang / o rgyan gyi bla
ma'i rnal 'byor stsal song ba'ang thob/ bdag chen rin po ches gong ma chos kyi spyan ldan gyi drung du bka' dbang rdo rje phreng ba gsan ring / nyin re bzhin phyag dbang
zhu bar phyin par dpe cha'i 'dzin mtshams sogs dri ba gnang bar shes rab la thugs dgyes pa'i tshul mdzad/ phar chibs kha bsgyur skabs lugs gnyis kyi sgo nas bstan pa la
phan pa dgos tshul gyi zhal ta dang phyag mdud byin rten sogs gnang sbyin kyang sger du stsal// ! shing sprel lor jur jid kyi rgyal po'i mchod gnas bla ma kun dga' rin chen
gyi g.yog bal khu dpon g.yog dang / nged rang gi 'bul dpon chog thuX bla ma dpon g.yog sum cu skor 'byor zhing / gong ma khu dbon gyi zhabs phyir nged rang bcas lhan
du gser dngul gos dar sogs 'bul ba rgya cher mdzad/ 'di lo nas gong ma chos kyi spyan ldan nyid sku na smin pa'i tshul bstan pa bcas lha sngags ye shes kyi rol pa'i sku'i
gcad rgyar bzhugs kyang / chog thu bla ma dpon slob rnams khag ches bas sku mtshams khog tu gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras kyi gdams pa rnams rdzogs pa dang / pod dmar
ma sogs lung gi rigs mang du stsal song ba'ang thob cing / rje dbon rin po che nas kyang tshe rta/ phyag rdor/ 'byung 'dul sogs rjes gnang kha shas/ kun rig /tshe dpag lha

dgu/ rnam 'joms sogs dbang gi rigs stsal ba rnams thob/ de dag gi bar skabs su brtag gnyis/ sdom gsum/ rgyud sde spyi rnams sogs dpe cha sbom che ba'i rigs la bltas shing /
gong ma khu dbon la rgyug 'bul kyang zhus/ 'jam dbyangs dmar ser/ dkar po/ gshed dmar rnams kyi bsnyen pa byas/ gong ma chos kyi rgyal po nyid sku mtshams dang / rje dbon
rin po che'ang lugs gnyis kyi thugs 'gan bzhes dgos dang / sku gzugs ma thang ba bcas kyi stabs sgom khang sogs dgon lag so sor dbyar chos dgun chos la phyin pas so so'i
'dod pa bzhin dbang / rjes gnang / khrid kyi rigs/ 'dzugs gtor brje ba/ dus mchod le'u tshan sogs sngar rgyun bzhin chag med byas/ phyogs 'gro phal cher la'ang nged rang
nas phyin/ skabs shig dam pa so chung gi slob ma rdo rje bkra shis kyi gnas rin sdings su a ma'i sar bsdad pa'i nub gcig rmi lam du/ nam mkhar 'ja' 'od kyi dbus na 'phags
pa rin po che las zhwa mchod pa zhig mthong bas dad pa dang dga' spro tshad med pa zhig skyes/ 'jam dbyangs nag po'i bsnyen pa zla ba gcig gi ring gong ma'i slob dpon
ltar byas// ! shing bya lor 'od zer bla ma dkon mchog rgyal mtshan dpon slob rnams pheb/ khong gis gsol ba btab pa'i ngor dpal ldan bla ma dam pa de nyid dkyil 'khor so so'i
gtso bor bzhengs te/ rdo rje phreng ba dkyil 'khor bzhi bcu zhe gnyis/ kr-i ya'i

dkyil 'khor gsum bcas zla ba gcig gi ring stsal ba thob cing / bde mchog dril bu pa dang / 'jigs byed ro langs brgyad skor sogs zur bka' du ma dang / phreng ba skor gsum/ rgyal
sras bka' 'bum sogs lung mang ba'ang thob/ dbyar rje dbon rin po ches dbus nged chos zhu ba sum cu skor la rje btsun nA ro mkha' spyod ma'i byin rlabs/ zab khrid/ rdzogs
rim/ cha lag rnams dang bcas pa/ bla ma gzugs kyi dpal bas mdzad pa'i chos skor dang / yig cha phyi ma rnams dang bcas pa'i lung indra dang mai tri mkha' spyod kyi gtsos
dmar mo skor gsum sogs tshar lugs thun mong ma yin pa'i gser chos rnams kyi rjes gnang dang byin rlabs/ lung gi rigs kyang du ma zhig stsal/ skye ba snga ma'i stobs
'di skabs rje btsun rdo rje rnal 'byor ma la mos gus shin tu che bas bla ma sangs rgyas dngos 'di lta bu la gdams ngag thun mong ma yin pa 'di thob nas gdams pa 'di la g.yeng
ba thams cad spangs nas nyams len rtse gcig tu bya snyam pa yod kyang / phyis zin med chu gnyer lta bu'i g.yeng bas 'dod pa bzhin ma grub/ 'on kyang khrid zhu ba'i skabs
der/ dad gus dung dung byas pa'i tshe bla ma rje btsun mar gsal lam lam mthong ba dang / rmi lam du bla ma rdo rje chos 'od du zhu nas rang la thim pa sogs byung bas
rje btsun mas rjes su 'dzin par dgongs pa zhig yin 'dra bsam/ ston a 'dus sku mched gnyis sogs

a mdo'i 'grul pa mang ba dang / kre bo e khe dpon po dang / tsha ba bla ma a 'bum sogs o rod nas 'khor ba'i 'grul pa rnams dang / tshogs chen du rje dbon rin po che nas sbyong

gnang dang lung sogs 'dod chos mang bar byas/ ! me khyi lor cho 'phrul gyi zla ba nas tshe dpag lha dgu/ rnam 'joms/ mgon po brag rdzong ma/ rta mgrin skyer sgang lugs
kyi bsnyen pa rnams byas/ dbyar spo bo bla ma don gnyer du byon pa dang lhan du rnam sras rigs chen brgyad/ rab brtan ma'i thun mong dang / thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang
sogs chos skyong skor gyi dbang dang bka' gtad kha shas thob cing / nged rang nas kyang nyer mkho kha shas kyi dbang lung byas/ ston sgam bde nas skyi rtsa bla ma ngag

zhing / tsha ba bla ma tshe dbang grags pa sogs 'grul ba mang tsam 'byor bar/ gong ma'i sku zhabs nas chos 'brel tsam dang / nged sku mched kyis 'dod chos dgos pa rnams
so so'i 'dod sbyar byas/ lo mjug gi dus chen khag dang gtor zlog sogs kyang rgyas par gnang song / me phag lor rje dbon rin po che nas tshogs chen du rnal 'byor dbang phyug
bi rU pa'i bzhed gzhung gsung ngag

rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i dbang / khrid/ byin rlabs/ glegs bam dang / pod dmar sogs lung rnams dang bcas pa rgyas par stsal ba zhus/ sems bskyed gnang ring bzhugs
khri'i steng 'phags pa rin po che lta bu'i sku'i snang brnyan las zhwa chos gos mchod pa/ sku sngar las gzi 'od 'bar ba/ tshul khrims kyi dris tshogs khang khyab zhing
/ phung po gsum pa'i mdo'i phyag 'bul skabs tshogs kyi rdul yang ldang bar mi nus pa kun gyis mthun par rtogs shing / nam mkha' las lha rnams kyis 'ja' 'od kyi gur phub
cing me tog gi char phab pas/ tshang ma dad gus kyis mig nas mchi ma 'khrug cing / lus kyi ba spu g.yo bas thal mo sbyar te dad gus sngar bas kyang che bar gyur/ rgyu dbang
gi dngos gzhi'i nyin sku'i g.yas phyogs su rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor yod pa'i bar snang du sprul pa'i dkyil 'khor gsal lam bar mthong zhing / dbang rdzas 'grims par
pheb pa'i tshe tshul khrims kyi dri bsung sna lam du ngam ngam byung bas sems la bde bar 'char ba zhig byung ba ni nged mched zlar song bas tha mal gyi snang ba dgag phyir
tshul de ltar gnang ba yin 'dug cing / bla ma 'di dgyes mdzad rdo rje dngos yin snyam pa'i mos gus dung dung pa yod/ chos ra grub nas rje dpon rin po che 'gro ba lha dang
bcas pa'i skyabs mgon rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen gzigs chen po dang / sa dbang chen po'i mjal kha zhu bar pheb/ nged gong ma'i gzims chung phyi mar mtshams la bsdad
nas kun rig gi bsnyen pa sbyin sreg dang bcas

pa dang / tshe dpag grub rgyal lugs dang / khyung khra/ seng gdong ma rnams kyi bsnyen pa zhig kyang byas/ ston khal kha nas gser pa shAkya dang / tshul khang dbon po gnyis
'khor ba dang / a 'bol kun dga' rin chen gyi grwa pa kun dga' mgon po dpon g.yog rnams byung nas/ sil sbubs/ dngul/ gos dar sogs kyi 'bul dpangs mtho ba byas shing / khams
'grul ba mang tsam byung bar gong ma chos kyi spyan ldan gyi zhal mjal dang / dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho'i dbang phyug dbon rin po che nas dgyes mdzad rdo rje'i bka' dbang
dang / gu ru zhi drag /gur zhal/ rnam sras/ lha mo'i rjes gnang sogs stsal song ba thob/ nged rang nas kyang tshe kun/ rnam rgyal ma/ rnam 'joms sogs kyi dbang lung 'dod
sbyar byas/ dgun dus mchod khag dang / mgon khang so so'i gtor ma brjes nas chos skyong rnams kyi bskang brgya rnams gnang ba'i zhabs phyi zhus// ! sa byi zla ba dang po
nas grub thob tshe dpag dang / gur drag /gshed dmar rnams kyi bsnyen pa byas shing / gur drag gi skabs dgong mo kha cig 'jigs zhum me ba dang / grib gnon byed pa zhig byung
bas gong ma rin po cher zhus pas rgyal po'i gnod pa yin 'dra/ sde brgyad gzhan las rgyal por gzir tsam gyis gsung bka' bsgo gnang / bka' bzhin byas pas 'tshubs zhi zhing
/ nub gcig rmi lam du ye shes mtsho rgyal yin snyam pa'i bud med gzhon nu ras gos ljang gu gyon pa zhig gis tshogs 'di gsol zer nas tshogs 'khor gyi sna bsdus pa sder
gang dang / bdud rtsi

thod pa gang byin par rmis/ gong mar zhus pas rtags shin tu legs pa byung 'dug gsung dgyes tshor gnang / de nas dbyar chos gnang ba'i zur chos su sgrub thabs rgya mtsho dang
/ tshe kun/ rnam 'joms/ gur drag sogs dbang rjes gnang gi rigs mang tsam byas/ sa sbug tu dmar khrid zla ba gcig tsam byas/ sgom khang du dbyar chos la tshems bu lugs kyi
khrid dang tshe khrid sogs byas/ ston dgon gnas su khu dbon gyi zhabs phyir bsdad/ dgun chos gnang ba'i zur chos su sbyong rgyud sogs dbang dang rjes gnang gi rim pa dang
/ gtor gzhi spo ba/ bskang ba brgya rtsa'i rim pa/ dus chen gyi ser sbreng sogs kyi zhabs phyi zhus// ! sa glang lor zla ba dang po'i nang du bde mchog dkar po dang /
tshe dpag med lcags sdong ma'i tshe sgrub/ mgon po brag rdzong ma'i bsnyen pa 'bum phrag bcu drug pa zhig dang / seng gdong ma'i bsnyen pa 'bru 'bum dang bcas pa slob dpon
zhu khyad gzims chung rab gsal du byas par/ bla ma bzhugs sa dang nye ba'i byin rlabs kyis khri mthon por bsdad pa dang / nyi zla 'char ba/ 'bras bu'i rigs kyis snod bkang
nas ster ba sogs dang / dar 'phyar ba/ dung 'bud pa sogs rmi lam du byung ba rnams zhus par dgyes pa'i tshul so so nas chos zhu ba byung ba rnams la slob dpon gnang
ba bzhin dbang rjes gnang khrid lung sogs byed pa dang / yon bdag gi 'dod kha bskang ba'i phyir mchod dbur 'gro ba/ sku gsung thugs kyi rten bzhengs pa tshor rab gnas byed
pa/ byang zhu ba rnams la gzims chung phyi mar byang zhu byed pa sogs

'phral gyi sne len rnams byas/ gtor spod/ bskang ba/ dus chen sogs char chen gyi rigs kyang zhabs phyi zhus/ lcags stag lor zla ba dang po'i nang du dkon mchog spyi 'dus tshe
sgrub dang bcas pa/ tshar lugs 'jigs byed phyag gnyis pa/ rgya mtsho nas gsung pa'i 'jam dpal rdo rje gtso rkyang / sgrol dkar rnams kyi bsnyen pa dang / dbyar sgom khang
du sgrub mchod/ bskang ba/ dmar khrid/ gcod khrid sogs byas/ ston nA lendra'i gtsug lag khang mgon khang chen mo'i thog gtsang khang gi bskor lam/ rung khang chen mo
spyi mdzod sogs kyi zhig gsos la gong ma chos kyi rgyal po khu dbon gyis bslab ston stsal ba bzhin klu kha stod nas dga' mo bar grong tsho rnams la dbang sbyin dang / dge
bskul la dpon slob mang tsam phyin pas lung pa sa lugs su dad zhen che ba dang / gong ma khu dbon gyi thugs rjes phyin pa tsam gyis dad gus kyi snang ba 'gyur te khrom shin
tu che ba dang / mig nas mchi ma 'khrug bzhin du phyag 'tshal ba/ smre bshags bya ba/ smon lam sogs 'ur dir byed cing nyin re bzhin grong tsho rnams su dbang sbyin dang
/ dgong re bzhin gtso che ba rnams la gur drag /rta mgrin/ mgon po sogs dbang / rjes gnang / bsngo ba/ byang bu/ rab gnas sogs gang 'dod kyi re ba bskangs shing / sbyin
bdag dpon khag dang gzhi gnyer yul grong tshang mas dar ras/ snam bu/ sha /mar/ phyugs che chung sogs shin tu mang ba dang / nas sran yul bre'i khal stong dang brgyad brgya
lhag tsam byung ba bla ma dang mchog gsum dgyes pa'i mchod sprin du phul zhing / dmigs yul shi gson gyi gtsos sems

can thams cad la 'khor gsum yongs dag gi smon lam btab/ yul tsho kha shas la hor tshong pa 'dug pa nas sems can du ma zhig srog bskyabs pa dang / ngan slong rnams la'ang sbyin
gtong ci nus byas/ rigs brgya'i khyab bdag khu dbon gyi sku zhabs su 'byor skabs dad gus kyi ba spu g.yo bzhin pas phyag btsal zhing / byin rlabs zhus pas mgo thog tu
dbu dang phyag gnyis sbrags ma'i byin rlabs yun ring por gnang zhing dges dges mdzad/ rje dbon gong ma'i zhabs drung du stan mtho bcas/ nged dpon slob rnams la gzhi len
zab rgyas gnang zhing dri ba bka' drin bskyangs par skyabs gnas khu dbon gyi thugs rjes legs po byung tshul gyi rgyu mtshan dang / dngos po rnams tho dang bcas phul bar/
dbon chung gi thog mar 'gro don la byon par 'bul ba shin tu rgya che ba 'di rten 'brel legs shing / slad nas phrin las rgyas pa 'ong 'dug gi bslab don stsal/ de 'phral tsha
ba dbu mdzad chos rgyal mtshan dang / sku tshab gsol dpon bsod nams grags pa gnyis la dad rdzas rnams gtsug lag khang gi zhig gsos las chud mi za bar dgos pa'i bslab don
bcas rtsis sprod dang zhig gsos kyi ljags bkod gnang song / dgun smad dus mchod sogs la sngar rgyun bzhin zhabs phyi zhus// ! lcags yos lor rang ston dang / sgra mi snyan
pa'i tshe sgrub gnyis bdun phrag re bslab ston ltar byas/ gzhan ma gong ma rin po che sku ltem pa'i zhabs phyir bsdad/ se ra nas 'od zer bla mas 'phags pa rin po che'i
thugs dam rten gur mgon 'khor bcas kyi

sku rdo nag las grub pas gtsos rten dang mchod cha/ gser/ dngul/ rta/ dre'u/ mdzo/ khal sogs 'bul ba shin tu che bar phul/ nged da lan dus kyi 'khor lo'i bka' dbang dang /
gzhan 'dod chos kha cig zhu 'dod la brtse 'dzin bka' drin che dgos tshul zhus song bar/ zhu ba po'i ngor dang / nged rang la dgongs nas zhal bzhes gnang / rje dbon rin po
ches kye rdo rje'i rgyu lam sogs chag med rnams dang / nged rang la sgrub thabs rgya mtsho dgos gsung ba thugs 'dod ltar zhus/ de nas gong ma chos kyi spyan ldan dpal dus
kyi 'khor lo'i skur bzhengs te rgyu skar bdag po lha drug brgya so drug gi dkyil 'khor du bdag po chen po'i dbang dang bcas pa rdzogs par gnang / mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho/
dril bu lus dkyil gyi dbang dang / thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang gi rigs kha yar stsal/ de skabs rje dbon rin po ches gong ma sku rten pa bcas brtag pa zhig mdzod/ 'od
zer bla mar gsungs song bar bka' bzhin zhu/ mar me legs pa zhig dang / 'bru gtsang ma zhig dgos zhus song ba bzhin gnang / phyir nyin 'ur ba'i tshul dang bcas gong ma rin
po che skye 'chi la rang dbang thob pas bzhugs mi bzhugs khong rang gis mkhyen/ 'on kyang nged rang dpon slob rnams kyis brtan bzhugs rgyas pa zhig 'bul dgos 'dug /rje
dbon rin po che la sku dog shin tu che bar 'dug pas sku rim du bka' 'gyur/ 'bum brgya/ shir snying 'bum gter/ phyogs bzhi'i gtor ma sogs sku rim mang ba gnang dgos 'dug
zhus song zhing / nged rang la gzigs nas dbu la rdo

brgyabs kyang mi 'chi/ khyed khu dbon gyi mjug zin pa 'ong gsungs/ brtag pa rnams zhus song / lugs gnyis kyi sgo nas tshim par mdzad de rang gnas su byon/ 'di lo sa gsum skye
rgu'i gtsug rgyan rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen pa chen po rgya nag pho brang nas spyan 'dren pa byon pa dang lhan du 'u du su nas nged rang gi 'bul dbon da rgan chos rjes
'bul skyel ba rdzong bda' byas pa dang / bi lig tu nang so gser mgon sku gnyer bla ma kun dga' rin chen gyi grwa pa rnams kyis bskur ma che tsam 'byor/ gser dngul gos
dar sogs kyi 'bul ba gya nom pa 'byor/ gong ma'i mjal kha khyug tsam btang zhing / der rang sku mched kyis dbang rjes gnang sogs 'dod chos dang tshogs bsngo kyang byas/
rtse gdong nas khri chen gong ma chen po pho brang du pheb rdzong 'bul bar pheb/ de zhor nA lendrar chibs kha bsgyur bar nged rang sku mched nas chibs bsu/ ser sbreng / gzhi
len zab rgyas zhus/ khri chen bco brgyad du gong ma chos kyi spyan ldan gyi drung du pheb/ gzims chung gi sgor pheb bsu mdzad/ rtse gdong nas na bza' cha tshang gis gtsos
dgu tshan gsum stsal zhing / nged sku mched la'ang sku skyes dang / nged rang gi las tshan so sor kyang gnang sbyin bka' drin bskyangs/ snga dro'i ring gzims chung du
gsung gleng rgyas pa gnang zhing / gong spyi'i 'phral phugs kyi snyan 'bul kyang zhib tu gnang song / nyin bstar ja zhus la ngos 'gro sogs skabs sbyar byas/ 'dus pa rgya
mtsho'i tshogs dbur thams cad mkhyen pa rong ston chen po'i bzhugs khrir

'jam mgon khri chen rin po che spyan drangs te/ gser dang / dngul gyi maNDal/ gos dar/ ja/ rta sogs kyi 'bul ba rgya chen po phul/ bstan 'gro'i phan bde spel phyir bsngo smon
gyi rgyas 'debs smin rgyas bka' drin che bar stsal/ tshogs chen du tshe dbang dang / 'jam dbyangs dmar ser sogs kyi chos 'brel stsal zhing gtsang du chibs kha bsgyur/
nged rang gis rgyal nang bar chibs skyel la phyin/ dges pa chen pos phyag mdud byin rten dang gnang sbyin stsal/ rje dbon rin po che'i zhabs phyi/ bla khag /las tshan rnams
kyis zhus nas pho brang chen por pheb rdzong 'bul bar pheb/ nged rang gis gong ma'i sku zhabs su bsdad/ tsha ba bla ma dpal ldan 'od zer gyis gtsos 'grul pa mang tsam
dang / nyag bre nas a hrang bla ma'i 'bul skyes ba 'byor pas sne len gang drag byas/ ! chu 'brug lor gong ma rin po ches sku skyom me ba zhig bsnyun gyin yod pas sku mtshams
bcad rgya dam par gnang / thugs dam nyams bzhes kyi rim pa ni khor yug chag med du nyams su bzhes pa ni gong ma nyid kyi rnam thar du gsal ba ltar phal gyi blo yul du
chud par dka' ba zhig go /rje dbon rin po ches ljags bkod gnang ste sku rim du tshe gzungs 'bum ther/ tshe chog stong rtsa/ bka' 'gyur/ 'bum rtsa thon tshar bcu tsam dang
/ gser 'od/ gzungs 'dus/ kun rig cho ga stong rtsa gsum/ rnam rgyal stong mchod/ sher snying 'bum ther sogs tshogs chen gyi dbyar ston gnyis sgor re ba zhig sgrub pa dang
/ chos lung nas grub pa'i dbang phyug chos grub dpal bzang spyan drangs/ tshe dbang

sogs 'bul ba dang / nA lendra dang / dgon lag so sos zhabs brtan phul zhing / 'phen yul gyi dgon che phra tshang mar mang ja/ bsngo rten rgya che ba dang / gdugs dkar/ sher
snying sogs sku rim gyi slob dpon gnang zhing / bco brgyad rang du bskang ba gsung sgrogs sogs sku rim gyi rigs nar mar bsgrubs shing / gtso bor rje dbon rin po che nas
gsol ba 'debs pa gnang bar/ nyid skye 'chi la rang dbang thob pa bdag sogs gdul bya rnams dang / bstan pa dang sems can thams cad kyi don du zhabs pad yun ring por brtan
pa zhig bzhugs dgos zhes u tshugs kyis zhu ba gnang song ba'i stabs/ gzhan don du dgongs bzhes kyang je 'gyang du song / ston a li chos rje kun dga' bzang po dpon g.yog sum
brgya skor 'byor bar bsu ba dang / gzhi len sogs kyi ljags bkod dbon gong mas gnang ba bzhin nged rang nas bsgrubs/ gtsang la ma byon gong nged sku mched kyis tshe rta/
phyag rdor sogs chos 'brel kha shas byas/ de skabs gzims chung rab gsal du gur drag gi bsnyen pa kha gso zhig gyis gsung byung ba ltar bdun gsum gyi mjug tshogs brgya zhig
kyang bslab ston ltar zhus/ 'di skabs gnyid gzir re ba zhig la gshag skor gyi steng du rta ri bong tsam la/ bande khru gang pa chos gos dang / bse theb gyon pa/ mig shin
tu che ba khra 'bur re ba sdang mig tu blta ba/ phar rgyug tshur rgyug byed pa zhig mthong byung ba/ re zhig nas bande smug po che ba zhig tu gyur te mtshams khang du
'ongs nas nged rang la mtho mtshams par

lha'i nga rgyal dang bcas sngags bzla bzhin pas lag pa g.yon gyis yun ring du bzung zhing g.yas kyis bsnun pas phag gi skad ngan lta bu mang du 'don 'dug pa/ mjug tu snying
rje'i sems kyis btang bar gar song cha med du song / phyi nyin snyan 'bul zhus par khyod la rgya 'dre'i gnod pas mi tshugs pa'i rtags su 'dug gsung / mtshams grub nas gong
ma sku rten du song 'dug pa'i zhabs phyir bcar sdod byas shing / nangs gcig snga bar gong ma grub thob lugs dang mthun pa'i tshe dpag med kyi sku 'od zer dang bcas pa
zhig mthong bas mos gus bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig skyes shing / da zhabs pad yun ring du brtan pa zhig 'ong 'dra bsam zhing / tha mal gyi gdul bya'i snang ngor zhing gzhan
du gshegs pa'i tshul las don gyi tshe dpag med yin par dngos su bstan 'dug /nub gcig rmi lam du nam mkharazla ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi nang du thams cad mkhyen pa sa skya
paNDi ta phyag gnyis chos 'chad kyis pod ral bsnams pa/ zhabs rol stabs/ chos gos rnam pa gsum dang / sa zhu'i lag gnyis sku pang du brkyang ba/ sku mtshar zhing 'dzum pa
dang bcas/ bdag la gzigs shing 'od zer gyi drwa bas phyogs kun khyab pa zhig mthong bas phyag dang mos gus byed pa byung / phyi nyin gong mar zhus pa shin tu legs/ 'chad
nyan gyis phan thogs 'ong / su la'ang ma zer gsungs/ yang sku rim du chos sgrogs dang / gtor zlog /rnam 'joms/ sme brtsegs sogs kyi sku khrus dang / zhabs brtan gyi rigs
mang ba zhig bsgrubs kyang zhal bzhes ngos gzung tsam las cher mi

gnang zhing / chos skyong gur zhal/ rnam sras/ rab brtan ma rnams la gtor bsngo brgya rtsa/ bka' sdod ltar sgrub pa'i ljags bsnyen dang / bskang ba phrin bcol sogs gang rgyas
nyin re bzhin gnang ba dang / khyad par rab brtan mas zhing 'dir bzhugs su gsol bar/ de bzhin thugs la ma babs pa'i rtags brngan pa'i tshul du bskang ba stong tshar gnang
'dug pa ni phyis kyi grwa pa dang / bla brang brgyud par bcas par phrin las sgrub shig pa'i bka' bsgo yin 'dra/ yang nyin gcig nged la bslab ston la spyir gyi sa skya
pa'i bstan pa dang / nA lendra khyad par bco brgyad kyi bstan chus gzhis dang bcas par 'dzin skyong sogs dgos pa'i bka' nan che ba dang / yang bstan pa'i 'dzin skyong dgos
brtse gdong zhabs drung dbon rin po che dang khyed gnyis la rag ces bslab ston gnang byung ba ni/ rje dbon rin po che bzhugs bzhin nged la gnang ba rje dbon rin po che'am
zhabs mi brtan par dgongs pa'i bslab ston du snang / tshe chog /chos 'don sogs sku rim gyi rigs mang bar bsgrubs/ grub pa'i dbang phyug chos grub dpal bzang spyan drangs
te bka' dbang / gtor zlog gi rigs/ dbon rin po che dbus tshang mas zhabs brtan mang bar phul/ lo de'i zla ba bcu gnyis pa'i tshes bco brgyad kyi nyin nged rang mthong
smon la mchod dbur phyin pas/ nam mkha' 'ja' tshon gyi gur dang / me tog gi char sogs ltas ngo mtshar ba mthong bar sems mi dga' zhing 'tshubs pa zhig byung bas mgyogs myur
log ste bla brang du 'ong pas/

zhabs phyi ba rnams kyis de ring snga dro gzhan don du dgongs grabs gnang zhing / nyid yod med kyi rtsad gcod gnang byung bar song tshul zhus pas/ re zhig bzhugs par zhal gyis
bzhes byung zer/ de 'phral sku zhabs su phyin pas byin rlabs dang / shin tu dges pa'i tshul gyis bslab ston brtse bas bskyangs pa ni byang chub bar du rjes su 'dzin pa'i
rtags su 'dug /de nas rje dbon rin po che'i bslab don bzhin sku rim dang / zhabs brtan la brtson par zhus kyang / nyer lnga'i nyin ya mtshan pa'i ltas du ma dang bcas
te sku mdun du 'khod pa rnams kyang yid mi bde ba med par mos gus dung nge bar byin gyis brlabs te/ rje dbon rin po che dang / nged sku mched lhan du zhal gdams bsdus tsam
dang / de nas nged la spyi dang bye brag gi bstan pa'i 'dzin skyong sogs kyi skor zhib par stsal zhing / phyag thal mo sbyar te pha mkhyen rab chos kyi rje pheb byung
gsung bzhin par 'ja' dkar po gzims khang thog tu zug cing / 'ja' kha dog sna tshogs pa'i rigs mang ba dang / me tog gi char sogs ltas khyad par can du ma dang bcas te dag
zhing du gshegs so/ /de nas bzung dbon rin po che'i bslab ston ltar gong ma de nyid kyi dgongs pa chos kyi dbyings su rdzogs thabs kyi rim pa'i grabs byed khul byas kyang
/ spyir dam pa 'di nyid kyi thugs rje dang mdzad pa gang la bsams kyang rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas dngos dang / nye ring dgra gnyen mchog dman thams cad du byang chub kyi
sems rgyud kho nas brlan cing bstan pa dang 'gro ba'i dpung gnyen dam par gyur pa dang /

lhag tu rang nyid lugs gnyis kyi sgo nas sku drin gzhal du ma mchis shing thugs brtse ba chen pos dus nam yang mi 'dor ba zhig yin gshis bzod thabs dang bral ba'i sems ngal
shin tu che bar gyur to/ /kye hud 'jigs rung 'khor pa'i chu mtsho las/ /sgrol ba'i ded dpon rigs brgya'i bdag po de/ /'og min zhing du gshegs tshe bdag sogs 'gro/ /mi bzad
'khor ba'i mtsho las su yis sgrol/ /'on te mos gus mchog gis thugs yid zin/ /zab rgyas gdams pa rgya mtsho'i bka' drin thob/ /rang sems bla ma'i ngo bor 'du 'bral med/
/ji ltar byas kyang bde ba khyod kyi drin/ /de tshe yid 'ong lag 'gro'i tshogs rnams dang / /'chi med gzhon nu'i mchod sprin sna tshogs kyis/ /lha lam dog por byas pa'i
me tog char/ /dbang po'i gzhu ris tshon gyis ci yang bris/ /gzhal med yid bzhin dam pa'i gdung / /rim gyis zag med phal cher yal/ /lo lnga'i khye'u'i tshad gyur pa/ /dgyes
rdor ngo bor sreg mchod phul/ /e ma 'bral med rjes 'dzin brdar/ /zab gsal chos kyi dbyings nyid las/ /rje btsun chen po'i sku bstan nas/ /mjal tshe dad gus spu long g.yos/
/de nas dbon rin po che'i bslab don ltar kye rdor dang / kun rig /bla mchod sogs kyi sgrub mchod/ nA lendra gtso bor gyur pa'i 'phen yul khul gyi dgon pa che chung thams
cad spyan drangs te mchod 'bul gyi rigs rgya che bar bsgrubs/ sku gdung rin po che rim gyis yal te khye'u lo lnga tsam du gyur pa dgyes mdzad rdo rje dang

dbyer ma mchis par kye rdor gyi sgo nas dpon slob kha shas kyis sri zhus zhugs su phul bas yid bzhin gyi nor bu lta bur rtsol ba la ma ltos par gdung ye shes kyi me rang 'bar
du gyur/ zhag bdun nas gdung khang zhal phye ba na/ gdung rus rnams kyang phal cher yal nas bre gang tsam lus pa sku dang / yig 'bru/ ring bsrel gyi phung bor gyur/ rje
dbon rin po ches rigs brgya'i khyab bdag rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen pa chen po rgya nag tu chibs kha bsgyur gshis/ mchod 'bul gyi rten rnams sde srid sku zhabs su 'bul
ba dang / de kha'i gnas tshul rgya nag la sku zhabs rin po cher snyan 'bul zhu grogs mkhyen zhu ba dang / sde srid sku zhabs mjal ba/ jo shAka gis gtsos gtsug lag khang
rnams dang / ser 'bras sogs la mchod 'bul du pheb/ gzhung sa chen po nas kyang gnang sbyin gzhan dang mi 'dra ba stsal 'dug cing / tshur pheb 'phral sa skya nas 'bri gung
bar gyi bla chen khag so sor mchod 'bul gyi rten rnams sgrig pa gnang nas 'bul mi rnams rdzong bda' gnang ba sogs dgongs rdzogs kyi rim pa ji snyed du sgrub pa'i zhabs
phyi zhus/ ! chu sbrul lor rje dbon rin po che gsung 'cham sku tshad du song bas shin tu sku ltem pa nor rgyas drung 'tsho ba bos/ 'phrod bsten zhus/ sku rim du bka' 'gyur/
zlog pa/ sher snying khri tshar/ chos srung rnams la bskang ba brgya tshar re/ 'phen yul khul gyi dgon che phrar mang ja/ zhabs brtan sogs shin tu grul bar zhus kyang
bstan dang bdag sogs 'gro ba yongs kyi bsod nams las

ma grub pa'i/ nged la gong ma chos kyi spyan ldan gyi dngul gdung sogs rten bzhengs dang / dgongs rdzogs kyi rim pa/ dgon pa'i 'dzin skyong sogs zhib par bka' gnang nas/ gong
ma chos kyi rgyal po'i drung du pheb bzhed kyi zla ba gsum pa'i tshes nyi shu'i nyin nam mkha' nas sgra shin tu che ba 'od dkar po nub tu rgyug pa dang bcas gzugs sku
chos kyi dbyings su thim pa'i tshul bstan/ bdag cag rnams ci bya gtol med du gyur te gdong mchi mas khengs pa dang / la la dran med du brgyal bar gyur to/ /dam pa'i rgyal
tshab rje dbon rigs brgya'i bdag /gzugs sku bde chen zhing du bsdus pa'i tshe/ /bdag la lugs gnyis bslab cha'i zhal gdams stsal/ /'od dkar sgra dang bcas te mkha' la byon/
/skyabs gcig thugs rje'i 'od stong ldan pa de/ /chos dbyings nub ri'i phag tu gzims pa na/ /mos gus ze'u 'bru rgyas pa'i chu skyes bdag /mya ngan gdung ba'i sems kyi 'dab
ma zum/ /de ltar khu dbon zung gi dgongs pa'i mtha'/ /mtha' bral chos kyi dbyings su rdzogs pa'i ched/ /ched du kun bzang mchod pa'i sprin phung du/ /du mar yid kyi sprul
dang mngon sum bsgrubs/ /de nas tshang ma gros dang bcas te sku gdung rin po cher chas zhugs phul te/ me tog /spos/ mar me brgya phrag du ma dang / maNDal/ bla bre/
'phen/ gdugs/ rol mo sogs mchod pa'i bye brag mthong ba tsam gyis yid 'khul ba bshams/ bla ma sangs rgyas la gsag sbyang ga la dgos kyang gdul bya rnams

bsod nams gsog pa'i phyir/ kye rdor ba bcu gcig /kun rig pa bco lnga/ bla ma mchod pa dang bcas zhag bzhi bcu zhe dgu'i bar/ bla ma dkyil 'khor gyi gtso bor bzhugs pa la mchod
pa phul/ zhag gsum song ba'i thog tshogs chen gyis kun rig gi sgrub mchod gnang bar/ bla khag so sor 'bul ba dang / dge 'dun rnams la bsnyen bkur gzabs par byas/ sku
tshigs rnams la 'phen yul gyi dgon chen khag rnams re re dang / chung ba rnams gnyis gsum sogs gdan drangs nas mchod 'bul zhus/ nged rang ngos kyi lha sar sde srid rin po
che'i sku zhabs su mjal rten dpangs mtho ba dang / gong sa chen por mchod 'bul rten thugs rje chen po sems nyid ngal bso'i sku brnyan gyis gtsos rol mo sogs mchod cha'i
rigs dang / bla bre bum gdan ma/ gos dar/ khrab gser gzhung ma sogs go mtshon gyi rigs/ rta/ ja sogs 'bum dpangs mtho ba phul zhing / rgya nag tu rigs brgya'i khyab bdag
rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen gzigs chen por snyan 'bul zhu ba gnang dgos tshul zhu ba bcas mchod 'bul la phyin par sku zhabs su gdan bzos dang gnas tshul gyi dri ba bka'
drin bskyangs pa gnang / nged rang lo chung bas dgon chos gzhis grwa rigs sogs la 'dzin skyong dka' ba 'dug pa brtse 'dzin gnang dgos pa'i snyan 'bul zhus par/ sku skye lta
bu sgug dgos pa ni min/ khyed rang bla ma brgyud pa'i rim byon gzhan dang mi 'dra zhing / khyad par gzhung nas mig rgyang dgos pa yin pas sngar rgyun ltar brtse 'dzin
'ong zhing / gang sar sngar las ma g.yos par mdzod gsung pa'i bslab

don bka' drin bskyangs shing / zur gsos dpangs mtho ba stsal/ jo shAka rin po ches gtsos rten gsum rnams la snyan dar/ spos/ zhal zas/ dkar me bcas mchod 'bul rgyas par bsgrubs/
'od khar ko 'ja' dang sbrags pa'i gnang sbyin gos rgyan bzhi'i ber/ pang khebs/ gan dkar/ gser sga cha tshang / rta sogs bla chas cha 'grigs dang / gos dar/ phrug ras/
ja 'khor drug lnga/ mar khal brgya sogs dgu tshan bdun dang / za dam nas 'bru khal sum brgya'i bka' 'dzin bcas lho brag lha khang nas gnas tshang du byon nas bslab don
rnams zhib tu stsal bas tshang mas 'gran med lta bu'i bka' drin bskyangs/ gtsang du 'gro ba'i lam yig kyang stsal/ bsti gnas su 'byor nas dbon gong ma'i sku gdung rin po
cher dar ras la dri bzang byugs te na bzar phul/ gzims chung du bye stems zhus te mchod pa rgyun ma chad par phul/ gong ma'i gdung thal bsres pa'i birWa pa/ sa chen/ sa
paN sogs bla ma'i sku/ kye rdor/ 'jigs byed/ gshed dmar sogs yi dam du ma/ ston pa dang byams pa/ tshe dpag med sogs sangs rgyas kyi sku/ rigs gsum mgon po sogs byang chub
sems dpa'i sku khri phrag tu nye bar gser gyi na bza' gsol ba dang / tshe dpag med kyi sku spar ma rgyug mtho re tsam yod pa nyis brgya dang bcu gsum la ring bsrel re
bzhugs par gser btul ma zho brgya dang drug cu re gcig song / a li chos rje dpon slob rnams gtsang nas 'khor/ sbyong dkyil dang tshe dpag med kyi dbang / sgrub thabs

brgya rtsa sogs rjes gnang gi rigs rnams thugs 'dod ltar byas/ bla khag /gzims khang / las tshan khag dang bcas bgros te thams cad mkhyen pa rong ston chen po'i chos kyi khrir
sdod dgos tshul gsung pa bzhin bsdad de/ bdag cag gi ston pa/ gnas brtan bcu drug gi rjes gnang byas shing / tshogs chen gyi khri 'bul ci nus kyang mdzad/ 'di kha'i gang
ci'i 'dzin skyong dang / gshegs rdzong gi mjug rnams gcung rin po ches gnang nas/ nged rang dpon slob bco lnga skor byang lam brgyud gtsang du phyin/ thog mar gdan sa
chen po rtse gdong du khri chen byams pa bsod nams pa sku mched khu dbon rnams dang mjal/ rten mchod/ gos dar/ ja/ rta sogs kyi mchod 'bul rgyas par phul/ tshogs su mang
ja rten mjal rnams zhus/ lugs gnyis kyi bdag rkyen brtse bas bskyangs/ sa skyar bgrod pa'i lam du mtha' 'dul gyi gtsug lag khang gtsang 'gram bye ma lha khang mjal/ snyan
dar dang mchod pa rgyas par phul/ gser mdog can du paNDi ta chen po shAkya mchog ldan gyi dngul gdung rin po cher snyan dar/ mkhan por bsngo rten/ tshogs su mang ja bcas
zhu mi btang / rim gyis bskyod pa gzhis rtser slebs pa rdzong nas zur gsos dang / bzan shing gi bdag rkyen/ bkra shis lhun por paN chen thams cad mkhyen pa mjal/ mchod
'bul dpangs mtho ba zhus/ bdag rkyen dang gnang sbyin gzabs pa gnang / gnas mjal rgyas par zhus/ zhwa lu dang / e wa~M chos ldan gyi rten gtso che ba rnams su snyan dar dang
/

bla khag so sor mchod 'bul dang / tshogs su mang ja zhu mi rdzong bda' byas/ snar thang gi gtsug lag khang mjal bar phyin/ snyan dar dang mchod pa phul zhing / sa lugs kyi
grwa tshang la grwa ja zhus/ chu mig gtsug lag khang du snyan dar dang mchod pa phul/ me 'bar gyi gtsug lag khang dar lung gnyan du phyin/ snyan dar mchod gtor rgyas par
phul zhing phrin bcol zhus/ zho ma la brgyud phyin te gdan sa chen po mthong bas lus kyi ba spu ldang zhing dad gus kyi dga' ba tshad med pa skyes/ gzhi thog tu gtugs pas
gnas tshang zhig tu zur chas gya nom pa dang bcas skyel ba gnang / gong bzhugs khams gsum chos kyi rgyal po'i mjal kha dgos tshul zhus par/ phyag mdzod nas deng sang sku
shin tu ltem pa zhig yod pas mjal kha mi 'ong 'dra'ang snyan 'bul zhu zer/ zhag gsum song ba'i tho rangs kyi rmi lam du nged rang bco brgyad bla brang du 'dug par/ mi zhig
byung nas gong ma chos kyi spyan ldan mjal bar shog zer bas zhing brjes kyang mjal rgyu yod khul gyi bla brang gi rgyab lcang rar phyin pas/ ne'u gseng yid du 'ong ba
ljon shing dang me tog gis brgyan pa'i dbus na/ seng ges btegs pa'i rin po che'i khri/ padma/ nyi ma/ zla ba'i gdan la rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan sku mdog
dkar la dmar ba'i mdangs chags pa/ zhal 'dzum bag dang ldan pa/ phyag g.yas mi 'jigs pa'i phyag rgya dang / g.yon pas bdud rtsi khol bzhin pas gang ba'i thod pa dkar po
bsnams pa/ 'ja'

'od kyi gur dang / me tog gi char 'babs bzhin pa dang bcas pa mjal zhing / phyag 'tshal/ byin rlabs zhus pas/ phyag g.yas skyabs sbyin gyi phyag rgya dang bcas bdag gi mgo
thog tu bzhag nas/ dbon chung byon pa e yin gsungs pas dga' spro dang sems la bde ba tshad med par gyur tshe/ rje nyid ni ma bzhugs/ rje btsun rin po che dang mjal snyam
pa'i mus la gnyid sad/ nyi ma rtse shar la mgron gnyer byung nas gong bzhugs mjal du shog zer byung bas/ rje gong ma de nyid dang / sngags 'chang bla ma gnyis rje btsun rin
po che grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis slar yang bstan 'gro'i don du sprul pa'i zlos gar bstan par gdon mi za bar mngon zhing / phyag dbang dang mchod 'bul gyi rten la sku
gsung thugs rten/ gser dngul gyi maNDal/ sil sbugs/ gos dar/ ja ras/ rta sogs 'bul ba shin tu bzang ba dang bcas yab sras mjal bar phyin pas/ gzhi thog gi tshom dmar du 'phags
pa rin po che'i bzhugs khri'i steng du bsnyun mi mnga' ba'i tshul du bzhugs/ sku mdun du gdan bzos che ba'i khar bsdad/ dgyes pa chen po'i 'dzum bag dang bcas gsol
ja gsum gyi ring dri ba dang 'phral phugs kyi bslab don bka' drin bskyangs shing / sde srid sku zhabs su snyan 'bul zhu rgyu'i ngag ma bslab don kyang stsal/ thams cad mkhyen
pa sa skya paNDi ta dang 'jam dbyangs dbyer med kyi bla ma'i rnal 'byor dang / 'od dpag med kyi snang ba bsgyur ba'i 'da' kha ma gnang zhing zhag bcu skor zhig bslab
ston bzhin bsdad/ de'i ring bdag

rkyen gzhan dang mi 'dra ba stsal zhing gdung brgyud rin po che 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang phyug la mchod 'bul gyi rten rnams phul te mjal kha zhus/ rab 'byams pa bkra shis
kyis sna shen mdzad de dbu rtse nas bzung lha khang thams cad du snyan shal spos sogs dngos 'byor yid sprul gyi mchod 'bul rgyas par zhus/ sgo rum du bse 'bag mjal bas
sku bong shin tu che zhing / zhal snum bag che ba zhig tu mthong / pu tra'i bla mtshor yang snum dwangs pa lta bu'i nang nas las mgon gyi zhal smug nag khro zhing brjid
pa/ dbu skra thor cog byas pa zhig mthong / lha khang chen mor mang ja dang / mkhan por mchod 'bul gyi rten kyang phul/ dkar po rgyang grags mjal/ lha khang so sor snyan
dar mchod pa gang rgyas phul zhing bstan 'gro'i don du smon lam yid tshim pa btab/ sgrol ma lha khang mjal/ sems dpa' sum brtsegs la snyan dar 'phangs ba thugs ka'i thad
du bsdad song ba phrin las rgyas pa 'ong 'dra bsam yid bde ba'ang byung / mchod 'bul smon lam yang dag byas/ kha'u/ khru ma/ byas 'gyur rnams mjal bar phyin/ snyan dar dang
/ mchod 'bul rgya che ba dang / bstan 'gro'i don du smon lam btab cing bsam gling du phyin pas sku gnyer mi 'dug pas sgo drung du ci drag bsams pa na/ sgo rang byer gyur
te mjal kha dang / snyan dar mchod pa sogs smin rgyas dang / sa lam gyi bar chad zhi thabs smon lam btab ste gzhi thog tu 'khor/ phyi nyin ston mo rgyas pa dang / gong
bzhugs kyi dbu zhwa/ sku gzan/ dam rdzas khri rdo/ stong rdo/

brgya rdo dang / bcu rdo gsum re/ sil bu mang ba/ 'gag rings/ gzan sham/ dar ras/ snam bu/ bur ltong sogs gnang sbyin gya nom pa stsal/ phyi nyin mgron gnyer dpon g.yog gsum
gsol ja dang bcas glang po ri'i bar skyel bar gnang / de nas bsnyen rdzogs zhu ba'i gza' skar stabs myur 'gros kyis rtse gdong lhun po rtser sku zhabs su sleb/ mjal kha
phyag dbang rgyas par stsal/ phyi nyin zla ba bdun pa'i nyer gnyis kyi nyin res gza' lha'i bla ma dang rgyu skar rgyal gyi 'grub sbyor bzang po'i nyin gyi snga dro'i cha'i
grib tshod rkang pa gnyis kyi dus su mkhan po yongs rdzogs bstan pa rin po che'i mnga' bdag 'jam mgon chos kyi rgyal po don gyi slad du mtshan nas smon te byams pa bsod
nams lhun grub bkra shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ las kyi slob dpon thub bstan rnam par rgyal ba'i mkhan rin po che bstan pa'i gsal byed dam pa gnas lnga yongs
su rdzogs pa'i paNDi ta chen po chos dkar rnam rgyal/ gsang ston gnas brtan 'dul ba 'dzin pa dpon slob rin chen sgang pa/ dus bsgo ba dbu mdzad bstan 'dzin/ kha skong
sogs dge 'dun grangs tshang ba'i dbus su 'jam mgon chos kyi rgyal po rim byon gyi rgyal bstan nyin mor gsal zhing / lugs gnyis mdzad pa'i phrin las phyogs brgyar 'gyed pa'i
gnas dpal rtse gdong srid pa gsum las rnam par rgyal ba'i chos sde chen po'i bla brang lhun po rtser bsnyen par rdzogs pa dge slong gi sdom pa thob ste 'dul ba 'dzin
pa'i gras su gyur to/ /yid 'ong padma'i rdzing bu nyams dga' bar/ /ring nas spro ba'i ngang mo

'jug pa ltar/ /rmad byung thub pa'i bstan gyis yid drangs nas/ /bshes gnyen dam pa'i drung du bsnyen par rdzogs/ /'phags pa'i yul du sde pa rnam bzhi'i nang / /che khyad 'phags
pa yod par smra ba'i lugs/ /kasmi ra pa'i paN chen shAkya shrI/ /grwa sar zhugs nas ngur smrig bla gos gyon/ /grogs dag dal 'byor ldan pa'i rten bzang 'di/ /dgos med
tshe 'di'i 'du 'dzis ma g.yengs par/ /bag yod khrims ldan ngur smrig 'chang ba 'di/ /bgrang yas bsod nams bsags pa'i 'bras bur nges/ /chag med kha gso'i dbang byin rlabs
rnams zhu bar thub bstan rnam par rgyal ba'i chos grwar mkhan rin po che thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang brtan pa'i rdo rje'i sku zhabs su phyin/ stabs 'gros su song gshis
dge 'dun rnams chos ra nas dbu zhwa mchod de ser phreng gi tshul mdzad/ spos bsu dang bcas te bla brang du 'byor 'phral thams cad mkhyen pa chen po'i sku zhabs su phyin
pas/ bzhugs khri nas sa gdan gyi steng du pheb 'dug par phyag dbang zhus te gdan bzos bzhugs stan dang mnyam par 'dug par nan gyis sdod gsungs pas bsdad/ dges tshor gsung
gleng rgyas par mdzad/ de dgong kye rdo rje'i rgyu dbang gi sta gon tshugs/ phyi nyin dngos gzhi dang lam dbang rgyas par stsal/ bdag med lha mo bco lnga'i byin rlabs/
lam zab phyi nang / bir srung phyi nang / sgrub pa lung sbyin/ brda chig brgyud/ brda don gsal ba rnams kyi byin rlabs/ ga ya dha ra nas brgyud pa'i mgon rkyang gi rjes gnang
rnams stsal/ sgrub

pa lung sbyin gyi skabs sku bong dang gzi brjid shin tu che bar mthong zhing / tshe'i tshad/ slob ma gtso che ba'i grangs/ phrin las sogs kyi lung bstan gsal bar stsal ba bzhin
phyis thog tu khel/ nyin re bzhin gzhi len/ 'ong khar tshe dbang dang gnang sbyin rgyas par stsal te gzims chung gi sgo'i bar skyel bar gnang / dad gus kyi mchi ma 'khrug
cing mos gus kyis 'ong mi phod pa lta bu'i ngang nas phyir log /rtse gdong du dbon rin po che 'jam dbyangs bstan 'dzin dbang po sku mched kyis rdo rje gzhon nu'i sgrub
mchod gzabs spros kyi sku 'cham gnang bar ltad mor shog gsung / legs 'bul dang bcas phyin/ ston mo gzabs par gnang / gdan sa gzhan dang ma 'dra bas gzi byin che zhing
thugs gra 'grigs par 'dug la/ yab bdag chen rin po ches bsgral las gnang skabs rtags khyad par can byung song / zhag kha shas bsdad/ so sor chos 'brel re zhus/ lugs gnyis
nas brtse bas bskyangs te phyir log /mar lam yangs pa can du gnas mjal la phyin/ mkhan por bsngo rten dang / tshogs su mang ja/ snyan shal/ mchod pa bcas gnas mjal rgyas
par zhus/ gzhi len kyang rtsal/ rim gyis bskyod pas nged rang gi chos gzhis bkra shis sgang du slebs/ phyi nyin gcung rin po che 'phags pa nye bar 'khor slar byon pa lta
bu'i mkhas zhing btsun pa'i dbang phyug dam pas gtsos bla khag dang / dbu chos/ mi sna sogs kyis bsu ba bcas shrI nA lendra rnam par rgyal ba'i chos grAr slebs/ gzims khang
sogs so so nas gzhis len dang legs so'i gter sbyin byung /

pho brang chen por sde srid sku zhabs su mjal khar phyin par 'phral tu mjal kha bka' drin bskyangs shing sku mdun du nye bar bzhag nas dri ba zhib tu gnang byung bar bka' len
rgyas par phul zhing / khyad par sa skya'i gong bzhugs sku ltem tshul dang / bslab ston gnang ba rnams gang legs kyi snyan 'bul nan chags pa ngos kyis zhus te/ mgron khang
du ston mo zab rgyas/ gos dar/ rta sogs kyi gnang sbyin dpangs mtho ba bka' drin bskyangs/ sa skya'i lha khang mkhan rin po cher dgongs khrel gyi zhu sgug la yun ring
thogs pa gsum skas mgor bzhugs 'dug pa dang mjal/ snyan 'bul dang bslab ston sogs gnas tshul dang / da cha mgyogs tsam thon pa 'dra zhus shing / zhag bzhi lnga tsam nas
dgongs pa dwangs shing phyir log pheb chog pa byung 'dug /rang gnas su 'byor/ nged rang dgyes mdzad rdo rje'i bsnyen par bsdad/ rig pa hur phyung ste brtson 'grus chen pos
nyams su blangs pas bla ma rnams kyi thugs rjes lus sems bde zhing bag pheb la/ lha sngags ye shes kyi rol pa'i ting 'dzin 'phel ba zhig byung zhing bsnyen pa'i ring mkhas
btsun grub pa'i dbang phyug gcung rin po ches 'phral dgos kyi dbang chos sogs lugs gnyis kyi 'gan bzhes gnang / zla ba brgyad nas kha skong la sbyin sreg zhag bdun dang
/ chos skyong rnams la gtang rag gi bskang ba brgya tshar re phul nas/ ! shing rta lor zla ba bzhi pa'i stod du mtshams grol/ nged rang mtshams la bsdad thog khams gsum
chos kyi rgyal po rgyal dbang thams cad

mkhyen gzigs chen po rgya nag pho brang nas chibs kha bsgyur ba bka' drin bskyangs pa'i pheb lam 'phen yul du gnang bar/ theg chen chos kyi rgyal po rgya nag nas pheb pa'i
pheb bsur g.yag rong gnyis kyis pheb pa'i gnas/ g.yag rong gdong du nA lendra nas gcung ngag dbang bstan 'dzin gyis gtsos bla khag las tshan grwa rigs dang bcas pa bzhi brgya
skor gyis ser phreng rgyas pa dang / pheb bsu'i rnam pa sogs nged rang gi ngag bkod ltar zhus 'dug cing / mjal rten gyi 'bul ba dang phyag dbang zhu bar khyed rang dpon
slob rnams dga' ldan chos 'khor du byon zhes bslab ston pheb pa bzhin dga' ldan chos 'khor nas mjal kha phyag dbang / bka'i dri ba sogs rgyas par stsal te dges dges gnang
zhing / de kha khungs btsun pas phyag dpe tho bkod byas pa bzhin lha sar skyel mi thong / bka' drin che 'dug ces gnang sbyin/ mang ja/ 'gyed sogs gzhan dang mi 'dra
bar bka' drin bskyangs shing / dgon gnas su log 'phral nged mched kyis bslab ston gnang ba'i phyag dpe rnams 'bul mi btang bar/ nged rang la bka' shog bslab ston zhib pa
dang gzan gyi gnang sbyin bcas gnang / bang chen du 'gro mir chas ka gnang sbyin sogs kyang brtse bas bskyang 'dug /'di skabs gong ma khu dbon ma bzhugs par tshor bas sgom
bde nas skyi rtsa bla ma/ wa shul nas tshul khang bla ma bsod nams/ nyag bre nas 'bul skyel sogs mdo khams nas 'grul pa tshan che tsam 'byor/ bco brgyad du/ ja/ rta/

dre'u/ mdzo sogs kyi rtsis sprod dang / tshogs chen du nged rang bos nas 'bul ba/ mang ja/ 'gyed sogs sgrub par/ nged rang nas kyang dmigs med 'khor gsum yongs dag gi bsngo
smon byas/ tshogs chen du grub chen brgyad cu rtsa bzhi dang / sgrol ma nyer gcig gi chos ra byas shing / sde srid sku zhabs su gong ma khu dbon gyi dngul gdung re bzhengs
bsams pas bal po dang / phog yon sogs kyi bslab ston zhus par/ bal po lnga 'phral gnang dang / phog yon sogs gzhung sa'i deb la 'di bzhin yod kyang / 'phar tsam byas na
'gab sogs bslab ston stsal zhing / shing bzo ba nged rang gi yon bdag bi lung pa dang / brag dbar sgung po che ba gnyis bos te shing dang dgos cha/ bal po rnams la'ang
rgyu cha gang dgos sprod de/ tshul khang bla ma bsod nams dang / gsol dpon bsod nams grags pa gnyis kyis do dam byas te las gra btsugs/ bzo dbyibs rnam rgyal dang byang chub
mchod rten du bzhengs pa'i bkod pa byas par/ shing bzo dngos gtsang zhing btsan thag pa bcas ma 'gyangs par shing bzo ba rnams grub bstun/ gos dar/ ja ras/ khro/ phyugs
sogs gla yon gang zab bcas rdzong bda' byas/ bal po rnams la phog dang / bar skabs su ston mo bcas kyis mgu bar byas shing / che ba thog tshad kyi rgyu rtsar lha nyag
gis zangs khal bco lnga/ dngul srang lnga brgya/ gser zho brgya dang

brgyad cu gya gnyis/ phra rgyan du me shel lnga/ chu shel gcig /shel 'ja' tshon ma bzhi/ g.yu bye ru mu tig sogs rgyan mang ba/ dngul chu bcas dgos cha gang dgos dang / chung
ba der lha nyag gis zangs khal bcu gcig /dngul srang sum brgya/ gser zho brgya dang drug cu/ phra rgyan du me shel gsum/ chu shel gsum/ 'ja' tshon ma gnyis/ g.yu/ bye
ru/ mu tig /dngul chu sogs rgyu cha phun sum tshogs pa sprod pas legs par grub cing / bal po rnams la'ang gla yon rtsis gzhi'i thabs la ma ltos pa'i 'phar bcas gser dngul/
gos dar/ ja ras/ rta phyugs sogs kyis tshim par byas te rdzong bda' byas/ gza' tshes dge bar nang gzhug gi bkod pa bsgrigs te/ che ba'i nang du khams gsum dbang sdud 'dod
pa'i rgyal po'i rnam sprul dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho'i dbang phyug rje dbon rin po che'i sku gdung byin rten dang / dri bzang sbags pa'i dar ras sogs kyi na bza' gsol te
nang rten gyi gtso bor gzhug /gzims dpon bla ma kun dga' blo gros grogs bcas kyis phyag bstar te/ ring bsrel rnam pa bzhi tshan che ba dang / rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi
ring bsrel/ gong ma chos kyi spyan ldan gyi gdung rus/ ring bsrel/ gdung tsha mang ba/ rgya bod kyi mkhas grub du ma'i gdung / ring bsrel/ dbu lo/ phyag sen/ na bza'/ rje
nyid kyi na bza' cha tshang / gzhan yang sku gsung thugs rten byin rlabs can kha shas dang / gser dngul sogs rin po che

mang ba/ dar sna/ 'bru sna/ sman sna sogs/ gnod sbyin bang mdzod 'khor lo dang bcas pa ngor chen rdo rje 'chang gi phyag bzhes ltar kho bo dpon slob brgyad kyis zhag bdun gyi
bar du bsgrubs pa bcas nang gzhug phyag len dngos gtsang ba phul te 'gro ba'i bsod nams kyi zhing du bzhugs pa dang / chung bar nang gzhug gong ma chos kyi spyan ldan
rigs brgya'i khyab bdag chen po'i sku rus las rang byon ring bsrel gyis gtams pa du ma dang / gdung tshA/ sbur ras/ rgya bod kyi mkhas grub chen po rim byon mang po'i gdung
/ ring bsrel/ dbu lo/ na bza'/ dam rdzas/ sku gsung thugs rten byin rlabs can mang ba/ gong ma nyid kyi na bza' cha tshang / zhal dkar bzhes spyad/ gsol sder sogs dang
/ rin po che'i rigs/ nor sna mang ba/ gnod sbyin 'khor lo snga ma ltar bsgrubs pas 'gro ba'i mchod sdong chen por bzhugs su gsol te dpal dgyes mdzad rdo rje la brten pa'i
rab gnas nub gsum nged dpon slob bzhi bcu skor gyis gza' tshes dge bar grub ste mthar phyin par byas so/ /rigs brgya'i khyab bdag zung gi gdung rten mchog /'gro kun bsod
nams gsog pa'i zhing sa ru/ /bzo dbyibs rnam rgyal byang chub mchod rten tshul/ /zung ni byin rlabs 'dus pa'i phung por bsgrubs/ /sku rgyu rin chen gser dngul las grub
pa/ /khyad 'phags rin chen sna tshogs phra yis spras/ /gzungs gzhug rab tu gnas pa la sogs pa/ /rang gis lag bstar gus pas sri zhur byas/ /lhag bsam cha shas rdzogs pa'i
'od dkar can/ /

dad brtson bsil bu'i shugs kyis rab drangs pa'i/ /legs byas rgyu skar bdag po bsil zer gyis/ /'gro kun phan bde'i padmo bzhad gyur cig /gza' tshes dge bar rgyal ba ma pham
pa'i rnam sprul thams cad mkhyen pa rong ston chen po'i chos khri la 'khod de gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i gdams pa btsugs pas chos sde chen po'i bla
ma grwa rigs sbyin bdag dang bcas pa rnams gong ma chos kyi rgyal po khu dbon gyis chos srid kyi bstan pa 'dzin pa la 'gran zla dang bral ba zhig 'ong 'dug ces gleng ba
dang rab dga'i sa thob pa ltar byed 'dug /ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub kyis/ lam gyi rtsa ba smin byed dbang dang 'brel/ /lam gyi snying po bskyed rdzogs nyams len brgyan/
/lam gyi dngos gzhi brjod bral lta ba mtho/ /lam mchog 'di 'dra shes na kun mkhyen nye/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar dus gsum sangs rgyas thams cad kyi bgrod pa gcig pa'i lam/
skal ldan rnams smin grol byang chub la 'god pa'i thabs mchog /stobs bcu'i mgon po 'jigs bral dpal ldan chos skyong gi bzhed gzhung / rje btsun bdag med mkha' 'gro'i zhal
drod ma yal ba/ gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i gdams pa yongs su rdzogs pa/ snang ba gsum gyi dus bla ma rnams kyi rnam thar gyi lung rdzogs pa/ chos
spyod kha shas/ gtor ma brgya rtsa sogs kyi lung / brgyud pa'i khyad par gnyis ldan gyi sems bskyed/ slob ma rjes 'dzin dang / bsnyen pa kha gso byas te/ dbang gi mngon
par

rtogs pa bdun dang ldan pa'i sgo nas rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bzhi yongs su rdzogs pa/ rgyud gsum gyi khrid kyi rigs glegs bam dang / pod dmar ma gnyis kyi lung
/ nang bskyed rim gyi sngon 'gror lus kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba/ gsang dbang gi sngon 'gror mkha' spyod gtso mo'i sindhu ra'i dkyil 'khor du byin rlabs/ bir srung
/ lam zab kyi khrid sngon du 'gro ba'i byin rlabs/ thun mong ba grol dbang la grub thob chen po'i lugs kyi tshe dbang bcas grub pas thams cad kyi blo'i re ba yongs su gang
bar gyur to/ /de 'phral chos sde chen po dpal ldan 'bras sbungs su rigs brgya'i khyab bdag rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen pa chen por phyag dbang zhu ba dang / po ta lar
sa dbang chen po'i mjal khar phyin/ sde srid sku zhabs kyi mjal kha zhus/ bslab ston ltar 'bras spungs su mjal kha phyag dbang rgyas shing / dri ba zhib tu stsal/ mgon po
phyag drug pa'i dbang bzhi byin rlabs kyi tshul tshar chen gyi yig cha'i thog nas smin rgyas stsal/ gnang sbyin dpangs mtho ba bka' drin bskyangs te lha sar 'byor/ thon
phyag zhus/ bdag rkyen gzhan dang mi 'dra ba bka' drin bskyangs te rang gnas su sleb/ dus dran mchod pa sogs chos sde chen po'i lugs gnyis kyi 'phral sel nged rang dang
dgon khag so sor gcung ren po che pheb ste grwa rigs yon bdag so so'i 'dod kha skong bar mdzad// ! shing lug lor gong ma chos kyi spyan ldan gyi gdung la rang byon du byung
ba ring bsrel nang gzhug khrod la ma song

bar lag tu yod pa rnams khams sog gi stabs phyi 'khyar byung dogs bcas rten bzhengs shig byed rtsis bcas sprul pa'i bzo bo lta bu'i glang thang sprul sku nor bu rgyal mtshan
