bos te/ 'jim pa la rgya bod kyi gnas chen rnams kyi sa sna/ rdo sna/ mkhas grub du ma'i byin rten mang ba/ gtso bor gong ma nyid kyi gdung rus/ ring bsrel/ dbu lo/ na bza'/
gdung thal/ sman sna/ gser dngul sogs rin po che'i rigs rnams bsres shing / gdung rus la chos skyong rnams kyi sku mang tsam byon pa yod gshis dar 'dam las grub pa'i
lcam dral lha gsum/ bram gzugs/ rab brtan ma/ rnam sras rnams bzhengs bkod kyi las grwa btsugs shing / mgon chen la rgyug mtho lnga lhag tsam/ gzhan rnams khru re lhag tsam
bzhengs pa'i rus shing tsher ma can la/ gri lcags/ gri snying / gri sha /gri khrag sogs rdzas rnams 'dzom par byas te/ thun mong ma yin pa'i 'khor lo sgrub pa sogs phyag
bzhes ltar dang / gtso bo gur gyi mgon por gong ma nyid kyi sku tshigs bdun par dbu klad babs par gur mgon gyi sku 'bur dod du byon pa ring bsrel gyis gtams pa dang /
thugs dam las bzhengs dus byang sems shangs gnyis las babs pa kha btags la sbags pa/ tshems dang / dbu lo bub/ 'phags pa rin po che'i thugs dam rten gur mgon 'khor bcas
rdo nag las grub pa dang / yum chen la gong ma'i tshems la thub pa grong khyer ma ring bsrel gyi drwa bas spras pa/ dbu thod kyi dum bur 'bru gsum byon pa/ 'dod khams mar
gong ma'i dbu

thod kyi tshal par bde mchog gi snying po byon pa/ dpal mgon la gdung rus su dpal mgon bram gzugs dang / a 'bur dod du byon pa/ rab brtan mar gdung rus la rab brtan ma dang
/ hU~M 'bur dod du byon pa/ rnam sras la gdung rus las byon pa'i rnam sras dang / dzambha la rang byon/ thams cad la gong ma'i ring bsrel gsum re/ rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas
kyi ring bsrel/ chos 'phags kyi tshems kyi dum bu re/ o rgyan yab yum gyi byang sems dkar dmar dang / dbu skra/ zab ber/ skye bdun ril bu/ bai ro'i shog ser/ birWa pa'i
bdud rtsi'i ril bu/ nA ro'i sku rgyan gyi rus phreng nas rdog re/ jo bo'i shangs mtshal dang dbu zhwa'i dum bu/ gong ma lnga dang / bu ston yab sras/ ngor chen yab sras/
mkhyen rab rje khu dbon sogs rgya bod kyi mkhas grub du ma'i gdung rus/ dbu lo/ na bza'/ dam rdzas/ spur ras/ spur thal/ sku mtshal dang sku zhun gyi ril bu/ ring bsrel
rnam pa bzhi/ gnod sbyin 'khor lo dang bcas pa gzhug pa'i gzungs gzhug kyi phyag len dngos gtsang bar grub cing / phra rgyan du me shel/ chu shel/ mu tig /gser dngul sogs
kyi sku rgyan dang phyag mtshan bcas bzo bkod phun sum tshogs pa kun gyi mthong yul du gyur pa rnams/ las rgyun lo gcig gi ring du sprul pa'i bzo bos bsgrubs shing / yon
gos dar/ dngul/ ja/ rta sogs kyis mnyes par byas shing / nged rang nas mgon khang gi rab gnas nas bshad pa bzhin zhag gsum du bsgrubs shing mnga' gsol bkra shis

dang bcas pa bgyis te/ mthu ldan rgyal ba'i bstan srung nag po che/ /mthu can phyi nang dregs pa'i 'khor bcas kyi/ /mthu stobs gzi brjid bskyed pa'i phyi nang rten/ /mthu dang
ldan pa bstan dgra'i gshed dmar bskrun/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar byin rlabs kyi gzi 'od 'bar bar grub pa ni khyad du mtshar ba zhig go /dpal 'bar ma hA kA la gur zhal dang
/ /dpal ldan lha mo 'dod khams dbang phyug ma/ /dpal 'byor dbyar mtsho ltar spel rnam thos bu/ /dpal ldan srid gsum bdag mo'i sku rnams bzhengs/ /bstan srung rgya mtsho'i
gzugs sku 'jigs rung can/ /bstan dgra'i gshed mar mnga' gsol rab tu gnas/ /bstan 'dzin bu bzhin skyong bar bka' bsgos te/ /bstan srung kun gyi gtso bor bzhugs su gsol/
/e ma 'di 'dra'i sku brnyan ngo mtshar can/ /sngon med sgyu ma'i 'phrul gyi ltad mo 'di/ /srung mas mngon gsum phrin las bsgrubs pa las/ /phal gyi bzo bos sgrub nus ga la
yin/ /nged rang sgom khang du dbyar chos la yod thog 'dam nas sa skya rab 'byams pas mang ja dang / sman rtse'i 'gyed cig btang bar gtsang pa phyogs gcig gi gzims khang
gnyer pas rogs byas pas khams tshan la la'i grwa pa kha cig phyogs su song bar skal ba ma sprad cing / tshang ma ko long yod pa'i khar gzims khang gi phyugs shig gi rkang
pa gser pas bcag pas las tshan rnams bsdus/ gang 'gab gnyer bas dri ba byas 'dug par/ dgon pa'i phyi nang gi bdag rkyen dang gtong sgo rnams ma byung bas gzhung du bla
mar zhu zer mna' gam bzhag

'dug pa/ nged rang 'khor nas bco brgyad kyang phyogs mthun byed dgos zer bar/ nged mched kyis sa skya bdag po 'di phyi'i skyabs gnas su song bas de rigs byed pa ga la srid/
khyed rnams kyang zhu sbyor mi 'gal tshul nan kyis byas kyang / nged rang na phra ba bcas rtsi med kyis las tshan tshang ma gzhung sar snyan 'bul du byon song ba/ rtse gdong
nas phyag mdzod gnyis rdzong bda' gnang / zhu gtugs la yun ring tsam 'gor song bas sa spre'i dbyar smad lhor dpung 'jug gnang ba'i thugs brel gyi stabs thag ma chod
par 'gor skabs/ phyag mdzod gnyis kyis rab nA lendra 'jags pa dang / dgongs pas ma bzhes tshe dpal ldan rtse 'di bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gi bzhugs gnas khyad par can yin
pas bka' drin skyong dgos tshul nan gyis zhus nas phyir log /las tshan rnams kyang re zhig slog pa gnang 'dug /'di skor nA lendra pa rnams de bzhin byed 'dug par kha brda
ma song ba las/ rang ngos sa skya bdag po'i thugs la phog pa rmi lam du'ang mi byed bsams pa yod cing / gzhung sa'i mjal kha zhu ba sogs la 'gro dgos yod na'ang / lha sa
phyogs la rdog bsngogs mang na rtse gdong gi thugs la gzigs phyogs go log pa byung dogs kyis lhor dpung 'jug la pheb pa'i pheb rdzong phyag mjal zhu dgos kyang phyis skyon
du lus shing // ! me sprel lor pho brang nas chibs kha bsgyur grub 'dug cing pheb rjes la bsnyegs pas 'bras spungs la mjal kha zhus skabs rtse gdong dang nA lendra ba'i
skor la dri ba gnang byung bar/ 'dzin skyong dang gtong sgo sogs la nA lendra pa

rnams bden pa tsam yod kyang / nged rang sa skya pa rnams la bla ma sa skya bdag po las lhag pa gzhan ma zhus na kha tshig pa zhig lags shing / lhag tu khri chen kun dga' bsod
nams nas da bar 'dzin bdag gnang bas gsang sngags kyi chos dam tshig dang 'brel ba'i grwa slob gzhan dang mi 'dra ba nas/ rtse gdong rang du sngar lugs bzhin bka' drin
skyong dgos tshul zhus par/ de na lam 'bras sogs 'chad nyan thub pa med tshul zer ba ji ltar yin bslab ston gnang byung bar/ snga sor lam 'bras rdo rje phreng ba sogs sa
skya'i chos kyi 'byung khungs su song bas rim par stsal ba/ bar skabs rgyang tsam zhig gnang ma bde bar/ da cha zhabs drung dbon rin po ches lam 'bras sogs gnang chog ma
lags pas/ mtshal dang btsag gi dpe bzhin 'ong bas rtse gdong rang du gnang dgos tshul nan gyis zhus pas/ de na lho nas 'khor 'phral 'od gnang byung zhing / sku zhabs su
drung yig pad rdor dang / mgron gnyer drung pa 'dug pa'ang dgyes song / rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen gzigs chen por phyag dbang zhus par chos kyi dri ba zhib tu stsal/ mgron
khang du ston mo dang / yas phyin lhan gyi gnang sbyin gos yug /gnam ja ko khra sogs rgya cher bka' drin bskyangs/ po ta la dang jo shAka gi gnas mjal zhus skabs rdzong
dpon gyi gsol ja gnang / snyan shal dang mchod pa gang rgyas phul zhing phyir log /chos sde chen por khams sog dang don gnyer gyi chos zhu ba rnams la dbang lung khrid
sogs byas/ dus dran mchod pa

sogs lugs gnyis rim sel dang / dgon lag gi chos sogs gcung rin po ches gnang / ! me bya lor zla ba dang por grub rgyal lugs kyi tshe sgrub dang / gnyis par brag rdzong ma'i
bsnyen pa 'bum phrag bcu drug pa zhig byas/ bzhi par slob dpon chen po a bhA ya ka ra dang / dar paN A tsaryas bkral ba'i rdo rje phreng ba dkyil 'khor bzhi bcu zhe gnyis/
dge legs su bya ba'i dkyil 'khor gsum dang bcas pa phyag len shin tu rgyas pa zla ba gcig gi ring btsugs par/ mkhas btsun grub pa'i dbang phyug gcung rin po ches dbus
phyogs nas byon pa'i bla khag /mdo khams dang / sog yul bcas kyi 'bul sdud sogs tshogs pa bzhi brgya skor byung / phreng ba skor gsum gyi lung dang / rab byung bsnyen rdzogs
nyis brgya skor kyang bsgrubs/ dbyar smad rgyal rtse nas mchod yon pho brang chen por chibs kha bsgyur ba'i mjal khar/ nged rang bla khag las tshan bcas kyis phyin skabs/
nA lendra pa rnams la rtse gdong dang zlos gzhi'i skor dri ba gnang song zhing / nged rang la mgron gnyer drung pa brgyud gzims khang gi bdag po khyed rang tshos byas
na babs 'brel yin 'dra/ 'dod par ma babs pa ni mi byed bslab ston gnang byung bar/ sa skya bdag po'i phyag nas zhus na tshang ma'i mig ltos la gnod pa zhig 'ong 'dug bsam
dgongs pa nan gyis zhus pas khrol cha gnang / las tshan rnams la rtse gdong nas byung bstun 'dzin skyong sogs kyi bslab ston gnang bar sku tshab btang rgyu yin pheb/

zur chas rgyas pa/ nged la gos dar/ ja/ rta sogs kyi dgu tshan gnyis dang / dmangs mar gcig kyang stsal/ ma 'gyangs par phyag mdzod gnyis sku zhabs su bcar 'dug par gtong sgo
dang 'dzin skyong gi bslab ston dang / khyed dpon slob bco brgyad rang la dogs pa zhig 'dug kyang / bco brgyad pas rtse gdong nas gnang dgos tshul nan gyis zhu 'dug /de
rigs la dogs pa mdzad na nang khul du mi 'gab tshul bslab ston gnang 'dug kyang / phyag phyi rnams kyis rgyur bsten dgongs par mi gtad tsam gnang 'dug /sku tshab dang bcas
nA lendra rdzong bda' gnang / mang ja 'gyed bcas gnang song thog /gtong sgo dang 'dzin skyong sngar lugs la ma song bar dgos tshul gyi bslab ston dang bcas gang legs
las khrims 'degs 'gel cha tsam yang ma gnang bar bka' drin shin tu che bar stsal song / 'u du su 'bul sdud pa dang / khams 'grul ba rnams phyir log la rdzong bda' sogs lugs
gnyis 'phral sel rnams nged rang mched nas byas/ 'di skabs chos sde chen po'i srung mar chos rgyal dpon blon kun mkhyen chen pos srung mar bka' bsgo bar/ gsol mchod rgyun
du byed kyang khog zhugs chos gzhis 'drar bud med la byed pa las grags cher med kyang / bar skabs shig khog zhugs byed mi sgrub sde'i bla ma dbon por nged la len bskur
du/ 'jam dbyangs kyi sprul pa mkhyen rab dge bshes kyis nges dgos/ sa skyid po pa tshab gzhis khar khog pa 'tshol du 'gro zhing / de nas chos sde chen

por 'ong rgyu yin pas chas dang mtshon cha grabs kyis/ bdag rkyen byas na nam langs pa dang nyi ma shar ba lta bu 'ong zer ba byung zhing / phyi lo pa tshab shar ba'i bu a
gsum zer ba gzhung gi mi grwar 'tsho byed bslab gra'i khrod la yod 'dug par khog zhugs byas te 'tshub 'gyur che bar byung 'dug gshis phyir slog gnang skabs/ thang lha ba'i
bu mo sogs la las mkhan kyang babs/ pa tshab tu mkhan chen rdzong shar pa pheb par bkra shis kha btags dang / gri bkug pa bskur nas dgon gnas su bdag gyis zer bar/ dpal
sa skya pa chen po khams gsum chos kyi rgyal po kun dga' bsod nams par gsung brtag zhus par/ de kha'i chos skyong khog tu zhugs nges yin 'dug pas bdag byas na legs par 'dug
gnang ba bzhin/ kun mkhyen chen po'i dus dran mchod pa'i nyin dpon blon gnyis kar so so'i khog tu zhugs par nged rang nas dbu rmog dang / ru mtshon/ khrab gdan/ phyag
mdung / ral gri/ snyan shal sogs phul zhing / bla khag las tshan gra rigs bcas pas snyan dar zhal ja sogs phul thog rgyal khang gi phyi nang tshang mar 'tshub 'gyur shin
tu che ba bstan par/ nged rang nas bka' bsgo dang phrin bcol rgyas par zhus par gsan te khri'u shing gi khar bzhugs nas/ srung ma la bdag byas pa shin tu legs/ slob dpon
chen po padma 'byung gnas kyi bka' bzhin sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa spyi dang / bye brag chos sde 'di nam langs nyi ma shar ba lta bu byed gsung ba sogs lung bstan mang du
mdzad/ de nas bzung yar zla

ltar rgyas par gyur/ dgon lag so sor gcung rin po che pheb// ! sa khyi lor zla ba dang por khams gsum chos kyi rgyal po rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen pa chen po dang / sa dbang
chen po'i mjal kha zhu ba dang / bstan 'dzin chos kyi rgyal po'i bzhugs khrir rgyal sras bstan 'dzin da yan rgyal po rgyal srid du dbang bskur ba gnang ba'i khri 'bul
du/ nged rang las tshan bcas pas phyin te ra sa 'phrul snang gi sde chen por slebs/ rtse gdong nas 'jam mgon chos kyi rgyal po byams pa bsod nams chibs kha bsgyur 'dug pas/
phyag dbang du phyin/ thugs shin tu dgyes pa dang bcas pas nged rang dpon slob khri 'bul gyi mjal khar lhan du shog gnang bar/ bslab don ltar zhu ba gzhir bcas zhus/
gnas tshang du slebs nas khyed dpon slob kyis mgron gnyer sogs la snyan 'bul gnang mi dgos/ 'di nas zhus chog gsungs/ phyi nyin rdo ring gi rtsa ba la 'byor skabs rtsi bzhag
gnang mi sku tshab gnyis kyis de ring gtsang pa rnams las dbus pa min gshis bslab ston zhu dgos pheb pa rgyang tsam song skabs/ sku zhabs nas gzims zhu ba gnang nas/
khyed dpon slob sang byon chog gi bslab ston gnang byung bas gnas tshang du log /phyi nyin legs 'bul bzhugs gral du nged rang dang / byams gling mkhan po gnyis la tshang
ma'i mgor gdan bzos che shing ston mo sogs dpangs mtho ba bka' drin gzhan las che ba gnang / phyi nyin gsol tshigs grol 'phral gong sa chen po'i mjal kha'i thog /brtse ba
chen pos dbang dang rjes gnang gi phyag len skor gyi dri ba zhib tu stsal/

dgong mo sde srid sku zhabs kyi mjal kha zhus/ gar tsam sdod kyi dri ba gnang byung bar/ sa skya gong bzhugs pheb tshul thos pas zhag gnyis sdod rtsis lags zhus par/ zhag bcu
skor nas pheb rgyu yin pas de bar bsgugs na legs par 'ong pheb/ zur chas sogs bka' drin che bar gnang / phyogs 'dus grwa slob mang tsam la dbang rjes gnang gi rigs kyang
phul/ zhag shas nas gong ma pheb cing phyag mjal zhu bar nged mched lhan tu phyin par mjal kha dang shin tu dgyes pa'i bslab ston sogs stsal/ zhag shas 'di khar sdod gsung
bslab ston bka' drin bskyangs pa ltar bsdad/ nyin re bzhin tshe dbang brgya rtsa rim bzhin stsal zhing / gur lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang kyang gnang / nged mched la phyag
mdud/ dam rdzas brgya rdo/ stong rdo/ sil bu mang ba/ gnang sbyin dpangs mtho ba bcas gnang / dgon par mang ja/ dam rdzas kyi 'gyed/ spyi 'gyed bcas stsal/ 'chad nyan
sogs bstan pa la gang spyir bsam pa che ba byed dgos pa'i bslab ston sogs zhib par stsal/ bsam yas su rgyang tsam sdod rtsis yin pas chos gang dgos pa 'ong bas pha gir byon
gsung par/ dgon gnas su 'byor nas gcung rin po sku shin tu ltem par byung bas nged rang 'gro ma nus par/ a ma lags dang / mched mgon po rab brtan bcas bsam yas su gong
ma'i sku zhabs su pheb/ nged rang nas sku rim du tshogs chen gyi sgrol ma khri tshar/ tshe gzungs dang sher snying 'bum ther/ kun rig gi cho ga stong rtsa rnams bsgrubs
shing /

dge 'dun zhal grangs sum brgya skor la grwa pa rer yon bkras btags dang / sman kha re/ bcu rer bzang ja sig re/ spyi yon du tshogs gdan la drum yug nyi shu rtsa gnyis/ spom
thag /bla chas na bza' cha tshang / zhal dkar sogs 'dren chas cha tshang / chibs sga cha 'grigs rnams phul te mnyes par byas/ 'tsho byed bkras sbug pa sogs kyis 'phrod bsten
zhus/ nged rang nas tshe dbang brgya rtsa phul bas 'tsho byed kyis phyag rtsa'i sdod phyir gshegs 'dug pas/ da dung tshe dbang mdzad nas sku tsher phan par 'dug zer
ba bzhin brgya rtsa lnga phul bas/ 'tsho byed pas da cha tshe dbang gi byin rlabs kyis phyag rtsar bltas na lo brgyad tshun khag theg zer ba bzhin phyis thog tu khel/ rnam
'joms dang / sme brtsegs kyi khrus brgya rtsa re/ gur drag /mgon po dang / 'byung 'dul sogs rjes gnang gi rigs mang bar phul/ chos srung rnams la bskang ba brgya rtsa/
phyogs bzhi'i gtor ma/ sngags pas brgya bzhi sogs mdos rigs mang bar bsgrubs pas bsnyung gzhi yar ldan du song / rtse gdong zhabs drung khri chen chos sdings nas pheb par
thab bsu dang / chibs bsu bar nged dpon slob drug cu skor gyis zhus shing / ser phreng kyang rgyas par bsgrigs te gzims khang du pheb 'phral dpon gnyer gyis gzhis byes tshang
mar gzhi len du gsol ja zhig zhus/ phyi nyin bco brgyad du spyan drangs te gzhi len gang zab dang / gos dang / ja/ rta sogs kyi 'bul ba che bar phul zhing / de zhor
gcung rin po cher tshe dbang lcags sdong ma zhig stsal/ chos srung gi sku gsar bzhengs rnams la

rab gnas su gdan 'dren zhus/ dgyes mdzad rdo rje'i sgo nas phyag nas rgyas pa bka' drin bskyangs/ rten 'brel shin tu 'jigs par gyur/ phyi nyin spyi sos spyan drangs te gzhi
len rgyas pa dang / gos dar ja sogs kyi 'bul ba zhus/ thams cad mkhyen pa rong ston chen po'i khrir pheb ste tshogs su 'jam dbyangs dmar ser gyi rjes gnang stsal/ gzims
khang du tshe dpag lha dgu'i bka' dbang tshang mar gnang ba dang / mgon khang chen mor thugs gsos bskang ba sogs rgyas par gnang / bla khag dang khams tshan che ba rnams
kyi gdan 'dren zhu ba dang / chung ba rnams kyis ja zhus thog 'bul ba rgyas par zhus/ 'phen yul khul bla khag dang / dgon khag /yon bdag rnams kyis che 'byor chung 'byor
lta bu'i so so nas 'bul zhabs rgya che bar byung song zhing / byin rlabs chos 'brel yang bka' drin che ste gtsang du chibs kha bsgyur/ yar lam dpal ldan rtser pheb/ nged
rang la bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gi sku srung gnyen lo chen po'i thugs dam rten zhal bzhi yongs rdzogs kyi sku'i mjal kha dang byin rlabs stsal/ rgyal nang bar chibs skyel
zhus te/ bsti gnas su log /de nas gcung rin po che'i sku'i 'phrod bsten dang / chos sde chen po'i dus dran mchod pa sogs dang / dgon lag so so'i chos grwa rnams kyang byas//
! sa phag lor zla ba dang po'i nang du brag rdzong ma'i bsnyen pa 'bum phrag bcu drug pa zhig grub skabs/ grub dbang thams cad mkhyen pa chen po pho brang po ta lar
chibs kha bsgyur te sde srid de nyid zhing gzhan du pheb pa'i gsang

brtol bka' drin bskyangs bas gong zhabs su phyag 'bul zhu ba dang / sde srid de nyid kyi bsngo zhus 'bul bar phyin par mjal kha rgyas par bka' drin bskyangs/ mgron khang du
slebs nas sde srid zhing la pheb pa'i gnas tshul gyi bslab ston gnang zhing / bsngo zhus kyi rgyu mtshan zhus par de rigs bzhes rtsis min/ bslab ston gnang bar bzhes dgos
tshul nan gyis zhus par thugs 'dod ma byung tshe pha gir mang ja sogs gnang chog pheb/ ston mo gnang sbyin zur chas sogs bka' drin che ba brtse skyong gnang zhing phyir
log /dgon par 'byor 'phral mang ja mchod khang so sor mchod pa snyan shal bcas phul/ bla khag grwa mang rnams ser tshogs la rdzong bda' byas/ bkra shis sgang du drug brgya'i
sras mo khyim 'dzin du yod par dge ba'i ltas dang bcas sras 'khrungs par zhag kha cig nas phyin/ tshe dbang brgya rtsa dang / khrus/ 'dod khams gtso mo'i rjes gnang
sogs byas/ mtshan ngag dbang rgyal mtshan du gsol/ 'di lo khyung 'bum dang / nyag bre gnyis nas 'bul skyel dang / khams tshan so sor kyang 'grul pa tshan che bar slebs/ mkhar
kha nas kun dga' mgon po dang / 'u du su nas da rgan chos rje'i 'bul skyel sogs kyang 'byor/ gser dngul/ ja/ gos dar/ rta/ dre'u/ mdzo/ khal sogs kyi 'bul ba rgya che
bar phul/ snga sor thub bstan rnam par rgyal ba'i chos grwa mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen par chag med gso ba'i byin rlabs zhu bar phyin skabs/ nA lendrar ngor lta bur lam
'bras rgyun du gnang dgos pa zhig yod 'dug par/ bdud rtsi ril bu sgrub pa ma

gnang tshe dam tshig gi rdzas la thabs chag pa zhig 'ong bas/ ces kyang sgrub pa mdzod gsung byung bas sa ltar phyag dbang la phyin skabs/ a ru ra 'tshol du btang bas gser
mdog byis pa lo brgyad kyi khu tshur tsam las mi chung ba brgya phrag zung lhag tsam rnyed 'dug pas/ da dung 'di'i gras mang ba zhig 'tshol dgos tshul byas/ zhib tu btsal
kyang gser mdog dkyus ma las ma rnyed 'dug pas sgrub pa dus babs kyi rten 'brel yin 'dra bsam/ rang gnas su 'byor skabs sa skya nas rigs brgya'i khyab bdag sngags 'chang
bsod nams dbang phyug gis dam rdzas khri rdo bum gzugs che ba zhig dang / stong rdo gsum/ brgya rdo/ sil bu bcas phon che ba zhig bka' drin bskyangs byung bar sgrubs shig
pa'i brdar go nas/ 'gol khyad kyi gzhis su dam rdzas 'phral tu sgrub mkhos kyi byin khyad du 'phags pa du ma dang / dam tshig gi rdzas rnams sbags nas gza' tshes dge bar
sgrub pa tshugs shing / 'di sgrub pa'i skabs 'phel che zhing ril bu'i skabs rdzong gi bad kyi steng dang / rdzing gi chu 'gram rnams su ril bu 'thor ba rnams rnyed mi mang
ba zhig byung 'dug cing / nam mkha' nas 'ja' dang me tog gi char sogs byung ba bla ma dang yi dam gyis byin rlabs dngos su stsal bar 'dug snyam/ gzims khang 'og grwa
tshang gi snga sor nas bshad grwa yin 'dug kyang gtan chags kyi grwa rgyun nyung zhing / bshad grwa'i slob gnyer dmar ba rang mi 'dug pas bla ma grwa rigs tshang mar/ mang
ja kha shas/ ja 'gyed/ tshan grangs kyi

'bul ba dang rnam gzhag sogs phul thog /lo sum cu man gyi grwa rigs rnams kyis ming btags re ma byung bar mdo lugs kyi thugs gnyer la brtson pa las phyir log mi chog pa'i bca'
sgrig khur blangs kyis bzos kyang lo lnga drug tsam las phugs 'khyol ba rang ni byung ma song / gzims khang 'og grwa tshang gi chos gzhis grwabs stag rtse nas bzhes grabs
gnang skabs/ nged rang nas gsol dpon zhib zhus 'bul bar rdzong bda' byas shing / grwa tshang nas chos skyong chen po'i phyag mdung zhig khyer nas bla ma las tshan rnams
zhu bar brdzangs pas srung ma'i 'tshubs shig kyang byung 'dug pa dang / zhu rtsa'ang pheb pa bcas phyir slog gtan tshigs bcas bka' drin bskyangs song / 'grul pa nyams
la paNDi ta lha'i rgyal mtshan dang / cha dkar bla ma u pa shi /dge slong rnams kyi bskur ma che ba 'dug pa sprad/ nged rang nas lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i gdams pa/ dbang
/ khrid/ lung / byin rlabs dang bcas pa dang / 'jigs byed/ gshed dmar sogs 'dod chos mang bar byas/ dus dran mchod pa sogs lugs gnyis 'phral sel sngar rgyun ltar/ ! lcags
byi lor gu ru dkon mchog spyi 'dus zhi drag seng gdong ma dang bcas pa'i bsnyen pa mjug tu tshogs brgya bcas gang rgyas byas par gtor ma mi rnying pa dang / rmi lam
du ltas bzang ba byung / chos sde chen po'i bla khag las tshan dang bcas pa gros byas/ gdan sa chen po rtse gdong du 'jam dbyangs bsod nams bstan 'dzin dbang po gdan 'dren
la las tshan gnyis rdzong bda' byas par/ yab bdag chen

rin po che dang lhan du chibs kha bsgyur bar rgyal nang du thab bsu dang / nged dpon slob bzhi bcu skor gyis chibs bsu dang / dge 'dun sum brgya skor gyis rol mo'i bye brag
ci rigs/ gdugs dang / rgyal mtshan/ ba dan sogs mchod rdzas sna tshogs thogs te ser phreng gis bsu ba dang / bsang / dar 'phyar/ bkra shis khra rigs sogs gang rgyas bcas
spyan 'dren zhus/ gzims khang nas gzhi len dang / zhag gsum nas bco brgyad du gdan 'dren zhus/ gzhi len gang rgyas zhus shing / gcung sku ltem par tshe dbang dang / rta
mgrin gyi rjes gnang zhus/ bdag chen rin po cher chibs pa sogs dgu tshan dang / gdung brgyud rin po cher phyi nyin tshogs su thams cad mkhyen pa rong ston chen po'i bzhugs
khrir spyan 'dren zhus/ dgu tshan lnga tsam gyi khri 'bul byas/ rtse gdong nas kyang mang ja byin rten gyi 'gyed/ nged rang la tshogs dbur gnang sbyin rgya che ba stsal/
yab sras lhan du pho brang chen por mjal kha zhu bar pheb cing / gdung brgyud rin po che tshur pheb nas rgyang tsam bzhugs/ tshogs chen du gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras
bu dang bcas pa'i gdams pa sogs 'dod chos mang du bka' drin bskyangs ba zhus/ nged rang nas kyang phyogs 'dus bcas mang bar mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho/ bde mchog /gsang 'dus/
'jigs byed/ gshed dmar sogs kyi dbang kha shas dang / sgrub thabs rgya mtsho dang / rjes gnang zur bka'i rigs mang bar lung bcas ci rigs byas shing / gdung brgyud rin
po

che gtsang du pheb par chibs skyel pheb skyel rgyas par zhus shing / sgom khang sogs la phyogs 'gro sogs sngar rgyun ltar byas/ ! lcags glang gsar 'phral rje btsun rdo rje
rnal 'byor ma'i bsnyen pa bzhi 'bum dang / tshe sgrub kyang byas/ gsum pa'i nang du dbang khang 'chi med pho brang gi mdo sbugs rgyag pa'i las grwa tshugs par/ mched zla
mgon po rab brtan gyis nged kyi ngag bkod ltar khur bzhes gnang zhing / shing bzo ba sgung po che ba bcas gsum/ rdo bzo tshes bcu/ zhwa mkhan tshe ring don 'grub/ 'u lag
bzhi bcu skor gyis zla ba bzhi'i ring sgrub par/ bzo bo rnams la phog yon gang gzabs kyis mgu bar byas shing / 'u lag rnams kyang sdod ring ja thug rgyun gtong ngos/ bla
khag /khams tshan so sor ston mo/ /nged rang la legs 'bul/ bzo bo rnams la ster cha sogs yang dag byung zhing / grub nyin dga' ston du nged rang nas 'u lag mi rer ja nyag
lnga re dang / bkra shis kha btags re byin te dge ba rdzogs byang du bsngos/ a ma lags sku ltem pas dbyar chos 'khyug tsam byas nas/ sku rim du tshe chog dang / kun rig
stong rtsa/ chos skyong rnams la bskang ba brgya rtsa/ tshe gzungs/ sgrol ma/ sher snying sogs mang bar bsgrub shing / nged rang nas rjes gnang gi rigs mang ba'ang byas/
gong gsal sku rim pa rnams la yon dang zhabs tog smin rgyas zhus/ sgom khang sogs la phyogs 'gro/ mchod pa/ chos ra sogs sngar rgyun bzhin byas/ gong sa chen po'i sku zhabs
su mjal kha zhu bar phyin par

zhal mjal/ phyag dbang / gnang sbyin sogs rgya cher bar bka' drin bskyangs/ ! chu stag lor gcung rin po che dang / yum sras gnyis ka sku khams ltem par sku rim dang 'phrod
bsten gyi rigs la brtson par byas kyang / a ma lags thugs dam kyi stabs ltas legs pa dang bcas te zhing gzhan du gshegs pas sems ngal bar gyur/ gshegs rdzong la nged mched
kyis dgung zhag pa nyi shu skor gyis kun rig /mdo brgya 'don mi/ zhag gsum thog tshogs mang gis cho ga /nged rang nas byang bu smin rgyas/ gong sa chen por bsngo zhus dpangs
mtho ba/ sa skya rtse gdong gi dbus rgyal rtse zhabs drung / 'bri gung / stag lung gi zhabs drung khag sogs bla ma che khag rnams la byang zhus/ dbus gtsang gi sa lugs
dgon che khag rnams su mang ja/ bla ma rnams la bsngo rten/ rten gsum la mchod pa sogs rgya cher bsgrubs shing / cho ga dngos gzhir tshogs chen gyi thog dgon lag rnams
bsdus te zhag gsum gyi ring kun rig gi sgrub mchod la zhabs tog dang yon shin tu rgyas zhing dngos gtsang bar phul/ bdun tshigs rnams su dga' ldan chos 'khor lha khang
gnyis kyi gtsos 'phen yul khul stod smad kyi dgon pa rnams dang / sgom khang / sa sbug /ri sdings bcas nged rang gi dgon lag sogs rim gyis bos te bsnyen bkur phun sum tshogs
par zhus/ dgung zhag gi ring nyin re bzhin nged rang gi cho ga /lho sgo/ byang bur bdun tshigs rer dbang bskur/ byang bu smin rgyas byas shing / zhe dgu thon nyin cho
ga pa mang ba dang / rgyun bzhugs rnams la yon shin tu rgyas par phul/

zla re bzhin dus dran mchod pa mang ba dang / byang bu mchod 'bul sogs gang rgyas zhus/ lo mchod la tshogs chen gyi cho ga dang / byang bu sogs dge ba'i rtsa ba ji snyid lo
gcig gi bar du bsgrubs pa rnams yum de nyid kyis gtsos sems can thams cad kyi don du dmigs pas dge ba rdzogs byang du bsngos/ sa skyong phrin las rgya mtsho'i khri 'bul
du phyin par mjal kha legs 'bul grwa 'grigs pa byung zhing / de skabs gong sa chen po nas lam zab kyi yig cha mtho ris dbang gi chu rgyun ljags rtsom gnang ba'i ljags lung
bka' drin bskyangs shing / cung zhig khams ma bde ba yod tshul zhus pas sku mdun du shog gsung bka' bsgo rgyas par stsal/ bla ma sangs rgyas dngos yin snyam pa'i snying
nas dad pa thob/ spang blang gi bslab ston dang / yas phyin gyi gnang cha/ ston mo sogs gzhan dang mi 'dra bar bka' drin bskyangs shing / dgon gnas su log /'grul pa khag
dang grwa rigs so sor 'dod chos mang ba dang / sngar rgyun gyi brel ba rnams bsgrubs/ 'u du su nas da rgan chos rjes rogs shig gtong dgos tshul byung ba bzhin gzhung sa
chen por snyan 'bul zhus par/ gzhan ma sog yul du 'gro sa med pa de bzhin yin kyang / chos rje rang gzhan dang ma 'dra zhing bco brgyad rang gi 'bul sdud pa sngar srol bzhin
byas chog gi bslab ston dang bka' shog shin tu btsan pa bka' drin bskyangs byung ba nas/ bla ma kun dga' rin chen dang / bsod nams bstan 'dzin gnyis rdzong bda' byas
par rta khal cha lag sogs sgrig bkod mched zlas byas te mi sna dang lhan du rdzong bda' byas/ zla ba bcu gnyis par lam 'bras bu dang

bcas pa'i gdams pa btsugs/ ! chu yos zla ba dang por cho 'phrul ring tshe sgrub dang / bsnyen pa kha gso byas te/ grol mtshams sngags lam tshugs/ gsum pa'i zla stod kyi bar
dbang lung khrid sogs rgyas par byas/ dbang khang 'chi med pho brang dang / mtshams kyi shing rtsi/ mchod sgam dmar po cha drug /ljang gu cha drug bcas gsar bzo byas par
brag dbar mkhar ba sogs shing bzo ba lnga dang / sprul sku ba bcas la so sor yon gyis tshim par byas/ khams sog gi 'grul pas gtsos grwa rigs mang bar chos 'brel ci rigs
dang / lugs gnyis kyi bdag rkyen byas/ pho brang chen po ri bo gru 'dzin du gong sa chen po yas phyin gyi mjal kha zhu bar phyin par/ mjal kha ma 'gyangs par stsal zhing
chos kyi bka' 'dri mang tsam gnang bar bka' len gang rgyas phul/ zur chas bdag rkyen thon phyag zhu nyin gnang cha sogs gzhan dang mi 'dra bar bka' drin bskyangs te phyir
log /chos sde chen po/ dgon lag sogs kyi dus mchod/ gtor ma brje ba/ chos bka' ci rigs sngar rgyun ltar byas/ ! shing 'brug lor mgon po bka' sdod ltar bsgrub pa'i bsnyen
pa dang / tshe sgrub byas shing / grub pa'i dbang phyug gcung rin po che sku ltem du song bar sku rim dang 'phrod bsten zhu ba sogs le shor med pa'i brel g.yeng mur/ pho
brang chen por bcar te mjal kha dang gsung brtag zhus par 'phral gnang dang / bdag rkyen gzhan dang mi 'dra ba bka' drin bskyangs shing / dgon gnas su 'byor 'phral gcung
sku zhabs su shog gsung ba ltar phyin par sku shin tu ltem par 'dug cing gnas tshul dri ba'i

mjug gang ci'i zhal ta hrug tsam mdzad/ phyag na rdo rje'i rim gnyis kyi rnam 'byor g.yel ba med pa zhig gnang gin yod gshis/ yid dam gyi lhas zhal gzigs te zhing khams gzhan
du gshegs pa'i lung bstan dang / dpal ldan lha mor kyang nged kyi rjes 'jug rnams la phrin las sgrub dgos tshul gyi bka' bsgo mdzad/ phyag g.yas sdigs mdzub dang / g.yon
mnyam gzhag mdzad/ spyan bar snang la gzigs te log 'dren zil gnon gyi ngang nas gzugs sku rdo rje 'dzin pa'i thugs kar thim/ zhag lnga tsam gyi bar sku drang por sngar
bzhin dang bcas thugs dam du bzhugs pa nyi phyed yol nas shangs nas byang chub kyi sems babs te ting nge 'dzin las grol/ sku gdung rin po cher chas bzhug phul te/ me tog
/spos/ mar me/ zhas zas sogs brgya phrag dang / 'phan/ rgyal mtshan sogs mchod pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa phul/ zhag bco lnga tsam gyi gsang khog tu sku rim gyi tshul gyis
nged sku mched kyis dgongs rdzogs gang 'grub dang / gong sa chen por skyabs 'jug gi ljags bsngo rten 'bul mi btang / gsang grol nas tshogs chen du grwa pa sum brgya tsam
bla khag bcas spyan drangs te kun rig gi cho ga nyin gang mar zhabs tog 'bul ba gang gzabs zhus/ dgung zhag pa nyi shus kun rig /mdo brgya pa gnyis/ zhag bdun gyi ring nged
dpon slob bco lnga skor gyis dpal kye rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga dang bla ma mchod pa phul/ bdun phrag rer dga' ldan chos 'khor dang lha khang sogs 'phen yul gyi
dgon che phra rnams spyan drangs te bsnyen bkur 'bul ba rgya che bar bsgrubs/

sku gdung rin po cher 'bul dpon bla ma bsod nams dpon slob kyis kun rig la brten pa'i sreg mchod phul bar/ nam mkha' las 'ja' sprin dang me tog gi char sogs sum rtsen pa rnams
kyis mchod pa rgya che bar phul zhing ngo mtshar ba'i ltas mang bar byung / zhag shas nas nged rang pho brang chen po ri bo gru 'dzin du gong sa yas phyin gyi mjal kha
dang mchod 'bul zhu bar phyin zhing / mchod 'bul rten du sku gsung thugs rten/ gser gyi maNDal/ rol mo/ mkhar rnga/ ja/ gos dar/ rta khrab sogs phul/ sa lam gyi bar chad
zhi thabs ljags bsngo bka' drin bskyangs/ thon phyag zhu nyin rdo rje phreng ba dang / mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho/ lo nag dril gsum sogs deng sang yig cha gang gi steng nas
byed dang / phyag len gyi skor/ bla ma brgyud pa sogs kyi bka' 'dri gnang bar so so'i zhu len phul bas shin tu dges pa dang gnang sbyin bcas stsal te/ 'dam bu byin gyi chos
grwa 'byor/ mchod 'bul gyi cho gar tshogs chen bla khag /lha khang rgyal smad/ sgom khang / sa sbug /ri sding sa sogs dgon lag rnams bos te nyin gsum gyi ring kun rig
bcas sgrub mchod la zhabs tog 'bul ba rgya chen pos so sor mnyes par byas shing / sa skya rtse gdong / 'bri stag khag sogs che kha rnams su mchod 'bul rten 'bul ba dang /
sa lugs kyi dgon pa rnams su mang ja'i thog bla ma so sor mchod 'bul rten 'bul bar rdzong bda' byas/ dgung zhag grol nyin bla khag dang tshogs chen gyis kun rig gi cho ga
gnang bar bsnyen bkur rgya che ba dang / dgung zhag pa rnams la ja/ dar ras sogs dpangs mtho

bas mnyes par byas shing / 'di skabs rmi lam du gong ma mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po bzhugs khri'i steng na na bza' gzabs sprod kyis bzhugs nas dgyes pa'i bslab ston gnang
ba zhig byung bas/ de nas bzung sdug bsngal gyis blo ma bde bas kar re bsdad pa de med par gyur/ 'bul skyel dang 'grul pa mang bar so so'i 'dod chos ci rigs dang / 'phral
sel rnams bsgrubs/ dgongs rdzogs kyi rten bzhengs su e nas lha bzo ba lnga/ gong dkar ba gcig bcas drug gis lam 'bras bla brgyud gtso bor rdo rje 'chang / dkyil 'khor
rgya mtsho'i dbang phyug rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin dpal bzang po'i sku brnyan thog tshad tsam dang / rdo rje 'chang nas gcung rin po che de nyid kyi bar sku
brnyan bzhi bcu zhe lnga lo bcu gnyis pa'i tshad/ rgya bod kyi sa sna/ rdo sna/ chu sna/ shing sna/ me tog /bye ma bcas khyad du 'phags pa rnams nas bsdus pa dang / byin
rten phon che ba/ gser dngul sogs rin po che'i rigs dang bses te dar 'dam las bzhengs par byon shin tu gtsang zhing / khyad par rje dbon gong ma'i sku de nyid ltar gzi brjid
dang ldan pa rang byon lta bur gyur cing / sku rnams la gser btul ma zho nyis brgya dang drug cu lhag tsam ljib gsol du byas pa'i nang gzhug tu gong ma chos kyi rgyal
po'i ring bsrel gsum re/ rgya bod kyi mkhas grub rnams kyi dbu lo/ /zhabs sen/ na bza'/ gdung rus/ spur zhun/ spur thal/ sku mtshal/ dam rdzas/ sman sgrub/ skye bdun ril
nag /'ja' tshugs ril bu sogs byin rten shin tu mang ba dang / gcung rin po che nyid kyi gdung tshA sku rer brgya phrag re/ zhwa lu lo tsA bas

zhus dag mdzad pa'i gzungs bla ma brgyud pa dang / rgyud sde bzhi'i lha tshogs rnams kyi gzungs sngags srog shing dang / sku gsung thugs skye mched rnams kyi byin rlabs dang
bcas pa cha tshang re sa skya nas ched gtad kyis zhus te phul/ lha mthong lo tsA bas zhus dag mdzad pa'i gzungs yongs rdzogs tshar re dang / 'di kha'i gzungs spar sogs
phon che ba/ ring bsrel rnam pa bzhi/ dbu gzungs/ zhabs gzungs/ bar gzungs/ pad gzungs kyi bar ma 'khrugs par phul zhing / gnod sbyin 'khor lo ngor chen rdo rje 'chang yab
sras kyi phyag len ltar bsgrubs pas bang mdzod du rin po che'i rigs mang ba/ 'bru sna/ dar sna/ sman sna sogs rdzas rnams ma tshang ba med cing zhabs bsdebs te byin rlabs
kyi phung po ltar grub 'phral/ res gza' lha'i bla ma dang / rgyu skar rgyal 'dzom par 'chi med grub pa'i 'grub sbyor bzang po'i tshes brgyad kyi nyin dgyes mdzad rdo rje'i
sgo nas nged rang dpon slob nyi shu skor gyis sta gon dang bcas zhag lnga'i ring rab gnas rgyas pa dang / mched zla mgon po rab brtan la yon bdag bsgo ba bcas shis brjod
kyi me tog gtor te mchod yul rnams zag med kyi thugs dgongs rdzogs pa'i phyir zab pa chos kyi dbyings dang / rgya che ba sems can gyi don du bsngo smon gyi rgyas 'debs
smin rgyas byas/ lha bzo rnams la gser dngul/ dkar yol/ dar ras/ ja/ rta/ rgyu phon che ba bcas rdzong bda' byas/ phyogs 'dus dang / 'di kha'i 'bul dpon bla ma khag rnams
kyis bskul ba'i ngor tshogs chen du dbang rdo rje phreng ba dang / phreng ba skor gsum gyi lung / dbang / rjes gnang / lung / byin rlabs sogs

so so'i thugs 'dod ltar byas/ sgom khang du thugs rje chen po'i dmar khrid dang / sa sbug tu spyod khrid sogs la zhag shas re byas/ rgyun gyi dbang por rab byung bsnyen rdzogs
mang ba/ dus dran mchod pa sogs sngar rgyun ltar bsgrubs/ ! shing sbrul lor gong sa chen po nas gong dkar ba mkhas pa'i dbang po dge slong phrin las bka' tham bslab ston
bcas rdzong bda' bka' drin bskyangs nas/ chos sder rgyun dkon gshis sgrub thabs rgya mtsho dang / brgya rtsa/ rgya gzhung so so/ /bod gzhung gnyis kyi lung dang bcas
pa/ gdugs dkar/ rnam 'joms dkar po bir lugs/ thig le bcu drug gi byin rlabs sogs bslab ston dang thugs bzhed kha shas 'dug pa rnams bka' dang bstun nas zhus/ gzhis nas tsha
mo che ba btsun ma byed gsung bar ming mkhyen rab bsod nams bzang mor btags te rin sdings su bzhag /nged rang chung ngu'i skabs gong ma khu dbon gyi zhal 'phros la ka
drug thad 'dir dge 'dun gyi tshogs khang sbug tu dus gsum sangs rgyas kyi sku bzhugs pa zhig byung na zhes gsung 'dug pa sems su gcags pa dang / gong sa chen po yas phyin
mjal khar phyin skabs chos gzhis rnams la phyi khral gyi dgongs pa zhu rtsis byas/ zhu rten du sa skya gong ma gsum gyi na bza' dang / bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i sku
chos gang rigs gcig bzhes nas chos gzhis rnams la phyi khral gyi chag cha bka' drin dgos tshul zhus par/ bco brgyad gal che ba gzhan dang mi 'dra tshul bcas bka' shog rin
po ches bka' drin bskyangs ba gnang byung ba'i byin rten rnams spyan 'bebs zhus par 'di rigs

gzhung du mang tsam 'dug cing / de khar mkho che zhing 'gangs che ba yin 'dug pas phyi 'khyar med par mdzod ces bslab ston gnang bar rten/ tshogs khang ka ba bcu drug /ka phung
ka ba gnyis bcas bco brgyad kyis gsar du bzhengs rtsis byas par gang ci'i bkod pa grwa sgrig mched zla mgon po rab brtan gyis mdzad cing / 'di lo'i ar spo nas bzung
rten bzhengs/ rtsi tshon/ rab gnas kyi bar du nged rang gis bkod pa ltar dngos gtsang khyad mtshar phul du phyin pa ni mched zla ge sar la 'gran bzod pa mgon po rab brtan
gyi phyag phyi mdzod pa lhun grub dang / gnyer pa lha mo nor rgyas gnyis kyis zhus te grub pa bkod bde khyad lo khongs 'di nyid du tshang ma bris pa zhig yin no/ /rdo bzo
ba spang lkog tshes bcu dang / bsam dar bcas lnga/ 'u lag nged rang gi chos gzhis tshang ma'i thog las g.yor du drug brgya/ grog mkhar/ dpal gnas sogs nas 'u lag mang ba
'go mi bcas rogs su btang bar mdzad/ shing bzo ba sgung po che bas gtsos lnga bcas las grwa btsugs/ shing ka gdung phal cher che ba khams tshan so so nas ster bar mdzad
cing / phyi'i bzo hang lam zla ba lnga'i khongs su bsam pa bzhin gegs med du 'grub cing / bzo bo rnams la phog bzang ba dang / tshang mar 'dzugs ston/ sgang ston/ grol ston
rgyas pa dang / bla khag /khams tshan/ nye ba khag /yon bdag rnams kyis nged rang la legs byas dang / so sor ston mo dang / tshan grangs kyi ster sbyin mdzad song / bzo
bo rnams la yon gos dar/ ja khrab/ khro/

rta phyugs sogs kyis mgu bar byas/ 'u lag rnams la phog dang ja chang rgyun gtong / grol nyin btsug lag khang bzhengs sar song ba'i lhag bsam gyis mi rer 'bri g.yag gang rigs
bzang ba re gla lta bur ster chas byas/ gong sa chen po yas phyin du mjal khar phyin skabs zha lu mkhan rin po cher tshar lugs kyi chos ma thob pa rnams zhus na legs po
'ong tshul bslab ston bka' drin bskyangs shing / mjal kha bdag rkyen sogs lugs gnyis kyi sgo nas bka' drin shin tu bskyangs ba gnang / gnas kyi dbang por tshogs pa rnams
la chos ra/ rab byung bsnyen rdzogs/ sgom khang / sa sbug sogs la 'gro ba dang / chos ra mchod pa sogs sngar 'khyud ltar byas/ ! me rta lor zhwa mkhan tshe ring don grub
bos/ chos gzhis rnams kyi 'u lag thog dgon lag /sgom khang / rin sdings/ sa sbug sogs kyi btsun ma brgya skor gyi tshogs khang steng shod gshag skor bcas kyi zha la byas
par dngos gtsang ba zla ba gnyis tsam gyis khongs su grub par/ so sor ster cha dang / sdod ring ja chang ston mo sogs gzabs par byas shing / ma 'gyangs par rten bzhengs
kyi las grwa btsugs par sprul pa'i lha bzo ba glang thang sprul sku nor bu rgyal mtshan dpon g.yog gnyis pos te/ sku rgyu dar 'dam las grub pa'i tshogs khang sbug tu dus
gsum sangs rgyas dang / gnas brtan chen po bcu drug gi sku bzhengs pas/ rten gyi gtso bo bdag cag gi ston pa shAkya'i rgyal po/ g.yas su sangs rgyas mar me mdzad/ g.yon
du rgyal ba byams pa gsum gyi sku brnyan khri rgyab yol bcas par thog tshad/

'phags pa'i gnas brtan bcu drug /dharmA ta la/ rgyal po ha shang rnams dang bcas pa'i sku mi tshad tsam gnas g.yog dang bcas pa/ brag ri/ hor brag /ljon shing / chu 'babs/
thod du sprin spungs/ g.yas g.yon du rten gyi bzhugs khang sogs bkod pa ngo mtshar ba sprul ba'i bzo bos khyad mtshar du sgrub pa'i sku rgyur 'phags yul rdo rje gdan/ bya
rgod phung po'i ri sogs rgya gar shar nub/ bal yul/ ri bo rtse lnga/ glang chen 'gying ri/ lho phyogs po ta la sogs rgya dkar nag dang / bod yul gyi gnas chen dang / sgrub
gnas khyad par can rnams kyi sa chu/ rdo shing / me tog /bye ma rnams kyi sne bsdus dang / sman sna/ lha klu mi gsum gyi rin po che'i rigs du ma/ ston pa rdzogs pa'i sangs
rgyas nas bzung rgya bod kyi mkhas grub rim byon mang po bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i byin rten gyi rigs ma tshang ba med pa bsres pa'i dar 'dam las bzos shing / bar mtshams
rnams su sngon byon mkhas grub rnams kyi gdung tshwa sbyar te byin rlabs kyis phyur bur gyur pa rnams su nang gzhug gtso bo shAkya'i rgyal por thams cad mkhyen pa rong
ston chen po'i phyag mtheb g.yas pa 'phel ba sku sha dkar dung du gyur pa ring bsrel gyis spras pa/ rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi 'phel gdung / khro phu thog thub ma/ mkhyen
rab rje'i thugs/ paNDi ta shAkya shrI'i gsol lhung / rdo rje 'chang bla chen sa skya pa chen po'i sku 'byar/ mkhyen rab chos kyi rgyal po'i sku chos/ gong ma chos kyi
spyan ldan gyi ring bsrel bdun dang / tshems rings bsrel ma/ dbu lo bubs/ sku chos/ rje dbon rin po che'i sku sham/ phyag phreng /

mar me mdzad la rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi 'phel gdung / chos 'phags kyi tshems kyi dum bu/ thams cad mkhyen pa sa skya paNDi ta'i snam sbyar/ bu ston rin po che'i snam sbyar
glegs bu gcig ma/ mkhyen rab rje'i gdung tshwa ring bsrel ma/ jo bo smr-i ti'i sgom dbyug /mkhyen rab rje'i sku gzan/ gong ma chos kyi spyan ldan gyi tshems ring bsrel
gyis spras pa dang / sku rus las a byon pa/ rje dbon rin po che'i tshems dang / sku 'gag /smr-i ti'i phyag tshA/ rgyal ba byams pa rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi 'phel gdung
/ jo bo'i zhabs 'chags/ 'phags pa rin po che'i snam sbyar rdo rje'i zab lam ma/ ngor chen gyi zhun thigs ring bsrel/ smr-i ti'i phyag tshA/ 'jam dbyangs chos rje'i sku
chos sngon mo chu gcod ma yongs grags/ gong ma chos kyi spyan ldan gyi ring bsrel/ tshems/ sku gzan/ rje dbon rin po che'i dbu lo bubs dang / sku ber/ rten gtso gsum dang
/ 'phags pa'i gnas brtan bcu drug /dharma ta la/ rgyal po ha shang dang bcas tshang mar byang chub sems dpa' skye ba bdun pa'i sku sha /sku mtshal/ gong ma rin po che'i
ring bsrel re/ rgya bod kyi mkhas grub du ma'i dbu lo/ /na bza'/ gdung rus/ shangs mtshal/ dam rdzas kyi rigs mang ba/ gtsug tor nas pad gzungs kyi bar gyi gzungs lo chen

ba/ gtso bo dus gsum sangs rgyas la so sor mdo sde bskal bzang re dang / brgyad stong gnyis gser pod re/

dpon g.yog gnyis dang / jog po dpon bsam gyis gtsos ri mo ba bcu gsum bos te zla ba lnga'i ring 'bur sku rnams la gser btul ma zho bdun cu don gsum/ gser shog stong bam

sta/ tho ba/ bod gri legs pa sogs mang ba dang / snyan dar sna tshogs bsgrigs te mthong bas yid 'gul ba/ chos sbyin khor yug spel ba'i khrir rdo rje re khAs brgyan pa'i gdan
mnyes 'bol/ lcog rtse dang bcas pa zung / 'dus pa'i tshogs gdan dang / gyang logs su dkar chag dang bcas bsgrubs/ dbu mdzad gnyis kyis gtsos lha bzo ba bco lngar gser
dngul/ gos dar/ snam ras/ ja/ nged rang gi zhon rta legs pa sogs rta drel/ mdzo phyugs sogs nyin rer kha ru'i khal re'i rtsis/ dbu mdzad gnyis la 'phar dang bcas pa phul

re dang / re rer bkras btags re phul/ mchod yul rnams kyi dgongs pa rdzogs pa dang / ltos bcas kyi gtsos sems can thams cad kyi don du mchod

pa dang / stag rtse'i bla sman sogs bos

nas sman dpyad/ rim gror chos sgrogs mang ba dang / cho ga stong rtsa/ chos skyong rnams la bskang ba brgya rtsa/ sngags pas mdos rigs sogs mang ba zhig mched zlas bsgrubs
