nas zhabs drung rin po che rtse gdong la yum gshegs pa'i stabs gtsang du chibs kha bsgyur/ nged rang las tshan dang bcas pas chibs skyel zhus/ nA lendrar 'byor nas tshogs
chen la lam 'bras kyi khrid/ lung / dbang / byin rlabs rgyas pa dang / khams su 'byon mi rnams la rab byung bsnyen rdzogs/ 'dod sbyar gyi chos dang bdag rkyen bcas brdzangs/
sa skyong de nyid zhing gzhan du gshegs pas dgongs rdzogs su gos dar/ dngul sga sogs dpangs mtho tsam stsal 'phral pho brang du mjal khar phyin skabs sde pa mchod
dpon sku zhabs su/ snga sor rtse gdong nas bdag tshor gnang ba'i rna mo dgon bar skabs su gzhung sa nas rwa sgreng dgon gong mar sku tshe'i ring bzhugs gnas su gnang / bdag
tshor tshab cig bka' drin bskyang rtsis la khong grongs pas slar zhus nas ji ltar lags kyi bslab ston

zhus par/ zhag shas nas zhu mi do chod cig btang bas 'ong 'dug gnang ba'i bslab ston bzhin mdzod pa lhun grub dang / mgron gnyer rin chen gnyis brdzang bda' zhus pas zhag nyi
shu skor nas dgon mchod gzhis 'ong 'babs stong phrag gcig dang bcas rtsis sprod pa ko 'ja' dang bcas pa bka' drin bskyangs/ nged rang mjal khar phyin te me shel shin tu
che ba zhig gis gtsos 'bul dpangs che tsam phul/ bka' shog gtan tshigs kyang brtse bas bskyangs/ bsti gnas su 'byor nas kun rig sgrub mchod/ bka' 'gyur sogs chos sgrog
/chos skyong so so'i bskang ba/ gtor chen brdzong ba/ gtor gzhi spo ba/ dus mchod kyi rim pa lo mjug gi rim gro rnams bsgrubs/ ! sa bya lor tshogs chen du dbang rdo rje phreng
ba/ grub chen brgyad cu/ bka' gdams lha bzhi/ sgrol ma nyer gcig gi rjes gnang dang / bka' gdams glegs bam/ rgyal sras bka' 'bum sogs dbang lung mang ba zhig byas/
sgom khang du dmar khrid dang tshe khrid kyi ring zhig gsos kyang byas/ gzims khang 'og tu tshogs khang grul btub cig med gshis tsha ba bla ma bkra shis skyabs la 'phros
byas par/ de kha byas chog gsung byung ba bzhin a mdo'i phyogs su 'byon par thag bcad de/ chos rje sogs bla khag yon bdag dang bcas par 'di kha'i yi ge bcas rogs dang dgos
chas gzims khang 'og rang nas bsgrigs te byon par/ chos rjes bdag rkyen gzhan dang mi 'dra ba bcas shin tu legs pa byung 'dug pa lo shas nas 'khor/ zhig gsos byed pa'i
bkod pa byas don bzhin 'bul dpon

rang dang / gzhan ma las byed kha shas bcas kyis khur blangs te/ mi lag drug cu skor la ja thug rgyun gtong dang / slar ja rang sprad de zla shas rogs legs par bsgrubs shing
/ grub bstun ri mo ba'i dbu mdzad bsam 'grub sgang pa bcas bcu skor la phog shin tu bzang ba bsgrubs te ldebs bris su dbus su kun mkhyen rong ston pa/ bkra shis rnam rgyal/
birWa pa/ sangs rgyas 'phel/ 'jam dbyangs chos rje/ sa skya pa chen po sogs gong ma lnga/ rgyan drug /mchog gnyis/ khri chen kun dga' bsod nams/ rtse gdong gi zhal ngo
rnams dang / mkhyen rab rje sogs nged rang gi zhal ngo / /shAkya'i rgyal po sogs sangs rgyas/ 'jam dbyangs sogs byang sems/ slob dpon chen po/ /lo ma gyon ma sogs yi dam
dang / gur zhal sogs chos skyong / dzaM lha sogs nor lha/ a li chos rje sogs yon bdag dang bcas dngos shin tu gtsang bar bsgrubs/ grub bstun nged rang dang 'dus tshogs
bcas pas rab gnas shig tu rgyas par byas nyin sprul pa'i chos skyong chen po che chung kyang khog tu zhugs nas thugs dgyes pa'i rnam 'gyur shin tu mang bar bstan/ ri mo
ba rnams la yon sogs kyang nged rang gi ngag bkod ltar bsgrubs te dga' ston rgyas par byas song / lo 'di nang gong sa chen pos khral med kyi bka' shog bka' drin bskyangs
pa za ngam rdzong bzhugs kyi sems la ma ran pas zhol du zhal ngo rgyal por zhu logs phul bar brten bka' shog rin po che spyan 'bebs zhus skabs khyed tshor 'di rigs babs 'brel
mi 'dug gsung yar bzhes pas/ gong sa chen po'i sku zhabs su snyan

'bul zhu khyad lha sar phyin/ mchod dpon chen mo 'bras spungs su pheb gshis rigs grwa'i mjal kha dang bstun dga' ldan pho brang du phyin par bsu bar pheb/ mgron khang du skyil
tsam gyis slob dpon gnang ba bzhin bsdad skabs pheb nas dri ba zhig tu gnang / snyan 'bul tshang ma zhib zhus dang / gong du snyan lhon gnang dgos tshul zhus pas/ khyed
rang dpon slob gu gu dang gnas gzigs grub nas pho brang du bcar nas dbu mdzad chen mor rim gyis zhus na legs par 'dug gsung spu ja sbags shig bcas gnang sbyin stsal/ bslab
ston pheb pa bzhin byas/ dbu mdzad lags brgyud zhu don gyi snyan lhon zhib par zhus skabs mchod dpon chen mo'ang 'bras spungs nas pheb/ gong sa chen po nas khyed rang
dpon slob tshor 'di kha bstan pa'ang bslab ston pheb nas/ mchod gzhis them bzhi bcu skor la rkang bco lnga bsgrubs pas 'thus pa'i gtan tshigs shin tu btsan pa zhig bka'
drin bskyangs pa ni thog ma nas gus zhen che ba zhig yin pa dang / phran bu rang yang gsang sngags kyi 'chad nyan gyis zhabs phyir 'gyur bas su dgongs pa'i brtse gzigs bka'
drin bskyangs pas/ nged rang chos gzhis phran bu rnams dang bcas pa ngan 'gro las thar pa lta bu'i thugs rje shin tu che bar gyur/ rgyun gyi dbang po'i chos grwar 'byor
nas khams sog gi 'bul skyel ba phyir log mi rdzong bda' dang / rab byung bsnyen rdzogs kha shas bsgrubs/ skyed tshal mkhan shes rab rin chen rdzong shar nas gzhan don
la gshegs skabs ngos kyis thugs dam gsal 'debs su phyin/ sku chas rnams chud mi zos par rgyun gyi dbang po dang skyed tshal

gnyis su mchod 'bul du 'gro ba'i bkod pa byas/ rje btsun rdo rings pa'i thugs dam rten rdo nag gi gur mgon gyi sku sogs nye gnas kyis byin byung / lo 'dir sa dbang gser gyi
'khor los sgyur ba blo bzang mthu stobs mi 'jigs seng ge'i khrir khams gsum chos kyi rgyal po rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen gzigs chen po nas rgyal srid du dbang bskur ba
gnang ba'i legs 'bul du nged rang bla khag las tshan dang bcas pas yas phyin tho bkod bka' drin bskyangs pa bzhin rten mchod/ gser dngul/ gos dar/ khrab ja/ khro rta sogs
'bul dpangs mtho ba dang bcas pho brang chen por bcar nas legs 'bul gyi mjal kha'i skabs nged rang nas sger mjal rgyas par zhus/ brtse ba chen pos ma dor ba'i gdan bzos
dang bdag rkyen gzhan dang mi 'dra ba bka' drin bskyangs/ rnam par rgyal ba'i chos grar 'byor nas kun rig sgrub mchod stong rtsa dang / rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum sogs chos
sgrogs/ dus dran gyi mchod pa sogs gnyis kyi bgyi ba rim sel du bgyis pa lags/ ! lcags khyi lor dbus phyogs su 'brum nad byung skabs rgyan mchog grub 'brum nad bsnyun par
tshe dbang rjes gnang sogs dang / sku rim 'phrod bsten grul tsam byas pas bsnyun las grol/ nged rang gis tshogs khang du phyogs 'dus kyi bla khag bcas tshogs chen 'dus
par rdo rje phreng ba'i dbang dang / phreng ba skor gsum gyi lung sogs so so'i thugs 'dod ltar/ mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho/ lo nag /gsang 'dus sogs mang ba dang / rab byung bsnyen
rdzogs du ma bsgrubs/ pho

brang chen por gong sa yas phyin gyimajal kha dang / chos sde chen por ngan song sbyong ba'i rtsa ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi sgrub mchod stong rtsa/ chos sgrogs/ dus dran gyi mchod
pa sogs lugs gnyis kyi bgyi ba rim sel du bgyis/ ! lcags phag lor skye ba snga ma rnams su gzhan la gnod pa byas pa tshe 'dir smin te zas ngan gyis na tsha shin tu lji
ba zhig byung bar 'tsho byed dbang phyug gis zas ngan yin 'dra bas mched zla bos pa 'gab zer bar/ mdzod pas de 'phral 'bod mi btang bas 'byor par/ 'di pa mkhyen dpyod gzhan
dang mi 'dra ba 'jig rten gyi mes po lta bur song bas/ de 'phral phug skor sogs tsha drag gis bcos thabs mdzad pas skyug 'byams sogs kyis cung zad phan gshis rjes su
'cho thebs che ba byung kyang / nged rang gis de rigs 'ong ba'i don med byas par/ lar mo dang 'di kha'i chos skyong la dri ba byas par yin gsung bas ci drag zer bar/ de rigs
'ong don gtan nas med/ da dung yin min bsams na gong sa chen po sangs rgyas thams cad 'dus pa'i ngo bo yin pas gsung brtag cig zhus byas par/ mgron gnyer rin chen la
skyabs 'jug zhu rten zhon rtas gtsos ja 'khor drug sogs tshan grangs zhu sam bcas 'bul bar btang ba dbu mdzad chen mo brgyud sku zhabs su phul 'phral gsung brtag bka' drin
bskyangs / 'di rigs 'ong don mi 'dug kyang brtag par yin nges babs pas/ thog mar bsdu sman dang / 'dus nas rin chen rta ri ma sogs gtong dgos tshul gsos sman phon che tsam
so sor yig chung / brtse ba chen

po nas ma bor ba'i rim gro sogs le dbar med pa dgos tshul gyi bslab ston/ phyag mdud/ rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi 'phel gdung bcas de 'phral tsha drag gis slog pa gnang / 'di
skabs mthong snang la 'ja' 'od kyi dbus su bla chen sa skya pa/ 'ja' 'od kyi dges mdzad rdo rje'i pho brang / lha'i bu dang bu mo du mas rgyal mtshan dang ba dan sogs
kyi mchod pa'i bye brag /mtha' skor du dur khrod kyi mchod rten dang / keng rus/ 'ja' sprin/ zhing skyong gi rigs sogs mang ba zhig mthong snang la shar ba ni nad kyis skye
ba snga ma'i sdig sgrib dag pa dang / bla ma dang lhas thugs rjes gzigs pa'i ltas yin nam snyam mo/ /sngon tshe gzhan la gnod pa'i lan chags kyis/ /'bras bu nam yang bslu
med bden pa'i mthus/ /tshe 'dir dal 'byor ldan pa'i g.yar khang 'di/ /bhiSha'i nad kyi zug rngus mang zhig mnar/ /'di dus rang sems nad kyis bslad pa'i mthus/ /'khrul
snang sems kyi 'char sgor 'di ltar mthong / /yid 'ong 'chi med gzhon nu'i lam yangs 'dir/ /'ja' tshon sna lnga'i gur khang phub pa'i dbus/ /rdo rje 'chang dbang bla chen
sa skya pa/ /gzugs sku 'ja' 'od las grub kye rdo rje/ /gzhan yang dur khrod keng rus la sogs pa'i/ /ngo mtshar sprul pa'i ltad mo mang du mthong / /bslab ston bka' drin
bskyangs pa bzhin gsos sman nas 'tsho byed dbang phyug gis 'phrod bsten byas shing / rim gro rnams mched zla'i zhabs phyi mdzod pa lhun grub kyis khur blangs kyis myur bar
bsgrubs shing /

nad g.yog bsod nams rin chen gyis cag thon byas pas zhag bcu skor nas tshe 'then tsam byung / pho brang du bslab ston yang bskyar zhu bar mgron gnyer rin chen zhu yig bcas
btang bas shin tu dges te/ 'di rigs la bshal zhig gtang dgos kyang 'phen yul gyi chu mjug gtsang pos bkag pas 'grim pa rang ma byung dogs/ da lam res rin chen ril bu btang
ba 'gab gnang / gtong lugs kyi bslab ston yig chung dang rin chen ril bu bcas stsal ba 'tsho byed dbang phyug gis bslab ston ltar gtong ba dang / 'phrod bsten le dbar med
par lus bsgyur dang shi sgra/ rim gro mang tsam gnang ba'i rim gror mang ja spom thag gi thog kun mkhyen chen po'i sku 'dra tshogs dbu mar nged rang gi smon lam btab ste/
snyan shal dang 'gan sbyar dbul bar btang bas/ lha'i lam nas 'ja' dang me tog gi char babs pas tshang ma dogs pa'i khar/ shi sgra dang lus bsgyur bslab ston ltar byas
pas rim gror 'gyur che bar byung / tshe chog dang / kun rig gi sgrub mchod stong rtsa/ rnam 'joms/ bum sgrub du ma/ bka' 'gyur/ rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum/ bka' gdams/ gzungs
'dus/ bskal bzang / grwa tog gser gsum/ mtshan 'bum sogs grangs mang ba dang / tshe gzungs/ sgrol ma/ sher snying rnams 'bum ther re/ chos skyong so sor bskang ba brgya
rtsa/ lha mor bskang ba brgya rtsa du ma/ phyogs bzhi'i gtor ma/ 'phen yul gyi dgon rnams la mang skol/ zan gtor 'bum ther/ sngags pas brgya bzhi/ sa bdag 'khrugs

mdos/ gdong rgyan chu mdos sogs mdos rigs mang ba dang / rdzong sogs rim gro dang gang cir mched zla'i zhabs phyi mdzod pa lhun grub kyis gcag thon dang / chos sde chen por
bla khag grwa mang rnams kyis rten 'byung dang bsdus nas mang skol/ dgon lag so sos kyang rten 'byung dang rim gro sogs byas shing / gtso bor gong sa chen po'i brtse klong
nas ma bor ba'i thugs rjes ma shi tsam gyis rim bde byung / dgong zhig rmi mal du dmyal ba'i yul ljongs su slebs nas lcags bsregs kyi thang gi byang phyogs su lcags khang
gi sgo bcad 'dug pa ban gzugs shig gis phye byung ba'i nang du bltas pas/ dmyal ba'i sems can nyam thag pa zhig lcags thag gis btags pa nged rang la dungs pa'i rnam pa
byed pa zhig mthong bas snying rje tshad med pa zhig skyes/ de 'phral gnyid sad/ de nas bzung zhag shas dmyal ba pa de la dmigs pa'i 'od zer gyi spro bsdu dang / gsol 'debs
dang / bsngo smon byas/ mched zla sogs khur len rnams kyis 'di rigs khyod rang gis shes yod pas gtong mkhan bshad dgos shing / mi bshad na so sor lung bstan zhu zer
bar/ sngon gyi lan chags la da dung len byas na 'khor ba'i rgyu las mi 'dug pas lan mi byed/ mi nyan na skye ba 'di las phyi ma'ang mi 'phrad byas/ don la lan chags sogs
sdig sgrib sbyong bar bzod pa dang rna ba'i dper gyur/ lo 'di nang du gong sa skyabs mgon chen po nas bstan 'dzin dA la'i rgyal po bstan 'dzin chos kyi rgyal po'i rgyal srid
du dbang bskur ba gnang bar/ nged rang bla khag las

tshan dang bcas kyis legs 'bul sogs snga ma ltar gong legs phul/ gong sa chen po nas chos kyi bka' 'dri gnang bar gang shes kyi lan phul zhing sger mjal gyi slog sogs gnang
sbyin dpangs mtho ba gnang ste rang gnas su 'byor/ a mdo nas chos rje dpon slob gnyis brgya skor byon par lam 'bras bsdus tsam dang thugs 'dod kyi chos rnams phul zhing
/ chos sde chen po'i dus mchod/ gtor gzhi spo ba sogs sngar rgyun ltar bsgrubs/ ! chu byi lor lo gsar dang / tshe sgrub byas/ pho brang chen por yas phyin gyi mjal khar phyin
skabs mkhan rin po che pho brang du bzhugs par gser dngul gyi maNDal/ shel/ gos dar/ ja/ rta sogs 'bul dpangs che ba dang bcas mjal bas/ gzims chung gi sgo nang du mjal
dar bcas bsu ba gnang / phyag rtse sprod dang / gdan bzos che ba'i khar bka' nan ches pas bsdad/ lugs gnyis kyi gsung gleng gnang / sang rnam sras be con can gyi rjes
gnang zhig stsal dgos tshul zhus pas/ de kha 'ong / gcod khrid cig nged rang gis 'bul dgos pheb/ phyi nyin rnam sras rjes gnang rgyas par stsal zhing / nged rang nas nam
mkha' sgo 'byed kyi byin rlabs dang gcod khrid stan thog gcig ma phul/ mgon po che chung gi khrid sogs bka' chos mang tsam dgos tshul zhus pas/ gong du zhus pa 'gab gnang
ba bzhin zhus pas/ gong sa chen po'i bslab ston la mgon po'i chos skor rnams de kha mdzad na legs par 'dug cing / gzhan ma tshar lugs kyi dbang / khrid/ lung rnams kyi
rgyun ji ltar yod zhib tu stsal bar/ gong ma chos kyi spyan ldan las thob pa

rnams phyag len bcas snyan 'bul zhus pas shin tu dgyes te/ da rung ma thob pa rnams zhwa lu mkhan rin po cher skabs sbyar zhus pa 'gab ces bka' drin bskyangs shing / zur chas
dang gnang sbyin gya nom pa stsal/ rnam par rgyal ba'i chos grwar 'byor/ 'di skabs mtsho kha nas er kho dbon po grogs mched dpon g.yog nyi shu skor byon te/ tshogs su
mang ja/ nged rang la rta bzhi bcu skor dang / dar/ ja/ zam so sogs kyi ster cha rgyas par byas/ rab byung / bsnyen rdzogs/ dge tshul dang / kun rig gi dbang / mgon po'i
rjes gnang sogs 'dod sbyar dang / bdag rkyen gang legs sprad de/ gong zhabs yas phyin gyi mjal kha dang ser 'bras su mang skol la byon/ nged rang nas tshogs chen la lam 'bras
bsdus tsam dang / sbyong dkyil bcu gnyis/ sgrub thabs rgya mtsho sogs chos ra byas shing / 'di lo sog yul nas da rgan chos rjes khong rang sku na bgres pas/ zhabs phyi
dga' ba gcig bcas 'bul sdud la bod pa kha shas btang na 'ong tshul byung ba bzhin gong sa chen po yas phyin la snyan 'bul zhus par/ gzhan ma sog yul du 'gro sa med pa
de bzhin yin kyang / chos rje rang gzhan dang mi 'dra ba dang / de sngon bco brgyad rang gi 'gro srol yod 'dug pa bcas bcu tsam las mang ba ma btang phyin de khas 'thus zhes
bslab ston bka' drin bskyangs byung ba nas/ gsung rab dbang gi sar bla ma dam chos dang / rogs bla ma bsod nams dar rgyas/ rgyal po dge 'dun

skyabs spel sa'i sar bla ma bsod nams dpal bzang bcas gsum rdzong bda' byas par/ rta khal/ gos zas/ cha lag sogs bsgrigs te gtong rtsis bkod pa ltar mched zlas bsgrubs song
/ nad ro langs par gong sa chen po nas gsos sman bka' drin bskyangs/ 'tsho mdzad dbang phyug gis 'phrod bsten dang / rim gror kun rig stong rtsa dang / bka' 'gyur tshes
sgrogs/ bskang ba/ gtor chen rdzong ba sogs mched zla dang mdzod pa lhun grub kyis bsgrubs/ nad g.yog bsod nams rin chen gyis byas pa sogs tshang mas cag thon byas pas nad
ro langs pa sangs/ dge slong phrin las bzang po grongs par thos pa'i nub rmi lam du dmyal ba'i yul ljongs su slebs/ thang chen po zhig gi dkyil na khrag gi gtsang po dmar
na ra ra 'gro ba'i dkyil du zam pa zhig 'dug pa'i steng 'dam rdzab kyis khengs par lhwam nub bzhin du phyin pas/ zam pa'i dkyil tsam nas bltas pas zam 'og chu nang thams
cad dmyal ba'i sems can sdug bsngal can gyis khengs nas ngud mo'i sgra di ri ri byed 'dug pas lus rtse zing nge ba dang / snying rje bzod blag med pa skyes/ grogs gnyis
gsum tsam dang bcas phyir log pa na gnyid sad/ de nas bzung zhag shas de la dmigs nas 'od zer spro bsdu/ gsol 'debs dang / bsngo ba byas/ yang nub gcig rmi lam du yi dwags
kyi grong khyer zangs khog lta bu dmar hang nge ba zhig tu slebs/ mi dga' bzhin bltas pas phug lta bu'i nang na sems

can skra g.ya' zhing lus gogs po nyam thag pa du ma 'dug pa/ 'ga' zhig mdun du 'ong ba mthong bas snying rje tshad med pa skyes shing ci drag tu gyur pa na gnyid sad/ gsol
'debs dang / bsngo smon byas/ dmyal ba dang yi dwags kyi yul du yang yang 'gro ba zhig rmis 'dug pa ni maunggal gyi bu chen po'i ma dmyal bar zhen chags byed pa ltar ngan
song du zhen chags ches pas da dung log 'dod pa 'dra/ chos sde chen po'i dus dran mchod pa sogs lugs gnyis kyi bgyi ba sngar rgyun ltar bsgrubs/ ! chu glang lor lo gsar
dang tshe sgrub byas/ chos rje dpon slob sogs 'grul pa rnams rang gnas su 'byor khar chos dang bdag rkyen thugs 'dod ltar bsgrubs/ sgom sde nas rim gnyis g.yo med ti tsha
bla ma khu dbon dpon slob rnams dang / wa zhur nas mkhyen rab dbang phyug /'bul dpon bla ma bsod nams dpon g.yog mang ba 'byor zhing / tshogs chen du mang 'gyed dang / nged
rang la khrab legs pa/ rta ja/ mdzo g.yag sogs kyi ster sbyin mdzad/ lugs gnyis kyi bdag rkyen rgyas par sprad de gtsang du pheb/ nad ros 'tshe bar mched zla mgon po
rab brtan rogs la pheb ste/ mdzod pa dang gnyis kyis gong sar gsung brtag zhus pa'i cho ga /chos sgrogs/ tshe gzungs 'bum ther/ sher snying khri zlog rnams bsgrubs shing
/ 'tsho mdzad dbang phyug yab sras kyis 'phrod bsten byas pas nged rang drag tu song skabs mched zla glo bur du glo tshad shin tu nyen pa zhig bsnyun par 'phrod bsten dang
/ chos skyong khag gi lung bstan zhu bar/

mang ja'i thog spom thag stobs che ba/ nged rang nas tshe dbang brgya rtsa/ rjes gnang kha shas/ bskang ba/ chos sgrogs/ sgom sde bla rgan 'khor bas khro bcu'i gtor zlog /sngags
pas rdzong dang mdos rigs sogs tsha drag gis bsgrubs kyang bsod nams las ma grub pas/ nged rang la gus pa'i zhal ta kha cig mdzad de zhing la gshegs pas sems khong
du chud par gyur cing / nged rang gis bla mar gsol ba drag tu btab ste 'pho ba'i rnal 'byor dang / sgom sde bla mas kyang gsol 'debs mdzad/ pho brang du skyabs mgon chen
por mgyogs bsngo'i rten dang zhu yig phul/ zhag gsum gyi cho ga tshogs chen du sde pa che gsum pas zhus/ steng du sgom sde dpon slob rnams kyis kye rdor gyi sgrub mchod zhag
bco brgyad kyi ring dang / shod du tshul khang bla ma bsod nams kyis dbus zhe dgu pa bco lnga/ mdo brgya pa gsum/ gzims phug sgrub chen sogs kyis zan gtor 'bum ther sogs
zhe dgu'i khongs su bsgrubs shing / bdun tshigs thog gong sa chen por byang zhus rten gos dar legs pa yug kha shas/ hor sil mdzam gling kun khyab/ kong rna phung chung
bcas cha 'grig /bye ru'i lag skor legs pa/ kha thi ding phon gyi stod gos sogs na bza' cha tshang legs pa/ sman rnying gi yol ba/ khrab/ gri/ rta/ dre'u sogs 'bul dpangs
mtho ba dang / sde srid sku zhabs su skrol sga/ gos dar yug /bzang ja/ khrab/ rta/ dre'u sogs dang / dbu mdzad chen mor tshan grangs/ byang chas dpangs mtho ba dang bcas
pa/ sa skyar khams gsum chos kyi rgyal po yab sras la byang bu skyabs 'jug zhu rten gos

dar bzang ba yug kha shas/ gos nag gi 'cham gos legs pa cha/ 'khar rnga che legs shin tu bzang ba/ bye ru'i lag skor che legs cha/ dbang gi sog khrab/ sag thag dngul shan ma
cha tshang / na bza' sku gzan/ phyag shan sogs dpangs mtho ba/ rtse gdong zhabs drung sku mched la gos dar yug /bye ru'i lag skor/ khrab/ gri sogs dgu tshan bzang ba re/
zhwa lu mkhan rin po cher gos chen gyi gsol btsag /bye ru'i lag skor rdog che legs bco brgyad/ gos dar/ rgya zam sogs kyi 'bul ba/ dga' ldan khri rin po che/ stag lung
zhabs drung rtse zur gnyis/ 'bri gung zhabs drung / 'brug pa thams cad mkhyen pa/ rdo rje brag sprul sku/ smin grol gling gter ston rin po che/ sde chen chos 'khor dang sdings
po che gnyis bcas rnams la gos dar/ bye ru/ spos shel/ ja/ rta/ mdzo/ mdzo mo/ snam ras sogs so sor byang rten gyi 'bul ba dang / rje drung rin po che dang / pha bong
kha/ ser 'bras kyi bla khag tshang mar bsngo zhus kyi tshan grangs dang / sku zhabs grwa tshang du mang ja/ jo shAka sogs lha sa/ ra mo che/ po ta la rnams kyi lha khang
so sor/ snyan shal/ dkar me/ sa skya'i lha khang chen mo'i dbus lha khang rnams dang / kha'u/ byas 'gyur/ zhwa lu/ ri sbub/ ngor/ thub bstan/ gser mdog can/ rtse gdong
chos sde/ skyed tshal gong 'og /kho pe/ gsang phu/ gong dkar chos sde/ dwags po grwa tshang / ra ba smad/ rdo phud chos 'khor/ grwa thang / bsam yas rab byung grwa tshang
dang / mchims phu/ 'phan yul gyi dgon che phra tshang ma/

stag lung tshogs chen dang grwa tshang / ra sgreng rnams su mang ja/ dgon khag so so'i rten gtso dang / grags che ba'i sku brnyan rnams la snyan dar gzabs rgyas dang / bla
khag so sor bsngo rten/ mang ja/ bsam yas dang / ra sgreng gnyis la dkar me 'bul bar so sor btang zhing / a ma lags de nyid spyir chos la dad cing nang don dang / ma Ni'i
thugs dam smar ba dang / lhag tu sngags 'chang bla ma mchog la sangs rgyas dngos su nges pa rnyed pa lta bu'i byin rlabs kyis bzhugs gnas dpal ldan sa skyar skye ba blangs
nas/ gsal por 'dug tshul dgon pa nas 'byon mi rnams kyis gsung byung ba bzhin mgron gnyer dpon g.yog zhu yig bcas mched kyi byang bu bzhu ba dang lhan du rdzong bda' byas
pas/ gong bzhugs nas shin tu legs pa 'ong tshul bcas gnang 'dug cing / 'di khar byon grub nas kyang skye ba sngon ma'i chas dang zla bo rnams la ngos 'dzin byed 'dug
pas nges shes rnyed par gyur/ dngos gzhi'i cho ga la tshogs chen steng 'di kha'i dgon lag sogs khag che ba rnams bos te/ zhabs tog dang yon rgyas pa/ bla khag so sor 'bul
ba/ thon thon dang bdun tshigs/ zla mchod rnams dang bcas par 'phen yul stod smad kyi dgon khag rnams bsdus te cho ga zhus shing / lo mchod la tshogs chen bla khag dang
bcas par nyin gcig gi zhabs rtog rgyas par zhus/ sgrib sbyong rten du gong ma khu dbon dang / rdo rje sems dpa'i sku stong / rigs gsum mgon po 'dus pa'i gser thang lnga bzhengs
te rab gnas rgyas par byas te/ de nyid kyis gtsos ltos bcas dang sems can thams cad kyi don du dge ba bla med kyi byang chub

tu bsngos/ pho brang ri bo gru 'dzin du gong sa yas phyin gyi mjal khar phyin/ zhwa lu mkhan rin po cher tshar lugs kyi mgon po che chung gi skor rnams zhu rtsis kyis bslab
ston yang bskyar zhus pas/ rgyang tsam nas bkra shis chos sde'i dpon dang lhan du mkhan rin po cher zhu rtsis byas chog bslab ston rtsal zhing / dpal gror mkhan chen rdo
rje 'chang gi sku zhabs su phyin/ grub thob tshe dbang dang / mkha' spyod ma'i byin rlabs zhus/ chos kyi snyan 'bul zhus pas/ dbyar nam dus kyi stabs phul na legs pa 'ong
'dug pas de rtsis kyis gnang / nged rang gis tshe dbang zhig phul/ gnas kyi dbang po'i bsti gnas su 'byor nas chos sde chen por chos ra dang dus dran mchod pa sogs lugs
gnyis kyi bgyi ba rim sel byas/ ! shing stag lor bslab ston bka' drin bskyangs pa ltar mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang lho mos su bzhugs pa'i drung du 'byor/ gnas gsar dbon rin
po che dang / 'dar pa rje drung sogs nged don gnyer ba 'ga' zhig la brag rdzong ma phyi nang gsang gsum/ rtsa gsum 'khor lo bzhi la brten pa'i gsang khrid/ zhal gyi gsang
khrid/ gur gyi lha brgyad thun mong ma yin pa dang / brag rdzong ma'i rjes gnang / zhal gyi sgrub dus dang / bsnyen dus/ las bzhi/ gdong brnyan can rnams kyi rjes gnang
/ gur zhal rnam sras gsum gyi snyan brgyud kyi be'u bum rnams dang / gong dkar lugs kyi be'u bum/ rnam sras lnga phrag gsum dang / rab brtan ma thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes
gnang / zhal gyi tshe khrid sogs zab cing rgya che ba'i chos

skor/ gzhung sa chen po nas dbang chos gnang ba'i phyag dpe g.yar gnang dang / mthun rkyen dpangs mtho ba thab shing gis mtha' brten pa bka' drin bskyangs shing / snyan brgyud
thun mong ma yin pa 'di rnams thob pa ni lhar bcas 'gro ba'i skyabs mgon rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen pa chen po dang / mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang chen po'i bka' drin
las gzhan du rnyed par dka' ba ni/ kun mkhyen mkhyen brtses/ skye ba gsum gyi gong nas gsol btab cing / /tshe 'dir longs spyod sgrub pas mnyes par byas/ /dad dang snying
rje shes rab mi dman pa/ /kun spangs chos rje'i bstan la lhag par dad/ /ces gsungs pa ltar gtso bor gong gi bka' drin dang / nged rang gi sngon gyi las 'phro de rnyed pa
ni shin tu skal ba bzang ngo / /de ltar gsang chen chos kyi bdud rtsi mang du thob cing / nged rang gis kyang klu sgrub lugs kyi bcu gcig zhal dang / mi 'khrugs pa'i dbang
/ kun mkhyen rong ston chen po dang / ngor chen/ mus chen sangs rgyas rin chen gsum gyi bka' 'bum gyi lung dang / tshe dbang brgya rtsa phul/ dbon rin po che sogs kha shas
la thugs 'dod kyi zur chos kha cig kyang phul zhing / mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang gi zhabs drung du gser dngul gyi maNDal/ rta/ mdzo/ mdzo mo/ gos dar sogs dpangs mtho
ba zab chos kyi bka' drin nos pa'i legs 'bul du phul/ nged rang la gos dar sogs kyi gnang sbyin shin tu bzang ba rtsal byung kyang byin rten las ma zhus/ dbon rin po che
dang / 'dar pa rjes drung sogs nas kyang dar ras gos chen sogs kyi gnang sbyin

stsal/ 'di skabs mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang sku khams cung ma bde ba dang / nged rang yang lung rgyun ring bas mig mi gsal bar byung ba gong sa chen po'i snyan du lhon pas sum
ldan rdo rje 'dzin pa 'jam dbyangs grags pa gzigs rtog tu gnang ba'i skabs/ rna mo dgon 'ong sgo stong du dud grangs nyi shu skor gnang ba brtse bas bka' drin bskyangs
kyang / thog ma nas gzhis dang khyim mtshes kyis zhe 'gras stabs/ sar skya drag zhan rnams kha 'grig cing yid ma rangs pas gzhung sa chen po'i bslab ston la rtsi med kyi
'ong sgo dang 'u lag gnyis kar sgrub ma nyan pas brjes shig zhu bsams pas snyan lhon zhu grogs dgos tshul zhus/ mig gi 'phrod bsten gser tshugs sogs gnang bar gso rig rgya
mtshor mkhyen pa'i dkyil 'khor rgyas pa'i em mchi dar mo nas gnang ste sman dpyad gnang bas mig gsal bar gyur/ zhag lnga tsam nas dge slong rin po che yang bskyar gzigs
rtog la pheb skabs/ gong sa chen po'i bslab ston la nad mi theg pa rang byung na ma gtogs pa rjes gtsang dang lho kha sogs nas byung na bed mi chod pa zhig 'ong bas mi
'gab 'dra bka' drin bskyangs byung bar/ gzhung sa nas brtse ba chen pos bka' drin bskyangs par bslab ston la rtsi med kyi 'ong sgo bre gang / 'u lag rogs bcol phran bu las
ma byung bas/ rnam mkhyen khrel ba'i rgyur 'dug rung thag ring kyang mi zhu 'thu med yin tshul snyan 'bul gnang rogs dgos tshul zhus pas yang bskyar pheb skabs shig /de
na do zhag gzhung gi deb spo rtsis yin 'dug pas/ de gong du zhu rtsis byas na legs par 'dug ces bka' drin bskyangs/ chos ra gnang grub nas gong sa

yas phyin gyi mjar khar phyin/ shin tu dgyes pas chos ra sogs kyi dri ba zhib tu bka' drin bskyangs/ gnang sbyin dpangs mtho ba stsal/ lo mjug gdan sa nas 'jam mgon chos kyi
rgyal po yab sras pho brang du mjal khar pheb skabs/ nged rang lha sar rgyang tsam bsdad/ gong sa yas phyin gyis mjal kha dang / mkhan rin po che po ta lar bzhugs par nyin
re bzhin mjal bar phyin/ tshe dbang brgya rtsa stsal zhing / zhabs drung yab sras g.yul kha lhor bzhugs par gos dar/ gser dngul/ tshems grub kyi bla bres/ ja/ rta/ mdzo/
g.yag sogs mjal rten dpangs mtho ba dang bcas phyin pas thugs shin tu dgyes pas chos phyogs dang zung du 'brel ba'i bslab ston mang du stsal/ rgyun du mjal bar phyin
zhing tshe dbang lcags sdong ma kha shas dang / gur lha brgyad kyi rje gnang rgyas par stsal/ gnang sbyin gya nom pa dang / chos sder mang ja/ dam rdzas kyi 'gyed bcas gnang
ste chos grwa chen por 'byor/ rab byung / bsnyen rdzogs/ dus dran mchod pa sogs sngar rgyun ltar bsgrubs/ 'di skabs mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang dpal gror bzhugs par mched
grongs pas brgyud spel la gzhan med cing / 'di rigs sun pa las mi 'dug pas brgyud 'dzin ma byas na ji ltar gyi mdzod pa bslab ston zhu bar btang bas/ thugs 'dod ltar dpon
de rab byung rang la 'jog dgos pa e yin bslab ston gnang bar mdzod pa lhun grub kyis phan tshun gnyis kar bslab ston 'di rigs gnang na grwa rigs dang bstan pa la 'phral
phug gnyis kar med pa zhig 'ong 'dug pas/ gong sa chen por bslab ston zhu ba gnang nas gdung

'dzin rang gnang ba 'gab tshul pha gir bslab ston bka' drin bskyangs dgos tshul nan gyis zhus par/ mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang gis bslab ston zhu ba gnang 'dug par/ bslab ston
la brgyud 'dzin gzhag pa gtan nas mi 'gab cing / kha seng 'di khar 'phrad par 'ong skabs kyi dbon des bslab pa phul nas brgyud 'dzin byas na bstan pa la phan pa re gnyis
mi 'byung ba'i nges pa mi 'dug /de lugs 'gab gnang 'dug pa bzhin/ dpal gro nas kyang bslab ston zhib tu rtsal ba bka' ma chogs par/ zla bo rnams la labs te lo phyi ma'i
nang brgyud 'dzin gyi thag bcad/ mdzod pas zhu lugs nged rang gi bsam pa dang mi mthun tsam byung 'dug kyang / phyis su bslab ston ltar bstan pa la phan pa byung 'dug bsam/
shing yos lor lo gsar dang / bde mtshams shig byas/ gdan sa 'og nas khri chen pho brang du mjal kha gnang nas gnas kyi dbang por pheb par chibs bsu sogs sngar rgyun ltar
dang / rgyang tsam bzhugs gdan 'jags bar gzhis len sogs gang ci'i zhabs phyi zhus/ rdzong shar gyi gtsang khang 'du khang du mchod cha rnams sgrub sde dbon por gnang
grub 'dug cing / bla brang zhol bcas khang stong du song gshis 'jig la khad 'dug pa gzims khang du yod pa ya gir thugs bed chod pa zhig mi 'ong 'dug pas bdag tshor bka' drin
bskyangs na ji ltar lags zhes khri chen sku zhabs su zhus par/ de kha 'ong dogs kha'ang / deng sang khur bzhes kyi stobs yum sras la bsdur gzhig byas nas lan byed pheb
cing / gtsang du pheb 'phral bka' shog bcas bla brang nged rang

la gnang zhing / chos gzhis rnams rtse gdong rang gi phyag na yod/ gong sa chen po nas sde srid la dgongs khrol gnang skabs pho brang du mjal khar phyin/ dgu tshan lnga tsam
gyi 'bul ba dang phyag dbang dang gang ci'i snyan 'bul zhus pas shin tu dges pa'i tshul gnang / dpon tshang dar mo nas mgron khang du gnang ste/ na ning lho mos nas gsung
ba'i sa brjes kyi skor la/ re zhig chos rje rang 'byon mi dgos/ do chod gnyis tsam zhu don la btang chog bka' drin bskyangs/ rnam par rgyal ba'i chos grwar 'byor 'phral
mdzod pa lhun grub dang / mgron gnyer rin chen gnyis rdzong bda' zhus pas zhag shas nas mkhar rtse rdzong bzhugs dar chung nas gzigs rtog zhib 'jug la gnang song zhing
/ 'di kha'i chos skyong chen po dang las mkhan la lung bstan zhus pas/ rta dang sga'i dpe yin thugs la bzhed pa bzhin don shin tu legs pa'i phrin las zhu gsung / de bstun
nged rang yang zhu don du pho brang chen por bcar/ lha sar zhu bsgug la bsdad/ nyin re bzhin gsang sbug gi tsha bo gnyis dga' dang / mgron gnyer rin chen gnyis kyis nyan
lan zhus/ rna mo ba skya ser rnams kyis zhu khra dang snyan 'bul sna tshogs shig zhus song / nged rang gi jo gdan gnyer pas bdag pa'i 'ong sgo dang / chos bzhin rnams gzhung
sar phul nas dgon pa dang thag nye ba zhig nas sa brjes thugs rje che ba zhig bka' drin bskyangs dgos shing / sgrub mchod rnams dang / swatstsha lo mjug gi rim gro sogs
kyi thebs dang / dkor pa rnams rna mo dgon rang gi chag thebs su bka' drin bskyangs na ji ltar lags zhus pas/ dgongs pas

bzhengs nas gnyer pa'i 'ong sgo dang / sgrub mchod kyi thebs sogs so sor dbye ba gnang grub skabs/ drung pa gnyis kyis bka' blon shag tu snyan 'bul la 'tshangs par/ khyed tsho'i
dgon pa 'debs mi dang / sku drin che ba'i bla ma su yin bka' 'dri zhib tu gnang 'dug par/ thog mar gyi bla ma gnyan dang / drin che ba'i bla ma thang sag ya mi yin
tshul zhib tu zhus/ bco brgyad pa dang nged tsho bla grwa dang g.yog byed pa mi 'ong tshul tsha nan gyis zhus par brten dgongs pa khrel te/ rten mchod rnams rgyal stod par
gnang / sgrub mchod thebs sogs gzhung bzhes dang / kho rang grwa pa brgyad tshe nam ring la phog phran bu re gnang / dgon 'thor zhig tu 'gro la thug pa zhig byung song
ba ni bya mkhan gyi shing rtser rkang pa mgor bzhag nas rang gis rang la byin rlabs zer ba bzhin rang nyes dang bsod de'i dpe byung song / nged rang rgyun gyi dbang por 'byor/
chos srung rnams la gtang rag gi mchod pa rgyas pa dang / lha gsol nyin gsum gyi bar byas/ de skabs chos sde'i phu nas ser drag 'brug bsgrags glog 'khyugs pa dang bcas
mthong smon phyogs su song zhing / gnod pa ma byas par ni chos skyong gis phrin las myur du sgrub pa'i brdar go /nged rang gis gzhis su phyin nas bsdad/ rna mo rtsis
bzhes su sde pa bsod nams phun tshogs dang dar chung pa gnyis pheb par/ mdzod pa lhun grub/ tsha bo gnyis dga'/ mgron gnyer rin chen sogs kyis rtsis 'bul zhib tu zhus/ nged
rang la mkhar rtse'i 'og mthong smon nas phyag 'debs dor sum cu lhag tsam sngo thog rang bka' drin bskyangs shing / 'ong 'babs

lnga brgya dang / g.yog kha tshang them lnga/ gzhis g.yog them nyi shu rtsa lnga rnams dang / mthong smon du gtogs pa'i sa rigs rtswa chu shing gsum sogs dbang rigs bdag thob
tshang ma gzhung 'dzin ltar brtse ba chen po'i klong nas ma dor ba'i thugs rje shin tu che ba bka' drin bskyangs pa'i sku tshab bka' brgyad pa bsod nams phun tshogs dang
/ dar chung pa gnyis gnang / dgon pa dang 'brel mtshungs shing 'ong 'babs smar ba bcas bla brang 'dzin pa'i mchog tu gyur pa byang chub bar du gzhal du ma mchis pa'i bka'
drin stsal ba'i legs 'bul du pho brang chen por bcar/ las gshin gyi sku rdo nag las grub pa/ chu shel stobs che ba zhig gis gtsos bdog pa'i dngos po'i legs 'bul zhus/
'byed khra dang gtan tshigs rin po cher gzhung 'dzin ltar bka' drin bskyangs/ zur chas kyang rgyas par stsal te phyir 'byor/ ston chos sde chen po'i tshogs chen dang / khams
sog gi 'grul pa rnams la dbang / khrid/ rjes gnang / byin rlabs/ lung / rab byung / bsnyen rdzogs/ byang zhu so so'i 'dod sbyar dang rim sel byas/ sku zhabs grwa tshang
nas mnga' ris rab 'byams pa grogs bcas dang khams la bla mar pheb pa'i stabs sgrubs thabs brgya rtsa zhu bar gong sa chen po nas bka' shog rin po che bcas rdzong bda'
bka' drin bskyangs par sgrub thabs brgya rtsa dang / khong rang gi thugs bzhed ltar sgrub thabs rgya mtsho/ bde mchog dril bu pa sogs chos rnams rdzogs par phul zhing /
bsnyen bkur gyis kyang mnyes par byas te pho brang chen por phyir pheb/ gong sa chen po nas gnas tshul gyi bka' 'dri bka' drin bskyangs par/ bco brgyad ban tshang pa tshos
gur zhal sogs kyi bskang ba rgyun tu gtong 'dug tshul zhus 'dug pas pho brang du mjal kha phyin skabs mchod dpon chen mo brgyud bco brgyad kyi ban tshang pa tshos dpal
ldan rtser zla ba bcu pa'i nang gur

zhal gyi bskang ba zhag lnga'i ring gtong bar chas mkhar rtse nas sprod pa yod pa'i bslab ston gnang ba bzhin/ dpyad khra nang bzhin dgos cha mkhar rtse nas gnang nas bslab
ston ltar zhus/ ngos kyis phyin te zhabs pad brtan pa dang bstan srid rgyas pa'i chos srung rnams la phrin bcol rgyas par zhus/ chos skyong thim pa'i brag gi rtsar phyin
pas rten rdo gru gsum rnyed pa dang / nags gseb nas rkang gling 'bud pa sogs dgyes pa'i rnam 'gyur kyang byung / pho brang ri bo gru 'dzin du lhar bcas 'gro ba'i skyabs
mgon rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen pa chen pos sa skyong blo bzang sbyin pa rgyal srid du dbang bskur ba gnang ba'i legs 'bul du nged rang bla khag /las tshan khag dang bcas
pa lha sar 'byor zhing / legs 'bul sogs khri pheb sngon ma ltar zhus shing sger mjal yang zhus/ ngos kyis khyab bdag zhwa lu bas phran bur lam 'bras slob bshad cig bka'
drin skyong ba'i bslab ston zhig pheb dgos tshul zhus pas/ zhal dkyil shin tu 'dzum pa dang bcas de kha e 'ong blta chog gnang / dgyes pa chen po'i gnang sbyin bcas bsti
gnas su log /ma 'gyangs tsam nas mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang la bslab ston stsal te dgun zla bcu gcig pa nas lho mos su bzhugs gdan chags/ ! me 'brug lor zla ba gnyis pa'i
nyer lnga'i gza' tshes legs par nged rang / gnas gsar dpon rin po che/ lcags zam zhabs drung / 'dar pa rje drung / drung yig 'jam dbyangs/ mchod dpon sogs nyi shu skor
la chos kyi 'khor lo zab cing rgya che ba bskor ba ni/ rje btsun 'khrul pa'i dri ma zad pa grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis/ bla ma brgyud pa dang ldan rgyud

don rig /dam tshig mchog srung man ngag du mas brgyan/ /snying rjes rgyud brlan bstan bcos du shes/ /de yi zhabs bsten gsol ba lan mang gdab/ /de yis gnang nas dkyil 'khor
chen po ru/ /zhugs la dbang bzhi po rnams rdzogs par blang / /byin rlabs phra mo tsam gyis ma yin te/ /zhes dang / tshar chen rdo rje 'chang gis/ nyams len gdams pa'i gtso
bo ni/ /rgyal yum bdag med mkha' 'gro mar/ /paN grub dbang po bi rU pas/ /nos pa nas bzung da lta'i bar/ /rtsa ba'i bla ma yan chad du/ /dbang bzhi'i chu bo ma nub pa/
/bla ma'i gsung ngag bdud rtsi'i rgyun/ /tshad ma bzhi ldan dbang bzhi'i lam/ /rdo rje theg pa'i snying po yin/ /zhes bdag med mkha' 'gro'i gtso mos 'jigs bral dpal ldan
chos skyong la gdams pa nas bzung dbang bzhi'i chu bo ma nub cing / snyan brgyud mkha' 'gro'i zhal drod ma yal ba/ 'jam dpal rdo rje'i gdung brgyud rim par chig brgyud du
byon zhing / sems dpa' chen pos bdag chen rdo rje 'chang la gdams pa/ kha'u brag rdzong pa rjes 'brang dang bcas pa las thun mong gdul bya'i mig dang rna ba'i lam du ma
grag pa gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa gsang chen slob bshad kyi smin byed kyi dbang / grol byed kyi lam/ rgyab rten lung byin rlabs dang bcas pa gegs med
du stsal ba ni/ kun mkhyen mkhyen brtses/ 'khor 'das chos kun gsal bar byed pa'i lam/ /pha rgod bla ma'i gsung gi nyin mor byed/ /yid ches 'od zer 'bum ldan 'di shar tshe/
/gnyis snang mun pa'i smag rum ga shed song / /zhes

gsungs pa ltar/ rgyun nub pa med pa'i rten 'brel gyi 'phel rgyas su gyur pa ni ma hA kA la gur zhal dang / 'dod khams gtso mo rab brtan ma/ dam can pu tra chen po rnams kyis
phrin las g.yel med du sgrub par mngon/ mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang sku khams cung zad ltem pa'i tshul bstan par/ nged rang gi rmi lam du bla ma paN zhwa gyon pa mang po
rta thog nas 'byor ba dang / sog po rgya zog gi khal du ma ded nas 'ong ba sogs 'tshub 'gyur che tsam byung bar/ phyi nyin gong sa chen po nas nged rang la bka' sam bka'
drin bskyangs par/ mkhan rin po che'i sku rim du rnam 'joms kyi khrus rgyas pa zhig gi mjug tu sku glud 'di bzhin la rdzong gzabs pa dang bcas dan bag phyogs su thong pheb
cing / nged rang gi rmi lam du byung ba de rnams phyag bris su stsal byung ba dang / tshe dbang brgya rtsa phul/ bslab ston pheb pa ltar zhus pas sku ltem pa dwangs pa'i
tshul gnang / nged rang gis khong dpon slob gnyis kyi nyan du'ang phul te/ gong sa chen por tshar chen nas mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang gi bar gyi slob bshad bla ma brgyud
pa'i rnam thar sngar med pa rnams gsung rtsom bka' drin skyong dgos tshul zhus pas/ tshar chen rdo rje 'chang gis gtsos pa'i rnam thar rnams ngo mtshar ba bka' drin bskyangs/
skabs shig pho brang du mjal khar phyin skabs gong sa skyabs mgon chen po spyan cung zad mi gsal ba'i tshul bka' drin bskyangs 'dug pas/ khams sog bod pa sogs mjal
kha ba mang bas sku grib lta bus spyan la gnod pa byung dogs blos ma bzod par lho mos su 'byor 'phral mkhan chen

rdo rje 'chang la tshang mar phyag dbang bka' drin bskyangs pa mi 'gab tshul snyan 'bul zhus na ji ltar 'ong zhus par/ de kha shin tu legs pa 'ong 'dug pas nged rang dpon slob
lhan du zhu pheb pa bzhin zhu sam phul bas/ ngo ma drag gras tshor phyag dbang dang / mang mar phyag nas bka' drin bskyangs song / nged grogs mched gsum gyis gong sa
chen por zhabs brtan gsung rtsom bka' drin bskyang dgos tshul zhus par/ sgrol dkar gyi cho ga la brten pa'i zhabs brtan gyi gsung rtsom gnang ba'i thog nas/ nged dpon slob
so so nas nyin rer 'chi bslu bcas zhabs brtan gyi zhabs thog /dngos po'i 'bul ba sogs rgyas par phul/ mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang gis sku zhabs dang / dbon rin po che nas
nged la byi bar glang po che dang / phyug por rnam thos kyi bu'i dpe ltar rten 'byung rgyas pa re bka' drin bskyangs/ nged kyis zur chos su sgrub thabs rgya mtsho/ sgrol
dkar/ gnas brtan bcu drug /bka' gdams lha bzhi rnams kyi rjes gnang lung bcas dang / mi 'khrugs pa dang bcu gcig zhal gyi dbang / mgon po'i rjes gnang lung bcas sogs dbang
rjes gnang mang ba zhig phul/ chos ra grol 'phral slob bshad kyi phyag dpe rnams nyid chos kyi bdag po yin pas bshad sgrub 'phel bar mdzod gsung gnang ste/ bla mas slob
bshad kyi bdag por rten 'brel sgrig par mdzad pa ni/ dbon rin po che chos 'di'i bdag por de lta bu bzhugs bzhin du bdag la bsngags brjod dang ched du gdams par mdzad pa
ni dbon rin po che ring por mi bzhugs pa thugs mkhyen gyis chod

pa dang / phran bus chos 'di'i 'chad nyan la cung zad phan pa la dgongs sam snyam mo/ /gsang chen sprin gyi rnga gsang sgrogs pa'i gnas/ /dbus 'gyur 'dzin ma'i sman ljongs
lho mos su/ /khyab bdag rdo rje sems dngos bla ma rje/ /nges don zab mo'i chos kyi 'khor lo bskor/ /mdzes mdzes tshig skam bsgrigs pa'i bshad yams tsam/ /'grigs 'grigs rna
bar sgrogs pa ma yin pa'i/ /zab zab lam gyi mthar thug slob bshad chos/ /snyan snyan gsung gis 'doms tshe skal ba bzang / /a ho bskal par bsod nams bsags pa'i 'bras/ /'bras
bu tshe 'dir legs smin zab chos thob/ /thob tsam ma yin nges shes snying nas skyes/ /skyes tshe gnyis 'dzin snang ba ga shed song / /de tshe pha rgod rdo rje 'chang
chen des/ /gsang chen bstan 'di'i bdag tu khyed 'os zhes/ /snyan brgyud gdams pa'i gnad 'gag ma lus dang / /phyag dpe stsal te chos 'di'i bstan pa gtad/ /chas gzhung nas
bka' drin bskyangs te chos skyong so sor dpon slob rnams kyis gtang rag rgyas pa re phul/ chos re'i ring dpon slob so sor gsol phog thab shing gi mtha' brten pa bka' drin
che skyong gi bdag rkyen gnang / pho brang du gong sa chen po'i phyag dbang la phyin/ bka' 'dri rgyas par gnang / thugs shin tu dgyes shing gnang sbyin kyang stsal to/ /e
ma gsang chen mthar thug zab mo'i chos/ /tshe gcig bcu gsum sar snyegs nye lam 'di/ /kha ba'i ljongs 'dir sa skya'i 'jam mgon dang / /mkhas grub bye ba'i gtsug rgyan kha'u
pa/ /blo gsal rgya mtsho rnams kyis ches cher rgyas/ /de lta mod kyi gdul

bya skal dman pas/ /zab mo'i chos kyang nyan bshad ches phra'i che/ /sngon byon rnal 'byor dbang phyug sa skya pa/ /thub bstan spyi dang zab mo slob bshad pa'i/ /bstan pa bsam
bzhin spel phyir slar byon pa/ /'gro ba lha dang bcas pa'i skyabs gcig po/ /thams cad mkhyen gzigs chen po'i bka' drin las/ /deng dus skal bzang kun gyis thob pa 'di/
/bsam gyin bka' drin snying nas dran par gyur/ /rgyun gyi dbang por phyir 'ong skabs mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang lho mos kyi lcang gseb tu skyel mar pheb/ bka' bsgo zhus skabs
phyag phreng gnang nas rgyang tsam 'di khar sdod rtsis yin pas gtsang du 'gro kha 'phrad par shog gsung / dad gus kyi ba spu g.yo zhing mchi ma 'khrugs bzhin pa dang
bcas sku'i 'phrod bsten dang / zhabs pad yun ring du brtan dgos tshul gyi snyan 'bul zhus/ phyir log skabs su bzhengs te nged 'gro ba'i sar gzigs bzhugs pa mthong tsam gyi
sa nas rta kha bsgyur ba'i tshe phyag gis bkra shis pa'i kha btags che ba zhig nged phyogs su g.yugs pa gnang bas bla ma sangs rgyas dngos kyis dad gus g.yo ba med pa
mkhyen pas thugs yid gcig 'dres kyi brdar go /rnam par rgyal ba'i chos grar 'byor nas so sor chos dang rim sel gyi skabs gzhis su khyim 'dzin mar shin tu dge ba'i ltas dang
bcas sras 'khrungs 'dug pa/ nged rang la 'phros byung 'phral pho brang chen por srung 'khor dang ming dgos tshul gyi zhu yig phul te zhus pas thugs shin tu dgyes te/ sku
zhang dbon gsal tshes la ming dang rten 'byung smon lam dang bcas pa bla ma dgyes mdzad ma dang phyag mdud bcas stsal/ nged rang gis kyang phyin te srung 'khor dang tshe
dbang sogs gang legs byas/ mkhan

rin po che gtsang la pheb rtses bka' 'phros gnang ba'i lho mos su mjal khar phyin skabs/ thang stong rgyal po'i lugs kyi tshe dbang brgya rtsa/ sgrol dkar/ tshe sgrub bu ston
gong khug ma rnams gnang nas tshe'i rten 'brel sgrig pa gnang / mkhan chen rdo rje 'dzin pa pho brang du pheb/ nged lha sar phyin te zhag gcig nas/ gong sa chen po'i mjal
kha zhus shing / khyab bdag zhwa lu pa'i sku zhabs su phyin nas gong sa sku zhabs su thang lha'i bka' gtad dgos tshul snyan 'bul zhu grogs zhus pas/ gsol tshigs lhan
du gnang skabs gong du snyan 'bul gnang 'dug par/ chos rje gzhan dang mi 'dra bas de kha byas chog gsung bka' bzhes gnang / phyi nyen nged/ mdzod pa/ mgron gnyer bcas gsum
la bka' gtad bka' drin bskyangs/ gsol ja'i ring rnying ma'i lugs kyi bka' gtad kyi phyag len rnams bslab ston stsal/ gong sa chen po nas khyab bdag zhwa lu par gsung ngag
slob bshad gegs med du stsal ba'i legs sor na bza' cha tshang / gser dngul/ gos dar/ ja/ bu ram sogs dngos po dpangs mtho ba dang / zhwa lur rnal 'byor rgyud kyi sgrub
mchod 'dzugs rten du nye skor nas chos gzhis phon che ba stsal song / nged kyi sa gzhi bsnyen sngar nas grub gshis mgyogs tsam nA lendrar slob bshad kyi zhabs phyi zhu rtsis
lags pas ji ltar lags dang / mi grangs kyang ga tsam la byas chog snyan 'bul zhus pas/ dgyes pas brtse ba chen pos bslab ston la/ slob bshad 'phral du byed rtsis shin
tu legs shing mi grangs kyang slob bshad la nyi shu skor las mang ba ma byung 'dug kyang chos rje la rten 'brel gyi sgo

zhig 'dug pas/ mi grangs drug cu skor la byas chog /mthong smon nas sngar sor byin pa'i 'phros them lnga re 'dod par yod 'dug pa/ lha sa na sde pas 'byed khra gnang ba yod
ces bslab ston pheb/ lha sar zhag shas zhu sgug la bsdad pas mi ser them lnga'i 'ong 'babs g.yul kha dang bcas pa bka' drin du stsal zhing / gong sa chen por thon phyag zhu
bar phyin pas gtan tshigs dang / dngos po'i gnang sbyin gya nom pa dang bcas brtse skyong bka' drin bskyangs so/ /thams cad mkhyen cing gzigs pa'i spyan ras kyis/ /nam
yang 'dor med 'di phyir rjes su bzung / /khyad par mthong thos smon pa'i gzhis kha 'di/ /g.yog rigs yong sgor bcas pa brtse bas bskyangs/ /'di 'dri bka' drin byang chub
snying po'i bar/ /bdag dang rjes 'brang bcas pas gzhal min na/ /rtse gcig dad pa'i spu long cher g.yos nas/ /lag pad snying gar zum las 'os ci yod/ /gnas kyi dbang por 'byor
skabs mdo khams nas/ mkhyen bslab mthar son 'bul dpon bla ma bsod nams dang / bla ma lhar rje sogs 'grul pa stobs che ba brgya skor 'byor/ tshogs chen du mang 'gyed shin
tu mang ba/ cho ga stong rtsa bzhi tsam bsgrubs song bas nyin re bzhin tshogs dbur phyin/ gser dngul/ rta/ dre'u/ ja khrab/ mdzo sogs ster sbyin dpangs mtho bar byung
/ nged kyis kyang so so'i 'dod sbyar bzhin sbyin bdag pho mo sogs la dmigs med 'khor gsum yongs dag gi bsngo smon bgyis shing / 'grul par sne len gyi bdag rkyen gzabs rgyas
dang pho brang chen por drag gras rnams gong sa yas phyin gyi mjal

khar sne sbyor bcas rdzong bda' byas/ 'khor bstun dbang lung / rjes gnang / rab byung / bsnyen rdzogs sogs 'dod sbyar dang / dgun lam 'bras kyi chos ra rgyas pa dang / dus
dran mchod pa sogs sngar rgyun ltar bsgrubs 'di lo snga sor byon dus nged rang tsho gros byas te nged rang gi 'bul sdud bzhag nas/ spyi chen la ja tshul zhig tshugs na legs
pa 'ong tshul zhus don bzhin mkhyen bslab mthar son bla ma bsod nams kyis ja tshul gyi thebs su ja mar phon che ba bcas 'bul bar mdzad cing / nged rang bla khag las tshan
dang yon bdag nyid bcas bgros te gnyer par tshul khang pa bsod nams gzungs dang / lag g.yog bcas bskos thog /'di kha nas mchod cha/ dkar chas/ gdan/ thab chas sogs/ zhing
sogs rgyas par sprad de ji srid bstan pa nam gnas pa tshugs par zhig 'ong res/ de thog nas tshong pa ru ba bcas sgor nams gra sgrigs shog che bar byas shing / rim gyis
'bul skyel yang yang byung song ba bcas lo bcu skor bsam pa bzhin byung song kyang / de rjes phyogs sger ma nas mdor bstan zhing / lhag tu las byed kyi spyi sems chung
bar brten nam mkha' la 'ja' yal ba ltar gyur pas grwa pa rnams sngar gsar sogs kyi thugs son mi dgos par gzims mal du bag phab ste bzhugs chog par 'dug go /de bstun kun
mkhyen chen po bkra shis rnam rgyal gyi dus ja chad pa sems kyis ma bzod par gser pa bla ma dbu mdzad la 'phros byas par khong pas mar phon che ba dang / ja sogs rgyas par
sprad nas rim gyis gnyer pa bsko ba dang 'bul sdud rdzong ba sogs kyi bkod pa byas pas

da lta dus ja ma chad tsam byung ba yin no// ! me sbrul lor rigs brgya'i khyab bdag khams gsum chos kyi rgyal po rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen gzigs chen por nged rang dang
/ bla khag las tshan grwa dmangs dang bcas pas bskal brgya'i bar du zhabs pad brtan pa'i gsol 'debs su pho brang chen por bcar te/ bcom ldan 'das ma tshe sbyin yid bzhin
'khor lo la brten pa'i cho ga dang / nged rang nas dgu tshan dpangs mtho ba lnga/ gzims khang nas dgu tshan lnga/ bla khag dang las tshan khag gi dgu tshan gnyis/ grwa dmangs
spyi pas dgu tshan lnga dang / dpon slob tshang mas mjal dar legs pa bcas zhabs brtan phul ba'i nyin nyi ma gdugs 'jam zhing nam mkha' 'ja' tshon gyis khengs pa dang
/ cho ga'i skabs gong sa chen po'i sku tshe mtha' yas kyi sku 'od zer 'phro ba zhig mthong ba sogs rtags khyad par can yang byung zhing zhabs pad yun ring du brtan pa dang
/ sku zhabs rin po cher yang gzigs snang zhig byung 'dug pas phran bu rang yang tshe ring ba'i rten 'brel du mngon/ ston mo dang zur chas gnang cha sogs rgyas par gnang
ste rang gnas su 'byor/ tshogs chen mkhar rtser zla ba gcig gi ring sgrol dkar gyi cho ga dang / chos sgog gi ring zhabs tog gzhan las bzang zhing yon mtho ba brtse bas
bskyangs/ khyab bdag zha lu ba gtsang nas dbus su chibs kha bsgyur/ re zhig lho mos gzhis khar bzhugs gdan 'jags/ dga' ldan khang gsar du mchod dpon lags dang / dge slong
rin po che khyab bdag zhwa lu pa'i sku zhabs su paN chen shAkya shrI'i sdom rgyun gsan sar pheb pa'i gral du shog gsung / bcar skabs gnod 'tshes rkyen byas nad ro langs
pas/ mkhan rin po ches tshe dbang

lcags sdong ma rgyas pa/ rta mgrin gsang sgrub kyi rjes gnang stsal/ gong sa chen po'i sku zhabs su shog gsung / gur drag dang / rta mgrin gyi rjes gnang bka' drin bskyangs
shing / bka' bsgo zhus skabs re zhig lho mos su 'phrod bsten la sdod gsung bka' gnang ltar lho mos su phyin/ phog sogs cha rkyen rnams gzhung sa chen po nas bka' drin bskyangs/
dpon tshang dar mo nas bslab ston bcas bka' drin che bas zhag gsum tsam bzhugs nas bshal gyi 'phrod bsten gnang bas bla ma mchog gi thugs rjes rtags shin tu thon
pa bcas legs par byung / dbon tshang dar mo nas yang yang pheb/ dbon po lo yag dang / khal kha chos rje gnyis bka' sam chu thog bar khag res rten gnang bcas bka' drin yang
yang brtse bas gnang / nad gzhi rim dwangs su song skabs rgyang tsam nas 'di khar byon nas gsang ba 'dus pa 'jam rdor dang / spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang dbon rin po che sogs
la dgos par 'dug pheb pa bzhin/ gong sa chen po'i phyag dbang la bcar skabs chibs chen kha shas/ a grung kha shas bcas bsu bar gnang / dgyes pa chen pos phyag dbang dang
/ dbang gi bslab ston bka' drin bskyangs nas brtan ma khang du bsdad/ bka' blon shag tu mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang / dbon rin po che/ mchod dpon lags/ dge slong rin po
che/ bzang ldan mkhan po/ /zhwa lu mkhan 'jam dbyangs/ drung yig bstan 'dzin dbang po sogs mang tsam zhig la gsang ba 'dus pa 'jam dpal rdo rje dang / spyan ras gzigs gnyis
kyi dbang dngos sta shin tu rgyas par phul bas/ mkhan

chen rdo rje 'chang la yang dag dang gshed dmar gnyis gong sa chen po nas bka' rtsom bka' drin bskyangs pa'i ljags lung zhus/ gong du thon phyag zhus skabs/ dus 'khor dang
mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i dbang dbon rin po cher 'bul dgos pa'i bslab ston dang gnang sbyin sku mdun du stsal/ lha sar log nas phyi nyin 'bras bu gling du mkhan chen rdo rje
'chang gtsang du pheb pa'i pheb skyel du phyin/ byang chub ma thob bar rjes su 'dzin pa'i snyan 'bul zhus/ lugs gnyis kyi zhal ta zhib tu stsal/ gtsang du chibs kha bsgyur/
nged bsti gnas su 'byor nas 'bul sdud khag dang grwa rigs rnams la dbang lung mang tsam dang / dgon lag tu 'gro ba dang dus dran mchod pa sogs sngar rgyun ltar bsgrubs/
! sa rta lor a mdo nas chos rje dpon slob/ nged rang gi 'bul dpon bla ma 'dun grong pa bstan 'dzin chos 'phel/ hor pa dang smar khams sogs 'grul pa nyis brgya skor 'byor/
nyin re bzhin mang 'gyed thog nged rang gis phyin zhing / chos rje sogs kyis rol mo'i rigs dang / mchod rdzas du ma/ gos dar/ ja rta/ mdzo g.yag sogs kyi dngos po dpangs
mtho ba'i ster sbyin rnams blangs/ nged rang nas zab pa chos kyi dbyings dang / rgya che ba sems can gyi don du bsngos/ 'bul dpon bla ma bstan 'dzin chos 'phel gyis
nged rang gi tshogs khang du gser sku rgya nag ma 'byon gtsang ba/ rgya sil/ gser dngul/ gos chen/ ja ko tra shin tu mang ba/ rta drel sum cu skor/ mdzo g.yag sogs kyi rtsis
sprod kyi 'bul ba mig rgyan la phan par byung / 'grul pa rnams la chos dang sne len 'dod sbyar byas/ chos rje sogs drag gras rnams gong sa yas phyin

la phyag dbang zhu bar btang zhing / 'grul pa rnams gtsang mjal du song / rgyal bas rgyu 'bras kyi 'bras bu bslu ba med pa mdo rgyud du ma nas gsungs pa ltar skye ba snga mar
gzhan la 'tshe ba byas pa'i 'bras bu tshe 'dir smin pa'i bhiSha'i zas yang bskyar zhig byung bas 'chi bar thug pa zhig na bar/ bla brang ma 'thor tsam dang / dngos po
sogs sngar rgyun ltar gyi re bas dbyug gu spun gyi thang sku gnyis bzhengs pa'i gcig 'di kha'i phyag mdzod sbug dang / gcig gzhis su bskur te zhabs drung la cag thon dgos
pa'i bkod pa bcas mgron gnyer rdzong bda' byas/ cung zhig thu ru song skabs bla ma dge slong gis glud brdzongs dang / cha gsum gyi stabs 'khris su bzhugs/ mdzod pa lhun
grub kyis mang ja'i thog sbom thag 'phral btang dang / pho brang chen por bslab ston dang / srung 'khor thugs dam skyabs 'jug zhu ba'i rten klu 'byin las grub pa'i sangs
rgyas kyi sku 'gangs che ba zhon rtas gtsos tshan grangs zhu yig bcas 'bul bar btang ba sku zhabs su 'byor 'phral thugs 'dzangs kyi tshul gyis gsung brtag 'phral du gnang
/ 'tshubs cha che tsam 'dug pas rim gro'i bslab ston dang / rin chen ril bu gnyis dang / dbang po'i ril bu gsum nyi tshod bka' sam du thebs pa'i 'phral rdzong gnang / 'tsho
mdzad rta mgrin tshe ring gis gsung brtag ma pheb gong skyon byung dogs kyi bshal btang bas bla ma rnams kyi thugs rjes shin tu thebs pa byung / rim gror tshe chog stong
rtsa/ kun rig stong rtsa/ tshe gzungs 'bum ther/ sgrol ma dang sher snying 'bum ther/ gdugs dkar khri tshar/ gtsug tor 'bar ba stong rtsa/ gzungs 'dus brgya rtsa/ bka'
'gyur/

'bum dang nyi khri/ brgyad stong rnams lo grangs/ bka' thang dang / gser 'od brgya rtsa/ chos skyong so sor bskang ba brgya rtsa du ma dang / mtshan rgyun/ phyogs bzhi'i gtor
ma/ bla ma dge slong gis gtsos dge 'dun rnams kyis cha gsum dang / glud kha brgya rtsa/ 'phan yul gyi dgon che phrar mang ja/ sngags pas brgya bzhi sogs mdos rigs sna
tshogs/ rgyal rdzong rnams bsgrub pa dang / seng gdong ma'i sgrub pa zhag nyer gcig bsgrubs nas gtor ma 'phangs pas/ gtor ma nas me stag gnod byed phyogs su song 'dug /gong
gi bslab ston ltar shi sgra brjod pa/ lus bsgyur sogs byas pas tshe 'then tsam byung / 'di skabs shig rmi lam du/ tsha dmyal du slebs nas rdo gzhong 'dra ba zhig gi nang
du nged nyal nas gnas pas mtha' skor du gshin rje'i skyes bu mang pos mtshon cha sna tshogs dang / tho ba mang du 'phyar te bsdigs grabs su 'dug pa mthong ma thag /dmyal
ba'i sems can rnams sdug bsngal las sgrol ba'i phyir nga rang gnas 'dir ci byung yang lo stong phrag du mar sdod snyam pas snying nas zhe dam bcas pa dang gshin rje rnams
mig phab ste mtshon cha rnams zhul gyis bzhag song ba'i ngang nas nged lha sa'i khyams ra nang ma'i sgo rtsar slebs/ mi kha shas dang bcas jo shAka gi sku mdun du 'byor
pa dang gnyid sad/ sems bskyed 'di bzhin byas na sdig sgrib sbyong ba la gzhan las lhag par 'dug snyam/ gong sa chen por bslab ston zhu ba dang / sku'i bla sman e ma phyi
dar mo nas la 'phrod bsten gyi bslab ston zhu bar zhu yig bcas mtsho mdzad rta mgrin tshe ring brdzongs pas/ dge slong rin po che brgyud phul

bar thugs shin tu dgyes te/ slad nas rim gro dang spang blang gi bslab ston bka' sam rim gro'i rgyur dngul srang bzhi bcu zhe lnga bka' drin du stsal/ dpon tshong rin po ches
kyang bslab ston zhib rtsol gnang nas 'khris su bcar/ 'di skabs rje btsun chen po/ g.yag rong rnam gnyis/ mkhyen rab chos rje/ gong ma de nyid sogs bla ma dang yi dam
chos srung du ma/ dpa' bo mkha' 'gro dur khrod kyi mthong snang dang / skabs 'gar rgya 'dre mang pos rtsod pa byed pa dang / cho 'phrul sna tshogs ston pa/ a tsa ra'i gzugs
kyis mtshon cha'i 'khrul 'khor byed pa sogs 'khrul snang du ma byung / gong gi bka' bzhin rim gro ba rnams la zhabs tog dang yon shin tu bzang ba mdzod pas bsgrubs/ 'tsho
mdzad kyis 'phrod bsten dang / nad g.yog mgron gnyer rin chen dang / gsol dpon kun bzang gnyis kyis cag thon dang / mdzod pa/ bla ma mdun grogs pas gtsos nang 'khor skya
ser tshang ma dang / nA lendra'i bla khag dang tshogs chen dgon lag so sos nye ba dpal gnas dang / gsang sbug mi ser rnams so so nas 'byor bstun gyis 'bul ba/ tshogs
'khor sogs zab rgyas kyi rten 'byung dang / rim gro khur blangs kyis bsgrubs pas nad las thar te lus kyi shed che ba rang ma byung kyang gong sa chen po mjal 'dod kyi phyag
dbang du phyin pas brtse 'dzin gyis dgyes tshor dang / nad mjug skyong dgos tshul gyi bslab ston dang gnang sbyin stsal/ mchod dpon lags/ dge slong rin po che/ dge slong
ngag dbang dkon mchog /dpon tshang sku zhabs sogs phyag phyi drag gras rnams kyis dgyes tshor gyi gsung 'phros dang / kha btags che ba'i gnang sbyin stsal te chos grar
'byor/

so sor 'dod sbyar gyi dbang lung sogs dang / rab byung / dge tshul/ bsnyen rdzogs/ byang zhu sogs rim sel byas/ rgya nag mi sna dang lhan du chos rje'i 'bul skyel ba/ dge slong
sangs rgyas dpon g.yog rnams 'byor/ bla bre/ dngul/ dar/ gos chen sogs dngos po rnams rtsis sprod dang / da rgan chos rje grongs pa'i gnas tshul byung bar tshogs chen
du zhag gsum dang / byin rten shin tu mang ba bsres pa'i sman 'dam las tshe dpag med kyi sku spar ma stong dang rtsa gcig bsgrub par zhal gser dang / gzhan mar zangs chu
ljib gsol bcas bsgrubs/ lo 'di'i dbyar khams gsum chos kyi rgyal po gong sa chen po nas gnas gsar gyi dbon rin po che rdor phreng gnas sar rdzong bda' byed rtsis yin pas
de lugs dgos tshul gyi bka' shog rin po che spyi bor pheb/ ma 'gyangs par yang bskyar gyi bka' shog bcas dpon rin po che dang / 'dar pa rje drung bcas lho mos nas nA lendrar
pheb/ 'di kha'i dbon rgyan mchog grub kyis gtsos bla khag las tshan rnams kyis chibs bsu dang / dgon gnas nas ser phreng rgyas pa bsang dang bcas pas/ bla brang du
spyan drangs te pheb 'phral mjal dar phar 'bul tshul gnang dang / phyag rtse sprod sogs kyis mjal 'phrad zhus/ dbu chos sogs gra dmangs rnams kyis kyang mjal dar phul/ gong
gi bslab ston sogs rna ba'i bdud rtsir gyur pa'i gsung 'phros 'jebs shin tu chags/ dpon slob rnams bla brang rang du bzhugs pa gnang zhing / gzhis len dang rgyun gyi zhabs
tog shin tu gzab par zhus/ gzhung sa nas zur chas kyi bka' shog nang bzhin mkhar rtse nas zhugs shing sogs 'bul mi gnang / phyi nyin nas

dbon rin po che gtso bor gyur pa'i dpal 'dam du byin gyi 'dus pa rgya mtsho'i tshogs la zla ba gcig gi bar rdo rje phreng ba dkyil 'khor bzhi bcu zhe gnyis dang dge legs su
bya ba'i dkyil 'khor gsum ste zhe lnga'i dbang dang / kr-i ya skor gsum gyi lung sogs rgyas par phul zhing / de skabs lo nas sems dpa' chen pos khong rang gi gzims dpon
bla ma sogs kha shas rdzong bda' gnang bar sbyong rgyud dkyil 'khor bcu gnyis kyi dbang dang / mgon po lcam dral dang / rnam sras sogs kyi zur bka'i rjes gnang du ma/ sgrub
thabs brgya rtsa sogs dbang / rjes gnang / lung mang tsam phul/ dbon rin po ches chos yon la gos dar/ snam ras sogs kyi gnang sbyin shin tu gzabs pa stsal/ nged kyis kyang
dar ras/ gos snam/ ja rta sogs kyi pheb rdzong rgyas par phul te phyir pheb/ sgrub sde dbon pos brag chen sgrub sde 'di 'ong sgo gzhan dang mi 'dra ba zhig yin kyang
/ sa thag ring gshis nged tshos mi 'khyongs 'dug pas bco brgyad nas bdag byed dgos gsung ba bzhin lo shas bdag byas shing / de nas dge slong rin po che sku drin gzhan dang
mi 'dra gshis chos gzhis su phul/ chos sde chen por dus dran mchod pa dang / lo mjug gi gtor brje sogs sngar rgyun ltar byas/ ! sa lug lor lo gsar dang / tshe sgrub zhag
bdun ma zhig byas/ khams nas mkhyen rab sku skye dpon slob nyi shu skor dang / 'grul pa kha shas 'byor/ mang 'gyed dang ja sogs kyi bsnyen bkur byung / lugs gnyis kyi
sne len byas/ 'di lo sa'i tshangs pa chen po sangs rgyas rgya mtsho khams gsum chos kyi rgyal po rigs brgya'i khyab

bdag rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen gzigs chen pos gser gyi 'khor los sgyur ba'i khrir dbang bskur te mnga' gsol ba'i legs 'bul du nged rang / bla khag /las tshan dang bcas pas
pho brang chen por bcar nas/ nged rang gis sku gsung thugs rten/ gser dngul/ gos dar/ me mda'/ khrab/ ja/ rta sogs kyi dgu tshan lnga dpangs mtho ba/ gzims khang nas dgu
tshan lnga/ bla khag las tshan dang bcas pas dgu tshan re/ spyi so nas dgu tshan lnga/ nged kyis gong sa yas phyin du sger mjal la dgu tshan gsum re phul/ ston mo dang
zur chas gzabs rgyas/ sger mjal gyi slog gnang sbyin stsal/ rang gnas su 'byor nas dus dran mchod pa dang / byang zhu/ gtor spod/ bskang ba/ bka' 'gyur chos sgrogs mang
ba/ lo mjug gi rim gro sogs sngar rgyun ltar byas/ lo 'di'i nang du lha khang rgyal smad par snga sor dgu gtor sogs kyi rgyun med 'dug kyang dge slong mchod gnas dang / mchog
ldan gnyis kyis bskang gso 'dzugs rtsis yin pas ji ltar 'gab gsung bar/ de kha mdzad na shin tu legs shing bstan pa la phan pa 'ong 'dug zhus/ bskang gso'i phyag len
dbyangs sogs dpyis phyin par bslab song zhing / 'di kha nas rgya sil legs pa/ gser rnga sogs cha lag /mang ja sogs phul zhing gzengs bstod/ lo phyi mar pho brang chen por
sku rim du dmigs pa'i bskang gso gsar du btsugs yod pas mthun rkyen bka' drin che dgos tshul gyi zhu yig phul zhing gang ci'i bkod pa byas pas gong sa sku zhabs nas rgya
sbub legs pa zhig bka' drin bskyangs 'dug/ ! lcags sprel lor lo gsar rgyas pa dang / tshe sgrub cig byas skabs shig sbo shog tu rgyal

pos yer khin mi khyim 'bum phrag bcu bdun yod pa zhig gzhungs chen por phul ba'i legs 'bul du phyin/ yas phyin du mjal kha zhus skabs dka' 'dri zhib tu gnang zhing zur chas
dang gnang sbyin stsal nas dga' ldan khri rin po che sgrub thabs brgya rtsa gsan par pheb pa'i bslab ston pheb/ 'di skabs rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams nges don mi shigs
rdo rje'i sku brnyes shing zhabs pad yun ring du brtan pa zhig 'ong ba gzhir bcas kyang / drang don du snyigs ma'i sems can skal ba dman shing sku na yar la pheb pa dang
ji ltar 'ong bsam blo cung zhig 'dzangs te/ zhabs pad yun ring du brtan phyir zhabs brtan zhig bka' drin che nges/ phran bu rnams mkhos chung bas nyi 'og gi grub mtha' ris
su ma chad pa rnams la 'dzugs pa gnang dgos tshul ngos kyis dge slong rin po che brgyud snyan lhon zhus shing / bya lo gsar 'phral mgron gnyer rin chen zhabs bskul dang
/ zhu rten rta sogs dpangs mtho ba zhu yig bcas rdzong bda' zhus par/ bya lo zla ba dang po'i nang du thugs dgyes pa chen pos mkhyen brtse nus mnga' mar grags pa'i khyad
par du 'phags pa bka' rtsom bka' drin bskyangs shing / dbus gtsang gi gra sa so sor 'dzugs pa'i bslab ston dang mang ja bcas lcags bya zla ba dang po'i nang du 'dzugs pa
gnang song zhing / 'gro mir gnang sbyin gya nom pa dang / phran bur yang bka' shog gnang rten bcas stsal/ nged rang pho brang nas 'khor 'phral dga' ldan nas rgyal tshab
dam pa khri rin po che pheb par chibs bsu sogs rgyas par zhus/ zhag nyi shu lhag tsam bzhugs gdan 'jags par sgrub thabs brgya rtsa/ rgya mtsho/ rgya gzhung so so'i lung
sogs thugs bzhed kyi chos mang tsam phul/ gser dngul/ gos dar sogs

rgyas par stsal zhing thugs shin tu mnyes par gyur te chibs kha bsgyur bar pheb skyel sogs gang legs zhus/ sde dge dbon po kun dga' rab brtan sogs khams 'grul pa mang tsam
'byor/ khams zog gi rigs ster sbyin dpangs shin tu mtho bar byung / lugs gnyis kyis mgu bar byas te 'jam mgon bla ma'i gdan sa dpal ldan sa skya dang / ngor e waM chos ldan
sogs gtsang mjal du rdzong bda' byas/ chos sde chen por chos dang / dus mchod kyi rim pa/ byang bu zhu ba sogs 'phral dgos rnams dang / dgon lag so sor 'gro ba sogs sngar
rgyun ltar byas zhing / pho brang chen por gong sa yas phyin gyi mjal khar phyin par zhag shas nas mjal kha shin tu legs pa bka' drin bskyangs/ 'di skabs gong sa skyabs
mgon chen po rgyal du chibs kha bsgyur grabs kyis bzhugs sgar gyi chas thugs grabs bka' drin bskyangs 'dug pas/ blo ma bde bar bzhugs gral grol skabs ngos kyi sku mdun
du phyin te rgyal tu chibs kha bsgyur tshul zhig thos byung bas/ pha gi lung pa dang chu bsil ba zhig yod 'dug pas sangs rgyas kyi sku la bsnyun pa ga la mnga' na'ang /
sems can rnams kyi ngor sku la gsol chab sogs mi 'phrod pa'i tshul bstan dogs pas bstan 'gro'i don du pho brang 'di gar bzhugs gdan 'jags pa gnang dgos tshul phyag dang bcas
gsol ba nan gyis btab pas/ spyan nam mkha' la gzigs te dal cig bzhugs/ de nas nged la gzigs te snga sor rgya nag nas 'khor skabs mchod yon dang lhan du phyin/ de nas
bying bas 'gro ma thub cing gtor spod sogs gang ci'i khyad nas 'gro dgos nges yin kyang / chos rje nan ches pas zhag gsum nas gsal byed bka' drin bskyangs/ zhag gsum

nas thon phyag zhus pas/ mchod dpon lags brgyud pheb len la chos rje rang gi gsol ba btab pa'i ngor pho brang rang du bzhugs gdan 'jags rtsis yin pheb byung bas sa dang po
thob pa ltar gyur// ! lcags bya lo steng du song bas tshe sgrub rgyas tsam dang / spar sme sogs kyi rim gro byas skabs khyu 'bum dang nyag re nas 'bul skyel ba sogs khams
'grul kha shas 'byor/ ja/ rta/ mdzo/ g.yag sogs 'bul dpon bla ma'i yi ge dang ngag bkod ltar gnyer pa a nu rgyal dang kun dga' dar rgyas kyis rtsis legs par sprad/ 'di skabs
gong ma khu dbon gyi phyag mdzod du rnam sras kyi sgrub pa gnang nas rgyang tsam song ba dang / rnam sras kyi sgrub pa zhig byas na legs pa 'ong 'dra bsam/ rten dang
gtor ma dgos 'dod 'byung ba nas bshad pa ltar phyi nang gsang ba'i rten dang 'khor lo sogs sgrub pa'i rdzas rnams ma tshang ba med pa/ spyan gzigs sogs mthong bas yid 'gul
ba bshams te/ nged rang / ma yum sku skye/ bla ma/ dge slong / mchod g.yog bcas kyis rgyal phur gyi 'grub sbyor mdzoms par dbu btsugs te phyag rdor gos sngon can gyi bsnyen
pa byas/ de nas dge slong brgyad kyis dgos 'dod 'byung ba nas bshad pa'i tshogs sgrub zla ba gcig gi ring byas par phyag rdor dang rnam sras kyi sku brnyan rnams nam
mkhar 'phar ba dang / spyan gzigs kyi mtshon cha bar snang du khyer nas rgyang tsam nas rang gnas su skyel ba/ sil snyan rang khrol dang / rnga brdung ba/ dung 'bud pa
sogs chos skyong 'khor bcas thugs 'khul ba'i tshul dang / gzi brjid kyis khengs par gyur/ gser/ dngul/ lung thang / ja/ 'bru sogs bar snang nas dngos

grub kyi tshul du yi ge dang bcas mchod bsham khar 'phang ba/ rigs brgyud dang / bla brang / dgon gnas/ mchod gzhis dang bcas pa 'phel zhing dar rgyas dgos tshul gyi yi ge
gtor ma'i mdun du bzhag pa re zhig nas mi snang bar gyur par/ phyi nyin rigs brgyud 'byung ba dang / rim gro sogs spang blang byed dgos lugs thabs dang rten 'brel/ dar rgyas
sogs 'ong ba'i lung bstan gyi yi ge gsal ba byung zhing / yang gnod sbyin rgyal po 'khor bcas kyi yi ge so sor 'dug par rta brgyad rnams so so'i ming gi kha yig dang
rnam thos kyi zhes pa'i kha yig 'dug pa'i nang du 'di bzhin 'dug go/ ! khyab bdag rdo rje 'dzin dang gsang ba'i bdag /'gro bzang snying po zangs mkhar lo tsA ba/ /khro lo
chen po bu ston yab sras sogs/ /mchog stsol rtsa brgyud bla ma'i zhabs la 'dud/ /dbang sngon ri bo'i spo la mtshams sprin gyi/ /cod pan g.yo 'dra'i 'jigs rung khyod kyi
sku/ /ha ha'i gad rgyangs 'brug stong dgod pa yi/ /gsang bdag rdo rje 'dzin la phyag 'tshal lo/ /gangs ri ltar dkar seng chen 'gying ba'i steng / /btso ma'i gser zhun ltar
brjid nor sbyin dbang / /rgyal mtshan ne'u les nor bu'i gru char 'bebs/ /bstan srung ngal bsos dbang por phyag 'tshal lo/ /de las phun tshogs dge ba gang thob pa/ /blo
gros khang bzang snyan brgyud nor gyis gtibs/ /rgyal mtshan 'phyar ba'i gzi brjid khams gsum 'gengs/ /dpal 'byor bzang pos dbul phongs zhi bar shog /skyabs mchog rin chen
gsum gyi bden pa dang / /rgyal chen chos skyong srung ma'i mthu stobs dang / /chos dbyings rnam dag bden pa'i byin rlabs kyis/ /lus dang

grib ma bzhin du 'grogs par shog /phyi rol mi mthun gnod pa kun zhi zhing / /nang du 'dod rgu'i dpal 'byor phun tshogs rgyas/ /gsang ba lung rtogs yon tan yar ngo yi/ /zla
shel lta bur rgyas pa'i bkra shis shog /dge'o/ /zhes pa 'di rnam thos bus dngos su stsal zhing / 'di rnams kyi ya mtshan ni rin chen mang sprul dang dngos su mjal ba lta
bur byung bas gzhan gyi blor mi shong bas bzhad gad kyi rgyur 'dug kyang sgro btags kyi tshig min pas shes ldan yid ches kyi zlos gar bsgyur 'tshal lo/ /rgyal ba'i bstan
srung chos skyong rnam thos bu/ /'khrul med brgyud pa'i gzhung bzhin legs bsgrubs pas/ /dngos grub 'dod rgu 'bad med 'byung ba'i brdar/ /ya mtshan rmad byung rtags mtshan
mngon du gyur/ /spyan gzigs bar snang khyed dang rang gnas skyel/ /sil snyan rnga sogs rang khrol dung 'bud pa/ /gser dngul ja 'bru dngos grub tshul gyis ster/ /yab yum

/ngal bsos rgyal po mngon sum byon nam snyam/ /e ma 'di 'dra'i ngo mtshar dbyar gyi rnga/ /thos pas blo gsal gtsug phud ldan pa rnams/ /ngo mtshar dga' ba'i sgro gshog
zlum por byon/ /spro ba'i zlos gar bsgyur te gar byos shig /ji ltar lung bstan pa rnams phyis thog tu khel bar byung zhing ya mtshan che bar bsam/ sgrub pa grub nas gtor

sku mched kyis nged rang rdo rje phreng ba sogs thugs bzhed kyi chos mang tsam 'bul bar rdzong bda' gnang dgos tshul snyan 'bul gsang ba'i gong sa mchog nas nged chos

nas mchod dpon lags dang / dge slong rin po che/ spos dga' sprul sku/ dga' gdong rab 'byams pa/ rab 'byams pa skyes mchog sogs grwa tshang gi sku drag kha shas la sgrub thabs
rgya mtsho lung bcas 'bul dgos pa'i bslab ston pheb cing / pho brang gi gzims chung nub tu sdod gnas bslab ston ltar 'phral 'bul gyi nyin re la rjes gnang nyi shu rtsa
gcig re gsol tshigs yan la phul ba'i nyin drug gis grub skabs gong chab bzhugs gnang ring / r-i Shi'i chu zhugs 'di lus la shin tu 'phrad par 'ong bas chos rje rang yang
'gol pa zhig tu chu zhugs mdzod ces bslab ston stsal zhing / ja mar bzhes spro mang ba bcas bka' drin bskyangs/ bslab ston ltar chu zhugs grub nas pho brang du bcar skabs/
'khor lo bde mchog dang / kun rig sogs gsan bzhed rnams la so so'i bka' gnang ltar phul/ gter ston rig 'dzin chen por tshar lugs kyi 'jigs byed thun mong ma yin pa'i
rjes gnang dgos pheb pa 'bul bar sku zhabs su 'ong zhus kyang nged kyi sar bka' nan gyis yar pheb/ gzims chung nub tu rjes gnang rgyas par phul/ dgyes pa'i gsung

'phros zhig tu gnang / zhwa lu nas mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang dgyes mdzad rdo rje'i thugs kar thim pa'i tshul bstan pa'i mchod 'bul du phyag mdzod dpon g.yog rnams 'byor bas

de ring stor snyam yid la mi bzod pa'i skyo snang dang dad gus cig car du gyur/ nged rang la'ang mkhyen rab rje'i sku brnyan phyag nas ma sogs mchod 'bul dpangs mtho bar

pa nged rang la gnas tshul dge slong rin po che brgyud stsal/ nged kyis gong zhabs su bla ma de nyid kyi mchod 'bul du rgya sbug dang gos yug gis gtsos tshan grangs

dang / g.yog rnams la dang stsal song / rnam par rgyal ba'i chos grar 'byor/ sgrub sde'i bla ma dbon po grongs nas sngar lugs bzhin sku skyes 'dzin bdag byed skabs sems

ba gzabs rgyas dang / rgyal yum la'ang rta bzang bas gtsos tshan grangs rgyas par phul/ gzhis len kyang rgyas par gnang / 'phel rgyas su bdag chen rin po che'i mjal khar
phyin/ khri thog nas bzhengs pa dang gdan bzos bcas shin tu che ba dang / gzhis len gzabs pa gnang / nged kyis kyang rta legs pa sogs phyag rten rgyas par phul/ phyi nyin
rten 'brel gyi stabs sras yum lhan du grub thob tshe dbang phul/ lhun po rtse nas 'bod mi gnang bas mjal khar phyin par phyag mdzod kyis gtsos drung 'khor rnams bsu bar
byung / sku zhabs su gdan bzos mtho ba dang bcas ston mo rgyas par gnang / zhwa lur pha bla ma de nyid kyi mchod 'bul du ja/ mdzo/ gos dar sogs 'bul mi rdzong bda' byas/

chos sde srid gsum rnam rgyal du mang ja dang / spyi 'bul/ bsngo rten/ rnam gzhag sogs gzabs rgyas su phul zhing / phyag mdzod sogs phyag phyi drag gras la skyes ma gzabs par
byas/ ma 'gyangs par slob dpon chen po a bha yA ka ra dang darlan A tsaryas bkral ba'i rdo rje phreng ba'i dkyil 'khor nyer gnyis dang / dge legs su bya ba'i dkyil 'khor
gsum ste bzhi bcu zhe lnga'i dkyil 'khor du dbang zla ba gcig tu ras bris kyi steng nas phul zhing / gzhan yang bka' gnang ltar sgrub thabs brgya rtsa sogs dbang / rjes
gnang / lung bcas mang tsam phul skabs gong sa chen po nas phran bu lus gcong ba dang chu'ang 'phrod mdog ma kha bas mgyogs tsam phyir log byas nas 'gab tshul gyi bslab
ston bka' shog rin po che'i spyi bor pheb pa dang / rgyun gyi dbang po nas mdzod pa'ang na ba bcas gang ci'i stabs 'bod mi byung bas/ sku mched la dgongs khrol zhus pas
gnang / ston mo gzabs rgyas thog gnang sbyin dpangs mtho ba stsal/ bstan pa'i 'dzin skyong gi snyan 'bul rgyas par zhus/ thugs yid gcig 'dres kyis phyir 'ong skabs bla brang
ser mo'i rdo skas mgo bar sku mched skyel mar pheb/ lhun po rtse dang yab sras so so'i phyag mdzod/ mchod gzims/ mgron gnyer sogs kyi thab skyel/ las tshan khag rnams
dang / gsol ja bcas sgrol ma ri bar gnang / nged rang nas kyang gang ci'i snyan 'bul bcas tshan grangs gzabs par byas/ 'bras yul skyed tshal nas mkhan rin po che dang spyi
bsod 'ong dgos tshul gyi phyag bris bang phyin bcas rtse gdong du yod skabs 'byor pa dang / bskyar mnan che tsam byung bas de phyogs su rim gyis phyin pas rong btsan

spun gnas pa'i thad du skyed tshal nas rta bsu dang / thab bsu bcas 'byor/ dgon gnas mthong tsam nas yid shin tu bde zhing dad gus kyi ba spu ldang bar gyur cing / nyi ma gdugs
'jam pa dang 'ja' sprin gyis khengs/ bla brang dang grwa khang so so'i steng nas bsang dang / dge 'dun rnams kyi ser phreng / tshogs dung mkhas pa'i dkar po rgyang grags
btang ste mchod rdzas bcas bsus/ bla brang rgyab tu mjal dar bcas mkhan rin po che bsu bar pheb/ nged kyis zhon pa las babs te phyag lan tsam byas/ dge 'dun rnams kyis
rdo gcal du mjal dar dang byin rlabs zhus grub nas/ bla brang gi gzims chung ngo mtshar du bsdad/ mang ja zhig 'phral du zhus/ mkhan rin po che gzhis len tshul du bzhugs
nas dgon gnas dang / 'chad nyan sogs kyi gsung gleng rgyas par mdzad/ phyi nyin mang ja sbyor sbrel thog mkhan rin po che tshogs su pheb bar rtas gtsos dgu tshan bzang
ba dang / grwa mang la sbyi 'bul dpangs mtho ba zhus/ gzhis len gyi ston mo dpangs mtho ba byung zhing / kun mkhyen chen po sangs rgyas 'phel gyi bzhugs khrir bos te mkhan
po dang / spyi so grwa mang gi ster cha rgya cher mdzad/ nged rang nas kyang tshogs su ston pa gnas brtan bcu drug dang / sa skya'i zab chos phyag rdor 'byung po 'dul
byed/ lo ma gyon ma rnams kyi rjes gnang dang / bsngo smon gyi rgyas 'debs rgyas par zhus/ dgong mkhan rin po che dang kho se dpon slob kyis gtsos bka' rams kha shas la mgon
po gur lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang byas/ phyi nyin grwa pa kha shas rab byung dang / khams pa grwa tshang du bos par phyin/ sne len dang ster sbyin mang du byung / nged
rang nas kyang grwa ja dang ster sbyin byas/

mkhan zur pa kun dga' nor bus gzims shag tu 'bod bar mdzad/ gzhis len gzabs par byung zhing tshe dbang zhig phul/ khro phu thog thub ma'i sku gnyis dang na bza' skor/ dar ras
snam bu sogs kyi ster sbyin mdzad/ de dgong bla brang du grwa pa kha shas la rta mgrin gyi rjes gnang dang lung kha cig 'dod pa ltar byas/ phyi nyin rdzong dkar ba rnams
kyis spyi dbang zhig dgos tshul byung bar tshe dbang byas/ mkhan rin po che grwa mang dang bcas pa thag shin tu ring bar skyel mar phebs pas rta las babs te 'chad nyan
sogs bstan pa'i mig rgyan la phan pa dgos tshul gyi snyan 'bul zhus/ rten 'brel mtshon byed tsam phul nas phyir 'ongs pa'i lam du gter ston rig 'dzin chen po lcog dkar du
bzhugs pas/ lcog dkar sprul sku dang lhan du bla brang rtse nas lha bsang dang / dung chen gtong ba/ mgron gnyer ko bas sgrol te gsol ja dang / rten 'brel mtshon byed bcas
gang ci'i gnas tshul gnang / nged rang nas kyang lan gyi snyan 'bul zhus/ de nas rim gyis 'phrang sgrol lha rgyal gling du bsdad skabs/ yul pa so sos bsngo zhus dang
'phrad mi shin tu mang bar byung ba rnams la 'dod sbyar byas/ skye tshal 'og nas dgon gnas su 'ong dgos tshul gyi phyag bris 'byor bas khas blangs/ phyi nyin dgon gnas su
phyin pas mkhan slob sogs kha shas kyis rta bsu dang / dge 'dun rnams kyis ser phreng rgyas par mdzad cing / bla brang dang grwa khang so so nas lha bsang btang / 'byor
'phral khri thog tu bos nas grwa dmangs kyis mjal dar gnang / nged kyis mang ja sbyor sbrel thog mkhan slob so sor tshan grangs dang / grwa mang la spyi 'bul gzabs par byas/
gzhis len rgyas pa dang spyi so/ mkhan slob/ grwa mang tshang mas ster cha dpangs

mtho bar mdzad/ tshogs su tshe dbang / rta mgrin/ phyag rdor/ seng gdong ma sogs kyi rjes gnang byas/ zhag gnyis bsdad ring yul pa rnams kyis bsngo smon/ byang bu bzhu ba/
ma Ni'i lung sogs dgos zer mi shin tu mang ba zhig byung bar so sor 'dod pa ltar byas/ mkhan slob dang grwa mang gis skyel ma mdzad/ dgon gnas 'dzin skyong slob gnyer sogs
kyi snyan 'bul zhus/ de nas rim gyis sne thang rgya grong du 'byor skabs/ 'phags sde'i brag sne'i dgon gnas su shog gsung pas phyin/ gzhis len rgyas par byung / khri thog
tu phyin skabs grwa dmangs kyis mjal dar blangs/ nang mjal rgyas par zhus/ spyi so dang grwa pa so sos ster cha bzang bar mdzad/ tshogs su 'dod chos kyi dbang dang / dgong
mo mgon po'i rjes gnang sogs thugs 'dod ltar zhus/ nged rang nas mang ja'i thog spyi 'bul dang sngags mdud byin rten sogs so sor phul/ bsngo smon gyi rgyas 'debs dpyis
phyin par byas/ 'or du lung bstan sgrol ma mjal bar phyin/ snyan dar dang mchod pa phul zhing bstan 'gro'i don du smon lam rgyas par btab/ de nas rim gyis gong sa chen
po yas phyin gyi mjal khar lha sar phyin/ phyag dbang gi snyan 'bul zhus pas deng sang nang mtshams shig yin pas zhag bcu skor zhig sgugs gsung pa'i bslab ston pheb/ zur
chas rgyas par stsal/ zhag bcu skor nas phyag dbang la phyin pas shin tu dgyes pa'i tshul dang bcas rtse gdong du chos phul ba sogs kyi dri ba zhib tu stsal/ mgron khang
du ston mo gnang skabs dge slong rin po che gnang nas sang nas rgyal sgo phye 'phral 'byor bar gyis/ dri ba zhib tu byed rgyud yod stsal/ phyin nyin nas snga bar sku zhabs
su bcar/ gzims chung nyi 'od 'khyil ba'i pheb skas

bar mgron gnyer gyis bskyal/ de nas e ma phyi lags kyis bsus nas mtshan gzims gzims chung du phyin/ sku mdun du gdan bzos bcas 'dug par phyag dbang zhus nas bsdad/ dgyes pa'i
ngang nas rgyud sde 'og ma gsum gyi phyag len bcas pa'i dri ba zhig tu stsal bar ngor lugs dang byings kyi phyag len so sor dbye nas snyan 'bul zhus par thugs shin tu
dgyes pas nyin lnga'i ring dri ba zhib tu gnang / slar 'phros rnams 'di khar 'byor skabs byed gnang / gnang sbyin rgyas par stsal/ mgyogs tsam zhabs brtan zhig 'bul bar 'ongs
na ji ltar lags zhus pas/ de kha mdzad chog bka' drin bskyangs/ sku zhabs nas phyir 'ong skabs mos gus gyi sems shin tu gdung bas 'ong mi phod pa lta bu zhig byung /
phyi nyin lha sa nas sgo la nang du 'byor/ sang rgyan rin po ches dbus nA lendra'i bla khag /dbu chos/ mi sna/ nged rang gi nang bzan skya ser rnams kyis rta bsu dang thab
bsu 'byor/ rim gyis bskyod de rnam par rgyal ba'i chos grwa mthong tsam na blang brang khag dang / khams tshan so so nas lha bsang / dar 'phyar/ dung chen sogs rgyas pa
dang / nam mkha' g.ya' dag cing 'ja' sprin kha dog sna tshogs shar ba ni 'khon rigs 'jam dpal rdo rje sku mched la chos bdag por phul ba gegs med du 'khor ba la rong ston
thams cad mkhyen pa thugs dgyes pa'i mtshan ma yin nam snyam/ dge 'dun rnams kyis gdugs/ rgyal mtshan/ ba dan/ rol mo'i bye brag sogs ser phreng gis bsu ba shin tu rgyas
par mdzad/ blang brang du 'byor 'phral tshogs chen rnams kyis mjal dar phyur bur spungs/ nged rang nas 'du khang chen por mang ja dang gsol ba zhus/ phyi nyin

mang ja'i thog skyes ma'i tshul du/ bla khag las tshan rnams dang tshogs su spyi 'bul byas/ de nas bzung zhag kha cig gi ring bla brang khag dang khams tshan so sos ja la bos/
legs bya'i ster sbyin rgyas par byas/ de nas chos gzhis mkhar gdong sogs su phyin/ g.yog rigs rnams dang yon bdag so sos 'phrad par byung ste ster sbyin rgyas par byung
/ de nas sgom khang sogs dgon khag rnams la phyin/ grwa rigs yon bdag tshang mas dad gus kyi mchi ma 'khrug bzhin pa dang bcas ster sbyin sogs legs pa byung / chos 'brel/
mang ja/ sngags mdud/ byin rten sogs tshim par byas/ rgyun gyi dbang por 'byor/ nyag re'i 'bul skyel ba dang / 'grul ba phyir log mi rnams la rab byung / bsnyen rdzogs/
so sor 'dod chos sogs lugs gnyis kyi bdag rkyen bcas phyir rdzong byas/ 'di skabs lcags zam nas zhabs drung rin po che phebs pa stabs 'gros su song bas ser phreng sogs
grwa ma 'grigs kyang pheb bsu sogs gang legs zhus nas/ 'di kha'i dbon dang lhan du mgon po brag rdzong ma'i khrid 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i yi ge bzhin smin rgyas su phul
zhing / tshur yang grub thob chen po'i tshe dbang sogs stsal te lugs gnyis kyis mnyes par byas nas phar pheb/ lo mjug rim gro sogs snga rgyun ltar bsgrubs/ ! chu khyi
lor gsal tshes kyi log gsar grub nas tshe sgrub cig la bsdad/ grol 'phral nyan po nas 'ong dgos tshul gnang ba bzhin phyin/ mdog ston brtse chen kun dga' bkra shis khu dbon
dang mjal/ tshe dbang dang rjes gnang kha shas phul/ mchod mjal rgyas par zhus shing / ston mo gnang sbyin dpangs mtho ba stsal/ dug gi nad ros 'tshe ba rgyun ring tsam
byung bar sman dpyad
