rim gro sogs byed skabs gong sa yas phyin du zhabs brtan 'bul bar bcar na ji ltar lags kyi zhu yig 'bul bar mgron gnyer rin chen rdzong bda' zhus par/ gong sa chen po sku shin
tu ltems pas mgron gnyer bka' blon shag tu bos nas/ rnam 'joms dang / khro bo sme brtsegs/ khro mo sme brtsegs kyi phyag len mang ba byed yod med kyi dri ba gnang bar
yod tshul zhus pas/ mkhar rtser sgrol dkar gyi zhabs brtan la yod thog rnam 'joms dang / khro bo dang / khro mo sme brtsegs kyi cho ga gtong dgos pa'i bka' shog dang / zhabs
brtan 'gyang tsam kyis gnang ba'i bslab ston pheb/ de skabs rmi lam du dgong gcig nyi ma gzas zin pa 'jas bskor bzhin gzhib pa dang / yang dgong gcig btsun pa zhig gis
gong sa mjal bar shog zer/ phyin pas lho phyogs kyi nam mkha' na gong sa chen po bzhugs 'dug pa'i sku las 'od zer 'phros pa nged la phog pas sems shin tu dga' bas dad
gus kyis lag pa thal mo sbyar te gsol ba btab pas/ re zhig nas 'ja' tshon gyi rnam par yal song bas sems skyo ba dang bcas gnyid sad pas mig nas mchi ma 'babs pa zhig byung
bas sems ma bde bas dge slong rin po cher sku khams ji ltar lags kyi bslab ston zhu ba'i zhu yig phul bar/ mdangs sang sku shin tu ltem pa byung kyang / da cha sku khams
re dwangs byung bas sems mi bde ba mi dgos pa'i lan zhig gnang byung zhing gcod rgya'ang dam par bka' drin bskyangs song / sde dge dbon po kun dga' rab brtan dpon g.yog
gtsang nas 'khor ba'i chos gsan par zla ba gnyis tsam bzhugs ring / kye rdor rgyu dbang / mgon po brag rdzong

ma'i phyi nang gi khrid dang / mgon po zur bka' mang ba/ rnam sras lnga phrag gsum pa sogs dbang / rjes gnang / lung sogs shin tu mang bar phul/ gos dar/ gser/ ja sogs kyi
ster sbyin bzang bar mdzad/ nged rang nas kyang byin rten/ gos dar/ 'khar rnga legs pa/ snam bu sogs kyis rdzong ba byas te bod chen po'i rgyal khams su phyir log /ston sku
mtshams bcad rgya'i skabs yas phyin du zhabs brtan 'bul bar phyin/ sgrol dkar gyi cho ga la brten pa'i zhabs brtan rgyas par phul zhing / 'bul ba'ang tshang mas sngar
rgyun ltar phul/ 'di dus sde srid sku zhabs zhal mdangs shin tu nag par 'dug pas blo ma bde bar byung / tshogs pa rnams zhag bcu'i ring sku rim gnang / de'i ring nged lhor
gnas tshang du bsdad/ zur chas gzabs pa stsal/ don gnyer kha shas la rjes gnang dang rab byung kyang byas/ sku rim grub nas thon phyag gi mjal khar phyin/ ston mo dang
gnang sbyin rgyas par stsal nas bsti gnas su 'byor/ 'grul pa mang bar ja len pa dang lhan tu 'byor bar lugs gnyis kyi bdag rkyen gang legs sprad/ lo 'dir gdan sa chen po
rtse gdong nas 'jam dbyangs sku mched yab chos kyi gtso bor gyur pa thun mong gdul bya'i spyod yul min pa zab mo slob bshad gsan bar chibs kha bsgyur ba'i pheb bsur 'di kha
nas mgron gnyer/ spyi so nas chos khrims mi sna bcas rdzong bda' byas/ rgyal na mo cher pheb skabs nged rang bla khag las tshan bcas bzhi bcu skor pheb bsur phyin zhing
/ mjal kha dang kha btags kyi phar 'bul tshur gnang tshar du dngar/ lha khang rgyal smad dpon slob rnams dang / rgyal nang yon bdag drag zhan tshang ma sprin ltar 'dus
nas zhabs drung

sku mched nged bcas la dngos po'i tshogs ring por bskyangs/ bsngo smon sogs so so'i blo bstun dang byin rten phyag mdud sogs byin/ phyi nyin pa tshab tu chibs bshol zhig gi
skabs pe kar chos skyong chen po dang / las mkhan bcas pheb bsu'i tshul du pheb cing mjal dar phul bar snyan shal dang phrin las bskul/ grub rgyal re sde pas chibs zhol
zhig zhus/ sku zhabs sku mched dpal rtser chibs kha bsgyur/ nged dgos gnas su 'byor nas phyi nyin mthong smon dang nye bar thab bsu zhus/ chos sde chen por pheb skabs tshogs
chen gyis gdugs/ rgyal mtshan/ ba dan/ rol mo'i bye brag du ma dang bcas ser phreng rgyas pa dang / bla brang khams tshan so so'i steng nas lha bsang dang bkra shis khra
ring brkyang zhing / bla khag las tshan bcas kyis spos kyis sna drangs te spyan 'dren pa sogs bkod pa ltar rgyas par byas nas gzims khang chen mor pheb skabs nged rang
sku zhabs su phyin/ gang ci'i gsung gleng zhus/ phyi nyin sku skyes kyi tshul du mang ja'i thog nged rang la tshan grangs rgyas pa dang / tshogs su 'gyed gnang / bco brgyad
du gdan drangs nas gzhis len gyi ston mo rgyas par zhus thog /rgyan rin po cher chibs/ chibs rol gyis gtsos pa'i 'bul ba dang / yum la rtas gtsos pa'i dgu tshan zhig
phul/ phyi nyin tshogs su thams cad mkhyen pa rong ston chen po'i mi 'jigs seng ge'i khrir 'jam mgon chos kyi rgyal po spyan drangs te/ gser/ dngul/ chibs/ chibs rol/ ja/
gos dar sogs kyi 'bul dpangs mtho bar phul zhing / bla khag las tshan sogs kyis kyang gang rgyas zhus song / chos sdings brgyud

pho brang du mjal khar pheb pa'i zhabs phyir zhu yig bcas mgron gnyer rin chen rdzong bda' zhus shing / de bstun sku mched la slob bshad 'bul rgyu'i mi grangs ga tsam tshud
kyi bslab ston zhus par/ chos 'di bka' gnyan gshis bcu gcig las mang ba mi 'gab tshul pheb/ sku bzos/ gnang sbyin/ bslab ston shin tu legs par stsal zhing rgyun gyi dbang
por pheb nas/ dgongs bzhed ltar gzims chung du sku mched kyi zhabs phyir gra phyi tshogs pa'i mkhan rin po che/ gsang phu mchod khang dpon slob/ rmor dpon slob sogs dpon
slob bcu gcig la snga dro lam 'bras slob bshad dang / phyogs 'dus kyi bla khag dang tshogs chen du phyi dro tshogs bshad so so'i phyag len dang / dbang / byin rlabs/ lung
sogs ma 'dres shing rgyas par phul/ 'di skabs gzhis nas dpon si bi bsnyun par phyin/ khrus rjes gnang sogs 'phrod bsten byas pas bsnyun las grol te rgyun gyi dbang por
'phral tu log /sku mched bzhugs gdan 'jags ring bslab ston ltar thugs 'dod kyi chos rnams dang / chos zhu ba so sor yang bzhed pa ltar 'dod chos mang du phul/ zhabs drung
dpon slob rnams gtsang du chibs kha bsgyur ba'i pheb skyel du nged rang bla khag las tshan bcas kyis rgyal nang bar phyin/ gang ci'i snyan 'bul bcas phar 'bul tshur gnang
mdzad de dgon gnas su log /de nas dgon khag gi gtor spod dang / dus mchod/ rim gro sogs sngar ltar bsgrubs// ! chu phag lor gsar tshes kyi lo gsar dang / tshe sgrub zhag
bdun ma zhig byas shing brel ba rnams rim sel dang / pho brang chen por gong sa yas phyin gyi mjal khar bcar/ gong gi mjal

rten rnams snyan 'bul dang bcas te gzims chung 'gag tu phul zhing / gsol dpon sngags rams pa lags brgyud bslab ston zhib tu stsal/ bla brang du sde srid sku zhabs rin po che'i
mjal kha zhus/ ston mo gzabs rgyas dang bka' 'dri rgyas par gnang / brtan ma khang du dge slong rin po cher chos kha yar phul/ thon phyag zhus thog gnang sbyin kyang
stsal te rang gnas su 'byor/ lo 'dir mkhyen bslab mthar son 'bul dpon bla ma bsod nams dang / rab 'byams pa gnyis kyis rta/ dre'u/ ja/ nor sogs yon gyi mnyes par byas te
li'u thang nas bka' 'gyur ro cog mtshal spar du btab pa'i pheb skyel du bla ma rab 'byams pa rang byon pa dang lhan du 'grul pa nyis brgya skor 'byor nyin/ bka' 'gyur rin
po che gdugs/ rgyal mtshan/ rol mo sogs mchod rdzas du ma dang bcas pa'i ser phreng dang / bla brang so so'i steng nas bsang dang dar 'phyar sogs bsu ba rgyas par zhus te
'du khang chen mor spyan drangs/ mchod pa rgyas par phul/ dpon slob rnams la spyi chen nas gzhis len shin tu rgyas par zhus/ sang nyin nas 'grul pa rnams kyis cho ga stong
rtsa dang mang 'gyed thog tshogs dbur phyin/ ja/ rta/ dre'u/ mdzo/ g.yag sogs kyi ster cha nyin re bzhin byung ba zab pa dang rgya che ba'i bsngo smon dpyis phyin par
byas/ sog yul du 'bul sdud la brdzangs pa'i dbang gi bla ma bsod nams dar rgyas dang / tshe ring spe se'i bla ma bsod nams dpal bzang / o chol du chos rje'i 'bul skyel ba
bcas 'byor/ gser/ dngul/ mu tig /ljon shing gi sga dang / gser sga/ gos dar sogs dngos po mang bar byung / tshogs chen du mang ja/ 'gyed sogs mang tsam zhus pa'i tshogs

dbur phyin nas dngos po rnams dkon mchog mchod sprin du spros te dmigs yul rnams kyis gtsos sems can mtha' dag gi don du chos kyi dbyings su bsngo smon gyi rgyas gdab ci nus
byas/ gzhis len sogs rgyas par bgyis te pho brang chen por bla ma gnyis mjal khar rdzong bda' byas/ phyag mjal gyi 'bul ba mi sna'i zhabs phyi zhus 'dug cing / bdag rkyen
kyang lhan du stsal/ sku zhabs grwa tshang du mang 'gyed so so zhus nas re zhig rang gnas su byung bar khams 'grul pa dang lhan tu dbang / rig gtad/ lung sogs bdag rkyen
so so'i blo dang mthun par byas/ chos sde chen po'i 'dus pa'i tshogs dang / dgon so so nas byon pa'i gsan bzhed rnams la/ 'jigs byed/ gshed dmar/ sbyong dkyil/ mi 'khrugs
pa/ tshe dpag lha dgu /rnam 'joms dkar po sogs kyi dbang dang / sgrub thabs rgya mtsho dang / sgrol ma nyer gcig sogs spyi bka' dang / zur bka'i rigs mang tsam byas/
dus dran mchod pa so so dang lo mjug rim gro sogs sngar rgyun ltar bgyis// ! shing byi lo gsar pa'i lo gsar dang / tshe sgrub zhag bdun ma zhig byas/ rgya nag mi sna phyir
log skabs bla ma bsod nams dar rgyas dang / tsha ba bla ma bstan 'dzin nor bu gnyis pho brang chen por thon phyag zhu bar gtang / 'khor 'phral chos rje dang / dpon khag
so so'i yig lan/ khong rnams la mdud pa/ byin rten/ rta khal sogs kyi ster sbyin bcas rdzong bda' byas/ skyor mo lung mkhan rin po che dung dkar 'brug sgra sgrub thabs rgya
mtsho gsan sar pheb pa thugs bzhed kyi chos rnams phul zhing dngul gyi maNDal sogs gnang sbyin dpangs mtho bar mdzad/ gzhis len gzabs par zhus te rang gnas su pheb/ nad
ro langs par 'phrod bsten rim gro sogs byas par yar ldan du gyur/

lo 'di'i zla ba bzhi pa'i tshes bco lnga rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi dus dran nyin res gza' lha'i bla ma dang / rgyu skar rgyal 'dzom pa'i 'grub sbyor bzang po'i thog dbon
ngag dbang mkhyen brtse rab brtan rab byung mdzad/ mtshan snga ma'i thog mkhyen rab kun dga' chos kyi nyi ma bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang por gsol/ nyi ma gdugs 'jam
zhing nam mkha' 'ja' sprin gyis khebs par gyur/ so sos legs 'bul byung zhing dga' ston rgyas par byas/ 'phrod bsten du gnyen drung gi chu tshan la nged rang dpon slob mang
tsam phyin/ zhag bcu skor bsdad ring rgyal rag gi ru ba rnams dang / sog po dang / o tog kha shas kyis rnyed bkur byung zhing / nged kyis kyang lugs gnyis kyi blo dang
mthun pa'i 'dod sbyar byas/ sen chen nas 'bul dpon bla ma bsam 'phel dang / cho hor dha ro kha sbra chen dang / dge slong gnyis kyis gtsos cho hor rnams/ o thog bla ma
bsod nams lhun grub dang / dpon phun tshogs sogs kyis ched gtad 'ong dgos pa'i 'bod mi 'byor/ lus gcong bas 'gror ma 'dod kyang gnam mtsho'i bkra shis do bo che gong ma chos
kyi spyan ldan gyis sgrub par bzhugs na 'ja' lus 'grub pa'i gnas yin tshul 'ja' tshon snying po'i gter yig na 'dug pas der mtshams shig byed 'dod kyi zhor la rib tsam
'ong ba'i khas blangs/ 'dam nas bskyod skabs sa skya mchod dpon 'phrad par byon nas gzhis len rgyas par mdzad/ da rgan lha rje sogs grwa rigs yon bdag rnams dngos po bzang
ba bcas 'phrad par byung bar rjes gnang dang bka' bsgo sogs byas/ la rgan brgyabs te mkha' 'gro'i bla mtsho mthong tsam du bsdad/ phyi nyin sngon du 'tsho mdzad rta mgrin
tshe ring nged rang sdod pa'i sgrub khang legs pa zhig tshol du btang / lam gyi 'brog pa

rnams kyis rnyed bkur mang tsam byung bar byin rten dang bsngo smon sogs kyis 'dod pa bskangs te do gnas su 'byor bar 'tsho mdzad kyis sgrub phug btsal bar dgongs pas o rgyan
yab yum gyi sgrub phug dang mjal 'dug pas rten 'brel rang 'grig tu gyur/ de nub nas sgrub phug tu o rgyan zhi drag gi sgrub pa dang tshogs 'khor byas/ phyi dgong lha chen
'bar brtsal gyis shin tu 'tshub 'gyur gyi rnam pas ser drag dang / glog 'khyug cing 'brug sgra drag po sgrogs pa/ gnam lcags thog gis g.yas g.yon gyi brag bkas te sa
rdo nyil ba sogs cho 'phrul bstan kyang / lha sngags ye shes g.yo med du gnas pas rang yal du song / phyi nyin nas bzung nam mkha' 'ja' tshon gyis khebs pa dang / rmi lam
du ye shes mtsho rgyal gyis mtshan ldan gyi thod pa bdud rtsis bkang ba gnang bar byung / brag sbugs ldebs na rtsa gsum 'khor lo bzhi'i rang byon gsal bar mthong ba dang
/ mtsho'i mdun du maNDal dang mchod pa 'bul bar phyin pa'i tshe mtshos mdog kha dog sna tshogs ston cing / mtsho rlabs kyi 'ja' gur phub pa dang / mtsho'i mtha' 'phel te
nged kyi gdan gyi thad du 'byor ba sogs ltas ya mtshan che bar byung / 'brong pa'i rub nas 'bul dpon bla ma bsam 'phel yon bdag du ma dang bcas te 'phrad par byon/ rta nor
sogs kyi ster byin bzang bar byung / dbang dang byang bu sogs 'dod par ltar byas/ skabs shig do ri'i rtser lha bsang gtong bar phyin/ mtsho la bltas pa na mtsho dkyil
gyi steng na bud med ras gos sngon po gyon pa skra thor tshugs su bcings pa zhig dga' ba'i rnam 'gyur du ma ston pa mthong / nyi ma'ang gdugs 'jam zhing 'ja' tshon rkyong
ba sogs byung bar lha chen rdo rje 'bar ba rtsal dang / yum gnam

mtsho phyug mo gnyis thugs dgyes pa yin nam snyam/ sems kyang spro ba mchog tu 'phel/ de'i phyin nyin do ri'i skor rar phyin pas sgrub phug rgwa lo phug dang / sa paN/ 'phags
pa sogs bzhugs gnas kyi phug pa du ma/ yi dam gyi lha tshogs du ma'i rang byon dang / bdag med rtogs pa'i phyag zhabs kyi rjes du ma mjal/ sgrub phug tu 'khor/ nyin re
bzhin gu ru zhi drag gi mchod pa dang / tshogs 'khor/ dgong chos srung rnams la bskang ba rgyas par byas/ cho hor nas 'bod mi kha shas 'byor nas rim gyis 'brong ba rnams
kyi ru bar sleb/ yon bdag pho mo rnams khrom bzhin 'dus/ smon lam phyag dang bskor ba'i sgra di ri ba'i ngang nas rta nor gyi ster cha mang du blangs/ nged kyis kyang bka'
bsgo dang bsngo smon gyi rgyas 'debs/ ma Ni'i lung sogs byas/ mtsho lung skyog tu slebs skabs bla brang dang gzhis nas bang phyin pa sang 'byor rgyu'i de nub kha ba shin
tu che ba babs pa nged rang la chos skyong 'phreng ba'i 'tshubs kyis gur ka bcag cing / gdung ma mda' bzhin brgyugs pas gur brtibs shing / rogs byed rnams grul shang dang
bcas te 'du dgos byung bas ha las shing dgod bro bar gyur/ sa skya ru ba dang gnam ru ba sogs kyi yon bdag pho mo rnams 'dus shing rta nor gyi ster cha bzang bar byung
/ tshang mar tshe dbang dang / ma Ni'i lung / bka' bsgo/ bsngo ba sogs 'dod sbyar byas/ phyi nyin cho hor gyi bsu ba ser skya rnams 'byor/ lam du grwa rigs dang yon bdag
rnams kyis phyugs kyi ster cha rim par byed bzhin pa dang bcas cho hor gyi sde nang du dung rgya gling bcas sgar du babs/ tshang mas 'dus te sne len dang ston mo gzabs
rgyas

byas/ nged kyis tshe dbang / rta mgrin/ ri khrod ma sogs kyi khrom dbang / byang zhu/ ma Ni'i lung sogs dang / drag gras kha shas la gur drag dang / mgon po'i rjes gnang /
'pho lung sogs byas/ gos dar/ snam bu/ ras phog che ba dang / khrab/ me mda'/ rta nor nyis brgya lhag tsam byung / nged rang gis kyang dmigs yul rnams kyis thog drangs rgya
che ba sems can gyi don dang / zab pa chos kyi dbyings su bsngo smon gang rgyas byas shing lugs gnyis kyi bdag rkyen gang legs byas/ o thog gi dpon phun tshogs dang /
tsha ba bla ma bsod nams lhun grub kyis bsu mi 'byor/ sde thog tu phyin skabs ser 'bras kyi dge slong rnams kyis gtsos ser skya lnga bcu skor gyis rta bsu byung ba dang lhan
du sder 'byor thog /mar thud sogs bzhis len shin tu rgyas par zhus/ dge slong rnams dang dpon khag rnams la rta mgrin dang / mgon po'i rjes gnang / tshe dbang / spyan
ras gzigs kyi rjes gnang / ma Ni'i lung sogs gang la gang 'tshams byas/ rta/ mdzo/ mdzo mo/ 'bri g.yag bdun cu skor byung ba bsngo smon gyi rgyas 'debs dpyis phyin par byas
te bdag rkyen legs par sprad/ de dgong sgar tsha ba bla ma bsod nams lhun grub yod pa'i sar sleb/ phyi nyin gzhis len dang mar/ phying pa/ rta/ mdzo/ mdzo mo/ 'bri g.yag
sogs mang bar byung / de skor yon bdag rnams kyis rta nor gyi ster sbyin byung zhing / tshe dbang dang / dge ba rnams rdzogs byang du bsngos/ bar rings nas em chi phrin
las bzang po yon mchod kyis bsu mi btang ba'i ru sder slebs/ ston mo gzabs rgyas zhus/ tshe dbang dang / ri khrod ma sogs khrom dbang du byas/ gos dar/ rta nor sum cu
skor

gyi ster cha byung / byang bu bzhu ba/ dge ba sangs rgyas kyi sar bsngo ba sogs so so'i blo bstun ltar byas/ gser gling gnyis kyi ru thog tu bos/ rta shin tu legs pa re dang
/ mdzo mo sogs byin/ tshe dbang dang / byang bu/ bsngo smon gyi rgyas 'debs sogs kyis bzhed pa bskang / lam thog 'brom mtsho'i ru ba rnams kyi sar 'byor bar tshang ma dad
gus kyis 'ur te 'bri g.yag gi ster cha dbyar gyi char sprin ltar gtibs/ so sor blo dang 'tshams pa'i chos dang zang zing gis blo'i re ba bskangs te/ dge ba rnams chud
mi za ba'i phyir rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu bsngos/ o thog gi sder slebs/ dpon dpon mo sogs yon bdag tshang mas gzhis len rgyas shing / rta/ mdzo/ mdzo mo/ /'bri g.yag sogs
bzhi bcu skor gyi ster cha byung bar blangs/ tshe dbang dang / ma Ni'i lung / dge bsnyen sgrub pa/ dpon khag so so'i 'dod sbyar gyi rjes gnang dang / bsnyen gnas kyi lung
mang bar byas/ dge ba sangs rgyas kyi sar rgyas 'debs kyi bsngo smon byas shing / byang bu sogs 'dod pa dang sbyar/ sgar po rigs nas na dmar chung ba'i mtsho 'gram du
bsdad/ bla brang bla ma/ yon bdag rnams dang bcas pa 'byor/ rta sogs dngos po'i ster cha byung / lugs gnyis kyi bdag rkyen sprad de tshe dbang dang / byang bu bsngo smon
ci nus byas/ rje'i mgur lha bsam gtan gangs bzang gi mtha' brgyud sho mo mtsho khar slebs/ dge slong grags pa phun tshogs kyis rgyus yod mdzad de sgom sde bla rgan gyi rten
'brel bsgrigs pa'i sar bod kyi mgur lha bcu gsum dang / brtan ma bcu gnyis sogs gzhi bdag rnams la bsang / khrus/ gsol mchod/

mnga' gsol rgyas par phul bas rgyab ri'i rtse mo nas smug pa 'phyur te dal bu'i char zhig babs pa dang / mtsho nang du las bzhi'i kha dog gi 'ja' shar ba ni rigs dang lugs
gnyis yar rgyas su 'gro ba'i rten 'brel du snang / glang ling la rgal/ 'ba' rang brgyud 'ongs pas yon bdag rnams kyis mar dang phyugs kyi ster cha mang du byung bar bsngo
ba'i rgyas btab/ lcog rtse la brgyud 'dam bu mar bsdad skabs sog po zhig glo bur na bas nged 'ong dgos tshul nan che bar byung yang / nged 'gro mi dgos/ grwa pa gnyis btang
nas bgegs bskrad gsol kha byas na phan 'gro byas/ phyi nyin kho pa sang bder song / dge tshul ma dpon g.yog nas ston mo rgyas pa dang ster sbyin kyang byas/ bsnyen gnas
kyi sdom pa phog cing gur la shis brjod kyi nas 'thor/ g.yang ra'i mdor bsdad/ ko khra gyi yon bdag rnams dang / 'dam gyi yon bdag pho mo rnams 'phrad par byung bar mar/
thud/ sha /nor sogs kyi ster cha kyang legs par byung / bka' bsgo dang bsngo smon sogs 'dod sbyar bgyis/ g.yang ra'i la dang bcom brgyud rgyal ba 'brom gyi gnas mchog
rwa sgreng gi gnas mjal la phyin/ gnas mthong ma thag dad pas ba spu g.yo zhing sems la bde ba'i ting nge 'dzin shar ba spro ba dang bcas rta las babs te phyag byas shing
/ maNDal dang yan lag bdun pa phul/ gnas tshang la 'byor/ dgong dad gus can kha shas la 'dod chos byas/ phyi nyin tshogs su mang ja dang / mkhan rin po cher bsngo rten rnam
gzhag sogs 'bul bar mdzod pa btang / nyi dros gtsug lag khang mjal bar phyin te thog mar ka gnyis mar byin rlabs zhus/ de nas tshogs khang du

spyan drangs/ 'phags pa rigs gsum mgon pos sems can thams cad sangs rgyas kyi sar bskrun pa'i phyir jo bo 'jam dpal rdo rje'i sku brnyan sprul pa'i zlos gar gyis bzhengs pa
a ti sha dang 'brom gyi thugs dam rten sangs rgyas dngos dang khyad par ma mchis pa mgo thog tu bzhag ste yid rtse gcig tu smon lam btab pas byin gyis brlabs pa'i rtags
su lus rtse bun ne ba/ yid brjod med du dar cig gnas/ jo bo nyid dang rten gtso kha shas la gser gsol dang / snyan shal gzabs pa/ g.yu/ byi ru/ mu tig sogs mchod pa rgyas
par phul/ dgon gong sogs lha khang rnams zhib tu mjal/ dkor gnyer rnams gus pa'i rnam 'gyur gyis nang rten gang yod zhib par bstan/ gling skor du phyin/ shug pa ming chen
rnams dang / bsod nams can thar lam du bgrod pa'i dur khrod bcas mjal/ snga sor gyi las 'brel zhig yin nam/ byin rlabs kyis nam mkha' g.ya' dag cing 'ja' sprin du ma dang
/ sems bde song nge ba'i ngang nas gnas su sdod spro bar gyur/ snying rje drag pos bskul te bdag gzhan brje ba dang / ngan 'gro'i sems can rnams thar lam du 'god pa'i
smon lam u tshugs su btab/ dad ldan gyi bla grwa kha shas kyi dgongs bzhed ltar gong sa chen po'i zhabs brtan phran bu rang gis zhus pa mkhyen brtse nus mnga' ma'i lung byas/
de nas rim gyis bskyod de kun ra'i thad du 'byor/ grwa rigs dang yon bdag du ma 'dus/ rgyun gyi dbang po nas bla ma dang / las tshan so so'i rta bsu dang / thab bsu
rgyas par 'byor/ dgon gnas su nye ba na dge 'dun rnams gyis gdugs/ rgyal mtshan/ 'phan/ sil snyan/ rnga/ 'khar rnga/ rgya gling sogs kyi

mchod pa'i yo byad bsnams te ser phreng dang / bla brang dang khams tshan so so'i thog nas bsang dang ba dan 'phyar ba sogs dar phyar rgyas par mdzad/ nged dpon slob rnams
bla brang lcang lo can du 'byor/ phyi nyin mang ja dang bla khag las tshan rnams la rnam gzhag rgyas par phul/ so so nas ja dang tshan grangs gi sne len dang / grwa dmangs
kyis mjal dar sogs legs par byung / nged kyis kyang dar ras/ rta phyugs sogs kyi skyes ma so sor phul/ pho brang du phyin cing rta nor sogs kyi 'bul ba rgyas pa dang bcas
te mjal kha zhus/ dge slong rin po che dang sku drag rnams la skyes mar rta bcas phul/ thon phyag zhus te rang gnas su 'byor/ dus dran mchod pas mtshon chos sde chen po'i
lugs gnyis kyi bgyi ba sngar rgyun ltar dbon gyis mdzad/ lo 'di'i hor zla bcu gcig pa'i tshes dgu la res gza' phur bu rgyu skar rgyal 'dzom pa'i 'grub sbyor bzang po'i
nyin zhabs drung dbon rin po che ngag dbang mkhyen brtse rab brtan rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos rje yab sras kyi chos kyi khrir mnga' gsol te tshogs chen du tshe dbang
/ 'byung 'dul gyi rjes gnang mdzad/ legs 'bul dang / dga' ston rgyas par zhus/ rim gyis thams cad mkhyen pa rong ston chen pos chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba'i khrir pheb par
tshang mas legs 'bul zhus song / sngar yod kyi steng du bla brang du rgya dkar nag gis gtsos rten gsum/ mchod cha/ shel spyad/ dkar spyad/ rgya hor gyi rol mo shubs bcas/
gser rnga/ dung chen/ rkang gling / dkar dung / snyan dar rgyu legs gling gsum gong ba dang bcas pa/ bla bre/ rten khebs sogs bla brang du mkho ba'i yo byad rnams rim
gyis bsgrigs/ dpal gnas su

gzhung sa chen po'i dgongs pa rin po che khrel tshab che bar byung song bar khong rang spun la bkod pa byas te zhu bsgug la song bar zla ba kha shas nas dgongs ba ma dwangs
bar nang mi tshang ma chu skyur gnang rtsis byung 'dug pas/ nged rang mtshan la brgyabs te phyin/ dge slong rin po che brgyud sde srid sku zhabs su de rigs dgongs pa rin
po che dag pa'i snyan 'bul zhu ma nus kyang / gong sa chen por tshang ma'i srog skyabs kyi snyan 'bul zhus par/ gsung ba bzhin srog la skyon mi 'ong ba'i bslab ston byas
yod gsung ba bka' drin bskyangs byung 'phral/ sde srid rin po che'i sku zhabs su srog skyabs zhus par de kha nas gong sa chen por zhus gnang grub 'dug pa bzhin 'ong ba'i
gzhal du ma mchis pa'i bslab ston bka' drin bskyangs pa sa dang po thob pa ltar du gyur/ lha rtse chos sde'i gnyer rtsis kyang mi dgos shing / kho rang tshe chos 'jig rten
gang byed kyang nged rang gis blos bcad byas chog pa'i bslab ston bka' drin bskyangs/ ! shing glang lor lo gsar dang / tshe sgrub grub nas/ lo 'dir nged rang gi dbon zhabs
drung / grub pa'i dbang phyug nyan po chos rje sku mched/ ra ba smad slob dpon mkhas mchog sogs dang / rab byung grwa tshang / rtses dong 'bras bu gling pa/ rtse tshogs
sa lugs nas dge slong phan bde sogs kha shas/ snye thang brag sna/ skyed tshal 'og /rgya ma/ 'chad kha sogs nas byon pa rnams dang / dpal rgyun gyi dbang po'i 'dus pa
rgya mtsho'i tshogs la slob dpon chen po a bha ya'i bzhed gzhung rdo rje phreng ba dkyil 'khor bzhi bcu zhe gnyis dang / darpan Atsaryas bkral ba'i dge legs su bya ba'i
dkyil 'khor gsum ste zhe lnga'i dbang rgyas pa

dang / phreng ba skor gsum gyi lung / tshe kun/ mi 'khrugs pa/ gur gyi rjes gnang zur bka' sogs 'dod chos mang tsam byas/ pho brang chen por mjal khar bcar/ mjal kha dang zur
chas gnang sbyin sogs rgyas par stsal/ zhag shas nas 'dam bu byin gyi chos grwar 'byor/ tsha ba dang sgom sde sogs kyi 'bul sdud pa dang / khams 'grul pa mang tsam 'byor
bar 'dod chos dang bdag rkyen 'dod pa ltar bgyis/ bdud rtsi ril bu sgrub pa dang / tshogs chen du kun rig stong rtsa nyin gsum bsgrubs pa'i yon du dge 'dun bcu rer ja
sig re/ bla khag las tshan dang bcas par rnam gzhag phul/ 'di skabs gzhis bkra shis sgang zhig ral ches pas tsha bo mgon po rnam rgyal dang / rogs lnga dar bcas la bkod pa
byas te shing bzo ba rgung chen pa dang / rdo bzo mi lag bcas sum cu skor gyis zla ba gnyis la yongs su rdzogs pa grub 'dug pa'i lta rtog la phyin pas bkod pa bzhin byung
'dug par shis brjod kyi me tog gtor/ las rin lto dang / thog mtha' bar gsum du ston mo/ bzo bo rnams la gla yon mgu ba bcas rdzong bkod byas/ rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum/
gzungs gser brgya rtsa sogs chos 'don gyi rigs mang ba dang / phyogs bzhi'i gtor chen sogs mang bar bsgrubs/ dgon khag tu tshems bu lugs kyi dmar khrid dang / gcod gtan thog
gcig ma/ tshe dbang / rjes gnang sogs byas shing so so'i 'byor pas mchod/ 'grul pa rnams phyir log khar 'dod chos dang / rab byung / bsnyen rdzogs mang tsam bsgrubs te
phyir brdzongs/ 'di skabs che gsum nas mda' dpon rin po ches gzhis kyi tsha mo che ba 'bog gong sbyor bar byin na legs par 'dug gnang bas/ gong sa chen por bslab

ston zhus te rdzong bda' byas/ mgon khang so sor gtor spod dang / bskang ba khri tshar dang / thug gsos tshar chen rdo rje 'chang gi yig cha bzhin rgyas par byas/ dus dran
mchod pa dang / lo mjug gi rim gro sogs snga ma ltar bsgrubs/ me stag lor lo gsar rgyas pa dang / grub chen thang stong rgyal po'i lugs kyi tshe sgrub zhag nyi shu tsam byas/
lo 'di nang du spyan yas mkhan po dung dkar 'brug sgra/ kho se dpon slob/ gsang phu mchod khang dpon slob sogs rim gyis pheb par sgrub thabs brgya rtsa/ rgya mtsho/
rnam 'joms dkar po/ sman bla/ mgon po'i skor sogs dbang lung mang tsam byas/ 'chad ka nas lha rin po che bsnyen rdzogs gsan sar pheb par dgongs bzhed ltar zhus/ kye rdor
man ngag lugs kyi dbang dang / mgon po'i rjes gnang sogs kha shas phul zhing / gzhis len dang 'bul ba rgyas par phul nas phyir pheb/ gzhis su lha lung dpal gyi rdo rje'i
rnam sprul 'od mchog sprul sku ngo mtshar ba'i ltas du ma dang bcas sku bltams par tshe dbang / 'byung 'dul/ rta mgrin sogs gegs sel 'bul bar phyin/ sku mthong ba na byis
pa gzhan dang mi 'dra ba'i ya mtshan pa zhig 'dug /sku'i rim gro ba rmor rab 'byams pas zhus nas phyir log /khams nas 'bul sdud bla ma bstan 'dzin rnam rgyal sogs kha shas
'byor/ ja/ rta/ mdzo/ g.yag /'bri/ zangs sogs kyi ster sbyin mang bar byung ba rgya che ba sems can gyi don dang / zab pa chos kyi dbyings su bsngo smon gyi rgyas btab/
tshogs chen du bka' 'gyur/ gzungs 'dus brgya rtsa/ rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum/ grwa tog gser gsum/ bka' thang kha shas/ chos skyong so

so'i bskang ba brgya rtsa/ khro bcu'i gtor zlog /gtor ma 'bum ther/ brgya bzhi dang / ba ri gtor chen sogs bsgrubs/ tshogs su grub chen brgyad cu dang / sgrol ma nyer gcig
/bka' gdams lha bzhi sogs kyi rjes gnang dang / bka' gdams pha chos/ bu chos/ rgyal sras bka' 'bum sogs kyi lung byas/ khams bod yon bdag rnams kyi shi gson la byang bu dang
bsngo ba rus tsha sogs khor yug tu byas/ chos sde chen po'i dus dran mchod pa dang / gtor spo sogs sngar rgyun ltar bsgrubs/ ! me yos lo gsar tshes la tshe sgrub zhag
bdun ma zhig byas/ smon lam mjug tu khams 'grul pa phyir rdzong gi rab byung bsnyen rdzogs sgrub pa dang / so so'i lan 'debs lugs gnyis kyi bdag rkyen bcas rdzong bda' byas/
'tsho mdzad rta mgrin tshe ring gis bco brgyad du g.yu thog pa'i rnam thar gras thang zhig bris na legs par 'dug ces bskul ba la brten nas/ gong sa sku zhabs rin po
che nas zhal bkod bka' drin bskyangs pa'i g.yu thog rnying ma'i rnam thar sku thang bzhi tshar em chi lags rin po che'i phyag nas dpe g.yar po zhus pa dang / sku thang gcig
la grub pa'i g.yu thog gsar ma'i rnam thar zhig kyang bkod par byas te/ thang kha lnga'i gtso bo sman bla rigs lnga la sman gyi grong khyer blta na sdug gi zhing bkod
la/ g.yu thog gsar rnying gi rnam thar gyis bskor ba sprul sku ba ngag dbang nor bu can gsum gyi yid dang mthun par byung bas gong gshams sogs legs par bsgrubs/ phog dang
/ zhag bco lnga re nas ston mo dang ster sbyin mtshon pa re byas shing / grub 'phral nged rang dang tshogs chen nas kun rig stong rtsa nyin gsum btang ba'i nyin re bzhin
rab gnas rgyas pa

re dang / sprul sku ba tshor nyen re la yon bre bcu re'i rtsis kyi ja/ gos dar sogs 'bul ba rgyas par byas/ 'bul sdud bla ma kha shas grongs pa dang / 'brel pa rnams kyi sgrib
sbyong la sems nas rdo rje sems dpa'i sku brgya sogs gser thang brgyad/ rim gror gzungs grwa lnga'i thang ka lnga/ lha mo/ /rnam sras kyi sku thang rnams bsam 'grub sgang
nas sprul sku bas bzhengs par gong gsham sogs legs par grub nas/ nged rang dang tshogs chen bcas kyis kun rig la brten pa'i rab gnas rgyas par byas/ sprul sku bar rta
ja sogs kyi yon mnyes par phul/ pho brang chen por mjal khar phyin/ mjal kha ston mo gnang sbyin sogs brtse 'dzin gnang / dge slong rin po cher chos kha shas phul/ em chi
lags dang / dge slong ngag dbang dkon mchog gi gzims bshag tu bos nas gsung gleng dang / gnang sbyin rgyas par mdzad/ dge slong ngag dbang dkon mchog la chos shig kyang
phul/ mchod dpon chen mos ja rgyugs gnang sbyin stsal/ pho brang dang lha sa'i gnas mjal rgyas par zhus nas rang gnas su bskyod/ gdan sa chen po nas sne gdong gi lcam la
gdung ma phebs pas khams gsum chos kyi rgyal po'i bslab ston bcas phyag mdzod lha sar phyag dbang dang bsdongs nas pheb/ bco brgyad du 'bog gong la byon pa'i lcam gyi mched
bstan 'dzin zer ba zhig yod 'dug pas de kha sa skyar bzhes na ji ltar lags kyi snyan 'bul zhus 'dug par/ gzhungs nas de kha legs pa 'dug tshul gyi bslab ston bka' drin
bskyangs 'dug pa dang / phran bur yang grub mtha' sogs gong spyi nas babs 'brel shin tu che bas 'phral 'bul dgos tshul gyi bka' shog rin po che pheb/

'jam mgon chos kyi rgyal po'i bka' shog phyag mdzod rang gi sa skya nas gsung brtag babs tshul gang ci'i bslab ston zhib pa/ gser srang gang / chibs gsar ma legs pas gtsos
gnang sbyin dpangs mtho ba bcas gzims dpon mgron gnyer dang / me nyag dbon po gnyis lcam 'bul dgos tshul gyi bslab ston gnang byung bar/ nged rang tsho sa skya pa'i gdung
pheb par shin tu dungs pa dang / bslab ston pheb phyin bka' dang blang zhu ba gzhir bcas zhus nas/ sku tshab phyir slog dang len 'debs phul bas/ zhag shas nas sa skya phyag
mdzod rgyun gyi dbang por pheb/ bzhugs sa sgrub sder mdzad/ nyin re bzhin bla brang du pheb nas gsung gleng zhib rgyas dang nang mjal sogs zhib par mdzad/ gzhis len rgyas
par zhus/ nged kyis gzhis su phyin/ phyi nyin phyag mdzod dpon g.yog pheb bsur gzhis khar pheb/ gzhis len dang tshan grangs rgyas par phul/ ma nas lcam 'di dkyus ma
zhig min 'dug pas/ mgon po mjal ba na snyan dar babs pa/ zhal khebs ma bsal bar bye ba sogs lo phyi nang du ltas ya mtshan pa byung 'dug cing / nged rang la'ang rmi ltas
su nyi ma shar ba/ dar po che btsugs pa/ chu bo 'babs pa sogs legs par byung / gza' tshes legs par gzhis nas gdan sar skya ser du ma dang bcas rdzong bda' zhus/ shab 'di
snga sor nA lendra'i dgon lag yin par yon bdag dga' mo bas bdag byed dgos gsung thog /kho rang tshos kyang de bzhin byed dgos pa'i 'phros byung ba bzhin bla ma mchog legs
bsko gzhag byas/ de nas chos sde chen po'i gtor spod/ bskang ba khri tshar/ tshe chog /bka' 'gyur/ rgyas 'bring bsdus

gsum/ sgrol ma dang sher snying khri tshar/ ba ri gtor chen sogs rim gro mang tsam bsgrubs shing / lho kha dang / rgya ma/ mal gro/ skyed tshal sogs nas gsan bzhed kyis pheb
pa dang / tshogs chen du lam 'bras kyi snang gsum lung dang bcas pa slob ma rjes 'dzin gyi bar grub nas/ grwa pa rnams smon lam chen mor byon/ nged bsnyen pa kha gsor bsdad/
tshur pheb 'phral rgyu dbang / lam dbang / rgyud gsum smin rgyas/ so so'i byin rlabs/ lung rnams dang bcas pa gong ma'i phyag len bzhin phul/ ! sa 'brug lor lo gsar
rgyas pa byas shing / lo 'dir sa dbang gser gyi 'khor los sgyur ba chen po nas bka' shog rin po che spyi bor pheb 'bras bzhin lhun grub rdzong du nged rang tshogs chen bcas
pas phyin pas/ lam thog nas chu rdol shin tu che bar byung zhing / rdzong du 'byor bstun dpal ldan dgyes mdzad rdo rje'i sgo nas zhi ba'i sbyin sreg brgya rtsa 'dug pa'i
zhabs phyi zla ba gcig zhus par/ dgos cha phog sogs shin tu rgyas pa bka' drin bskyangs/ 'di skabs chos skyong rnams kyi bskang ba'i dus nub gcig btsan skya rdo rje 'bar
ba'i sprul pa sprags btsan nyid thog mar 'od shin tu che bas nang thams cad khengs pa dang / de rjes sku dngos su mthong bar chibs rag dkar la gser chas spras pa/ dar
dkar gyi na bza' gsol ba/ gzi brjid dang ldan pa zhig mthong bar/ nged kyi dpung pa g.yas pa'i steng nas thog mar dre'u dang / de rjes dpal ldan lha mo nyid kyi sku gzi
brjid dang ldan pa zhig byung ba/ lha mo'i sku de je che la song bar zhang lha nyid je chung la song bas mthar yal ba'i snang ba zhig byung bar/ sprags btsan 'di zhang

lhar song bas brtse ba'i tshul gyis byon par bar chad byung dogs lha mo nyid pheb par sems/ 'di dus rmi lam du gong sa skyabs mgon chen po nyid dang mjal bar/ zhabs phyi ban
gzugs shig gis gser gyi rdo rje rtse lnga pa 'od 'phro ba zhig sprad de/ 'di khyod la gnang ba yin 'dug zer zhing / sangs rgyas kun dngos dpal ldan bla ma nyid dgyes pa'i
tshul gyis bslab ston mang po gnang ba zhig gsal bar dmigs/ me phra shin tu legs pa dang bcas rgyud sde nas ji ltar gsungs pa bzhin sbyin sreg mtshan nyid dang ldan pa
legs par grub nas/ rdzong bzhugs kyi sku rim du sger nas dgos cha gnang ste/ sbyin sreg kyang thugs bzhed ltar bsgrubs/ de zhor spras nang gi yon bdag rnams kyi byang bu/
tshe dbang / dbang / rjes gnang / bsngo smon dgos pa rnams kyang 'dod sbyar chos 'brel dang / 'khor gsum yongs dag gi dmigs med bsngo smon gyi rgyas 'debs sogs byas nas/
sbyin sreg grub par gnang sbyin sogs rgyas par bka' drin bskyangs ngos rang gi bsti gnas su 'khor 'phral/ pho brang chen por mjal khar zhu bar phyin skabs/ sa dbang chen
po'i sku zhabs su sbyin sreg me pra sogs legs tshul snyan 'bul ngos kyis zhib par zhus/ zur gsos dang gnang sbyin rgyas par stsal te phyir 'ong / skabs shig rmi lam du
nub byang mtshams kyi nam mkha' 'ja' sprin gyis khebs pa'i gseb nas rta pa shin tu mang ba chas sogs rgyas pa dang / gtso bo de 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po'i chas mig gis
mthong ba'i tshe yid 'gul nus pa zhig 'dug pa rim gyis bar snang nas shar phyogs nam mkha' bskor te lho phyogs su pheb dus gtso bo de rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas dang /

'khor rnams gnas brtan bcu drug sogs dgra bcom pa/ yon bdag rgyal po ha shang yang gzi brjid che la bag dro ba/ rta spu log la chibs pa/ gzhan yang mchod pa'i lha pho mo rnams
kyis rgyal srid sna bdun/ bkra shis rtags brgyad sogs mchod rdzas du ma thogs pas bar snang khengs ba mthong / dad mos kyi snang ba byung tshe sems spros bral gyi ngang
du re zhig lus/ ji zhig nas gnyid sad/ ci yin/ ngo mtshar ni che snyam pa byung / phyis su bsams na rigs brgya'i khyab bdag khams gsum chos kyi rgyal po lnga pa chen po
nyid bstan 'gro rnams la phan bde stsol phyir sku drug par 'pho tshul ston slad/ lho mon mtshams su mnyam med o rgyan chen po'i sgrub gnas su che ba'i yon tan bsam gyis
mi khyab pa dang ldan pa o rgyan gling pa'i gdung du sprul pa'i zlos gar bsgyur te 'dzam gling sa'i lte ba pho brang chen po ri bo gru 'dzin du pheb ste 'gro ba rnams rdzogs
ldan gyi bde ba la 'god pa'i brdar go /mjal khar phyin skabs e ma chi lags kyis sku bgres shing bsnyun gzhi yang ro mar song bas gnyen drung gi tsha chur phyin pa 'gab
tshul sbang blang gi bslab ston gnang ba bzhin nged dpon slob bzhi bcu skor gyis phyin pas sprags kyi mdor rta thog tu gnyid ze re ba zhig la 'brog pa dang 'brog mo rgyan
ldan gnyis kyi rkyal pa gnyis khur 'dug pa phyag dbang zhu ba'i tshe rkyal pa kha bshig pa nor bus gang 'dug pa byin byung ba ni lha chen yab yum gyi dngos grub kyis
bsu bar go /bod sog gi ru ba rnams kyis bsnyen bkur rgyas par byung / dbang dang / byang bu/ bsngo smon/ ma Ni'i lung / sngags mdud/ byin rten/ ster sbyin sogs kyis tshim
par byas/ cho hor nas 'bul sdud

bla ma bsam 'phel dang / bum rdza dang nye ba nas bla ma sku skye rin po ches 'bod mi 'byor ba nas gnam mtshor bskor ba zhig kyang sngar sor phyin dus ma grub pas la rgan brgyud
phyin skabs/ rda ro kha zhig gis bos/ ston mo dang ster sbyin bzang bar byas par bsngo smon dang / sbra/ nor lug sogs la shis brjod kyi me tog gtor skabs zim bu'i char
gyis bsu ba byung / bsang mchod rgyas par phul te/ phyin pas nam mkha' g.ya' dag cing me tog gi char dang / mtsho zhal shin tu dwangs pa'i chu'i gnyer ma rnams 'ja' tshon
kha dog sna lnga bkra bar rgyug pa dang / 'khyil nas mtsho dkyil du rlabs gur tsam g.yo ba sogs lha chen zur phud lnga pa dang / yum rdo rje phyug mo mnyes pa'i rnam
'gyur bstan par go zhing / mtsho rdzas dkar yol/ gser dngul sogs rin po che'i rigs/ gos dar dang / 'bru sna/ stag ras/ gzig ras sogs rgyas par phul ba na mtsho steng du
thag ring bar ma bying bar song ste/ de nas mtsho nang du bzhes/ bsang dang phrin bcol rgyas par zhus te phyin/ thang lha'i sku mdun du dkon mchog spyi 'dus kyi tshogs 'khor
dang / bsang mchod/ gsol kha rgyas par phul/ sku mdun mthong sa zhig tu gsol kha 'bul par mchod dpon dge 'dun g.yog bcas btang / rim gyis ngam chu brgal te phyin pas
'dam sogs lam log zhig tu 'gro grabs byas pas/ ga nas 'ong cha med pa'i mi zhig byung ste lam bstan pa ni gnyen gyi rgyal pos bstan pa yin 'dra bsam mo/ /bod skyong lha chen
rdo rje 'bar ba rtsal/ /yum mchog rdo rje phyug mo dang bcas pa'i/ /bla mtsho gnam sngon zhun mar 'khyil 'dra la/ /mchod rdzas dngos 'byor yid sprul

mchod pas mchod/ /de tshe lha chen yab yum dgyes pa'i brdar/ /nam mkha' dwangs shing mtsho rlabs gur ltar phub/ /rgyus med log pa'i lam la chas pa'i tshe/ /mngon sum ma nor
lan ston ngo mtshar rmad/ /rim gyis byang phyogs yangs pa'i yul du phyin/ /dad stobs 'byor ldan rnams kyis bkur stis mchod/ /rta nor mar sogs dngos po'i longs spyod 'dis/
/ngal bsos rgyal po'i khengs pa phrogs kyis dogs/ /de nas dred chu brgal te phyin/ /gser mtsho'i 'gram nas rim gyis gnam ru ba dang / bya rigs rnams kyi so sor bos nas
bsnyen bkur byung / dbang dang bsngo smon gyi rgyas 'debs sogs 'dod sbyar byas/ san chung nas 'bul dpon bla ma bsam 'phel gyis mgyogs bskul gyi bsu mi 'byor/ rim gyis san
chen du sman ral pa'i ru bar 'byor/ ston mo ster cha gzabs par byas/ de skor gyi yon bdag tshang mar dbang dang / byang bu/ bsngo smon sogs la tshogs te ci nus kyi dngos
po dpangs mtho bar byung / lugs gnyis kyis so so'i re ba bskangs/ 'bul dpon gyi sgar nas rta bsu ba mang tsam byung / sgar thog tu 'byor nas ston mo sogs legs shing / cho
hor gyi sde rnams tshogs par tshe dbang / phyag rdor/ ri khrod lo ma gyon ma sogs kyi rjes gnang / bsnyen gnas dang ma Ni'i lung / byang bu bsngo smon sogs kyis blo'i re
ba bskangs/ 'bul dpon dang yon bdag sbra chen gyis rta nor drug cu skor byin/ tshe dbang lcags sdong ma/ rjes gnang kha shas dang / byang bu/ bsngo smon/ byin rten gyis
tshim par byas/ de nas bar rings kyi sder slebs/ tshang mas rta nor gyis

gtsos ster cha gzabs par byas/ tshe dbang grub rgyal ma dang / rta mgrin dbyu gto can/ seng gdong ma/ ri khrod ma sogs kyi rjes gnang / byang bu/ bsngo smon/ bsnyen gnas kyi
sdom pa/ skyabs sdom/ spyan ras gzigs kyi bzlas lung dang / byin rten sogs kyis mgu bar byas/ de nas 'brom mtsho khar nor bu'i sder tsha ba bla ma bsod nams lhun grub yon
mchod kyis 'ong dgos tshul byung ba ltar phyin/ rta bsu ba mang tsam byung zhing / sde thog tu 'byor nas gzhis len bsnyen bkur rgyas par byas/ cho ga dang / sbra/ nor
lugs sogs la shis brjod dang me tog gtor/ thang sku dang chos bris pa rnams la rab gnas/ bsngo smon gyi rgyas 'debs 'dod sbyar dang / spyan ras gzigs/ phyag rdor gos sngon
can/ 'jam dpal rdo rje'i rjes gnang / grub thob tshe dbang / ma Ni'i lung / 'pho lung / bsngo smon rnams blo dang mthun par byas/ mdzo/ mdzo mo/ 'bri/ khal mang ba/ me
mda'/ mar sogs dngos po dpangs mtho bar byung / /sngags mdud/ byin rten sogs gang legs sprad/ de nas rim gyis rla dbar gsang du 'byor/ der gnas kyi o thog /ge mo/ hor gyi
sde rnams dang / sbra chung lha rje sogs kyis bsnyen bkur dang / rta nor bzhi cu skor byin/ na dmar che ba brgyud dkar mo khugs su 'byor pa'i lam bar gyi sde rnams kyis
rta nor gyi ster sbyin du ma byung / bsngo smon bka' bsgo/ nas 'thor sogs 'dod mthun dang ster sbyin byas/ de nas lam thog bla ma sprus sku rang gis dbus grwa pa dang / yon
bdag lnga bcu skor gyi rta bsu ba 'byor/ thab bsu dang gung tshigs drangs/ rim gyis sgar thog tu 'byor/ zhag lnga'i ring

bsnyen bkur shin tu rgyas par byung zhing / de skor gyi grwa rigs hor sogs yon bdag pho mo mang bar tshogs/ byang gter gyi tshe dbang / grub thob tshe dbang / kun rig dang
/ tshe dpag lha dgu /sman bla/ gur lha brgyad/ rnam sras ser chen/ khyung khra nag /seng gdong ma sogs dbang dang rjes gnang mang ba dang / cho ga'i thog yon bdag shi gson
gyi byang bu/ rus tshwa/ bsnyen gnas/ skyabs sdom/ ma Ni'i lung dang / skra phud len pa/ dge rtsa byang chub tu bsngo ba sogs mang ba zhig byas/ nyin ltar dad gus kyis
khrom che bar tshogs shing / phyag dang / bskor ba/ smon lam gyi 'ur sgras yid 'gul bar gyur/ bla ma sku skyes rta sum cu so lnga/ nor lnga bcu skor/ mar sogs dngos po gya
nom pa/ de skor yon bdag rnams kyis rta sum cu lhag tsam dang / mdzo/ mdzo mo/ 'bri/ g.yag sogs nor brgya skor gyi ster sbyin byung bar blangs/ phyag mdud/ byin rten so
so'i blo dang mthun par byas/ sprul sku dpon slob rnams kyis la thog bar skyel mar byon/ srung mdud dang gang cir ngag bkod byas te dkar mo khugs su 'byor/ de skor 'brog
rigs rnams kyis rnyed bkur dang 'bul nod mang bar byas shing / dbang dang / bsngo smon/ byin rten/ ster sbyin blo dang 'tshams par byas/ rim gyis rma bya khugs su 'byor/
yas mas kyi hor rnams dang / 'bul sdud bla ma bstan 'dzin grags pa/ hor gyi sde bla rdza rad sku skye rjes snyegs su 'phrad par byung / tshang mas rta nor/ mar sogs dngos
po phyur bur du spungs/ phyag rdor gtum po dang / sor 'brang gi rjes gnang / byang bu/ bsngo smon/ bsnyen gnas/ skyabs sdom/ lung sogs 'dod chos dang /

sngags mdud/ byin rten/ ster cha sogs lugs gnyis kyis bzhed pa bskangs/ lam du zhugs nas na dmar chung bar 'byor/ dge slong bsam 'grub rgya mtsho sogs o thog shog drug gi ru
ba phar cher 'phrad par 'byor/ zhag gnyis sdod ring so so'i blo dang 'tshams pa'i tshe dbang grub rgyal ma/ gzungs grwa lnga/ bka' gdams lha bzhi/ rta mgrin lcags ral can
rnams kyi rjes gnang dang / byang bu/ rus tshwa/ skra phud/ bsnyen gnas kyi lung / dge rtsa chos dbyings su bsngo ba sogs byas shing / tshang ma dad gus kyi gdung shugs
kyis smon lam dang gsol 'debs kyi sgra 'ur dir sgrog cing / phyag dang bskor bas lam byang bar gyur/ mar thud sogs kyi ston mo dbyar mtsho ltar chal chil du gyur cing /
rta bzhi bcu skor dang / mdzo/ mdzo mo/ 'bri/ g.yag sogs nyis brgya skor byin/ mdud pa/ byin rten sogs kyi ster cha blo dang mtshams par byas/ de nas rim gyis phyin/ mtsho
skya'i 'gram du bsdad skabs/ bla brang bla mas gtsos che chen dbon po'i sde rnams 'phrad par 'byor zhing so sos ster cha gzabs par byas/ 'dod sbyar gyi dbang dang / byang
bu/ bsngo smon sogs gang rgyas/ byin rten/ ster sbyin sogs legs par byas/ gsol 'debs dang smon lam byed bzhin pa'i ngang nas rim gyis bskyod de se ter 'byor/ sbyar kho
che'i sde dang / 'brong pa rnams kyis ston mo dang / rta nor sum cu skor byin/ dbang / byang bu/ rus tshwa/ bsngo smon rnams gang legs dang / byin rten/ ster sbyin 'tshams
par byas/ la rgan brgyud 'ong skabs 'dam nas da rgan chos rje'i grwa rigs rnams kyis 'ong dgos tshul byung bas dred kyi mdor 'byor/ zhag bzhi bsdad/ dge lugs kyi grwa
rigs dang /

yon bdag pho mo rnams la kun rig gi dbang nyin gnyis kyi ring mang ba zhig byas/ grwa pa rnams kyis ston mo'i thog grwa pa rer 'bri re phul song zhing / yon bdag rnams kyis
bsnyen bkur dang / rta nor gyi ster cha mang du byung / tshe dbang dang rta mgrin sogs kyi rjes gnang / byang bu/ bsnyen gnas/ skyabs sdom/ bsngo smon sogs 'dod chos dang
/ byin rten rgyas par byas/ de nas bskyod de gnyan drung du 'byor/ dri za'i rgyal por gsol mchod rgyas par phul/ de skor ru ba rnams kyis bsnyen bkur yang dag byung bar
dge rtsa byang chub tu bsngo ba dang ster sbyin sogs gang la gang 'tshams par byas/ rim gyis sprags su 'byor/ 'brog pa rnams kyis rnyed bkur legs shing / zhang lhar song
bas sbrags btsan gyi mkhar la gsol kha phul/ pho rog la nas dar yul du slebs/ dgon lag sgom khang du nged rang gi chos mdzad ma ngag dbang bzang mo 'phrad par phyin/ zhag
gsum bsdad/ skyes ma rgyas par phul zhing / mkhas grub dam pa nyan po chos rje bsod nams bstan 'dzin rgyal po bsu bar pheb par rta legs zhig kyang skyes su phul/ sgom khang
du mang ja dang / spyi sar 'bri zhig byin/ rim gyis thams cad mkhyen pa rong ston chen po'i gdan sa dpal rgyun gyi dbang por 'ong skabs bkra shis gling du bla khag las
tshan dang bcas pas thab bsu dang / dgon gnas nas bla brang / khams tshan so sos lha bsang dang / dar 'phyar/ dung 'bud/ rgya gling sogs mchod rdzas du ma dang bcas dge
'dun rnams kyis ser phreng gi mdun brdar de gsang chen dbyar rnga sgrogs pa'i bsti gnas bla brang lcang lo can du slebs/ de 'phral ser ja zhus/ phyi nyin mang ja sbyor
sbrel thog bla khag rnams la rta res

gtsos tshan grangs dang / tshogs su zhon rtas gtsos nor gyi spyi 'bul gzabs par phul/ thag nye'i yon bdag 'phrad par byung ba rnams la babs 'brel dang bstun pa'i skyes ma byin/
gzhis su 'ong dgos tshul byung ba bzhin phyin/ skyes ma gzabs pa dang / g.yog rnams la ster sbyin byas/ rgyun gyi dbang po'i chos grwa 'byor nas pho brang chen por mjal
khar bcar te rta nor gyis gtsos 'bul ba dpangs mtho bar phul/ ston mo rgyas par stsal/ mchod dpon lags dang / dge slong rin po che/ em chi lags/ dge slong ngag dbang
dkon mchog /gsol dpon sngags rams pa lags/ drung yig lags/ gzims dpon lags/ mgron gnyer lags sogs la rta/ mdzo mo sogs kyi skyes ma gzabs par phul/ so so nas shin tu dgyes
shing gang ci'i bslab ston gsol ja sogs gnang / dge slong rin po cher gsang sgrub zhal bzhi pa'i rjes gnang zhig phul/ sa dbang chen por thon phyag zhus nas shin tu dgyes
pa'i dri ba dang gnang sbyin stsal te bsti gnas su 'byor/ dgon khag gi grwa rigs yon bdag rnams 'phrad par byung bas skyes kyi ster sbyin byas/ sgom khang nas sring mo
grib skyon byung bas 'bod mi byung 'phral du phyin pas khams ma 'tsho 'dug par 'pho ba dang / zhag gsum ring nged rang nas kun rig gi cho ga /lho sgo dang dbang bskur sogs
byas shing / dgung zhag pa bcu skor gyis cho ga dang / gtor ma sogs byas/ zhag gsum dang / dngos gzhi'i nyin tshogs chen dang / bdun tshigs rnams su dar yul rang gi dgon
khag rnams bsdus nas so so'i cho ga dang / sa skyar rta legs pa gcig bcas byang zhus/ gzhan ma bla khag che ba rnams su byang zhus dang / chung ba rnams su

bsngo zhus byas shing / lo mchod la tshogs chen sogs la zhabs tog dang 'bul yon gyis mnyes par byas/ chos sde chen po'i dus dran mchod pa dang gtor spod/ bstan srung rgya mtsho'i
tshogs la bskang ba khri tshar skabs/ tshogs chen du bka' 'gyur/ kun rig stong rtsa/ phyogs bzhi'i gtor ma sogs rim gro mang bar byas par yon sogs kyi mnyes par byas/
lo mjug gi gtor zlog sogs bsgrub nas// ! sa sbrul lor lo gsar dang tshe sgrub cig byas/ dus 'khor gyi dbang rgyun dkon pa zhig 'dug gshis zhabs drung dbon la byed rtsis
yod skabs mchims phu nas dpal ri ba me rag dpon slob dbang gsan sar ched gtad byon byung gshis/ rgyu skar bdag po lha drug brgya dang so drug gi dkyil 'khor du slob ma'i
gtso bo zhabs drung dbon rin po che/ rmor zhabs drung / me rag dpon slob sogs gtso bor gyur pa'i skal ldan gyi slob ma nyi shu rtsa lnga la byis pa 'jug pa'i dbang bdun/
dbang gong ma gsum dang / bdag po chen po'i dbang bcas phul ba'i sta gon gyi nyin dzo ki zhig byung nas dbang rdzas su mkho ba'i dung rwa chen gyi dung chos legs pa zhig
dang / tsandan dkar po'i 'bras bu yin zer ba'i rgya 'phrang khyad du mtshar ba zhig byin byung nas bla ma dang lhag pa'i lhas rten 'brel bsgrigs par mngon zhing / dngos
gzhi'i nyin nyi ma sngar las ring zhing 'ja' 'od sogs ltas legs par byung / tshogs chen du 'jigs byed rwa lugs ro langs brgyad skor gyi gshor dbang sogs me rag dpon slob
kyi thugs bzhed kyi chos rnams rdzogs par phul te/ o rgyan sangs rgyas gnyis pa'i sgrub gnas su phyir pheb/ bla brang du mchod pa dang ban tshang /

gtong sgo sogs kyi 'gro gron che gshis dang / chos gzhis cher zhan pa dang bcas lo gsum re nas 'phen yul stod smad du dbang gzhis byed dgos kyin yod pa'i stabs/ skabs shig
'jog po phyin skabs khrom dbang gi dus nam mkha' 'ja' 'od kyis khengs pa'i dbus su mkha' 'gro rnams kyis mchod pa'i yo byad du ma dang bcas te 'ja' tshon gyi mdo le lta bus
btegs pa'i dkyil du rje btsun mkha' spyod gtso mo bzhugs pa'i zhal mngon sum du mthong bas mos gus dung dung / sems dga' bde'i rang bzhin du dar cig gnas pa ni skye ba
snga ma nan tan du bsgrubs pa'i nus mthu dang / gnas der rA hu la badzra dang / khyung po rnal 'byor gyi sgrub gnas su song bas byin rlabs mngon du stsal bar 'dug go /khyab
bdag dang po'i sangs rgyas gdon ma'i mgon/ /rgyu skar bdag po sprul pa'i dkyil 'khor du/ /rigs dbon dam pa gtsor gyur skal bzang la/ /smin byed dbang gi sa bon legs par
btab/ /de tshe 'phags pa'i yul nas dzwa ki zhig /lhag pa'i lha yi thugs rjes legs bskul nas/ /gu ru khyed kyi dbang rdzas 'di na zhes/ /bgrang phreng dung chos khyad mtshar
skyes su byin/ /sprul zhing mkha' la spyod pa'i gnas kyi gtso/ /ring nas bskyangs pa'i yi 'ong lha mo des/ /skye bar 'bral med rjes su 'dzin pa'i brdar/ /sku yi snang
brnyan mngon sum gsal bar bstan/ /khyung 'bum gyis 'bul skyel phyir rdzong sogs rim sel sngar 'khyud dang / pho brang chen por gong sa yas phyin mjal khar phyin par bdag
rkyen gzhan dang mi 'dra bar bka' drin bskyang / rdo rje 'dzin pa chen po dge slong rin po cher rta mgrin yang gsang gi dkyil 'khor du bka' dbang rgyas

pa dang / gying lnga gza' gdong sogs chos kha shas zhus/ dge slong rin po che dang / dge slong ngag dbang dkon mchog gnyis la chos kha shas phul zhing gnas su slebs/ gzhis
kyi khang pa gcong ches pas khang las mi byed kha med byung ba rdzong las zhol du byas na khag sun chung bar zhal ngo rnams dang / g.yog rigs tshang ma gros 'chams te/ zhaul
du nged rang gi khang gzhis rnying pa g.yog cig gi lag tu yod par sa tshab sprad/ do shol du khang pa rgyag par tshang ma bgros te gong sa chen por gsung brtag zhus par
zhol du 'gab tshul pheb pa bzhin khang tshab sprod rgyag rtsis kyi thag chod kyang / gzhan ma'i ngan bslab kyis khong tshang bsam blo 'gyur te brjes na mi 'ong tshul labs
par nye ba zhig bcas byung ste de kha'i rgyu mtshan mang ba lab mur/ nye ba de'i ske 'gags shing tshir nas skad ma thon par log dgos byung song ba ni dgos med mgo las
grod pa mkhregs pa dpal ldan lha mo thugs khrel ba'i cho 'phrul dang phrin las bsgrubs par mngon zhing / gang ltar kho rang tsho'ang dogs gzhi byung 'dug pa bcas sa brjes
skor rang grol du song bas ar po'i bca' bsgrigs/ ston spyi chen 'bul dpon bla ma rab 'byams pa dpon slob brgyad cu skor 'byor zhing / gzhis len sogs lugs gnyis kyi sgo
nas gang legs zhus/ nged khu dbon tshogs su bos te bla rgan zhing gshegs kyi dgongs rdzogs su cho ga stong tshar mdzad par nyin bstar phyin te lho sgo dang / bsngo smon gyi
rgyas 'debs yang dag byas/ grol nyin nged khu dbon la rta legs pa dang / gzhan yang rta/ dre'u/ mdzo/ khal/ ja/ khrab/ gos dar sogs dngos po'i rigs

gzabs rgyas dang / tshogs par kyang 'gyed gya nom par mdzad cing / de dag zab pa chos kyi dbyings dang / rgya che ba sems can gyi don du rgyas 'debs yang dag par byas/ 'grul
pa gzhan rnams kyis kyang / ja/ rta phyug sogs che 'byor chung 'byor gyi 'bul ba mang bar byung ba'ang bsngo smon gyi rgyas btab/ dgun tsha ba bla ma bkra shis tshe ring
dang / spyi chen 'bul sdud bla ma dbu mdzad bcas 'byor/ tshogs su stong chog mdzad pa'i gral dbur phyin/ rta/ dri'u/ ja/ mdzo phyugs sogs mang bar byung zhing / byang bu
dang dge ba rdzogs byang du bsngos/ dus chen khag rnams grub 'phral dbon rin po che dang / mtshungs med chos rje rin po che/ gling smad zhabs drung / glang thang grwa tshang
gi drung chen/ gsang phu mchod khang dpon slob kun dga' dpal bzang sogs gtso bor gyur pa'i 'dus pa'i tshogs la rnal 'byor dbang phyug chen po 'jigs bral dpal ldan chos
skyong gi bzhed gzhung gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i gdams pa/ dbang / byin rlabs/ cha lag /rgyab rten gyi lung rnams dang bcas pas smin rgyas byas
shing / 'di skabs rgyal bstan spyi dang / bye brag gsang chen slob bshad pa rnams kyi bsod nams las ma grub pa'i bkra shis chos sde nas dbon rin po che dag zhing du gshegs
pa'i thugs dam gsal 'debs pa 'byor zhing / tshogs su mchod 'bul zhus/ snang gsum gyi ring dbon gyis kyang tshogs su tshar lugs kyi dkar po rnam gsum/ sgrub thabs brgya
rtsa/ sgrol ma nyer gcig /bka' gdams lha bzhi sogs ngag bkod ltar mdzad/ sems bskyed dang / slob ma rjes 'dzin grub nas/

lcags rta lor lo gsar dang / tshe sgrub bsnyen pa kha gso byas/ grol 'phral nged rang nas zab mo rdo rje theg pa'i smin byed kyi gtso bo rgyu dbang dang / lam dbang / mkha'
spyod ma/ lam zab/ bir srung sogs dang / dbon nas rigs gsum spyi dbang / tshe dpag lha dgu/ mi 'khrugs pa'i dbang sogs mdzad skabs/ gong sa chen po nas bkra shis chos sder
dgongs rdzogs kyi tshogs dbu dang zhugs 'bul la 'gro dgos pa'i bka' shog rin po che spyi bor pheb cing khong rang gi thugs bzhed ltar rgyang tsam nas 'ong ba'i khas len
zhus/ smin byed kyi dbang dang / byin rlabs rnams grub nas/ lho kha phyogs su dus tshes dang mthun par gnas kyi dbang po nas rta kha bskyod de rim gyis rngog lo yab sras
sogs mkhas grub du mas byin gyis rlabs pa'i gnas gsang phu ne'u thog gi chos grar 'byor skabs mchod khang dpon slob kyi dbus gzhis dgon rnams kyis ser phreng / dar 'phyar/
thab bsu sogs gang rgyas mdzad cing / mang ja/ sbyor sbrel/ rnam bzhag /mchod khang dpon slob la tshan grangs kyang phul/ zhag gnyis bsdad/ mchod khang pas gzhis len
yang dag byung / phyi nyin sgrol ma rtsod rgyal ma sogs rten rnams zhib par mjal skabs/ jo bo yab sras gsum bar snang du bzhugs pa'i snang ba shin tu gsal ba byung zhing
/ me tog gi char babs pa der gnas kun gyi mig yul du gyur pas tshang ma yang mtshan pa byed 'dug pa dang / rang yang ngo mtshar snyam pa byung ba ni gnas gzhan dang mi 'dra
ba'i byin rlabs su mngon/ dam pa du mas byin rlabs gsang phur slebs/ /dam pa'i sku gsum nam mkha'i dbyings nas mthong / /de tshe sum rtsen lha yis

mchod pa'i phyir/ /me tog char dang 'ja' 'od gur khyim phub/ /sems bskyed gling pa'i 'dra 'bag kun mkhyen gyis phyag bzo mar snyan dar dang / rten mchod rnams la mchod bsnyan
dar sogs gang legs phul/ mchod khang bla ma sogs la sgrol dkar dang / gur mgon gyi rjes gnang / lung sogs thugs 'dod ltar zhus/ gling stod bla brang du zhabs drung cung
zhig sku ltem 'dug par/ dbang la shog gsung / phyin pas sgo rtsar bsu bar pheb cing phyag rtse sprod byas/ nged rang la khri shin tu mtho ba dang bcas bzos sgo gzhis len
zab rgyas gnang / tshe dbang / rta mgrin/ 'byung 'dul gyi rjes gnang phul/ gnang sbyin rgyas par stsal/ sku gzugs kyi 'phrod bsten sogs snyan 'bul zhus/ thugs dgyes par
byung song / mchod khang dpon slob kyi dzhe khyim las grub pa'i nam mkha'i snying po'i sku li ma shin tu legs pa zhig gi gtsos ster sbyin gzabs rgyas byung zhing / phar
yang byin rten sogs phul/ mdor skor byas/ 'od 'chang rdo'i lha khang du zhag gcig bsdad/ rten mchod rnams la snyan shal mchod pa gang rgyas phul zhing / bstan 'gror phan
bde 'byung ba'i smon lam yid ches pa btab/ sang nyin chos gra chen po rab smad du 'byor zhing / bla brang grwa khang so so nas bsang / dar 'phyar sogs gang rgyas mdzad/ sku
rten pa'i bshag la 'byor skabs su pheb grabs mdzad byung bar sang snga dro legs par 'dug tshul zhus pas de 'phral zhi song / gzhis len yang dag byung / phyi nyin chos
skyong chen po sku pheb zhus shing / de 'phral nged rang phyin pas rdo skas mgor bsu bar pheb/ btsan khang du 'byor 'phral snyan shal/ tshan grangs sogs rgyas par phul zhing
/

spang blang gi lung bstan zhus par dgyes tshor dang / 'phral yun gyi bslab ston zhib par gnang / chos skyong gi lcog tu thugs bzhed ltar me tog gtor/ 'ong khar gos chen gyi
rgyal mtshan/ stag stan/ dar tshon sna lnga sogs stsal te/ rgyal mtshan gyi sham bu rlung gis ma bskyod par byas pas sa gzhi thams cad khengs par byed do ang zhes sogs lung
bstan kyang shin tu legs par mdzad/ 'ong dus rdo skas mgor skyel mar pheb cing 'phreng ba'i tshul gyis khang pas ma bsgribs par gzigs shing dgyes pa'i 'dzum zhal lhug
par bstan to/ /shAkya'i mtshan can mkhas grub dam pa yis/ /dam btags ma g.yel dam tshig dang ldan pa'i/ /sems bskyed gling pas bstan dang rgyal mtshan sogs/ /stsal te dus
kun bsrung bar zhal gyis bzhes/ /de nas 'du khang du tshogs par 'byung 'dul dang / gur lha brgyad thun mong ba sogs kyi rjes gnang byas/ mang ja spyi 'bul dang slob dpon
la tshan grangs sogs rgyas par zhus/ bla brang nas kyang gzhis len gzabs rgyas gnang byung zhing / spyir sger tshang mas ster sbyin gzabs par mdzad de zhag gnyis bsdad/
phyi nyin sdu phud chos 'khor du 'byor/ bsu ba sogs gzhan dang ma 'dra bar byung zhing / 'byor 'phral gzhis len kyang rgyas par mdzad/ thub dbang dang dpal mo gser gyi snying
thag can sogs rten rnams zhib par mjal zhing mchod pa snyan dar rgyas pa phul te bstan 'gro'i don du smon lam yid tshim par btab/ grwa tshang bcas spyi sger tshang
mas ster cha gzabs rgyas mdzad/ mang ja/ byin rten/ sngags mdud sogs dang tshogs su 'byung 'dul/ gur mgon/ tshe dbang sogs

dang / thugs bzhed kyi chos mang bar yang phul/ phyi nyin gra thang du 'byor par bsang / dar 'phyar/ bsu ba sogs byung zhing / bla brang du bsdad par bsnyen bkur shin tu gzabs
pa byung / mang ja sogs gang la gang 'tshams kyis tshang mas mnyes par byas shing / so so nas dar ras snam phrug sogs ster cha mang bar mdzad/ kun rig /tshe dpag lha
dgu/ tshe dbang sogs thugs 'dod ltar/ zhag gcig bsdad/ phyi nyin gtsug lag khang dang lha khang so sor snyan shal dang mchod pa rgyas par phul zhing smon lam btab/ rten mchod
rnams byin chags shing dngos gtsang bar 'dug /zhang blon chen po'i gsob la snyan dar dang phrin bcol zhus/ de nas gra phyi tshogs su phyin/ mkhan po bsu bar pheb cing
dar 'phyar/ bsang sogs gang rgyas par mdzad/ slebs 'phral gzhis len dang ster sbyin sogs rim par byung / mang ja/ spyi 'bul/ mkhan por 'bul ba sogs gang legs dang / so
sor sngags mdud/ byin rten kyang phul/ gong sa chen po nas bka' drin bskyangs pa'i sman bla'i mdo chog gi lung dang / 'dod chos kha shas kyang byas/ paN chen gyi sku 'dra
phyag nas ma/ rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi 'phel gdung / karma pa de bzhin gshegs pas tshogs su phul ba'i tshogs dung khyad mtshar sogs rten mchod 'gangs chen shin tu mang
ba mjal zhing / rten so sor snyan dar sogs gang rgyas phul nas/ yid sprul gyi mchod sprin kun tu bzang po'i rnam thar las 'gran bzod par spros shing / phan bde 'bad med
du 'byung ba'i smon lam dpyis phyin par btab/ phyi nyin ja sar bkra shis chos sde nas thab bsu 'dug pa dang / sger ba nas kyang sde pa rin po ches tshur lam 'ong dgos pa'i
phyag bris kyang byung /

chos rgyal na rim gyis byin gyis brlabs pa'i thub dbang gi sku sogs mjal/ mchod pa snyan dar phul/ zhabs drung zhabs ma brtan gshis bkra shis chos sder dgong slebs byas/ song
gdung 'bul du ja rta sogs dgu tshan lnga tsam phul zhing / mchod 'bul yang dag byas/ 'gor ring ri bo bde chen nas dge 'dun kha shas pheb pa gtso bor gyur pa'i don gnyer
ba rnams la kye rdor gyi dbang tshan gnyis sogs 'dod chos 'dra phul/ gza' tshes dge bar sku gdung rin po che dgyes mdzad rdo rje'i sgo nas zhugs la phul bas/ nam mkha'
dwangs shing 'ja' sprin sogs ltas ngo mtshar bar byung ba ni dam pa de nyid rje btsun kha'u pa'i bstan 'dzin bla na med par song gshis sum rtsen pa rnams kyis mchod pa phul
bar mngon/ yum bu bla mkhar dang / stag chen 'bum pa/ khra 'brug sogs mjal bar phyin/ lam du chos kyi rgyal po sa skya paNDi ta la chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa rin po che
'khrungs pa'i gtam snyan 'bul mi byung dus bzhugs pa'i gtam snyan bzhugs khrir grags pa'i steng du bsdad skabs shing thog ster sbyin byed mi mang tsam byung ba ni rten
'brel legs par sems shing / bzhugs khrir kha btags kyi cod pan shin tu che bar btsugs/ rten rnams zhib par mjal zhing snyan dar mchod pa gang rgyas kyang phul/ khra 'brug
tu rgyal ba rigs bzhi rdo la rang byon du byung ba gong po ri nas spyan drangs tshul zer ba dang / nye sras brgyad rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas 'od srung gi phyag nas ma li
yul nas gdan drangs pa/ jo mo sgrol ma sogs rten byin rlabs can du ma mjal/ mchog gi slob dpon chen po nga 'dra mar grags pa o rgyan dngos dang khyad par ma mchis pa rnams

zhib par mjal zhing / de dag la byin rlabs kyi gzi byin gzhan las che ba sems rgyud khul nus par 'dug cing / snyan dar mchod pa sogs dngos bshams yid sprul gyi mchod sprin
tshar du dngar ba phul/ rgyal bstan spyi dang bye brag gi ring lugs 'phel zhing phan bde 'byung ba'i smon lam yang dag byas/ mchod rten dbu lnga sogs la bskor ba byas shing
nyin 'khor byas/ chos sder zhag gnyis bsdad/ 'ong khar thams cad mkhyen pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyi sku phyag nas mas gtsos mchod 'bul gyi ster cha dpangs mtho bar stsal/
rim gyis bskyod pas tshes bcu dang sgon thang 'bum/ tsan thang lha khang sogs mjal/ slob dpon chen po padma ka ra'i sgrub gnas shel brag tu phyin/ yar lam mthil gyi
rten rnams zhib par mjal zhing mchod pa dang snyan dar phul/ smon lam yang dag btab/ brag phug gi nang du slob dpon chen po'i sku byin rlabs can phyag nas ma'i mdun du gu
ru dkon mchog spyi 'dus kyi tshogs mchod rgyas pa dang / snyan shal/ mchod sprin rgya che ba phul zhing / byin rlabs kyis lus sems bde la bag pheb pa zhig byung / rang
byon kyang mang bar 'dug /skas las babs dus brag gi logs shig la thugs rje chen po bcu gcig zhal gyi sku rang byon zhig gsar du mthong / de dag la bzhugs pa'i sgrub pa pho
mo rnams la 'tsho ba'i 'brel pa'ang rags rim phul/ sne gdong gi rtser 'byor dus bkra shis chos sde'i tshogs chen sku rim du yod pa rnams mjal dar bcas 'phrad par byon zhing
/ mang ja byin rten sogs gang legs phul/ zhol pa rnams kyi 'phrad mi dang bsngo zhus sogs mang bar byung / so so'i 'dod sbyar byas/

de nub grub pa'i dbang phyug thang stong rgyal po'i gdung brgyud sde pa sger pa'i sar 'byor bar bsu ba bzos sgo gzhan dang mi 'dra bar gnang zhing / gzhis len gzabs pa mdzad/
phar rta sogs dgu tshan dpangs mtho ba skyes su phul/ phyi nyin dpal ldan bla ma dam pa'i bzhugs gnas rtse gdong bsam gtan gling du phyin/ nged rang 'ong tshul gsan gshis
sne gdong nas sku tshab kyang byon 'dug pa bcas/ bla ma dam pa'i sku phyag nas ma na bza' sogs 'gangs che ba rnams dang / mgon khang du lcam dral gyi sku dang / pu tra'i
bla mtsho sogs rten khyad du 'phags pa du ma mjal/ snyan dar mchod pa/ chos skyong gi sku rnams la spyan gzigs rnams rgyas pa dang phrin bcol zhus/ phyir 'ong lam du
'bras bu gling gi dge 'dun rnams kyis gtsos 'phrad mi shin tu mang bar byung / bka' bsgo dang sngags mdud sogs gang 'tshams kyis 'dod pa bsgrubs/ nyin 'khor gyi sger pa'i
gzhis khar slebs/ grub thob chen po'i sku 'dra phyag nas ma sogs nang rten shin tu mang ba rnams zhib tu mjal zhing / dad rten kyang mang bar gnang / rten rnams la snyan
shal rgyas par phul/ zhal ngo tshor tshe dbang dang / gur mgon lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang tshar lugs thun mong ma yin pa zhig kyang phul/ phyi nyin 'ong khar dang ras snam
bu sogs kyi ster sbyin dpangs mthong bar gnang zhing / sngags mdud byin rten sogs kyang phul/ sde pa rin po che gru khar skyel mar pheb par sngags mdud phul zhing / gang
ci'i snyan 'bul rgyas par zhus/ chur thon rim gyis bskyod de bka' drin gzhal med khri srong rjes bzhengs pa gnang ba'i gnas chen dpal zab

yangs mi 'gyur lhun gyis grub pa'i gandho la chen por de nub 'byor zhing rtsal mang ba'i sar bsdad/ rab byung grwa tshang rnams kyis ja zhus kyang byung / phyi nyin snga bar
thog mar dbu rtser phyin te byang chub chen po dang / thams cad mkhyen pa zhi ba 'tsho'i dbu thod sogs 'og khang dang / bar khang / steng khang sogs kyi rten mchod rnams
zhib par mjal/ rim gyis gling bzhi/ gling phran/ yaksha ltag 'og /mchod rten lnga sogs zhib tu mjal/ jo mo gling gsum dang pho brang gong kyang mjal/ slob dpon chen po'i
zhabs rjes sogs gong gsal gtsug lag khang gi sku brnyan rags par snyan dar/ gser chab dngos bshams yid sprul gyi mchod pa nam mkha'i mtha' klas par phul zhing rgyal ba'i
bstan pa rin po che dar zhing rgyas pa dang / gong sa chen po yas phyin gyi dbus bstan 'dzin gyi skyes bu dam pa rnams zhabs pad yun ring du brtan cing / sems can rnams
la bde skyid 'bad med du 'byung ba sogs smon lam yid tshim par btab/ stag rtse'i sku tshab bzhugs mi sgrub grogs pas ja zhus kyang mdzad/ dkar po pa'i nang du phyin/ mchog
gi slob dpon chen pos lha sras mu khri btsan por sku tshab tu gnang ba'i gu ru mtsho skyes rdo rjer grags pa'i khyad mtshar byin can de mjal dus/ sku mdun du thog mar
gu ru dkon mchog spyi 'dus kyi tshogs mchod cig byas rjes/ yon chab cher 'bul ba sogs stsol bar ma ltos par zhal nged rang la gzigs te pheb pa sogs rjes su 'dzin pa'i brdar
sems/ mchod mjal rnams grub rjes mkhan chen bodhi sa twa'i bzhugs khri'i steng du 'khod de/ rab byung grwa tshang gi dge 'dun rnams gtsor gyur pa'i skya ser shin tu mang
bar/ 'byung 'dul gyi rjes gnang byas shing /

gnas tshang du 'byor 'phral dregs pa'i ded dpon chos rgyal dpon blon gyi sku khog so sor/ sang nyin sku pheb byed tshul gyi 'phros byed par mgron gnyer btang ba'i lan dang
/ lcog gi grwa kha shas kyis kyang dus min du song gshis ga 'dra 'ong zer kyang / nged rang brel ba'i stabs sang nyin snga bar lcog tu phyin zhing / nged rang nas dpal sa
skya pa chen po khams gsum chos kyi rgyal po'i gzims chung du bsdad/ tshogs 'khor rgyas pa dang bcas pa lcog pa rnams kyi spyan 'dren zhus par/ tshar gcig song 'tshams sku
ma pheb par ci drag zer ba lcog pa zhig byung bar da dung bskyar nas zhus na pheb 'ong tshul zhus/ yang bskyar byas par pheb song / gzhan ma bskyar zhus byas na pheb par
sku shin tu 'tshub par yong yod 'dug kyang / pheb 'phral nged rang gis phyin par/ zhi ba'i tshul gyi rdo skas mgor bsu bar byon zhing / btsan khar du 'byor 'phral chos
rgyal chen po dang / chos skyong chen po so sor snyan shal phul te/ gser zhal dang tshan grangs rgyas pa bcas rgyal bstan spyi dang bye brag la bsrung bskyab dang / 'phel
rgyas 'ong ba'i phrin bcol byas shing / gang ci'i spang blang gi lung bstan dang / snyigs ma'i dus 'dir yang yang khog zhugs byed par shin tu dka' yang / da lam dge bshes
yid ma ches dogs rib tsam 'ong ba zhig gsung ba sogs yid ches kyi bslab ston shin tu mang bar stsal/ dpon blon 'di gnyis 'jig rten gyi lha srung drag shul can yin zer
ba tsho dang mi 'dra ba'i zil shin tu che bar 'dug /grub 'phral mchims phur phyin par rta thog tu thon nas bzung / nam mkha' shin tu dwangs pa dang / 'ja' tshon sna lnga
rkyong ba/ yid la'ang o rgyan chen po mngon sum du

bzhugs yod snyam pa'i mos gus dung nge ba'i ngang nas gnas su slebs/ slob dpon chen pos sgrub pa bka' brgyad kyi dkyil 'khor zhal phye ste lha srin rnams dbang du bsdus skabs
dkyil 'khor yong rdzogs brag phug gi thod du rang byon du byung ba'i sgrub phug brag dmar ke'u tshang du nyid kyi phyag nas ma'i slob dpon chen po'i sku dang / bod 'bangs
bde thabs su rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen pa lnga pa chen po'i sku brnyan gsar du bzhugs su gsol ba sogs rten byin rlabs can rnams kyi mdun du bsdad/ 'ja' tshon snying
po'i gter ma'i las byang gi tshogs mchod rgyas par byas shing / phyi nang gsang ba de kho na nyid kyi mchod pas mchod cing / bla ma dang rang sems dbyer med kyi ngang du
yun ring du gnas pa sogs byin rlabs kyi ltas kyang byung / a ho thugs rjes nam yang mi 'dor ba'i/ /skyabs gsum kun 'dus slob dpon chen po yi/ /byin rlabs sku dang gnas
sogs mjal ba'i tshe/ /sems nyid 'od gsal ngang du re zhig 'byams/ /sgrub gnas der bzhugs pa'i rten dang rang byon shog ser sogs nang rten shin tu mang ba mjal/ rten so sor
snyan shal dang mchod pa rgyas par phul/ dpon slob me rag pas dkar spro dang / dar ras/ gzan sogs kyi ster sbyin dpangs mtho bar mdzad cing / der bzhugs sgrub pa pho mo
sogs kyis kyang ster cha byed mi mang bar byung / do nub bsam yas su 'byor/ rab byung grwa tshang gi grwa pa dang / yon bdag don gnyer ba kha shas la phyag na rdo rje dang
/ gur lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang thun mong ma yin pa sogs 'dod chos mang bar byas/ rab byung grwa tshang la mang ja spyi 'bul/ mkhan por tshan grangs rnam gzhag sogs kyis
mnyes par byas/ yon bdag so sor yang sngags mdud byin

rten sogs ster sbyin byas shing / tshur yang so sos dar ras dang snam bu sogs kyi ster cha rgyas par byung / ma nas lho kha phyogs 'dis lugs su dad zhen che ba dang / grwa
tshang rnams kyang grwa 'grig cing thugs dam sogs gzhan dang mi 'dra bar 'dug pas dag snang yang dag byung / nged rang yang gar phyin zhag sdod dang nyin rgyug sar dad mos
kyi mi thams cad khrom bzhin tu 'du ba zhig byung / ster cha sogs rgyas par byung zhing / phar yang gang la gang 'tshams kyis so so'i 'dod pa bsgrubs/ phyi nyin rab byung
grwa tshang gi skyel mi rnams dang 'phrad mi mang bar byung zhing / dal 'gros kyis sngar mgor 'byor/ rgod dkar brgyud chang tshul khang du gung tshigs byas/ grong mgor
bsdad/ phyi nyin chu rab brgyud bstan pa'i sbyin bdag dga' mo ba'i sar 'byor/ gzhis len gzabs rgyas byung / de nub zhal ngo rnams la tshe dbang sogs byas/ phyi nyin 'gro
ba'i mgon po chos rgyal 'phags pa'i dbu zhwa byin can zhig dang / nas/ gro/ sran sogs kyi ster sbyin rgyas par mdzad/ yon bdag 'di dad dad zer ba gzhan ma tsho dang mi 'dra
ba'i sbyin bdag gi mchog cig yin gshis rjes su gnas bshis de bzhin byung song skabs kyang shogs gong thon gyi phan cha gang drag do khul du byas/ phyi dro dgon lag shab
tu phyin te grwa rigs tshor mang ja/ bla mar bsngo rten dang / gzhan yang yon bdag sogs tshang mar gang 'tshams kyi ster cha dang / byang bsngo zhu mi mang thag byung
/ lam du dga' mo nang so sku mched 'phrad sar pheb par sngags mdud sogs phul/ ting gsar du nA lendra nas nged rang gi gnyer pa rogs bcas bsu bar byung / lhang rtser du rgyan
drung gis gtsos rgyun gyi dbang po'i rta bsu

ba mang ba dang bcas pheb cing / rim gyis dgon gnas su 'byor ba'i tshe 'dus tshogs kyis ser phreng / bla brang grwa khang so so nas dar 'phyar sogs rgyas par mdzad/ 'byor 'phral
ser ja dang / bla khag las tshan bcas par ster cha'ang skyes ma'i tshul du phul/ zhag shas ngal bsos shing / de nas lam 'bras kyi 'phros rgyud gsum btsugs te khrid
lung sogs rgyas par grub cing / gzhan yang dbang lung mang tsam gyi 'dod chos kyang kha shas byas/ 'di skabs nged rang gis gzhis kyi dbon chung ba 'od mchog sprul sku'i sku
skye yin 'dug pas ngos 'dzin byed 'jug dgos zer bar khong rang gi rdor slob skyid sdings nas dang / 'di kha'i yon bdag nyi ma dbon po bcas dge slong rin po che dang /
drung yig lags kyi phyag bris bcas 'byor bar/ nged rang la khong sku mched gnyis las med gshis brgyud 'dzin byed mir song bas sems la ma babs kyang / bla ma'i sku skye yin
nges na gang ci nas mi btub snyam gzhis su ngos 'dzin la btang bar/ gsal ba rang gi ngos 'dzin sogs ma byung 'dug cing / lhag tu rgyan drung dang dpon sa bcas ngos kyis
byon te de bzhin byas na mi 'ong tshul dang / mdzod sar tsha drag gi 'phros pa bcas dge slong rin po cher zhu bar rdzong bda' mdzad song zhing / nged rang gi 'di rigs lhus
thengs dgos pas tshas na mi 'ong tshul labs kyang / tsha rdog brdung bar bod 'brog gi dpe ltar pha gir zhu nan gyis sku skye gtan nas min tshul zhus 'dug par/ chos ster
gling mkhan po grwa slob bcas par bslab ston la gang zhus ltar bka' drin bskyangs pas sku skye min 'dug tshul dang gzhan du btsal ba 'gab tshul bcas phyir slog gnang 'dug
kyang / de nas bzung shin tu bsun pa byung song zhing /

kho rang tshos kyang gzhan nas ma rnyed gshis lo phyi mar yang bskyar byung bar nged rang ngos kyis gzhis su phyin te ngos 'dzin byed bcug par shin tu gsal bar byung song zhing
/ lhag tu pho brang chen por gsung brtag zhu bar 'od mchog sprul sku'i sku skye de khar yod 'dug par zhes bslab ston pheb par khong rang tshang la'ang de rtsis kyi 'phros
pa dang / nged rang la gdung byung na dang ma byung tshe sngags 'chang byed par thag bcad do/ /'di rigs thams cad mkhyen pa sa skya paNDi tas/ chu mig rang nyid ma
bskams na/ /sa yi mnan pas ga la khebs/ /zhes gsungs pa'i don la song zhing / rjes su gza' tshes dge bar mkhan gdan sa ba dang bcas sprul sku rin po cher legs 'bul dang /
nged rang la'ang 'bul ba bcas byung bar legs lam gang che byas/ pho brang du gong sa chen po yas phyin gyi mjal khar skabs drung dbon bcas phyin/ so so nas mjal rten dpangs
mtho bar phul/ mjal kha rgyas shing grwa tshang gi zhabs brtan 'bul ba gnang ba dang 'grigs/ gzims chung 'gag tu mjal rten rnams phul skabs/ gsol dpon sngags rams pa
brgyud bka' 'dri zhib tu stsal/ dbon la chos thams cad bum pa gang byor byed dgos shing / phyag len rnams kyang ji bzhin rgyun ma nyams par dgos tshul bslab don rin po che
pheb/ dge slong lags dang / dge slong ngag dbang dkon mchog lags dang / em chi lags sogs zhabs phyi drag gras rnams dang mjal zhing / so sor 'bul ba rgyas par phul/ gnang
sbyin kyang stsal/ dge slong rin po che'i thugs bzhed kyi chos kha shas phul/ karma shag gi gnas gsar gyi gdung sku bgres pa sku chos grub ma song gshis thugs

gnyer sogs kyi stabs mgyogs myur gnang dgos pa'i bslab ston rin po che gnang dgos tshul gyis snyan 'jags zhu nan che bar byas/ nged rang gi gzhis kyi khang par ming zhig gnang
dgos tshul gong du snyan 'bul zhus par bsam grub bde chen du stsal/ lha sar sdod ring lcags zams zhabs drung rin po che/ rnam gling paN chen/ shel dkar khri zur pa sogs
la bde mchog bong zhal can gyi dbang phul/ lcags zam zhabs drung rin po cher khrid brgya'i lung zhus/ bkra shis chos sde'i dbon rin po cher phyag rdor 'gro bzang gi rjes
gnang phul zhing / sku chos 'phral gnang ngos thugs gnyer sogs gnang dgos tshul zhib rgyas zhus pas thugs la babs pa byung song / pho brang chen po dang / ra sa 'phrul
snang / ra mo che sogs kyi rten rnams zhib par mjal zhing / snyan shal dang mchod pa rgyas pa phul/ zhag shas nas thon phyag zhus par hub ja 'khor drug phyed gnyis sogs
gnang sbyin dpangs mtho bar stsal zhing rang gnas su 'byor/ dbon sogs don gnyer ba kha shas la 'khor lo bde mchog nag po pa'i dbang zhig byas/ gzhis su phyin/ zhag gsum bsdad
skabs nyan po nas grub pa'i dbang phyug chos rje rin po che gdan drangs te dpal ldan lha mo dud pa'i sol ba can gyi nang dang gsang ba'i rjes gnang rngog ston gnyis
kyis mdzad pa'i yig cha'i thog nas zhus/ dpal ldan bla ma 'di nyid la lha mos mnal lam gyi tshul du gnang ba'i yang gsang gtso rkyang gi rjes gnang sogs zhus zhing / bla
ma 'di dud sol lha mo bran du 'khol zhing / rdzogs pa chen po sogs kyi nyams rtogs mthar phyin pa nges par grub pa'i dbang phyug kho nar nges shes snying nas skyes/ phar
yang bde mchog

nag po pa'i dbang zhig phul/ dgon khag sogs la phyogs pheb dbon gyis mdzad/ chos sde chen po'i dus chen rnams grub nas sa skyar 'gro dgos pa'i stabs grwa rigs yon bdag rnams
kyis 'phrad mi shin tu mang bas khor yug tu gyur cing zla ba bcu gnyis pa'i nang du gdan sa chen po dpal ldan sa skya nas gong ma chos kyi rgyal pos nged rang la chos gsan
bzhed kyis gong sa chen po yas phyin la snyan 'bul zhu ba gnang 'dug par 'gro dgos pa'i bka' shog rin po che dang / gdan sa'i bka' shog bcas spyi bor pheb 'phral pho
brang chen por mjal khar phyin/ gzims chung bde ba can gyi 'gag tu dge slong rin po cher brgyud phyag mjal rnams phul skabs/ de khar sa skya nas chos gsan bzhed 'dug pa rnams
gang rgyas phul ba 'gab cing / de kha'i dbon kyang khrid nas thob rgya che zhing bstan rgyun la phan pa 'ong / grub 'phral chu'i stobs 'gor gzhi che bar ma byed sogs
gang ci'i bslab ston zhib par bka' drin bskyangs/ sa dbang chen po'i mjal kha/ gnang sbyin/ zur chas/ pho brang nas sa skya bar gyi gzan shing / 'phrang sgrol sogs la bka'
shog rin po che bka' drin brtse bas bskyangs/ chos sder 'byor nas bla khag las tshan gzhis su bzhugs mi rnams dang bcas par gang ci'i bkod pa dang / mgon khang so sor
bskang gso/ snyan shal/ phrin bcol/ chos skyong dpon blon la snyan shal/ tshogs 'khor sogs rgyas par phul zhing phrin bcol byas/ lung bstan legs par byung / sku yal khar
'phreng nyams shin tu che bas yal zhing / yang phab ste gdan sar yun ring ma sdod gsung nan che bar mdzad/ lcags lug lor lo gsar grub nas tshes gsum gyi nyin nged khu dbon
dpon slob bzhi bcu skor gnas kyi

dbang po nas bskyod skabs bla khag las tshan bcas kyis gzhis par thab skyel mdzad de skyel mar byon/ gzhis kyi zhal ngo rnams la tshe dbang dang / 'byung 'dul gyi rjes gnang
byas/ phyi nyin rta kha bsgyur bar pa chab nas bzung 'phrad mi mang zhing / lha khang rgyal smad du shog zer/ phyin/ ston mo dang rdzong pa'i ster cha rgyas par byung /
rgyal stod pa dang sde pa lha khang ba rnams kyi ja zhus dang ster cha bcas 'phrad mi mang bar byung / rgyal stod smad du mang ja/ bsngo rten sogs phul/ de nub ko thang
du bsdad/ byang bu/ bsngo zhus sogs byed mi mang bar so so'i 'dod pa bsgrubs/ phyi nyin la dmar la phyin/ nyi ma gdugs 'jam zhing kha reg gi rtser 'ja' 'od 'khyil ba zhig
'dug par/ der o rgyan gtso 'khor dpa' bo mkha' 'gro sogs kyis bskor nas bzhugs yod snyam pa'i mos gus dung pa byung / stod lung nas gzhis gnyer sogs 'phrad mi mang ba rim
gyis byung zhing / bde can yangs pa can du slebs/ spyi sos grwa khang bde ba zhig tu bskyal/ mkhan po dang spyi gnyer 'phrad par byon zhing / ster cha zur gsos rgyas par
byung / mang ja/ bsngo rten/ spyi 'bul sogs gang legs phul/ mchod mjal du phyin/ zhwa dmar dkon mchog yan lag gis dngul gdung gi gtsos steng shod kyi mchod mjal zhib tu
zhus/ byang chub sems dpa' chos 'phags kyi tshems/ mar pa'i dbang bum/ 'phags pa rin po che'i dbu zhwa nyin mo bde legs sogs mjal/ rten rnams la mchod pa/ snyan shal/ dngos
bshams yid sprul gyi mchod sprin spros/ phan bde 'byung ba'i smon lam yid tshim par btab/ zhwa dmar bdun pa sku mtshams su bzhugs 'dug par mjal ma thub kyang gnang sbyin
dang zur gsos rgyas par stsal/ de nas

srin sna brgyud gzhu nang du slebs/ tshang mas su yin ma shes kyang dad mos kyi rnam pas 'dus te ster cha byed mi mang bar byung / rim gyi snye mo gzhis khar slebs/ ru ba'i
grwa rigs kha yar byung bar mang ja bskur zhing bdag rkyen sprad/ rong chung brgyud chos grwa chen po 'bras yul skyed tshal du 'byor dus nged khu dbon la dge 'dun rnams
kyis tshogs dung mkhas pa 'du ba'i dkar po rgyang grags spor zhing / mchod rdzas du ma thog ste ser phreng gis bsu ba dang / bla brang grwa khang so so'i thog nas bsang /
dar 'phyar mdzad/ rdo gcal nas mkhan rin po ches dbus tshogs dmangs kyis mjal dar gnang / bla brang du gzims chung ngo mtshar snang bar bsdad/ sleb 'phral mang ja zhus shing
/ phyi nyin mang ja sbyor sbrel thog /mkhan rin po cher bsngo rten dpangs mtho ba dang / tshogs su spyi 'bul zhus/ nged rang gi kun mkhyen chen po'i bzhugs khri'i steng
du phyin/ mkhan po dang / bla ma zur pa gsum/ grwa dmangs bcas la 'jam dbyangs dang / byams pa'i rjes gnang phul/ ster cha gya nom pa bstar/ khams pa grwa tshang du bos/
gzhis len dang ster cha rgyas par byung / sger du grwa ja dang tshan grangs phul/ mkhan zur pa kun dga' nor bu'i sar 'bod mi byung bar phyin/ gzhis len dang / khro phu
thog thub mar grags pa'i sangs rgyas kyi sku gnyis dang / gzan gyis gtsos gnang sbyin rgyas par mdzad/ de dgong bla brang nas grwa pa kha shas la rab byung dang / mkhan
po dang / kho spe zur pas gtsos kha shas la dpal ldan ma hA kA la gur gyi mgon po'i rjes gnang phul/ de nyid chos gter gling nas gnyer pa bsu bar 'byor/ phyi nyin drag gras
kyis skyel ma mdzad cing / shar gru thon/ chos

gter gling nas thab bsu dang gung tshigs rgyas par byung / mkhan gdan sa ba sogs grwa rigs kyis chibs bsu dang / grwa tshang gis ser phreng mchod gar sogs bsu ba rgyas shing
/ bla brang grwa khang so so'i thog nas bsang / dar 'phyar/ dung / rgya gling sogs rgyas par mdzad cing / gzims chung 'chi med pho brang du bsdad/ nyi ma gdugs 'jam zhing
'ja' 'od kyis nam mkha' khyab pa zhig byung / zhag gsum bsdad/ gzhis len ster cha rgyas par mdzad/ skyed stod kyi sras shig thugs bzhed ltar skra phud blangs/ nged rang
nas kyang mang ja sbyor sbrel thog /mkhan por rta legs pa sogs bsngo rten dpangs mtho ba dang / grwa tshang la ja 'gyed dang spyi 'bul gang rgyas phul/ sde pa wa sras pa
dang skyil stod pa sogs 'phrad mi mang bar byung / bro gzhas sogs rtsed sna mang ba dang / gzhan yang 'phrad mi mang bar gang la gang 'tshams kyi ster cha byas/ 'tshams
pa sgom chen 'ga'i bug sgo'i gdong du phyin/ bslab bya dang byin rten sogs kyi ster cha byas/ sprul sku gong ma zhing du pheb nas rgyang tsam song 'dug gshis de tsam 'ong
bar dka' na'ang / mkhan gdan sa ba sogs las tshan rnams dang tshang mas theg pa khur blangs mdzad yod 'dug gshis/ sgrig lam kun spyod/ thugs dam/ dgon pa'i 'dzin spras
sogs gang sar gra 'grigs par 'dug cing / lhag tu sprul sku gong ma'i dngul gdung dang / phur pa rigs lnga sogs rten bzhengs kyang mang par mdzad 'dug /de dag la nged rang
gis rab gnas kyi me tog 'thor zhing steng 'og gi rten rnams mjal/ snyan dar sogs gang rgyas phul/ thon khar sil snyan dang dngos po'i tshan grangs shin tu mang ba/ grwa
pa rnams kyis kyang so so nas
