ster cha gzabs rgyas mdzad/ btsun pa gsar du byed mi rnams la so so'i 'dod sbyar byas/ mkhan rin po ches dbus rags bsdus kyis skyel mar byon/ de khul yon bdag chos gzhis rnams
kyis mjal dar dang / rtsed sna sogs ci shes byed 'dug cing / gang 'tshams kyi ster cha byas/ mdzod pa dpon g.yog mar lam rtse gdong la zhal mjal zhu bar 'ong tshul gyi
snyan 'bul zhu bar rdzong bda' byas/ rim gyis thar pa'i chos gzhis dge 'phel du gnyer pa sogs bsu bar byung / chos sder 'byor skabs bla brang sogs nas dar 'phyar dang dung
'bud/ bsang / dge 'dun rnams kyis mchod pa'i bye brag sna tshogs thogs te mchod gar dang / ser phreng gis bsu ba rgyas par mdzad/ 'di skabs rgyal po'i cho 'phrul gyi
ban gzugs bse theb byon pa zhig byung ba'i tshe/ lha mo sngon mo ral gri thogs pa zhig gis ded pa'i snang ba zhig kyang byung / mjal dar gnang / bla brang du phyin/ 'byor
'phral mang ja zhus/ sku zhang rin po che bsu bar pheb cing / dpa' rnams dkyil stod pa sogs byon/ bzhes spro dang ster sbyin dpangs mtho bar byung / nged rang nas kyang
nye regs su song gshis de lugs kyi skyes ma byin/ phyi nyin mang ja sbyor sbrer thog mkhan por bsngo rten gzabs pa/ tshogs su mang ja dang / ja 'gyed dang / spyi 'bul sogs
rgyas par phul/ gzhis len dang ster cha rgyas par byung / las tshan grwa rigs so so nas kyang dngos po'i tshan grangs dang / nye skor chos gzhis rnams kyis ster cha bcas
'phrad par byung / so sor gang 'tshams kyi 'dod pa'ang bsgrubs/ phyi nyin grwa tshang gi phur pa'i 'chams sogs rgyas

par mdzad cing / deng sang dge lugs su song gshis gang ci nas grwa 'grigs pa 'ong pa ni gzhir bcas shing / chos sde 'di snga sor dpyal gyi dgon par song gshis rten mchod byin
che ba mang zhing / nang rten paN chen shAkya shrI'i lhung bzed/ mdo le/ dung rang skad ma/ nA ro'i sku rgyan sogs gzhan dang mi 'dra bar 'dug pa rnams mjal kha zhus/
snyan dar dang mchod pa rgyas par phul zhing / phan bde'i smon lam dpyis phyin par btab/ mkhan rin po ches dbus dge 'dun rnams la tshe dbang dang rjes gnang kyang phul/ ma
hA kA la stag zhon gyi rten khyad du 'phags par mjal/ snyan dar phul zhing phrin las bcol/ 'byor nub shin tu 'tshubs pa zhig byung kyang rim gyis 'tshubs zhi nas/ rmi lam
du 'khri mthon por sdod pa dang / dar 'phyar ba dang / dung 'bud pa sogs byung ba ni phrin las rgyas pa'i brdar go /drag gras kha shas kyis skyel mar byon/ gam la zer
ba'i la zhig 'dug pa brgyud phyin skabs rlung 'tshubs sa g.yo ba lta bu'i shin tu che zhing 'jigs zhum me pa dang bcas byung ba ni/ dpal ldan lha mo bsu bar pheb par sems/
sku zhang rin po che dang / mkhan bde bar gshegs pa'i phyag mdzod bcas kyang bsu bar pheb/ zhwa lu'i chos 'khor shar chen du slebs/ gzhis len rgyas par byung zhing skyes
ma gzabs par phul/ tshogs su mang ja bsngo rten/ bla khag so sor tshan grangs re/ spyi 'bul rnam gzhag rnams phul/ bla khag rnams dang / khang mo che la sogs kyis gtsos
'phrad mi shin tu mang zhing / ster cha gzabs par byung / phyi nyin rang byon thugs rje chen po zung dang / yum chen mo sogs gtsug lag khang gi rten khyad par can rnams
dang / mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang chen po de

nyid kyi dngul gdung mjal bar/ ma nas dam pa de nyid kyi thugs rje nam mkha' mdzod la mnga' brnyes pa'i phyag rdzas thog /gzhung sa chen po nas kyang zhal 'debs dpangs mtho
ba bka' drin bskyangs song gshis gzhan dang mi 'dra ba yod bsams kyang / blo kha khengs pa rang ma byung / dngul gdung rin po ches gtsos rten rnams la snyan dar/ spos/ mar
me sogs mchod pa rgyas par phul/ phan bde'i don du smon lam btab/ mgon khang mjal bar las gshin yab yum gyi zhal 'bag de nyin cung zad shig 'dug /snyan dar phul zhing
phrin bcol byas/ ri phug gi gnas mjal du phyin/ sku zhang gi zhal ngo rnams bsu bar pheb/ bla brang shar chen du gzhis len rgyas par mdzad/ drung chen gyis bzhengs pa'i mkhyen
rab chos kyi rgyal po'i sku phyag nas mas gtsos gnang sbyin byung / nged rang nas ja/ gos dar sogs kyis skyes kyang phul/ grwa tshang du mang ja bsngo rten rgyas par
phul zhing / dkar po grwa tshang la sger du ja/ gnas brtan bcu drug gi sku thang che ba/ mkhar rnga sogs spyi gzhag byas/ gtsug lag khang gi thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston
rin po che'i gzims mal sku 'dras gtsos mkhan brgyud tshang mar snyan shal dang mchod pa rgyas par phul zhing / smon lam kyang rgyas par btab/ de nyin lha khang du tshul
khrims kyi dri bsung 'phro ba dang / nyi ma gdugs 'jam zhing 'ja' 'od kyis khengs pa sogs byin gyis brlabs pa'i rtags byung / chos khrir thams cad mkhyen pa'i sku tshab kyi
sku bzhugs pa dang / thugs dam sku 'bum chen mo sogs mjal kha zhib tu zhus/ phyi dro dam can rgya mtsho sprin bzhin

du 'du ba'i gnas rgyan gong du thams cad mkhyen pa sa skya paNDi tas dbu skra bsil ba'i rdo gzhong dang rten rnams mjal/ 'dod khams gtso mo'i pho brang du phyin par zhal ras
la mkhan pos phyag dam zhig gnang srol yod 'dug kyang / de nyin zhal ras rang gsal du 'dug pa mjal ba'i tshe sku zhi khro dre'u'i rgyab tu bzhengs nas 'dug par smon lam
btab ste bltas pas/ sku brnyan gyi rgyab tu sku mdog sngo nag shin tu khro ba zhig mthong / 'dod khams gtso mo'i gnas su phyin pa'i tshe/ /sku mdog phyag mtshan yang yang
'gyur ba dang / /khyad par dpal ldan lha mo nyid kyi sku/ /mthing nag drag shul ldan pa'i sku brnyan gyis/ /rgyab tu gsal bar bzhugs pa mngon sum mthong / /phrin las bsgrub
phyir bstan la spyan gzigs dang / /mchod gtor rgyas par phul te bstan dar zhing / /dgra bgegs sgrol ba'i phrin bcol bka' bsgo byas/ /las bzhi'i snyan dar g.yas g.yon
du nyin bde ma re/ dkar yol/ khrab rmog /gri sogs kyi spyan gzigs dang / mchod gtor/ bskang ba rgyas par byas pa'i tshe/ snga sor zhwa lu pa rnams kyi mkha' 'gro ma yin
zer ba'i khog ba zhig 'dug par rang pheb bsu byung nas/ lha mo rang gi skye brgyud mang tsam zer zhing snga sor phrin las 'di dang 'di bsgrubs tshul gyi kham spo dang / phyis
nas bsam don 'grub pa dang bstan pa rgyas pa'i lung bstan dang / phrin las bsgrub tshul gnang / sangs 'phral chu srin ma yin zer ba zhig kyang pheb/ nga dmar 'dab phur
pa'i lha yin/ yid mi ches mi dgos/ snga sor lus dang grib ma bzhin 'grogs nas phrin las kyang byas/ da dung sngar bzhin bstan pa nyi ma shar ba ltar byed/ gtor ma re zur
du ster dgos/ gsung pas phyis su srid zhi kun khyab ma'i mjug tu shlo ka gcig gi phrin bcol brtsams/ phyag mdzod sogs kyi tshong dus 'gur mo'i

bar bskyel zhing / de nub zhag sa byas/ g.yu thog pa'i sku 'bum bzhengs par rab gnas mdzad nyin/ a ru ra rnam rgyal gyi char babs pa'i sa ngo mtshar can de rgyang mjal dang
/ yid sprul gyi mchod pa dang bcas smon lam btab/ de nas rdo ring brgyud chu mig tu slebs/ mchod khang dang chos brtsigs rnams gog nyams shin tu che bar 'dug kyang / byin
rlabs kyis snang ba bsgyur thub pa zhig 'dug pas snyan shal/ mar me/ spos/ zhal zas sogs kyi mchod pa rgyas pa dang / yid kyis mchod sprin kun tu bzang po'i rnam thar bzhin
spros te 'di phyi dang phan bde'i don du smon lam btab/ stobs 'phrog dbang po'i pho brang dar lung gnyan du phyin/ gnyan lo chen po'i thugs dam rten rdo nag gi zhal
bzhi yongs rdzogs kyi sku mdun du mchod gtor dang bskang ba rgyas par byas shing / snyan shal dang mtshon cha'i spyan gzigs phul/ bstan dgra tshar gcod pa'i phrin bcol rgyas
par byas/ rang byon pas ja zhus dang ster cha byung bar/ nged rang nas len du tshan grangs phul/ dgon pa rgyal du slebs/ las chen dpon gyi gzims khang du bsdad cing gzhis
len rgyas par byung / dgon par mang ja dang bsngo rten gzabs par phul/ phyi nyin zho ma la brgyud phyin pa'i lam du nged rang gi rta'i rmig 'og nas chu rdol shin tu
che bar byung bas/ phran bus chos phul bar bstan rgyun la phan pa zhig 'ong snyam par shar/ zhabs phyi drag pa lnga dang nged rang gi lcam gyi zhabs phyi gcig bcas chibs
bsur gnang ba dang 'phrad/ 'jam dbyangs rim byon gyi gnas gdan sa chen po dpal ldan sa skyar 'byor/ g.ya' skor du gnyer dpon lags dang gzims dpon lags sogs sku 'khor drag
gras rnams kyis mjal dar bcas bsu bar pheb/ phyag mdzod 'gag tu phyag mdzod kyang

mjal dar bcas pheb par so so'i go babs dang bstun pa'i bzos sgo zhus/ zhabs drung khams gsum chos kyi rgyal po'i gzims chung du 'jog par gnang / 'byor 'phral nged rang gi lcam
pheb bar gdan sa'i bdag mor song gshis khri las babs te ldang ba sogs sku bzos che bar phul zhing / gzhi byes kyi gnas tshul 'phel par byung / gong bzhugs sku zhabs nas
gzims dpon gnang nas/ sang gza' tshes stabs mjal kha gnang rtsis yin tshul pheb/ sang nyin gos khyad 'phags kyi gnam rgyan/ 'khar rnga legs pa/ sil snyan/ ja/ ja rta sogs
dngos po dpangs mtho ba bcas nged khu dbon so so dang / zla'u rnams kyis kyang gos dar/ rta sogs rgyas pa'i 'bul ba dang bcas dbang khang du mjal kha zhus par/ gong ma'i
sku zhabs nas kyang mjal dar gnang ba sogs dbu bla gzhan ma las bzos sgo che bar bka' drin bskyangs shing / stan mtho ba'i thog tu bka' nan ltar bsdad/ lugs gnyis kyi
bka' 'phros shin tu rgyas par byung / sku tshe'i rten 'brel du tshe dpag dkar po'i rjes gnang zhig thog mar phul/ nged rang gi lcam la'ang rta/ ja/ mdzo mo/ /na bza' sogs
skyes ma gya nom par phul zhing / lcam sku bgres par rta sogs dgu tshan phul/ phyag mdzod/ gnyer dpon/ gzims dpon rnams la rta res gtsos pa'i dgu tshan re dang / zhabs
phyi gzhan ma rnams la'ang gang 'tshams kyi skyes ma byin/ phyi nyin nas bzung snga dro nyin bstar gsol ja bzhi re'i ring lung phul bar/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang gi bka'
'bum pod bzhi ma/ dkon mchog spyi 'dus/ gur drag /rnam sras zhi drag /dud sol lha mo sogs kyi pusti rnams dang / dkyil chog rjes gnang sogs kyi lung shin tu mang bar phul/
phyi dro rnam sras rigs chen brgyad dang / drag po thang lha/ tshe ring mched lnga sogs

zur bka'i rigs shin tu mang bar/ dus kyi 'khor lo/ bde mchog bong zhal can/ thig le bcu drug /sangs rgyas thod pa rnams kyi dbang rnams phul/ tshur yang sems dpa' chen po'i
bka' 'bum/ dgon gsar ba bsod nams chos 'phel gyi rnam thar/ gtso chen chos sna dmar po skor gsum/ mgon pod gyi ljang / byang gter thugs sgrub rnam gsum sogs kyi ljags lung
dang / stod las byang chub sgrub pa/ smad las drag po sgrol dbang / rje btsun nA ro mkha' spyod ma/ dpyal lugs phag mo skor gsum sogs dbang / byin rlabs/ 'jam dbyangs
nag po/ gur mgon lha brgyad sogs kyi rjes gnang shin tu mang bar zhus/ skabs shig gzims chung steng du bka' chos zhu dus/ sngags 'chang bla ma nyid 'jam dbyangs dmar ser
pod ral bsnams pa zhig tu mthong zhing / nam mkha' la 'jam 'od kyi drwa ba drwa phyed dang / me tog gi char babs pa sogs byung ba'i tshe/ sems dga' bde bsam gyis mi khyab
par byung zhing / bla ma 'di sangs rgyas thams cad 'dus pa'i ngo bo dngos yin snyam nges pa gting nas rnyed pa byung / 'byor nas zhag shas song skabs chos sde phan tshun
du mang ja bsngo rten sogs gzabs par phul/ rim gyis mchod mjal bar gseng rnams su byas par sgo rum mjal dus/ bse 'bag sku gzi brjid dang / bong yang che ba/ mthing nag cig
tu mthong ba bstan pa rgyas pa'i brdar go /skabs shig bse 'bag 'jal du phyin par gong ma gsung bskang la pheb 'dug pa dang 'grigs pas sku mdun du bka' bsgo zhus pas rgyas
par stsal/ bar chad kyi g.yul las rgyal song snyam pa'i gdeng yang rnyed/ rgyal ba kun dngos dpal ldan bla ma yi/ /rgyal ba'i bstan srung mchog der bka' bsgos tshe/ /rgyal
bas rjes bzung sngags 'chang bdag nyid la/ /rgyal kun srung ma'i

tshogs kyis bar chad bsrungs/ /dkar shAkya grags kyis bzhengs pa'i rje btsun chen po'i sku 'dra rin po che mjal ba'i tshe lus sems bde ba chen po'i ngang du yun ring du gnas
pa sogs/ byin gyis brlabs pa'i ltas kyang byung / thams cad mkhyen pa sa skya paNDi ta'i phyag bzo gnang ba'i 'jam dbyangs gzi 'od 'bar ba mjal ba'i tshe phyag mtshan la
lces reg pa'i tshe thugs ka nas 'od zer 'phros/ snying gar thim pa'i snang ba gsal bar byung / dbu rtse rnying ma mngon dga' bde chen/ bde mchog bde chen gling gi tshogs
khang / 'bum thang / g.yu thog /'khon dkon mchog rgyal po'i sku 'bum/ sa chen phug /phag mo sgrub khang / nyi lde rdzong chung / rin chen sgang / grang mo che/ bla brang
shar sogs kyi mchod khang / mgon khang nub/ pu tra'i bla mtsho sogs mgon khang rnams dang / mgon khang chen mo/ /rig 'dzin pho brang / rgya gar/ rgya nag /gser khang /
gnas bcu lha khang / dbang khang / mtshams dmar/ khyad 'phags lha khang / khyad 'phags mgon khang / jag 'dul mgon khang sogs/ mdor na dpal ldan sa skya nyid du bzhugs pa'i
rten byin rnams lan gcig dang / 'gangs che ba rnams yang yang mjal/ lha khang rnams la snyan dar/ spos/ mar me/ zhal zas sogs dngos bshams yid sprul gyi mchod pas mchod
cing / mgon khang rnams la spyan gzigs kyang rgyas par phul te/ rgyal bstan spyi dang / bye brag dpal ldan sa skya pa'i gdung sras myur du phebs shing bstan pa rgyas pa
dang / gong sa sku zhabs rin po che yas phyin dang / sngags 'chang bla ma nyid sogs bstan 'dzin gyi skyes bu dam pa rnams zhabs pad yun ring du brtan cing / 'gro ba rnams
la bde skyid 'byung ba'i smon lam phrin bcol yid tshim par btab/ gnyer dpon las thog pas bzhengs pa'i lha khang zhig tu shis brjod kyi me tog gtor/ mchod khang 'di bzo bkod
phun sum tshogs shing

'gangs che ba zhig 'dug cing phyis su gdan sar phul 'dug pas/ phar gang 'thob byed mkhan tsho dang mi 'dra ba'i zhabs phyir 'gyur bar sems/ gong sku zhabs sku cung zhig ltem
pa'i tshul byung bar/ tshe dbang brgya rtsa sogs sku rim bar chad zhi ba'i thabs dang rten 'brel sogs zhus shing / de'i ring chos dbar byas/ nged rang gi lcam la sor 'brang
/ tshe ring mched lnga/ thang lha'i zur bka' sogs rjes gnang mang bar phul/ mkhan chen bzang po rgyal mtshan la ku ru kulle tshar lugs thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang
zhus/ dbon la kun mkhyen sngags 'bum gyi lung gnang dgos tshul zhus shing bka' drin bskyangs par pusti phyed gsum tsam song 'dug /gong sku zhabs sku dwangs nas bsam gling
du 'phyar chen gyis mnga' gsol gnang bar pheb pa'i zhabs phyir bslab ston ltar phyin zhing / rta rgyug pa tshor mgyogs dar sogs kyi ster cha byas/ mgon khang du spyan
gzigs snyan dar phul zhing phrin bcol dang nyin skor byas/ bka' chos tshur gnang ba rnams gzhan dang mi 'dra zhing / khyad par drag po sgrol dbang gnang dus/ sku 'chams
sogs gzhan gyi 'chams mkhas zer ba sogs dang mi 'dra ba'i sku gzi brjid shin tu che ba/ nyi ma bye ba'i 'od kyang zil gyis gnon nus pa lta bu/ gsung dbyangs yan lag drug
cu dang ldan pa'i sgo nas shin tu rgyas par stsal/ nged rang la nad ros cung zad 'tshe bar nged rang gi lcam nas rten 'byung rim gro sogs rgyas par mdzad/ gong sku zhabs
nas tshe dbang lcags sdong ma brgya rtsa/ sme brtsegs kyi byab khrus/ gur mgon lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang rnams stsal zhing / 'tsho byed lcam 'di nged rang gi nad ror las
'brel lta bu'i snga sor nas 'phrod ngo shin tu che ba zhig 'ong gin yod gshis da lam yang 'phrod bsten gyis rim bder song / gnas lnga mthar phyin

thub bstan mkhan chen nas thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyi bka' 'bum dang / grub pa'i dbang phyug rje drung rin po che nas lam sbas bshad kyi khrid gong nas gsan
pa'i zhor la zhus/ lha khang chen mo'i rten rnams dang / sgrol ma sems dpa' sum brtsegs kyang zhib par mjal/ 'di phyi'i don du smon lam yang dag btab/ bstan srung rgya
mtsho'i bzhugs gnas kha'u brag rdzong mjal bar phyin/ spyan gzigs dang snyan dar phul/ bskang ba rgyas par byas skabs sgra chen po zhig dang lhan du/ dpal mgon nyid bram
gzugs sku mdog mthing nag ral pa'i thor gtsug can/ rgyan phyag mtshan sogs zhal bzhi yongs rdzogs ltar/ drag shul mi bzad pa dang ldan pa zhig zhal mngon sum du bstan pa'i
tshe/ sems thog mar 'jigs zhum pa dang / de nas bde ba dang ldan pa zhig byung / grub dbang du mas byin rlabs kha'ur slebs/ /bdud dpung tshar gcod bstan srung dbang po
yi/ /sku nyid mngon sum mthong zhing byin brlabs tshe/ /rgyal bstan srung ba'i bka' bsgo phrin bcol byas/ /gzhan yang gnas der bzhugs pa'i rten rnams zhib par mjal/ snyan
shal/ spos/ mar me/ zhal zas sogs rgyas par phul zhing / smon lam yang dag btab/ nyin skor gyis phyir 'byor/ sngags 'chang bla ma nyid zhabs pad yun ring du brtan pa'i phyir
nged rang dpon slob rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das tshe sbyin yid bzhin 'khor lo'i cho ga dang 'brel ba'i 'chi bslu dang zhabs brtan rgyas pa zhig phul zhing / ya gir sdod
ring phog /zur chas/ nyin kha shas re nas ston mo shin tu rgyas pa sogs lugs gnyis ka nas thugs nang gtsang zhing / gang ci thams cad du gzhan dang mi 'dra bar

bka' drin bskyangs/ chu de gzugs bzhir shin tu gnod par 'dug kyang / chos bdag por phul grub pas sems kha rdzogs pa zhig byung zhing / na so'i stabs yang yang slebs ma thub
gshis nan bskyed kyis zla ba bzhi'i ring phar phul tshur zhu sogs dam pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo bla na med pa bskor ro/ /rgyal kun mkhyen brtse'i ye shes gur khyim nas/ /bsil
ldan 'gro la rjes chags 'jam mgon gyi/ /snang brnyan sku'i bkod zlos gar rim bsgyur ba'i/ /ya mtshan zhing mchog dam pa'i gdan sa cher/ /nges pa don ldan 'jam mgon gong
ma'i drung / /bskal bzang dge sbyor ngur smrig gos can kyang / /sngon bsags las dbang ldan pa'i legs byas kyis/ /gsung gis 'tsho ba'i dga' ston gnas skabs 'dir/ /legs par
bsams na deng nas byang chub bar/ /mi 'bral thugs rje'i spyan gyis gzigs sam snyam/ /snyan brgyud ma dros tshangs pa'i ral klung las/ /bdag 'dra'i thos chung zil dngar
phra mos kyang / /dam pa'i thugs bskyed ye shes bum bzang gi /cha shas yongs su khengs 'di ngo mtshar gnas/ /ji snyed gsung gi gsang ba dbyar skyes sgra/ /bdag cag mdongs
mtha'i sgra 'dzin la 'gyed na/ /bla gos sgro gshog 'phrul gyis dga' ba'i gar/ /ci nas mi sgyur snyom las dal ba su/ /a ho 'di 'dra'i skal bzang rab snyan glu/ /ji bzhin
rdzogs par blangs na dbyangs can gyi/ /rgyud stong phang 'gro'i sgra dang dri za'i glu/ /snyan par sems pa phal cher rdzun du thal/ /de nas dgon gnas dang gzhi nas myur
du 'ong dgos tshul gyi yi ge byung ba dang / lhag tu gong sa chen po nas mgyogs tsam 'ongs na 'gab pa'i bka' shog rin po che

spyi bor pheb cing / chos skyong nas kyang gsung shog gnang 'dug pa dang / 'tsho byed kyis kyang phyin pa 'gab tshul gsung ba bcas gong du dgongs pa zhus par/ de bzhin 'ong
tshul pheb/ 'ong khar sku tshe'i rten 'brel du sgrol dkar yid bzhin 'khor lo'i tshe khrid zla ba'i chu rgyun tshar lugs ji bzhin dang / stobs 'phrog dbang po'i tshe sgrub
thun mong min pa phul/ tshur rwa pod kyi dbus nas shog bu kha shas 'phros rjes ma 'ong dus gnang zhes rten 'brel bsgrig pa gnang zhing / ser gos chas cha tshang / chibs
sga 'khor/ bur ltang / 'bras ltang / dar gos chen/ ras sogs dpangs shin tu mtho ba chos yon gyi tshul du stsal zhing / dbon la'ang gos cha tshang sogs gnang sbyin rgyas
pa dang / zla bo rnams la'ang gang la gang 'tshams kyi gnang sbyin stsal song / nged rang gi lcam nas kyang nged so sor byin rten dang / bur ltang / ras sogs kyi rdzong ba
rgyas pa dang / zhabs phyi sku drag rnams dang / lcam gyi phyag g.yog rnams kyis gang 'tshams kyi rdzong ba shin tu rgyas par byung / so sor gtso cher bstan pa'i lar rgya
dang / gong ma zhabs drung rin po che'i zhabs phyir gang 'gyur dgos pa'i 'phros shin tu zhib par zhus/ 'ong nyin dam rdzas khri rdo sogs byin rten mang ba bcas/ phyag
mdud/ dbon dang g.yog rnams la'ang phyag mdud/ byin rten sogs stsal zhing lus kyi 'tsho skyong dang / gang ci nas zhabs phyi gang 'gyur dgos tshul gyi bslab ston zhib par
stsal/ phar yang rgyal bstan spyi dang bye brag gi don du zhabs pad yun ring brtan cing gsung gi bdud rtsi 'gro ba rnams la stsol bzhin pa nas bstan pa'i 'dzin skyong sogs
lugs gnyis ka

nas sngar lugs g.yo med gnang dgos tshul sogs shin tu rgyas par zhus/ 'ong khar bka' bsgo zhus/ sku zhabs nas 'ong mi phod pa lta bu byung / sngags 'chang bla ma nyid kyang
thugs 'phreng ba'i tshul gnang ba ni byang chub bar du rjes su 'dzin pa'i brdar go /nged rang gis lcam gyi gzims chung du phyin/ 'phral yun kun tu phan pa'i bslab bya byas
shing / rten 'brel gyi stobs gzims chung gi sgo nang nas bzhugs zhus pa bzhin mdzad song / zhabs phyi rnams kyis skyel ba sogs shin tu rgyas par gnang zhing / dar rgyas
sogs chibs skyel ba mang tsam gyis la rtse'i bar skyel ma byas shing so sor ster cha byas/ dpal mgon gyi bla rdor kha'ur mthong snang byung ba bzhin sku bris pa de lus
shing / char babs pa sogs ltas kyang legs snyam pa mang dag byung / de nub bkra shis rtags brgyad du bsdad/ rim gyi snar thang du slebs/ rten rnams zhib par mjal zhing snyan
dar mchod pa rgyas par phul/ sa lugs kyi grwa tshang la mang ja bsngo rten kyang phul/ gzhis rtser 'byor/ tsho dpon pa'i sar gnas tshang byas/ rdzong nas zur gsos sogs
rgyas par byung / phar rdzong bzhugs so sor skyes rgyas par phul/ rim gyis 'ong pa'i lam gtsang 'gram lha khang du phyin/ rten rnams mjal zhing snyan shal mchod pa rgyas
par phul/ bstan 'gro'i don du smon lam yang dag btab/ de nub gdan sa chen po rtse gdong du slebs/ gsol dpon sogs chibs bsu gnang ba dang 'phrad/ bla brang ser mor slebs
dus drung 'khor rnams kyis mjal dar bcas bsu bar byung / rgyal yum nyid kyang skas mgor bsu bar pheb par mjal dar dang sku bzos zhus/ gzims chung 'gag tu 'jam mgon sku

mched mjal te mjal dar phar phul tshul gnang zhus/ gzims chung du gsol ja bzhi'i ring lugs gnyis kyi bka' lung zhib par gyur/ phyi nyin rta shin tu legs pa/ dar gos/ ras sogs
'bul tshan rgyas par phul/ yum drung la tshan grangs dang / zhabs phyi rnams la'ang so sor ster sbyin byas/ ston mo dpangs mtho ba stsal zhing / dpon sogs la khri chen
nas grub thob chen po'i lugs kyi tshe dbang zhig stsal song / phyi nyin lhun po rtser sku zhabs su mjal khar phyin dus/ zhabs phyi rnams kyis mjal dar bcas bsu bar mdzad/
rta sogs 'bul dpangs mtho bar phul/ byang gter gyi tshe dpag med kyi tshe dbang zhus/ 'ong khar gnang sbyin byin rten sogs rgyas par gnang zhing / lugs gnyis kyi bslab
ston bka' drin bskyangs/ phar yang zhabs pad yun ring du brtan cing bstan pa'i 'dzin skyong sogs snyan 'bul zhus/ chos sde dang klu sdings dus mchod mjal du phyin/ rten rnams
la snyan shal mchod pa sogs dngos bshams yid sprul gyi mchod pas mchod/ bla brang du 'byor nas zhabs drung sku mched la tshe dbang zhig phul/ dar ras sogs gnang sbyin
rgyas par stsal/ phyi nyin bstan 'gro'i dpung gnyen du zhabs pad yun ring du brtan ngos/ bstan pa'i 'dzin skyong sogs lugs gnyis kyi snyan 'bul rgyas par zhus te/ phyir
'ong skabs skyel mar rdo gcal bar pheb/ so so'i phyag mdzod khag sogs kyis rgyang tsam bar rta skyel mdzad/ dar ras sogs kyi ster cha byas/ de nub 'tshal du bsdad/ rim gyis
sgo ba la brgyud yangs pa can du 'byor/ ya gir chu'i stabs lam du'ang gzugs gzhi bde ba rang zhig ma byung bas/ 'phrod res zla bo mang ma rnams stod lung phyogs su btang
/ nged drug tsam gyis yo re'i chu tshan du phyin

par chos srung rnams 'phreng ba'i 'tshubs kyi rnam pas mig la thor ba zhig byung bas chu tshan byed ma thub cing / yon bdag rnams kyis rta/ 'bri g.yag /mar sogs ster sbyin
byed mi mang bar byung bas/ byang bu/ bsngo smon/ bsngags mdud/ byin rten bcas kyis so so'i 'dod pa bsgrubs/ mgyogs myur 'ongs pas rim bder gyur cing / lam gyi stabs gzhis
su phyin/ zhal ngo rnams dang / yon bdag /g.yog sogs la byin rten sogs kyi ster cha byas/ dgon gnas su 'ong nyin bla khag las tshan bcas byon pa dang lam du 'phrad/ yon
bdag rnams kyis 'phrad mi mang tsam byung stabs rgyag tu song gshis ser phreng ma 'grigs 'dug kyang bsang / dar 'phyar rgyas par mdzad/ 'byor 'phral mang ja zhus shing /
bla khag las tshan rnams dang / dgon khag gi bla ma rin sdings nas chos mdzad ma gnyis/ grwa rigs yon bdag /g.yog sogs 'phrad mi mang bar byung bar dam rdzas/ dar ras sogs
kyi ster cha ci rigs byas/ zla ba phyi ma'i nang zhabs drung dbon rin po che byang du pheb rgyur rta khal cha lag sogs gang 'grigs dang / mdzod pa dang / zhabs phyi ser
skya mang ba dang / bla sman pa don grub bcas tshes bcu gsum la pheb par gang ci'i bslab bya rgyas pa dang / byes res 'di la bar chad med par 'phrad 'ong byas pa phyis
thog tu khel bas kha 'don legs pa zhig byung 'dra bsam/ bkra shis gling dang / dar yul sogs su rgyan drung / bla khag /las tshan/ nang bzan sogs chibs skyel la rdzong bda'
byas/ zhag shas nas pho brang chen por mjal kha zhu bar phyin pas 'khor los sgyur ba chen po'i mjal kha'i skabs/ sa skya

sogs kyi bka' 'dri zhib tu stsal/ gzims chung 'gag tu dge slong ngag dbang dkon mchog lags brgyud nas gong sa skyabs mgon chen po'i phyag mjal rten rnams phul/ gdan sar chos
gang phul sogs bka'i 'dri ba mang tsam bka' drin bskyangs/ thon phyag nor bu gling khar gnang zhing chos kyi dri ba'ang stsal/ ston mo/ gnang sbyin/ zur chas brtse bas
bskyangs shing phyir 'byor/ rab byung bsnyen rdzogs sogs rgyun gyi bya ba rnams dang / ston zhabs drung dpon slob nas 'bul skyel du rab brtan can 'byor bar rta phyugs sogs
rtsis sprod byung zhing / khams byang gi 'bul pa mang ba dang / sde dge dbon po kun dga' rab brtan sku ma 'tsho ba'i bsngo rten skye kha mi 'byor 'phral gser dre'u sogs
kyi rten rgya che ba dang / dbon po bsod nams kyi dre'u ja bcas byung bar dge ba rdzogs byang du bsngos nyan po nas yab kyi gshegs rdzong gi tshogs dbur 'ong dgos tshul
gnang ba bzhin phyin/ bcom ldan 'das kun rig gi cho ga dang / byang bu sogs zhus/ rnyed bkur dang gnang sbyin dpangs mtho bar stsal/ dgun dus mchod sogs sngar ltar dang /
mdzod par chu ma 'phrod pas phyir 'byor pa dang 'phrad/ 'di lo byang du kha stib tshan che ba sngar ma grags pa zhig byung 'dug pas khong dpon slob kyang rnyed 'tshol gnang
dka' bar byung 'dug /or thog tu pheb khar bla ma bsam 'phel 'bul skyel du rdzong bda' gnang ba kha ba'i stabs lam du 'gor che'ang skyon med du 'byor/ khong dpon slob
kyi sar bang chen yang yang btang / lo mjug gi bskang ba khri tshar sogs dang dgon lag gi bya ba rnams dkyus bzhin byas// ! chu sprel lor lo gsar dang / zla ba gsum pa'i
nang du mdzod pa sogs khong dbon

slob kyi zhabs phyir rdzong bda' byas/ dbyar zla ba bzhi'i ring nad ros yun shin tu ring tsam 'tshe bar rim gro sogs gnyer pas khur len dang / 'tsho mdzad lcam gyi gsol sman
gzhan dang ma 'dra bas rim bde byung skabs rtse gdong nas rgyal yum pheb par chibs bsu zhus te klu sdings su bzhugs/ phyi nyin bco brgyad du gdan 'dren zhus par gcad rgya'i
stabs khong dpon g.yog nyung bsdus dang mjal 'phrad zhus/ gang ci'i gsung gling dang nged rang nad las grol ba'i legs cha gnang / phyi nyin ston mo rgyas pa'i thog rta
legs pa sogs dgu tshan phul nas phyir pheb/ bstan pa'i sbyin bdag dal jing sogs yon sho po'i rgyal khag rnams 'phrad par byon zhing / tshe dbang dang rkyen sel gyi dbang
/ sku 'dra byin rten bcas rdzong ba rgyas par byas/ dbon dpon slob kyi sar mdzod pa bcas 'byor nas khams phyogs su pheb 'dug par sgom bde nas 'bul skyel dang gnas tshul
skyel bar shes rab pa dang kun dga' bkra shis can rdzong bda' gnang bar 'byor zhing / phyag bris sogs sprad cing 'gro don gzhan dang mi 'dra bar byung tshul yang gleng
/ nad ros gzugs gzhi skyor re ba las drag skyed che ba rang ma byung zhing / na ba'i skabs 'di dag tu nam mkha' las 'ja' sprin gyis khengs shing / lha'i bu dang bu mo'i rnams
pas mchod rdzas du ma thogs pa sogs mthong snang byung zhing / me tog gi char babs pas tshang ma dogs pa'i rang bzhin du gyur/ pho brang chen por gsung brtag zhus pa'i
rim gro rnams bsgrubs/ rkyen 'pho ba lta bus nged rang gi zhon rta de glo bur du shi bas nad gzhi sangs drag tu gyur/ rin sdings kyi tsha mo lha ldan sde pa lha khang
pa'i sar dgos tshul byung ba bzhin

cha lag sogs tsha mo ngo ma dang cha 'dra bsgrigs nas rdzong bda' byas/ khams kyi 'bul skyel shes rab pa can yi ge dang / dar ras/ snam bu bcas rdzong bda' byas shing / sgom
khang du phyin/ ston a mdo nas chos rje kun dga' bstan 'dzin dpon slob nyis brgya skor 'byor bar mgron gnyer dang / dgon gnas kyi bla khag las tshan bcas chibs bsur rdzong
bda' dang / a mdo khams tshan du 'byor 'phral ja zhus/ phyi nyin bco brgyad du gzhis len rgyas par zhus/ zhag shas ring nyin bstar 'grul bsdebs grwa rigs rnams kyi tshogs
su cho ga dang mang ja ci rigs thog /nged rang bos te bsngo rten rgyas par byung zhing / dge ba rdzogs byang du bsngos/ chos rje rang gi tshogs su cho ga stong rtsa
mdzad dus nyin re bzhin tshogs su bos/ byang bu bsngo smon nyin bstar byas/ grol nyin gdugs/ rol mo/ mchod rdzas mang ba/ rta/ ja/ ras dar sogs dngos po'i brgya 'bul mdzad
par zab pa chos kyi dbyings dang / rgya che ba sems can gyi don du rgyas 'debs byas/ chos rje dpon slob la ston mo rgyas par zhus/ khyung 'bum nas 'bul sdud bla ma byams
pa bzang po khu dbon dpon slob 'grul bsdebs mang bar bcas 'byor zhing / rta drel/ ja/ rgun zangs sogs rtsis sprod shin tu rgyas par byung / sne len gzabs par byas/ 'dus
tshogs la cho ga mdzad par phyin/ byang rten dngos pa'i 'bul ba rgya cher bar mdzad cing / dge rtsa byang chub tu bsngos/ phyogs nas 'byon mi bla ma rnams dang nged rang
bcas pho brang chen por mjal kha zhu bar phyin/ gong sa chen po'i mjal rten rnams gzims chung 'gag tu phul/ dge slong rin chen brgyud bka' 'dri mang bar stsal/

sa dbang chen mo'i mjal kha rgyas shing / 'bras spungs bde yangs pa'i rigs grwa'i sku mgron la chibs kha bsgyur ba'i zhabs phyir bslab ston ltar phyin/ ston mo sogs bka' drin
che bar gnang / mgron gnyer lags dang zhabs phyi drag pa rnams la rta sogs 'bul tshan ci rigs phul/ tshang mas ja 'dren dang mtshams 'dri kyang gnang / dge slong rin po
cher thugs bzhed ltar chos kha shas phul/ chos rje dang 'bul sdud bla ma bcas la'ang mjal kha bdag rkyen bka' drin che bar stsal song / khong gnyis la gong sa chen po'i
bka' shog zhus par shin tu btsan pa dang / chos rjer cho lo bcas gzhan dang mi 'dra bar bka' drin bskyangs shing / thon phyag /zur chas/ gnang sbyin so sor rgyas par bcas
phyir rdzong gnang / tshur lam gzhis khar sde pa a 'bar lags sku zhabs mjal bar phyin zhing / rta sogs 'bul rten rgya che bar phul/ mjal kha bdag rkyen che ba bka' drin
bskyangs/ pha bong khar grub pa'i dbang phyug grub brgya sgrub chen sku zhabs la phyin/ ja sogs sku rim sgrub rten phul zhing / gang ci'i gsung gleng rgyas pas 'byams klas
par gyur/ dgon gnas su 'byor 'phral lo dus kyi brel ba dus chen khag sogs lo mjug gi rim gro dang / rab byung bsnyen rdzogs bcas lugs gnyis rnams rim sel byas/ chu bya
lor gsar tshes kyi lo gsar dang / keg thog tu song gshis tshe sgrub kyang byas/ sos kar dug gi nad ros 'tshe bar nyan po nas grub pa'i dbang phyug chos rje rin po che gdan
drangs/ tshe dbang sogs rkyen sel gyi rigs dang / tshogs chen gyis gsung sgrogs/ ban tshang rnams kyis bskang ba/ sngags 'chang bsam 'grub kyis mdos

rdzong sogs rim gro mang bar gnyer pa dgos rdeg gis gra sgrig byas shing / 'phen yul khul dgon so sor mang skol kyang byas/ nyan po nas chos rje rin po che sku mched kyis rten
'byung rgyas pa/ tshogs chen dang / khams tshan so so/ sgom khang bcas dgon lag gsum/ ban tshang rnams dang / nang bzan skya ser/ spyi bsdus mkhar gdong dang / gzhis
khag gi mi ser bcas tshang mas brtan bzhugs kyi rigs rim pa khur blang mdzad song zhing / ban tshang rnams dang drung 'tsho bcas nang skor gyis rten 'byung yang bskyar dang
/ 'tsho mdzad lcam bcar bzhugs kyis sman bcos gang zab gnang ba bcas nad las grol zhing / chos srung dang chos skyong gnyis sogs tshang mar gtang rag gi gsol kha snyan
dar rgyas par phul/ sde pa rgyal phur rin po ches grub rgyal zhal bdag gnang bar chos gzhis smyu kyu ba rnams kyang grub rgyal gyi sa khog tu gtogs pa'i yin tshul gzhan
mas zhus pas 'bul dgos tshul bslab ston gnang bar/ ma nas bka' gang gnang las zhu ci la nus kyang / sngar babs kyi gnas rgyus dang bcas rang 'jags bka' drin che na ji ltar
'ong tshul zhus par/ dgongs dbyings rin po che nas ma dor bar phyir slog bka' drin bskyangs pa'i legs 'bul du rgyan drung 'bul tshan rta bcas rdzong bda' byas par mjal
kha bdag rkyen shin tu legs par gnang 'dug /dpal gnas kyi tsha bo rnams kyis phyag 'bul zhu bsgugs la tsha bo mgon pos lo bdun tsam song ba/ 'di lo zla ba gsum pa'i nang
du phyag 'bul grub nas khong pa spun tshang ma chos rang byed pa'i blo bzhed che bar 'dug par/ chos 'jig rten gang byed kyang nged rang gis byas chog pa'i bslab ston rin
po che

yod pa ltar/ gzhon pas dge slong rin po che'i sku zhabs dang / rgan pas 'di khar dge tshul bsgrubs shing rim gyis bsnyen rdzogs kyang bsgrubs/ zhabs drung rin po che yar pheb
dgos tshul zhu bar bang chen gnyis rdzong bda' byas/ dbyar smad ston pheb pa gnang rtsis yin tshul gyi bang chen 'byor/ sgom khang gi dbyar mjal sogs lo dus kyi brel ba
rim sel byas/ gsang sbug tshong dpon gyis tsandan gyi sku kha shas dang / gnas bcu gra tshang gis zhal thang / 'bum sogs bzhengs pa'i rab gnas la phyin/ rab gnas dang /
dbang / rjes gnang sogs kyis thugs bzhed khengs par byas/ ston mo dang ster cha rgyas par byung / ja pa ngag dbang can pheb bsur rdzong bdar byas par/ 'dam du 'gor che ba
byung 'dug gshis/ khong dpon slob nyung bsdus sgom bder pheb cing / mdzod pa sgar gzhis byings bcas shar rgyag byon pa dang lcog rtse lar 'phrad 'dug /mdzod pas gnas tshul
skyel bar snga 'gros rab brtan can rdzong bda' byas par 'byor/ zhag kha shas ring mdzo g.yag gi khal ma rnams rim gyis slebs shing / khyon snga phyi bsgril ba'i khal
ma gsum brgya skor sngon ma 'byor ba'i steng khal ja sogs ci rigs 'dug pa 'du khang du bzhag /rgyan drung pheb bsur pheb pa dang mdzod pa 'dam nas mjal zhing / dbon dpon
slob 'gor ches pas mdzod pa 'phrad 'dod kyi sngon ma mgyogs skor du byon pa dang 'phrad/ nyag bre'i 'bul skyel ba gnyer pa klu mgon can 'byor zhing / 'bul dpon bla ma'i yig
nang ltar dngos po rnams rtsis sprod byung / nged rang gi dbon chung ba 'od mchog sprul sku'i gtsug phud 'bul ba'i

gza' tshes stabs dpon rin po che dpon slob rnams mgyogs tsam e pheb kyi chos skyong la dri ba zhus par/ tshes pa nyi shu tshun la pheb grub pa'i khag khyag byed sogs lung bstan
gnang / khong dpon slob rnams 'gor gzhi che bar 'ong rgyu yin 'dug kyang / dpal ldan lha mo dang chos skyong gis bskul ba lta bur/ rta glo bur du 'ur ba dang tshang
ma blo shin tu 'tshubs pa byung 'dug pas khal rnams rjes su bzhag /khong dpon slob rags bsdus drel khal bcas pheb pa'i bang chen snga 'gros pa 'byor 'phral/ chos mdzad ngag
dbang grags pa gzhis su 'phros dang pheb bsur de 'phral brdzongs/ phyi nyin mdzod pa'ang pheb gdong du dar yul la byon/ dbon dpon slob rnams sgom khang mdor bzhugs par
gzhis nas dpon sa'ang pheb bsur byon te gzhis len gzabs pa mdzad cing / pheb bsu ba rnams dang / sgom khang grwa rigs bcas mi tshogs che ba byung 'dug /tshes bcu dgur sprul
sku rin po che rgyan drung bcas kyi dbus chos sde chen po'i bla khag /las tshan/ tsha bo chos mdzad rgan pa/ gsang sbug gi tsha bo a bsam sog ser skya mang ba gzhi sdings
bar chibs bsur btang / bkra shis gling du thab bsur tsha mo chos mdzad ma spun kyang rdzong bda' byas/ chos sde nas ser phreng / dar 'phyar rgyas par byas shing / dbang
khang 'chi med pho brang du mjal 'phrad byas/ gzhis byes kyi gsung gleng rgyas par byung / sang nyin 'dus tshogs su cho ga stong rtsa dang / mgon khang so sor bskang
gso/ spyan gzigs kyi rigs mang ba/ khyad par 'dod khams dbang phyug rdo rje rab brtan ma'i sger bskang rgyas pa/ spyan gzigs bcas 'bul bkod dang / nged rang la rten/

mchod cha/ dkar yol gyi rigs/ tshos mdog sogs mi gcig pa sna tshogs/ dkar yol gyi mchod rdzas mang ba/ bkra shis pa'i kha btags sna lnga/ gser/ dngul/ g.yu/ bye ru/ spos shel/
shel spyad/ shel ril/ gri/ khrab/ rmog /mda' gzhu/ sag thag /me mda'/ khro zangs spyad/ lcags 'gu sogs lcags cha shin tu mang ba/ ja/ gos chen/ dar ras/ sle'u/ mar/ phying
pa sogs byang khams kyi dngos spyad shin tu mang ba dang / rta/ dre'u/ mdzo/ g.yag /mdzo mo/ gur g.yab/ thab chas kyi rigs sogs sgar gzhis kyi cha lag ci rigs pa dang
/ rta sga/ drel sga/ bka' gcegs/ mdzo khal gyi sga stan sogs dngos po'i rigs ji snyed pa zhig rtsis sprod kyi tshul du brgya 'bul mdzad cing / nged rang khu dbon gyis
gtsos gzhi byes tshang mar 'tshe ba med par zhal 'dzoms pas legs tshogs kyi gsung gleng dang / mdzod pas kyang khams phyogs su pheb ring gi lo rgyus khams pa'i gtam ring
mo lta bu yun ring la dar drag pa mdzad/ chos sde chen po'i bla khag /las tshan/ gzhis kyi zhal ngo / rin sdings ban tshang / nang skor drag zhan/ nang bzan/ gzhis gnyer/
yon bdag gal che gras/ dgon lag gi bla ma sogs tshang mar skyes mar gnang lugs kyi gros dang bkod pa byas shing / ltos bcas kyang yid tshim par mdzad song / nyin lnga'i
ring stong rtsa tshugs pa grol nyin thog mar gzims khang gong 'og /bco brgyad sogs kyi rten gsum rnams la snyan dar/ mchod rdzas/ dkar me sogs mchod 'bul dang / 'dus tshogs
la ja 'gyed/ bla khag so sor bsngo rten bcas tshogs gsog gi rigs rgya che bar mdzad pa'i bkod pa

byas shing / mdzod pas kyang nyin gcig tshogs chen la stong chog gi zhabs tog rgyas pa dang / ja 'gyed/ so sor bsngo rten bcas dge rtsa'ang byas song / dbon dpon slob 'grul
bsdebs dang bcas par gzhis len ston mo gzabs rgyas thog /dpon rin po cher na bza' cha tshang / mdzod pa sogs zhabs phyi rnams la ster cha/ gos rgyugs kyi rigs gang la gang
'tshams sprad/ chos skyong dpon blon spyan 'dren thog snyan dar/ spyan gzigs/ ja sogs kyi gtang rag phul/ khong dpon slob rnams byes res 'dir thugs grwa shin tu 'grigs
pa byung 'dug pa ni gtso cher zhabs drung dbon rin po che nyid sku na phra'ang gzhan dang mi 'dra ba'i lugs gnyis la mkhyen pa yangs shing khyon che ba sogs tshang ma'i
yid yul du gsal ba ltar dang / mdzod pa chung 'dris kyi zla bo myong byang che zhing / tsha bo chos mdzad/ bla ma bsam 'phel/ dge slong grags pa/ mgron gnyer rab 'phel/ gsol
dpon rgya mtsho sogs drag gras rnams dang / 'tsho mdzad don grub bcas tshang mas thugs bsam che zhing las kha 'gangs che ba gang gi sar yang thegs pa khur blangs/ phyar
ba zur 'degs kyi zhe rus che zhing gros bsdur mdzad 'dug pas/ dbon rin po che'i zhabs phyir 'gyur ba/ grwa 'grigs pa/ mig ltos la phan pa zhig byung 'dug /drung 'tsho
ba don grub zhabs phyir 'bral med sku la bcar gshis drag zhan thams cad la phan thogs che zhing / skabs 'gar dbon rin po che sku khams phran bu ltem skabs dang le'u thang
du cung zhig bsnyel tsam byung 'dug skabs sogs la gsol sman dang sku'i 'phrod bsten gyi zhabs phyir shin tu 'gyur bar mdzad 'dug /khams nas pheb pa dang /

nged rang rgyun mjal zhu dgos dang / sprul sku'i gtsug phud 'bul ba dang bcas nged sku dbon lhan du pho brang chen por gong sa chen po yas phyin mjal kha zhu bar phyin par/
sa dbang chen po'i mjal kha bka' drin bskyangs shing / nged rang nas rgyun gyi mjal phyag gi 'bul ba/ dbon rin po che khams nas pheb pa'i phyag 'bul rten/ dbon chung ba
sprul skus mjal kha zhu rten rnams so so nas dpangs mtho bar phul zhing / bka' 'dri rgyas pa dang bdag rkyen che ba bka' drin bskyangs/ gong sa chen po'i mjal rten rnams
gzims chung 'gag tu phul zhing gsol dpon sngags rams pa lags brgyud bslab ston rgyas par gnang / mgron khang du ston mo sogs bka' drin bskyangs/ phyi nyin 'bras spungs blo
gsal gling pa'i rigs grwa'i sku mgron gyi zhabs phyir bslab ston ltar dbon dang nged gnyis kyis phyin zhing / ston mo rgyas par stsal/ nyer gnyis gza' tshes rgyal phur
'dzoms pa'i thog dge slong rin po che brgyud sprul pa'i sku'i gtsug phud phul bar/ thar pa'i mkhan po'i stabs re zhig rab byung rang 'gab tshul dang / slar brgyud 'dzin ma
byung na bltas chog bslab ston pheb pa ltar gong sa chen po nas ming bka' drin bskyangs/ dge slong rin po che'i sku zhabs su bar ma rab byung zhus/ ra ma rtse rgyal bur
sku zhabs su mjal kha zhu bar dbon rdzong bda' byas shing der brten pha bong khar drug brgya sgrub chen mjal bkod kyang zhus/ mchod dpon lags/ dge slong rin po che/ dge
slong ngag dbang dkon mchog /em chi lags/ gsol dpon sngags rams pa/ drung yig lags/ gzims dpon lags/ mgron gnyer

zhal ngo bcas zhabs phyi nang ma'i gras rnams la rta/ mdzo/ ja sogs mdo khams nas byon pa'i skyes su phul/ 'chi med dga' tshal du'ang skyes 'bul dpangs mtho bar byas/ dbon
sku mched kyi sku nye rnams la'ang gang 'tshams phul/ tshur yang bzhes spro/ kha btags/ na bza' sogs kyi ster cha'ang byung / pho brang chen po dang / lha sa ra mo che sogs
kyi mchod mjal rnams zhib par byas/ dkar me snyan dar sogs kyi mchod pa'ang rgyas par phul/ thon phyag thog gnang sbyin/ zur chas/ ston mo sogs rgyas pa bka' drin bskyangs
te/ rang gnas su log /sprul sku rin po che'i phebs bsur 'byon mi thar bas pa dang / chos sder gling pa bcas kyis gshin rje 'char kha'i gtor zlog shin tu rgyas par byas/
sprul sku rin po che'i zhabs phyir tsha bo dge slong ngag dbang grags pas gtsos rgyun sdod lnga dang / pheb skyel du rgyan drung / mdzod pa sogs dpon g.yog mang ba bcas
grwa bsgrigs dang / sku 'dra/ mchod cha/ dkar spyad kyi rigs/ phyag dpe sogs nyer mkho'i sku chas rnams dang / chibs pa gnyis/ dre'u/ ja/ gos dar sogs pheb rdzong dang
bstan pa'i 'dzin skyong sku yon gsan sbyong sogs kyi snyan 'bul shin tu rgyas par zhus te/ chibs kha sgyur ba la nangs par zhabs drung rin po ches dbus chos sde'i bla khag
/las tshan/ nang bzan ser skya sogs chibs skyel ba shin tu mang ba rdzong bda' byas/ 'u du su nas nged rang gi 'bul sdud e chol thu chos rje 'byon yod tshul gyi yi ge
byung bar nag chu'i khar bsu mi rdzong bda' dang / chos sde chen po'i dus chen khag rnams byas shing / se ra nas a mdo grwa tshang mkhan po rje btsun nA ro mkha' spyod ma'i
skor kyi zab chos

rnams gsan bzhed kyis pheb par chibs bsu dang / zhag nyi shu skor bzhugs ring gzhis len sogs sku bzos shin tu che bar zhus/ chos rnams 'phral du phul/ chos yon du gos ber/
dngul sga sogs dngos po dpangs mtho bar stsal te/ chibs skyel la mgron gnyer can rdzong bda' byas/ zla ba bcu gnyis pa'i nang du o chol du chos rje dpon slob rnams byung
bar rta bsu dang / ngos 'phrad/ gzhis len sogs rgyas par byas shing / chos rjes dngul/ gos dar/ mchod rdzas/ rol mo sogs rtsis sprod rgyas pa dang / bla ma bsod nams dar
rgyas pa'i gzhi ma dngul thog tu bsgril ba rtsis sprod kyang byas/ chos sde'i 'dus tshogs la mang ja/ cho ga stong rtsa 'dzugs pa dang / mchod rdzas 'bul ba sogs tshogs gsog
rgya che bar mdzad song zhing / nged rang nas dmigs med 'khor gsum yongs dag gi bsngo smon yang dag byas/ chos rjes dbus sog po rnams pho brang chen por phyag mjal zhus
bar rdzong bda' dang / lo mjug gi rim gro rnams byas/ zhabs brtan tshogs mchod chen mo gsar 'dzugs bka' drin bskyangs par dge 'dun rnams tshogs dgos pa'i bka' shog rin
po che spyi bor pheb/ shing khyi lor gsar tshes kyi brel ba rnams dang / zla ba gnyis pa'i nang du grwa pa rnams tshogs mchod la rdzong bda' byas/ chos rjer dgongs pa dgos
tshul nan gyis gsungs kyang / yon bdag gi rgyal po sogs dad zhan ches pas 'di kha dgos tshul nan gyis byung ba dang / nged rang gi'ang rogs su 'gyur che bar byung gshis
phyir rdzong byas/ dbyar nad rol langs par rim gro 'phrod bsten gyis

rim dwangs byung / zla ba bdun pa'i nang sha ba bla ma rin chen/ mgron gnyer rin chen bcas sprul sku rin po che'i pheb bsur rdzong bda' byas/ dbyar smad byang lam brgyud pheb
par chos gzhis bkra shis sgang du rgyan drung sogs kyi chibs bsu dang / thab bsu rgyas par zhus shing / rgyun gyi dbang po'i bla khag /las tshan rnams kyis kyang chibs
bsu dang bsang / dar 'phyar/ ser phreng sogs rgyas par byas te/ dbang khang 'chi med pho brang du mjal 'dzoms zhus par/ gang ci'i gsung gling rgyas par byung / gzhis len
gang rgyas zhus shing / tshur yang rten 'byung dang sku skyes shin tu rgyas par stsal/ rgya nag gong mas sa dbang gser gyi 'khor los sgyur ba chen por gser tham sogs phul
ba'i legs 'bul du pho brang chen por zhal mjal la bskyod de dar ras/ rta/ ja sogs 'bul dpangs mtho bar bcas mjal kha zhus par bka' 'dri ston mo sogs rgyas par bka' drin
bskyangs/ thon phyag chab zhugs ser nor bu gling khar gnang zhing / rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi rnam thar dang mthun pa'i chos kyi dri ba yun ring bar gnang bar lan rgyas
par phul/ gnang sbyin zur chas bcas phyir thon zhing / lam zhor pha bong khar grub pa'i dbang phyug nyid mjal 'dod kyis phyin/ lugs gnyis kyi gsung gling rgyas par stsal
zhing / sku khams cung zhig ltem 'dug par thugs bcag gnang dgos tshul zhus/ dgon gnas su slebs 'phral mngar ris rab 'byams pa don gnyer gyis pheb par 'khor lo sdom pa dril
bu rim lnga'i dbang dang khrid rgyas par phul/ ston zhabs drung rin po che dpon slob kyi lo snga ma yar pheb dus ja rta sogs dpangs mtho ba

bcas li'u thang nas bka' 'gyur rin po che spar du rgyag par 'bul dpon bla ma bsam 'phel dpon slob 'jog pa gnang 'dug par gegs med du grub nas 'byon yod tshul gyi bang chen
byung bar stag lung bar du bstan 'dzin rgya mtsho can bsu bar rdzong bda' byas/ dgon par pheb nyin bka' 'gyur rin po che'i pheb bsur nged rang gi zla bo drag gras kyis rta
bsu dang / 'dus tshogs kyis ser phreng / lha bsang / dar 'phyar bcas kyis spyan drangs shing bka' 'gyur rin po che 'du khang gsang sngags pho brang du bzhugs su gsol te/
mchod pa'i phreng ba tshar du dngar bar phul/ 'bul dpon bla ma dang / sde dge'i tshong dpon 'grul bsdebs bcas par zhal gro'i ston mo gzhis len rgyas par zhus/ 'bul dpon
bla mas rta drel drug /mdzo so drug /khal nyi shu rnams la sga stan bcas rtsis sprod mdzad/ dge slong ngag dbang grags pas sa skyar nged rang gi lcam gyi zhabs phyir re
zhig rdzong bda' byas/ 'bul dpon bla ma bsam 'phel gyis 'dus tshogs la stong chog btsugs shing / 'di kha'i bla brang gi steng du ganydzi ra zhig 'dzugs rgyu'i gser ja sogs
sprad byung bar/ slar bzo bkod legs par grub nas da lta kun gyi spyan lam du smin pa 'di bzhin lags/ sde dge tshong dpon gyis dbon po so so'i phyag bris rten bcas rnams
dang / dbon po bsod nams kyis 'bul skyel du khal ma/ ja/ rta sogs dpangs mtho ba rnams gnang 'dug pa rtsis len byas shing / dge ba byang chub tu bsngos/ dgun tsha ba nas
'bul sdud bla ma mkhyen rab lhun grub dang / dger slog bstan 'dzin grags pa gnyis 'grul bsdebs mang ba bcas 'byor bar gzhis

len byas/ rta/ drel/ ja sogs so so nas rtsis sprod rgyas pa dang / tshogs chen du cho ga stong rtsa mdzad par tshogs dbur phyin zhing dge ba dzogs byang du bsngos/ dgon gnas
bshad grwar song bas sngar 'chams sogs kyi rgyun mi 'dug par/ 'di kha'i ban tshang rnams gtso bor gyur pas 'chams shig tshugs nas bsams pas 'chams chas skor la/ gos can
gyi phod ka nyi shu skor dang / zhwa nag /phur pa/ bandha/ zangs ral/ phyag mtshan gyi rigs mang po/ 'bag sna tshogs pa bcas bca' lag rnams chos sder gling nas 'jim bzo
ba sogs bos te legs par bsgrigs shing / zhabs drung dbon rin po ches dbus ban tshang rnams kyis sa 'dul 'chams sna bco brgyad/ 'don bdun/ grub 'chams sogs chos sder gling
gi phyag len ji bzhin bslabs shing / zla ba bcu gcig pa'i tshes bcu gnyis la sta gon byas te snga dro kye rdor dang / phyi dro khro bcu'i gtor sgrub bcas zhag brgyad kyi
ring sgrub mchod gsar btsugs la zhabs tog sogs deb gsal ltar rgyas pa dang / bco brgyad dus chen nyin 'chams nyin gang / bcu dgu'i nyin gtor rgyag sogs ji srid bstan pa
rin po che nam gnas bar tshugs pa'i srol btod de grwa sgrigs legs par byas so/ /'di lo phan yul khul du 'brum nad shin tu gzan pa yod kyang zhabs drung dbon sku mched 'brum
pa ma bzhes pas sgrub mchod dus ji ltar 'gab chos skyong dpon blon la bslab ston zhus par/ bar chad med pas khas len byed gsung ba bzhin dus chen skabs dgon par 'brum
pa mang bar yod gshis mi tshogs che ba'i khrod pheb dgos gshis blo 'dzangs che bar byung kyang / bla ma dkon mchog gi thugs rjes 'brum pa ma bzhes pas/

slar yang chos skyong rnams la nges shes che bar byung / dus chen nyin grwa 'grigs shing / gtor rgyag dus rdor slob kyis zor 'phangs dus/ khad nyer spyang ki glo bur du rgyugs
shing lug gcig ded de dus kyi chos nyid du gyur pa sogs ltas legs par byung ba ni bsgral rtag gsal bar mngon/ pha bong kha nas grub pa'i dbang phyug de nyid sku ltem
yun ring bar sku rim mthun rkyen gang drag yang yang phul zhing / zla ba 'di nang du sku lus ma spangs par dag pa mkha' spyod du gshegs tshul bstan pa'i mchod 'bul gyi mthun
rkyen sogs rgyas par phul zhing / chos mdzad ma sku mched la'ang rim gyis phan cha gang drag zhus/ rab byung / bsnyen rdzogs/ 'dod chos sogs sngar rgyun rnams bsgrubs
shing / dgon khag tu phyogs 'gro kyang byas/ shing phag lor lo gsar grub nas/ dbon rin po che sku mched kyi 'brum pa'i stabs chos gzhes mkhar gdong du kun rig dang / dzam
dmar sogs kyi bsnyen pa mdzad pa'i dmigs skor sogs gang ci'i bslab bya byas/ tsha ba'i 'bul sdud pa khag gnyis dang / sde dge'i tshongs pa rnams rim gyis phyir rdzong byas/
ra ma rtse nas sde pa rgyal bur sku zhabs grub rgyal du chibs kha sgyur bar mjal kha zhu bar sku zhabs su bcar te rta sogs 'bul dpangs mtho bar phul zhing / gdan bzos
bdag rkyen che bar bka' drin bskyangs/ dbon rin po che sku mched sku mtshams grol gdong du phyin/ khad nyer 'brum pa gzan tsam 'dug par chos skyong la bslab ston zhus nas
chos gzhis bkra shis sgang du gcad rgya dang / kye rdor gyi gzhi bsnyen mdzad pa'i bkod par byas/ dbyar nad ros yun ring tsam 'tshe bar

'tsho mdzad rta mgrin tshe ring gis gsos sman dang / rim gro 'dus tshogs su chos sgrogs/ dgon khag so sor mang ja sogs rgya che bar mdzod pa lhun grub kyis bsgrigs/ nad g.yog
mgron gnyer rin chen gyis byas shing rim bder gyur/ dbon rin po che gzhi bsnyen gnas sar nged rang na bas ngos kyis 'gro ma thub kyang dmigs skor sogs la sam Ta zhig par
phul ba/ de shog bur bshu bar gnang yod 'dug pas slar re gnyis kyis dpe thog tu phab pas bsnyen thabs la mkho ba zhig kyang byung 'dug gzhung sa chen po nas zhabs brtan
mchod sdong chen mo grub pa'i legs 'bul du nged rang nad ma drags pas 'gro ma thub par/ rgyan drung dang / bla khag /las tshan bcas pheb par/ 'bul tshan du bco brgyad nas
rta/ ja/ khrab sogs kyis gtsos pa'i dgu tshan kha shas dang / spyi so nas dgu tshan kha shas bcas rdzong bda' byas par/ sa dbang chen po'i mjal kha sogs rgyas par byung
'dug /bka' 'gyur rin po cher glegs shing / zhal khebs/ gdong dar/ glegs thag sogs dngos gtsar bar bsgrigs/ nged rang tshogs chen bcas kyis zla ba bdun pa'i nang du bcom
ldan 'das ngan song sbyong ba'i dkyil 'khor la brten pa'i rab gnas legs par byas shing / rten 'brel stabs sprul sku rin po cher yon bdag gi bkra shis kyis mnga' gsol/ zhabs
drung dbon rin po che dpon slob rnams la bsngo 'brel sogs zhu mi rnams dge ba rdzogs byang du bsngos/ dbyar smad 'dam gnyen drung du sprul sku rin po che bcas bskyod
par chu tshan 'phrod zhing / yon bdag rnams kyis 'phrad mi mang bar byung / zhag bco lnga skor nas rang

gnas su slebs/ dbon rin po che sku mtshams sar ngos kyis phyin/ ltas legs pa kha shas byung 'dug /sprul sku rin po che chos sder gling du pheb pa'i pheb rdzong chibs skyel
sogs rgyas par byas/ dgun chos sde chen po'i dus chen khag rab byung bsnyen rdzogs/ khams byang gi 'grul pa rnams kyi mang ja/ cho ga sogs kyi tshogs dbur phyin te byang
bu dang bsngo ba byas/ 'dod chos dang / lo mjug gi rim gro rnams bsgrubs/ dgon lag gi brel ba rnams kyang dkyus bzhin dang / me bya lor lo gsar sogs rgyas par byas/ rdzogs
pa'i sangs rgyas kyi 'khrungs rabs mdzad pa brgya pa sku thang dgur tshang ba bsam sdings sprul sku ba lhun grub bkra shis dang / a ngang bcas sku mched kyis lo gnyis kyi
ring phyag bris mdzad par phog yon shin tu rgyas par phul zhing / gegs med du grub pa'i rab gnas dang / 'bul dpon pas rgyu cha bsgrubs pa'i ganydzi ra gnyis lhan du nged
khu dbon dge 'dun lnga bcu skor gyis kun rig la brten pa'i rab gnas rgyas par byas/ nged rang na so'i stabs rgyun gyi bya ba rnams dbon rin po ches mdzad de/ nged rang
gcad rgyar bsdad pa'i zla bo tsha bo chos mdzad rgan pas bcar sdod byas shing / zla ba bdun brgyad ring mtshams dam par byung / zhol khang nas bka' 'gyur rin po che mtshal
spar ma gdan drangs pa dang / slob dpon chen po'i gser sku sogs bzhengs pa'i rab gnas la phyin/ rab gnas shin tu rgyas pa dang / dbang sogs thugs 'dod ltar byas/ rnyed
bkur yang dag byung / ma yum sku skye dang bla ma chos mdzad gnyis khams phyogs su 'bul sdud la rdzong bda'i gra bsgrig dbon nas

mdzad/ mtshams khog la phyogs 'byon gnyis kyi stabs zhabs drung dpon rin po ches dbus nyung bsdus la rje btsun rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i khrid/ gsang 'dus 'jam dpal rdo rje sogs
zur bka' mang bar byas/ bla ma gnyis thon nyin lugs gnyis kyi bslab bya rgyas pa dang bka' bsgo bcas thon par/ rta skyel sogs 'bul sdud pa gzhan las lhag par byas/ dbyar
smad nad gzhi phran bu langs pa'i mjug bskyang du 'dam gnyen drung chu tshan du phyin par zhag bdun 'phrod bsten byas pas gzugs bzhir phan ngo che bar byung / sde dge
dbon po tshe dbang rdo rje gong sa chen po yas phyin gyi mjal kha zhu bar byon pa'i snga 'gros dang / nag chu'i ja khral la bka' 'dzin zhu rogs snga sor nas bcol bar brtse
bas gzigs pa len pa bcas bang chen 'byor bar/ bka' 'dzin rin po che dang / bsu ba'i chas dang bcas mdzod pa dang / dge slong grags pa phun tshogs gnyis rogs bcas chu tshan
kha nas rdzong bda' byas/ 'dam nas o thog dang yon bdag rnams kyis mar phyur/ 'bri g.yag sogs ster cha byed mi mang bar byung / tshur lam dge slong mchog ldan gyis rgyus
yod mdzad de kyi ri'i la brgyud klu kha stod du phyogs su 'ong bar/ kha rag gi ri'i 'dabs su slebs dus nam mkha' shin tu dwangs par 'ja' 'od kyi gur phub pa/ zangs mdog
dpal ri'i rtser dbus su rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan g.yas sa gnon/ g.yon mnyam gzhag gi steng du ka pA la bdud rtsis gang ba bsnams pa/ g.yas phyogs su
gong sa skyabs mgon lnga pa chen po phyag g.yas rdo rje sdigs mdzub bcas pa nam mkha' la 'phyar zhing / phyag g.yon mnyam gzhag gi steng na tshe bum bsnams pa/ g.yon du
gong ma mkhyen

rab bstan 'dzin bzang po phyag gnyis mnyam gzhag gi steng na tshe bum bsnams pa/ de'i 'og tsam gyi g.yas su brag dkar po zhig gi thog rdo rje phag mo dang / g.yon du bye ma
shur re ba'i steng nA ro mkha' spyod ma/ ri'i dbus su slob dpon chen po na bza' za hor lugs gzi brjid dang ldan pa/ 'og tu rgyal po chen po ngal bsos po phyag mtshan spyi
mthun dang / dpal ldan lha mo rgyan phyag mtshan mngon rtogs nang bzhin las/ sku mdog nag mo/ phyag g.yon gyi gru mo na zhags pa brkyang bas mi zhig rke nas bzung te 'khrid
pa/ chu srin gdong can dang bcas pa zhal mngon sum du bstan zhing / gzhan yang bar snang du mkha' 'gro mang pos mchod pa byed pa/ gnas srung gi gnod sbyin gnyis sogs
mthong snang shin tu mang ba byung zhing / pha mas thog drangs sems can thams cad rjes su 'dzin pa'i smon lam yang dag btab/ a ho du ma'i skye ba'i sngon rol nas/ /rjes
bzung dam pa'i zhabs pad yun bsten pas/ /slar yang ngo mtshar thugs rje'i dga' ston du/ /grub pa'i gnas nas rjes bzung zhal mchog mthong / /'dzam gling spyi dang khyad par
gangs can kun/ /chos kyi gnas su byin brlabs lha srin rnams/ /'dul mdzad o rgyan che dang mkha' spyod ma/ /nor lha'i tshogs dang 'dod khams dbang mo sogs/ /bla ma yi dam
lha tshogs zhal mthong tshe/ /sems nyid brjod bral ngang du yun zhig 'byams/ /de dag legs par sems na bla ma dang / /yi dam srung mas byin rlabs rjes su bzung / /rim gyis
thod ler 'byor zhing mgon khang byin rlabs can 'dug pa mjal/ snyan dar dang dkar me sogs mchod

pa rgyas par phul/ klu kha stod kyi yon bdag rnams kyis byang bu bsngo smon gyi rten sogs ster cha shin tu rgya che ba/ mar 'phyur/ tshwa bal gtso bor gyur pa ci rigs byung
zhing / spyan legs kyi byams pa mjal/ snyan shal mchod pa rgyas par phul/ klu kha stod du zhag gnyis thogs par dbang gi rigs kyang mang ba sogs so so'i 'dod pa bsgrubs/
sde pa lha khang bas 'bod mi gnang byung ba ltar phyin te zhag gcig bsdad/ gzhis len yang dag mdzad cing zhal ngo rnams la tshe dbang dang / gur drag sogs dbang kyang phul/
tsha mo lha ldan dang sde pa yum sras bcas par ster cha'ang byas/ rgyal smad grwa rigs rnams dang / rgyal stod yon bdag sogs tshang mas dar ras/ mar 'phyur/ gos snam sogs
ster cha byed mi mang bar byung / dge slong mchog ldan gyi spyil bur bos te gzhis len dang / gzhis mis gson byang sogs gang legs mdzad/ lug lhas gser gyi lha khang mjal
te snyan dar mchod 'bul dngos bshams dang yid sprul gyis mchod cing / bstan 'gro'i phan bde spel phyir smon lam btab/ rgyal stod smad du mang ja bsngo rten bcas phul zhing
bskyod lam rgyan drung pheb ste gzhis su 'ong dgos tshul gsung ba ltar phyin/ zhal ngo rnams dang g.yog rigs bcas par tshe dbang phul/ phyi nyin snga bar dgon gnas nas
zhabs drung dbon rin po che dpon slob rnams bsu bar pheb pa dang mjal/ khams phyogs nas a li chos rjes dbus 'grul ba mang bar 'byor zhing / chos rjes cho ga stong rtsa
mdzad pa grol bar gtugs par bcas 'phral 'byor dgos tshul gsung ba bzhin gzhis nas bskyod de dgon gnas su 'byor 'phral tshogs dbur phyin/ gos dar/ rol

mo mang ba/ mchod rdzas/ rta khal/ ja sogs dngos po'i brgya 'bul mdzad par dge ba rdzogs byang du bsngos/ chos rje dpon slob la gzhis len 'dod chos sogs dpon rin po ches gang
legs mdzad 'dug cing / pho brang chen por mjal kha zhu bar 'byon rtsis 'dug par mgron gnyer rin chen bcas rdzong bda' byas/ rgyal smad pa'i dgon lag ral lung gi bla ma'i
khur len dge slong mchog ldan gyis mdzad pa nas sngar dang mi 'dra ba'i gra gtsang zhing dar rgyas che ba yod 'dug cing / mang ja dang tshogs dung bsngo rten bcas sprad/
bla ma mchog ldan gyis tshogs 'don du bla mchod gsar rtsom dgos gsung pa ltar bsgrig 'dun khas len kyang byas/ tshe gsum gyi sras mo dpon pa dgos yum sras gzims shag tu
gnas gshis stabs lha sar zhu sgug la pheb par phan cha gang drag dang gang ci'i bkod pa/ lo 'di nang du sde pa thon pa'i sar byon par pha ming gi dod lta bur byas/ bla
ma bsam 'phel dang / chos mdzad ngag dbang grags pa gnyis gzims khang gong du kye rdor gzhi bsnyen gyi mtshams la yod par phyin/ brda don gsal ba dang / brda chig brgyud
sogs zab chos kha shas byas shing / bsnyen pa'i rigs snga phyir thengs gsum bzhi tsam phyin te bslab cha gegs sel kyang byas/ sde dge dbon po dpon g.yog rnams la rta bsu
dang gzhis len gzabs par byas/ tshogs su mang ja dang gser sogs 'gyed sna kha shas gtong bar mdzad song zhing / gling khams tshan la'ang mgo 'don bdag rkyen che bar gnang
song / ngor pa'i grwa rigs la song bas de tsam mdzad pa dka' na'ang / nged rang nas gang cir phan cha byas

pa'i stabs su 'dug /nged rang la gser/ ja/ rta drel/ mdzo g.yag sogs ster sbyin dpangs mtho bar mdzad cing / dge rtsa byang chub mchog tu bsngo ba'i smon lam yang dag par byas/
rjes gnang sogs 'dod chos phul zhing / pho brang chen por gong sa chen po yas phyin gyi mjal kha zhu bar pheb pa'i/ bslab bya dang rogs ram la mdzod pa lhun grub can
rdzong bda' byas shing bdag rkyen bka' drin che ba gnang 'dug /tshur 'byor 'phral bde mchog bong zhal can sogs dbang dang rjes gnang gi rigs mang bar byas te gtsang du pheb/
rab byung bsnyen rdzogs sogs rgyun gyi brel ba rnams dkyus bzhin dang / pho brang chen por mjal kha zhu bar phyin/ mjal kha rgyas shing bdag rkyen gnang sbyin shin tu
rgyas par bka' drin bskyangs/ de rjes bod khams bstan 'gro yongs kyi bsod nams kyis ma 'chun pas thams cad mkhyen gzigs rgyal dbang lnga pa chen po re zhig gzugs sku'i
bkod pa chos kyi dbyings su mnyam par gzhag pa'i tshul bstan to/ /sa dbang gser gyi 'khor los sgyur ba chen pos 'dzam gling spyi dang / khyad par kha ba ri pa rnams kyi bsod
nams kyi zhing du rigs brgya'i khyab bdag lnga pa chen po'i dgongs pa rdzogs thabs dang / 'phags mchog 'jig rten dbang phyug slar yang 'gro ba mtha' dag gi skyabs mgon
du pheb pa khams gsum chos kyi rgyal po mchog gi sprul sku drug pa chen po'i zhabs pad bskal brgyar brtan pa'i phyir sngon byon chos rgyal mes dbon gyi mdzad pa dang mtshungs
pa'i zhabs brtan lha khang chen mo zhes gandho la 'dzam gling rgyan gcig bzhengs pa bka' drin che ba'i rten gtso lnga pa chen po'i

sku gdung yid bzhin nor bu bzhugs pa'i lha khang rnams kyi rten mjal du phyin skabs/ sgo nang du phran bu slebs 'phral gser gdung rin po che las tshe chu babs pa nged dpon
slob bco lnga skor gyis lce thog tu myong chog pa byung ba ni sku dngos su bzhugs pa dang mtshungs par 'di phyi thams cad du brtse ba chen po nas mi 'dor ba'i brdar sems
shing / snyan shal dang mchod pa sna lnga dngos bshams dang yid sprul gyi mchod sprin dang bcas maNDal rgyas pa/ gsol 'debs/ smon lam yid rtse gcig tu btab/ de bzhin byung
tshul sku gnyer dbon thar rgyas pas gong du bsnyan 'bul zhus 'dug pas thugs shin tu dges par gnang 'dug /dgon gnas su 'byor te bcu bzhi dus chen thog chos skyong sku khog
gsar pheb la snyan shal legs cha'i sku chas spyan gzigs sogs rgyas par phul zhing / lung bstan ci rigs zhus/ sku khog a gsum lo snga mar dus kyi chos nyid du gyur skabs
bu rgan pa'i rmi lam du nged rang gis btang ba yin zer bla ma mgron gnyer byung ste sku chas rnams rtsis long zer ba zhig byung 'dug pa dang / nged rang gi rmi lam du chos
skyong chen po'i sku chas rgyas pa dang bcas bu rgan sar sku pheb ste/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa rgyas/ dge 'dun gyi sde dar/ gnas su dbang phyug gi mtsho 'khyil/ don
brag ri dbang gi tshe chu dang gsang ba'i lung bstan bcas dgyes tshor chen por mdzad pa zhig byung bar/ lo gcig bar 'gying gi rnam pas sku ma phebs par 'phen yul nang gi
yas mas nas yin zer ba'i khog zhugs mang ba zhig byung kyang bdag med du bzhag nas/ sku rten 'di khar khrus dang gtsang sbra/ sku

chas gra sgrig /gsol kha dang 'byon dgos pa'i dam bsgrags byas pa thog tu khel bas tshang ma yid ches pa'i gnas su gyur to/ /dus chen khag rnams dang dgon lag gi phyogs 'gro
dkyus ltar byas/ lam 'bras kyi chos ra tshugs/ me glang lor lo gsar dang lam 'bras grub nas a li chos rje dpon slob rnams la 'dod chos ci rigs dang / gang cir sngar 'jags
kyi gong sa chen por bka' shog rin po che zhus te phyir rdzong byas/ snga sor nas gong ma khu dbon gyi gser sku zh-ig bzhengs 'dun yod kyang zin med kyi bya bas g.yeng
ste ma grub par/ 'di lo zhabs brtan lha khang gi dbu mdzad can bal po shin tu mkhas pa bzhi bos te las grwa btsugs par zangs lhas nyag gi khal bco lnga skor dang / gser
zho nyi shu rtsa grangs bcas pa'i rgyu char/ gong ma khu dbon gyi sku sor bcu drug gi tshad tsam dang / thub dbang grong khyer ma li tshugs mda' gang lhag tsam gyi rgyab
yol bcas pa/ dbon rin po che dang mdzod pas nan gyis bzhengs dgos tshul byung ba bzhin nged rang gi 'dra 'bag kyang tshad bla ma gnyis dang mtshungs pa bzhengs par lugs rgyug
cing bzo bkod legs pa rang byon lta bur grub ste/ bal po rnams la zhag bco lnga skor nas ster sbyin tshan grangs dang / ston mo rgyas pa re/ rgyun phog gzab cing zla
ba gsum tsam nas legs par grub pa'i yon shin tu rgyas par bcas bzo bo rnams rdzong bda' byas/ gza' tshes dge bar nged khu dbon/ ban tshang / nang skor sum cu skor dang bcas
pas dgyes mdzad rdo rje'i cho ga la brten pa'i sta gon bcas rab gnas byas te mchod sprin rgya mtsho'i dbus su bzhugs su gsol/ grub 'phral mtshams la

bsdad skabs nad ro langs te 'chi bar thug pa zhig byung bar/ nyan po nas grub pa'i dbang phyug chos rje rin po che gdan drangs te tshe dbang sogs rkyen sel gyi rigs mang ba/
tshogs chen du bka' 'gyur sogs rim gro phon che ba/ gzungs 'dus dang bka' thang rgyun 'don/ chos gter gling pa rnams kyis mkha' 'gro sun zlog sogs mdos rigs mang ba/ ban
tshang rnams kyis bskang ba/ lha mor phrin bcol gyi sger bskang brgya rtsa sogs ci rigs bsgrubs shing / spom thag la nged rang gi dril bu bcas chas ka 'gangs che ba kha
shas phul/ dgon khag tu mang ja sogs rim gro mang tsam dbon rin po che'i bslab ston ltar mdzod pa dang / gnyer pa gnyis bcas nas bsgrubs shing / 'tsho mdzad rta mgrin tshe
ring gis gsos sman dang / nad g.yog bsod nams rin chen dang / chos mdzad spun gyis cag thon dang / dpon rin po che sku mched/ chos rje rin po che/ mdzod pa/ ban tshang
slob dpon bsam 'phel/ tsha bo chos mdzad/ dpon 'tsho mdzad/ gsang sbug nas tshong dpon gnyis dga' sogs kyis rten 'byung dang / yun ring 'tsho dgos pa'i bslab ston yang yang
nan gyis mdzad pa dang / ban tshang / nang skor/ nang bzan a bo/ rta mgrin phrin las sogs yon bdag re gnyis/ dgon khag chos gzhis khag gi mi ser bcas ltos bcas tshang
mas che 'byor chung 'byor lta bu'i dngos po'i maNDal ci rigs bcas ring 'tsho'i rten 'byung mdzad pas zla shas nas rim bder gyur skabs/ zhabs drung dbon rin po che'i mnal

lam du dpal ldan lha mos nged rang bar chad las rgyal ba'i gtang rag tu bskang ba rgyas pa zhig dgos tshul bskul ba byung 'dug pa bzhin/ zla ba brgyad pa'i nang du sngar gyi
gsol kha'i steng du mngon rtogs bstod pa dang / mchod pa gsar brtsams bcas chog bsgrigs byas te ban tshang rnams kyi zhag bdun gyi ring lo bstar sgrub mchod lta bu'i tshul
du gsar 'dzugs byas shing / na skabs mkha' 'gro sun zlog mdzad pa'i nyin 'ja' tshon snying po'i gter ma'i gnam lcags kyi rdo rje rtse lnga pa zhig lag tu byung ba ni
bar chad zhi zhing rten 'brel sgrig pa'i ltas su 'dug /mkha' 'gro bsu bzlog gi phyag dpe g.yar po zhus skabs sum ldan rdo rje 'dzin pa dge slong rin po ches rten 'byung gi
gnang sbyin gzabs pa gnang ba dang lhan du rgyas par mdzad/ ston nyag bre nas 'bul dpon bla ma mkhyen rab phun tshogs byon par rta bsu dang gzhis len gzabs par byas shing
/ ja phon che ba/ mdzo g.yag sogs rtsis sprod rgyas par byung / rtses bzang bla ma grongs pa'i mchod cha dang chas ka 'dug pas kyang sprod/ dge ba rdzogs byang du bsngo
ba'i smon lam yang dag btab/ cho ga stong rtsa'i tshogs dbur dbon rin po che pheb cing rta legs pa dang dre'u bcas phul 'dug /khri 'du nas bla ma chos mdzad kyis 'bul skyel
du shes rab pa can 'byor zhing ja sogs 'bul skyel rgyas pa dang / rten 'byung du 'bul ba kyang logs su 'byor/ 'di skabs rmi lam du bande gzhon nu zhig gis rdzogs pa'i
sangs rgyas la 'khor dgra bcom pa'i tshogs kyis bskor ba dang / byang nas rgyal po chen po rnam thos sras 'khor dang bcas pa'ang pheb yod pas pheb bsu'i grabs dang mjal
khar shog zer/ phyin pas gtso bo bcom ldan 'das nyid dgung

lo bcu drug bcu bdun tsam lon pa sprul pa'i sku'i cha lugs dbu'i gtsug tor dang bcas pa 'khor rnams kyang chos gos rnam pa gsum gyis brgyan pa du mas bskor ba zhig dang mjal
ba na phyag grangs med pa btsal te byin rlabs zhus pas dad mos kyi snang ba dpag tu med pa byung zhing / rjes su snye thang nas mjal kha zhu dus khams gsum chos kyi rgyal
po mchog gi sprul pa'i sku drug pa chen po dang mjal ba'i tshe sngar gyi rmi lam dang sku'i dbyibs shin tu mthun par 'dug pas rmi lam la nges shes rnyed/ zla ba dgu pa'i
nang du pho brang chen po nas sa dbang gser gyi 'khor los sgyur ba chen po'i lung gis skyabs mgon lnga pa chen po nyid sku'i bkod pa dgyes mdzad rdo rje'i thugs kar bsdu
ba'i tshul bstan kyang / slar yang rigs brgya'i khyab bdag mchog gi sprul pa'i sku drug pa chen por bstan te mi ring bar lugs brgya'i sgo 'phar phye pa'i gnas pho brang
chen po ri bo gru 'dzin du chibs kha bsgyur te bstan 'gro'i dpung gnyen dam par zhabs zung mi 'jigs seng khrir bkod pa'i dga' ston legs 'bul gyi gra sgrig bka' drin che
ba'i gtam tshor 'phral 'gro ba spyi dang khyad par bdag cag mgon med pa rnams kyi skyabs mgon du zhabs pad yun ring du brtan pa zhig 'ong bsams kyang / de lta bu 'ong ba
bsam sems dran med lta bur gyur kyang / legs par bsam tshe zhing khams su pheb nas lo de tsam song 'dug kyang 'khor los sgyur ba chen po'i bka' drin gyis sems can thams
cad rdzogs ldan ltar du byams pas skyong bar gnang zhing / khyad par mchog gi sprul sku rin po che'ang sku tshad longs dang mjal bas gus zhabs pa'ang de bar ma shi ba bsod
nams che bsam zhing gzugs

bzhis 'gro thub pa rang gis gdeng khel med kyang mjal 'dod sems kyis ma tshugs pas snye thang du zhabs phyir bcar chog pa'i zhu yig 'bul ba dang gtam snyan legs 'bul bcas dbon
rin po che pheb par mjal kha dang bdag rkyen bka' drin che bar gnang zhing / bslab ston la chos rje rang sku bgres pas 'o brgyal ba 'dra'ang / pheb bzhed che na snga
sor gzhan mar khas len ma byas kyang / de kha gzhan dang ma 'dra bas de kha mdzad chog pheb pas tshes pa bcu dgu la nged khu dbon sprul sku rin po che bcas sum cu skor pheb
bsur lha gdan sprul pa'i gandho la chen por 'byor/ phyi nyin 'khor los sgyur ba chen po'i mjal kha zhus/ slob bshad sogs kyi bka' 'dri rgyas par gnang / mgron khang du
rna ba'i bcud len sgrogs pa gnang skabs rten skal du khams gsum chos kyi rgyal po'i sku 'dra'i gdung tsha bka' drin bskyangs/ nyer bzhi'i phyi dro na so'i stabs stod lung
bar snga 'gros su phyin/ nyer lnga'i nyin shin tu snga bar mkhar nag gi 'phrang sner pheb bsgugs zhus skabs mchod yon gnyis kyis chibs rags pa chen po'ang dog por byed
nus pa'i mang la rgyas pa/ tshangs pa dang brgya byin kyang zil gyis gnon nus pa'i gzi byin phun sum tshogs pa dang ldan par chibs kha bsgyur ba'i zhabs phyir bcar dus mig
mthong mi bzod cing bsam las 'das pa zhig tu gyur cing / nor bu sgang gi bzhugs sgar gyi phan tsam du mchod yon bzhugs khrir pheb cing / bla ma/ slob dpon/ rgyal rigs/
dbon rigs sogs/ mdor na 'dzam gling gi ser skya drag zhan gyi skye bo stong gsum gyi 'jig rten khengs nus pa lta bus gang bar gyur pa na/ rgyang tsam nas khams gsum 'gro
ba'i skyabs mgon rgyal ba'i dbang po thams cad mkhyen pa chen

po zas gtsang gi sras 'khor dgra bcom pa'i tshogs kyis bskor ba la mchod rdzas du mas mchod pa'i lha rnams kyis gang ba lta bus blta bas mi ngoms pa'i tshogs bcas pheb par
zhal mjal zhus shing / bzhugs sgar du phyin te/ mjal rten nged khu dbon so so nas phul zhing skyabs mgon chen po yas phyin gyi mjal khar bcar skabs phran bu rang gi kha btags
shin tu che ba zhig bcas ngos kyi bdag ma shi gong du mchog sprul rin po che pheb pas 'gro ba spyi dang / khyad par bdag sogs rnams thugs nas ma dor ba bka' drin che
tshul zhus par spyan hur gyis yun ring du gzigs shing zhal gyi dkyil 'khor 'dzum par gyur/ bzhugs gral du mkhan po thams cad kyi mgor nged rang la gdan mtho ba'i steng du
'jog pa bka' drin che ba sogs gzhan dang mi 'dra bar brtse bas bskyangs/ gsol ja bzhi'i ring 'khor los sgyur ba chen pos rna ba'i bcud len dang mthun par gsung bshad dbyangs
can mgrin pa'i dbyangs kyi khengs pa 'phrog nus pa zhig bka' drin bskyangs shing / ston mo dang dga' ston gyi bye brag ji snyed pas 'gro ba rnams dga' bde'i dpal yon
du 'khod par gnang bas rgan po'ang blo'i re ba yongs su rdzogs par gyur to/ /de nub brag sna dgon du phyin/ zhag gsum tsam bsdad ring dge slong phan bdes gzhis len rgyas
pa dang / rogs dan ci shes mdzad cing / 'phrad mi mang ba'ang byung / rjes gnang sogs 'dod chos kyang ci rigs byas shing dgon par mang ja dang / mkhan por bsngo rten bcas
phul te phyir log pas rang gnas su 'byor/ sog yul nas chos rje bstan 'dzin nor bu dpon slob rnams 'byor bar gzhis len rgyas par byas shing /

zhag shas nas dngul/ gos dar/ rol mo/ mchod cha sogs rtsis sprod rgya che bar byung zhing / tshogs chen du mang ja/ 'gyed/ nged rang khu dbon la bsngo rten bcas tshogs gsog
par mdzad cing / dge ba byang chub tu bsngos/ pho brang chen por mjal kha zhu bar rdzong bda' byas/ 'di lo nas bzung rnam sras kyi sgrub pa bstod chen rgyas pa bcas zhag
lnga pa zhig kyang ji srid bstan pa rin po che ma gnas bar du 'dzugs srol gtod/ zla ba phyi ma'i nang du nged rang khu dbon bzhi bcas bzhi bcu skor gyis legs 'bul zhu bar
sro brgyud de rim gyis ra sa 'phrul snang gi sde chen por slebs/ nyer lnga'i nyin pho brang chen por chibs kha bsgyur ba'i zhabs phyir snye thang du rgyan drung rdzong
bda' byas/ skyed tshal klu sdings su nged khu dbon gsum rgyun gyi dbang po'i 'dus tshogs bcas kyis mjal dar bcas pheb bsu dang phyag dbang la phyin/ phyi nyin zhabs drung
dbon rin po che dang rgyan drung bcas dpon slob mang tsam gyis chibs bsu dang / dge 'dun sum brgya skor gyis ser phreng zhus/ phyi nyin mkhar rtse khul dang lhan du legs
'bul zhus par dngul srang bdun cu don gnyis bslab ston du pheb kyang / nged rang nas brgyad cu tham par skor ba'i 'bul tshan dang / spyi so nas bla khag las tshan bcas tshang
mas bslab ston ltar zhus/ gdan bzos dang ston mo rgyas par bka' drin bskyangs/ sger mjal du gong sa chen po ni 'gro ba spyi dang / khyad par phran bur bka' drin gzhal
du ma mchis pa yin pa dang / sa dbang gser gyi 'khor los sgyur ba ni skyabs mgon chen po dag zhing du gshegs pa'i tshul bstan cing / mchog gi sprul pa'i sku sku na ma
phebs par du 'gro ba spyi dang / khyad par

phran bur spyan rgyang gzhan dang mi 'dra ba zhig yin pa nas dngos po yod na gang yod phul kyang ches pa'i gnas su gyur pa gnas yin kyang phran bu tshos mkhos chung bas che
bar ma 'byor par/ rigs brgya'i khyab bdag khams gsum chos kyi rgyal po drug pa chen po'i sku zhabs su/ sku'i rten du mgon po tshe dang ye shes dpag tu med pa'i sku lcags
sdong ma gser zangs las grub pa/ gsung gi rten du dus 'khor pusti sa skya pa mkhas pa gzhon du dar gyi thugs dam rten/ thugs kyi rten du gu gu zhal gyi rnam rgyal mchod
rten kun mkhyen bkra shis rnam rgyal gyi thugs dam rten/ dzhe khyim gyi ting shag nyi ma tshangs dbyangs gdan sa mthil nas zhwa dmar bas bzhes pa/ za dam li ma lha khang
nas byung ba sra btags kyi sku brnyan/ 'gyur med rdo rjes mtshan pa'i gos bzang bsgrigs kyi bzhugs gdan/ gser srang gang / dngul srang bcu yod kyi maNDal dang / dngul srang
bcu/ kha btags kyi rtags ris la mchod pa'i lha mo brgyad kyis mtshan pa sogs dgu/ sman rtse yug dgu/ byang dar yug brgyad/ gos padma mthon mthing sogs yug legs pa lnga/
rta legs pa gnyis/ ja nag po 'khor drug sogs lnga/ rgya khro che ba/ khrab/ gzhan yang dar ras/ snam bu bcas khyon dgu tshan dgu dang / 'khor los sgyur ba chen po'i sku
zhabs su tshe dpag med kyi sku brnyan/ gos kha thi dang hus bsgrigs kyis bzhugs gdan/ gser srang gang / dngul srang bcu yod kyi maNDal/ dngul srang bcu/ kha btags che legs
bdun/ sman rtse yug bdun/ byang dar yug bdun/ gos yug legs pa gnyis/ rta/ khrab/ ja nag po 'khor

drug sogs 'khor drug lnga/ gzhan yang dar ras/ snam bu sogs kyi dgu tshan bdun bcas sger mjal dpangs mtho ba zhus par/ mjal kha bdag rkyen sogs shin tu legs pa brtse bas gzigs/
'gro kun bsod nams dpal las legs grub pa'i/ /'gro ba'i skyabs gcig pad dkar 'chang ba de/ /'gro ba'i dpung gnyen ched du slar yang ni/ /'gro ba'i zhing du sprul pa'i
zlos gar bsgyur/ /'dzam gling sa yi lte ba rdo rje gdan/ /rang byon 'phags pa'i gzhal yas khang chen por/ /pheb ste zhabs zung 'khor lo'i re khA can/ /slar bcas 'gro ba
yongs kyi cod pan du/ /bkod pa'i ngo mtshar gtam gyi phreng ba ni/ /ngag la dbang thob tshangs pa'i sras kyis kyang / /brgya phrag bskal par brjod kyang mi lang na/ /bdag
'dra byis pa'i blo yis ci zhig nus/ /a ho tshe rabs du mar rjes bzung ba'i/ /khams gsum 'gro ba kun gyi skyabs gcig pu'i/ /zhal dkyil slar yang bdag gis mthong ba ni/ /dpag
med bsod nams bsags pa'i 'bras bur nges/ /zhag shas bsdad de dge slong rin po cher tshe dpag med dwangs ma bcud 'dren sogs 'dod chos kha shas zhus te sro brgyud dgon
gnas su slebs/ de sngon nas nad ros yang yang 'tshe ba'i gzugs bzhi shin tu mi thong ba zhig yod kyang / gong sa chen po dang mjal nas bzung byin rlabs kyis na tshod rim
slebs ma gtogs nad gzhi cher med pas gzugs bzhi thong du song ba zhig byung / rtse gdong nas zhabs drung rin po che gong sa yas phyin mjal khar pheb zhor rgyun gyi dbang
por chibs kha sgyur bar chibs bsur rgyan drung gis gtsos chos sde chen po'i bla khag las tshan bcas mang ba dang / dge 'dun

sum brgya skor gyis ser phreng gis pheb bsu sogs shin tu rgyas par zhus shing / nged rang nas rta legs pa sogs 'bul dpangs mtho ba'ang phul/ ston mo sbom 'bul zhus/ bla khag
/spyi so/ las tshan/ khams tshan khag sogs nas kyang gang 'byor gyi 'bul ba rgya che bar zhus song / yar chibs kha sgyur skabs chibs skyel sogs rgyas par zhus/ chos sde
chen po'i dus chen khag rnams grub nas sprul pa'i sku gtsang du pheb par pheb skyel sogs sngar ltar byas/ sog yul du chos rje'i gdan sar tsha ba mkhyen rab phun tshogs dang
/ dge 'dun spel so'i thog tu a mdo bla ma dbu mdzad bcas rdzong bda' byas/ lo mjug gi rim gro rnams sngar ltar dang dgon khag gi chos ra sogs dbon nas mdzad/ sa stag
lor lo gsar dang / dbyar mtshams la bsdad skabs nad ro cung zad 'phar bar rim gro 'phrod bsten sogs byas pas yar ldan du gyur/ zla ba bzhi pa'i nang du sa skya nas 'jam mgon
sa skya pa chen po gong sa yas phyin gyi mjal khar pheb par gung thang du phyag dbang zhu bar phyin/ bzhes spro sha rtsam sogs sbom 'bul dpangs mtho ba dang / 'gyur med
rdo rje rgya gram gyis mtshan pa'i stan dkar/ gser dngul gyi maNDal/ rgya sil legs pa sogs dgu tshan kha shas kyi 'bul ba rgyas par phul/ bka' dbang / phyag mdud/ dam
rdzas/ gnang sbyin sogs shin tu legs par bka' drin bskyangs shing / gang ci'i snyan 'bul dang bka' 'phros zhib par byung / phyi nyin pheb skyel zhus te gung thang gi zhang
g.yul las rgyal ba'i sku brnyan gyi gtsos mchod khang rnams

zhib par mjal/ snyan dar dang mchod pa rgyas par phul/ bstan 'gro'i don du smon lam yid tshim par btab/ sri gcod 'bum par bskor ba kha shas kyang byas/ tshur lam bde chen gyi
gnas tshang du bsdad par grub thob rin po che'i sku yin zer ba zhig 'dug pa lag tu blangs par stobs 'phrog dbang po'i sku gnyan lo chen po'i phyag nas ma yin nges shig
'dug par mtshon cha zhig bslu yon tu btang nas bslu gtong dgos tshul labs par/ los 'bul zer sprad byung ba rten 'brel legs par sems/ rang gnas su 'byor te nyag bre'i 'bul
dpon ba rdzong bda' mdzad pa'i bkod pa dang / chu bzang gi chu tshan la phyin par phar phyin yon bdag rnams kyis gzhis len dang ster cha rgyas par byung / gong sa skyabs
mgon chen po dpal ldan 'bras spungs su chibs kha bsgyur te tshad ma'i gsan sbyong bka' drin bskyangs pa'i legs 'bul du zhabs drung dbon rin po che pheb par bdag rkyen sogs
legs pa bka' drin bskyangs 'dug /zla ba bdun pa'i nang du de sngon nas gsang sbug tshong dpon lags kyis tsandan dmar po gnang bar/ mdzod pa lhun grub kyi sger nas yon
bdag byas te/ dpal ldan lha mo'i sku mda' gang tsam zhig bzhengs pa dang / dbon rin po che dpon slob lha sar pheb skabs bar khang nas rnam sras kyi sku brgya rtsa brgyad
grub par gser dngul lji ba gsol tu btang ste/ nged khu dbon/ mtshungs med chos rje rin po che/ ban tshang sum cu skor bcas kyis rab gnas legs par byas te zhag bdun gyi ring
gsol kha bskang ba sogs rgyas par byas/ sde dge nas legs 'bul du tshong dpon can btang 'dug par dpon po so so'i phyag bris 'dug pa

blangs/ gtsang nas dbon po bos te legs 'bul du rdzong bda' byas/ zla ba brgyad pa'i nang du zhabs drung dbon rin po ches tshogs chen du dpal rdo rje phreng ba'i dbang gzims
khang 'og ma pa rnams kyi thugs bzhed ltar zhag bco brgyad par rgyas pa zhig mdzad/ ma yum sku skyes 'bul skyel du dpon gnyer kun dga' bkra shis rdzong bda' mdzad pa 'byor/
phyag bris nang bzhin rtsis sprod rgyas par byung / tshogs chen dang phyogs 'dus tshor lam 'bras kyi chos ra zhig dang rab byung / bsnyen rdzogs/ 'dod chos/ byang bu/
bsngo smon/ dus chen khag sogs rgyun gyi bya ba rnams dang / dgon khag gi chos ra sogs dbon gyis mdzad/ sa yos lor lo gsar dang / gong sa chen po yas phyin bdag sogs 'gro
ba rnams kyi mgon du zhabs pad yun ring du brtan pa'i phyir zhabs brtan 'bul bar/ nged khu dbon/ bla khag /las tshan/ 'dus pa'i tshogs dang bcas pa phyin par/ nged rang
na so'i stabs kyis mda' skor la phyin/ dbon rin po che dpon slob rnams lar pheb pa'i lam du sde pa drung yig lags kyis zhabs brtan dus tshes kyis gtugs pas 'phral 'byor
dgos tshul gyi phyag bris gnang 'dug par/ dgon gnas nged rang bcas kyi sar bang chen so sor btang 'dug pa 'byor 'phral phyin pas/ lha sar sleb dus 'bul tshan sogs tshang
ma 'grigs pa byung 'dug pas/ sang snga char zhabs brtan du phyin/ spyi 'bul la nged rang nas dgu tshan dpangs mtho ba lnga/ gzims khang nas lnga/ spyi sos lnga/ mjal dar
legs pa gnyis re bcas shin tu rgyas pa dang / sger mjal du nged rang nas dgu tshan gsum re phul/ gdan

bzos ston mo sogs gzhan dang mi 'dra bar bka' drin bskyangs/ byams gling mkhan rin po cher rnal 'byor ma'i byin rlabs dgos gsung bar phul/ lugs gnyis kyi bka' 'phros kyang
zhib par byung / cho 'phrul zla ba'i tshes bcu bzhi'i rgyal phur 'grub sbyor thog gnas brtan chen po 'jam dbyangs grags pa'i sku zhabs nas dbon rin po che bsnyen par rdzogs
pa dge slong gi sdom pa legs par stsal ba'i phyag phyir mdzod pa/ ban tshang slob dpon bsam 'phel dang / 'bul dpon chos grags rnams kyis bsnyen rdzogs zhus song / de bstun
nged rang gis kyang pho brang du phyin te mchod mjal zhus par/ gong sa chen po sku mtshams stabs mchod sdong chen mo'i thugs mjal ji ltar 'gab zhus par/ chos rje gzhan
dang ma 'dra bas khu dbon de kha byas chog tshul bka' drin bskyangs pas mchod mjal rnams shin tu legs par byung / dge slong rin po cher gang ci'i bslab ston zhib par zhus/
zur chas dpangs mtho ba dang / dge 'dun rnams la zhag bcu'i ring sku rim bka' drin bskyangs par/ yon sogs bka' drin che bar gnang 'dug /rim gyis bskyod de gnyan lo chen
po'i bzhugs gnas me 'bar gyi gtsug lag khang 'brom stod du phyin/ bskang ba spyan gzigs sogs rgyas par phul zhing / rgyal bstan spyi dang bye brag gi bstan pa dar zhing
/ 'gro ba rnams la bde skyid 'bad med du 'byung ba'i phrin bcol byas skabs/ yum chen bzhis gtso bo'i sku la dngos su bskor ba byed pa sogs kyi mthong snang shin tu gsal
bar byung / dgon lag shab tu phyin/ bla mas gzhis len rgyas par mdzad cing / zhag gnyis bsdad ring

mda' phyogs kyi yon bdag rnams sprin bzhin 'dus te yul babs dang bstun pa'i ster cha yang dag byung zhing / mang ja/ bsngo rten/ yon bdag so sor ster cha sogs gang la gang
'tshams byas/ rgyun gyi dbang por 'byor 'phral nad ro ya mar babs pa lta bu'i shin tu thub zhig na bar/ nyan po nas mtshungs med chos rje rin po che gdan drangs te bka' dbang
bsu bzlog sogs rkyen sel gnang ba dang / tshogs chen gyis bka' 'gyur/ ban tshang gis bskang ba/ dgon khag so sor mang ja/ sngags pas mdos rigs sogs rim gro rnams dbon
rin po ches zhal bkod mdzad cing / 'tsho mdzad don 'grub kyis gsol sman sogs gzhan dang ma 'dra bas rim bder gyur/ 'tsho mdzad sku mched 'di gnyis nged rang rnams kyi bsod
