nams las grub pa lta bu'i las 'brel gyis phan thogs che ba'i sku drin gzhal du ma mchis pa las/ gzugs bzhir dpags na da tsam sdod par dka' ba zhig gi gnas su 'dug /sgom
khang 'di bla ma gong ma na rim gyis bzhugs gnas yin par ma zad/ gong ma chos kyi spyan ldan gyi thugs 'dun gzhan dang mi 'dra ba'i gnas yin pas bdag rkyen dgos gras yin
kyang / bar skabs bla ma sogs las tshan rnams khur bsam chung ba dang / sa khad 'gyangs pa bcas nyams chag che zhing / khang pa'ang zhig ral ches pa sems kyis ma bzod
par dbon rin po cher mkhar las mdzad dgos pa'i bkod khyab bcas pheb par gra sgrig las bkod sogs kyi zhabs phyi dge slong chos mdzad dang / mgron gnyer rab 'phel/ gnyer pa
rgyal po bcas kyis byas shing / btsun ma rnams

dang mkhar sngong gi mi lag sogs kyis gz-ims phug tshogs khang / bla yer skor/ 'bum pa rta lam sogs/ mdor na zhig gsos dgos gras gang yod dang / gsar bzo bcas tshang ma zla
ba phyed gnyis kyi khongs su legs par grub 'dug cing / zla ba drug pa'i nang du shar bar tshe sgrub cig dang sbrags blta rtog dang rab gnas la phyin/ dgon gnas 'di me 'bar
gyi gtsug lag khang dang khyad par med pa'i dam can chos srung rnams sprin bzhin 'du ba'i gnas mchog dam pa yin gshis/ gong sa chen po yas phyin gyi dbus bstan 'dzin gyi
skyes bu dam pa rnams zhabs pad bskal brgya'i bar du brtan cing / rgyal bstan spyi dang / khyad par rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab yab sras kyi bstan dang de 'dzin rnams kyi
bar chad zhi phyir/ ma hA kA la stobs 'phrog dbang po'i sku rten du gnyan lo chen po'i phyag nas ma dang / 'gro ba'i mgon po chos rgyal 'phags pa'i thugs dam rten bram
gzugs kyi sku gnyis/ gnyan lo'i shang mtshal las grub pa'i sku thang / gsung rten be'u bum ha la nag po dang / dam rdzas khri rdo/ thugs rten 'ja' tshon snying po'i gter
ma gnam lcags rdo rje/ yon tan gyi rten du mtshan ldan thod pa gter bum khyad 'phags/ phrin las kyi rten du sa skya pa sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros kyi sku phur/ gzhan
yang rten thug go mtshon sogs spyan gzigs dang bcas pa legs par bsgrigs te phyin skabs bsang / dar 'phyar/ rol mo sogs shin tu rgyas par byed 'dug /zhag bco lnga skor bsdad/
tshogs khang / mgon khang / sgrub phug sogs la shis brjod kyi me tog 'thor/ rten 'brel stabs sgrub

phug tu zhag bdun gyi ring tshe sgrub cig byas pas/ gnas de gzhan las khyad par du 'phags pa zhig 'dug /btsun ma rnams la 'dod chos/ mang ja/ ja 'gyed kyi ster cha sogs yang
dag byas/ tsha bo chos mdzad spun bcas/ btsun ma rnams kyis rten 'byung tshe sbyin yid bzhin 'khor lo'i cho ga dang 'brel bar dngos po dar ras/ snam bu/ 'bru cha sogs rgyas
par byung / dbyar mjal dang / sger mjal/ bzhes spro sogs gzhis len ci shes gang drag lta bu byas song / yon bdag lcab pa sogs 'phrad mi mang ba'ang byung / 'ong nyin
btsun ma rnams kyis la rtser thab skyel du byung bar dgon pa'i sgrig lam slob gnyer sogs mthar phyin dgos pa'i bkod pa dpyis phyin pa dang / bsngags mdud/ ster cha rgyas
par byas/ gzhis su phyin te zhag gnyis bsdad ring yon bdag g.yog r-igs sogs 'phrad mi mang bar byung / sa sbug tu 'ong dgos tshul byung ba bzhin zhag lnga bsdad ring gsol
chas sbom 'bul dang / so sos gzhis len che 'byor chung 'byor gyi gang yod chal chil du gyur cing / spyod khrid kyi chos ra dang / spyi dbang sogs 'dod chos rags rim byas/
dge slong mchog ldan bcas rgyal smad grwa rigs/ grub rgyal sde pa/ yon bdag sogs 'du tshogs shin tu che bas sha mar/ snam bu/ dar ras/ 'bru cha sogs ster cha ci rigs dang
/ btsun ma rnams kyis nas sran gtso bor gyur pa'i 'bul ba shin tu rgyas par byung / sa sbug tu 'byor/ mang ja/ ja 'gyed/ ster sbyin/ bsngags mdud/ gang spyi'i bkod pa
sogs rgyas par byas/ la rtse'i bar thab skyel du byung bar ster sbyin yang dag byas/

gzhis su phyin te zhal ngo rnams la tshe dbang sogs thugs bzhed ltar phul te/ dgon gnas su 'byor/ gsang sbug nas o rgyan chen po'i gser sku bzhengs pa'i rab gnas la 'ong dgos
tshul byung ba bcas phyin/ rab gnas rgyas par byas shing / zhal ngo tshor tshe dbang / gur drag sogs rjes gnang kha shas byas/ zhag gcig bsdad ring bsnyen bkur shin tu
gzabs par byung / de sngon nas mgon khang du pha mes brgyud pa'i srung ma ma gcig dpal ldan lha mo rdo rje rab brtan ma'i sku che ba zhig bzhengs 'dod kyis snga sor nas/
dus gsum sangs rgyas kun gyi spyi gzugs khyab bdag zhwa lu ba chen por lung bstan zhus par/ de kha shin tu legs par 'ong 'dug cing bar chad sogs mi 'byung bas nang gzhug
tu/ sher ston gyi phyag nas ma 'di gnang na legs par 'ong pheb ste/ khyab bdag bla ma nyid kyi sku srung lha mo'i sku thang byin can de stsal ba 'di lo skabs su babs par
mthong nas/ zla ba brgyad pa'i nang du bzhengs pa'i sta gon rnams legs par bsgrigs te gza' tshes dge bar/ ja khra nas 'jim bzo ba tshe chog dang / tsha ba dge slong 'brog
mgon gnyis kyis ru shing lag 'tshags dam par tshugs te/ zhabs drung rin po che dang / ban tshang slob dpon bla ma bsam 'phel gnyis kyis phyag bstar te nang gzhug tu ru
shing sdom pa gnang dus ser drag babs pa sogs 'tshub 'gyur gyi rnam pa cung zad byung / nang gzhug la sku rten gtso bo sher ston gyi thugs dam rten gyi sku thang dang / slob
dpon chen po'i sku bye ma a krong sogs mang ba/ gsung rten nor bu'i dung rwa can sogs khyad du 'phags pa du ma/ thugs rten rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos rje

dang thugs rgyud gcig pa'i DA ki'i gtso mo rin chen mtsho mo'i thugs sogs byin chen mang ba/ yon tan gyi rten du mtshan ldan thod pa sogs du ma dang / phrin las kyi rten du
gong ma rin po che'i thugs dam gyi phur pa sogs mang ba/ slob dpon chen po sogs 'phags yul gyi paN grub du ma dang / rdo rje 'chang gong ma lnga dang / dkyil 'khor rgya
mtsho'i dbang phyug mkhyen rab yab sras sogs bod yul gyi mkhas grub du ma rnams kyi na bza'/ dbu lo/ ring bsrel/ dam rdzas/ gdung tshwa/ gnod sbyin bang mdzod du nor bu'i
rigs du ma sogs ma tshang ba med par phul zhing / gsod byed chu srin gdong can gyi sku la sku rten sgrol ma'i gser sku khyad mtshar/ gsung rten dung khra mgo ma/ thugs rten
lcags kyi rdo rje/ yon tan rten du dam rdzas/ phrin las kyi rten du li dkar gyi phur pa/ rgya bod kyi mkhas grub rnams kyi byin rten sogs gtso mo dang mthun par phul
ba sogs/ mdor na dkar chag nang du gsal ba ltar legs par grub 'phral/ rab gnas sogs rgyas par byas te mthar phyin to/ /bzo bo zung la zla ba gcig gi ring phog /ston mo/ ster
cha sogs shin tu gzabs par byas shing / bar chad zhi phyir zhag lnga re nas sbyang ba khrus gsol byas pas 'di khar 'tshubs sogs ma byung kyang / sprul sku tshe mchog
tshang la kha mchu dang / god ka kha shas byung song bas dogs pa che bar byed 'dug /sku gnyis la tshon rtsi sogs legs par grub nas mgon khang du spyan 'dren zhu nyin rten
'brel stabs nged dpon slob bzhi bcu skor gyis rol mo'i sgra sa g.yo ba tsam bsgrags shing bkra shis khra ring sogs dar 'phyar dang / lha bsang gi

dud pa sprin phung ltar 'khrigs pa dang bcas zhabs drung rin po che dpon slob mang bas gdan drangs pa mgon khang du pheb 'phral zhal gro'i ston mo gsang sbug nas tshang dpon
lags rnam dpyod 'jig rten gyi mes por 'gran bzod pas khur bzhes mdzad de rten 'brel rang 'grigs su gyur/ de nas bzung zhag bcu gcig gi ring nged khu dbon/ mtshungs med
chos rje rin po che bcas gtsor gyur pa'i dgong bstar rab gnas tshar re dang / tshes bcu gcig gi nyin res gza' nyin mor byed pa dang rgyu skar me bzhi 'dzom pa'i 'grub sbyor
bzang po'i thog dbu btsugs te/ zhag gsum gyi ring nged dpon slob bzhi bcu skor gyis mgon khang gi rab gnas nas bshad pa bzhin rab gnas shin tu rgyas par byas pa'i tshe/
nyin gnyis pa'i nyin dpal ldan 'dod khams gtso mo nyid kyi sku khru gang pa zhig thim pa'i snang ba shin tu gsal ba zhig byung zhing / nyin gsum par sbyin sreg bcas/ mdor
na rab tu gnas pa cha lag tshang ma legs par grub pa'i tshe sku de sngar las gzi brjid che ba sogs ye shes sems dpa' mngon sum du thim pa'i rtags mtshan khyad par du 'phags
par gyur to/ /e ma mchog gsum kun 'dus bla ma dang / /yi dam lha tshogs chos srung nor lha sogs/ /sras bcas rgyal ba'i thugs rje'i char rgyun gyis/ /mos gus ldan pa'i
'dod don yid bzhin 'grub/ /'jigs rung gang sku dpa' brjid rab ldan zhing / /'jigs bral gsung gis dam nyams klad 'gems pa/ /'jigs med bde chen thugs kyi klong dkyil nas/
/'jigs bral rig 'dzin rnams la dngos grub ster/ /de ltar ma gcig dpal ldan lha mo yi/ /sku brnyan

gzi byin ldan par legs grub par/ /rab gnas byas tshe 'og min zhing khams sogs/ /rab 'byams rgyal ba'i gnas nas srid gsum bdag /'khor bcas sprin bzhin 'dus te thim pa'i tshe/
/sku nyid mngon sum 'phar ba kun gyis ni/ /mthong sogs ya mtshan du mas gang bar gyur/ /legs par grub nas sprul sku ba gnyis la yon sogs shin tu rgyas par bsgrubs/ tsha
mo lha ldan lha khang pa'i gnas ma gshin stabs phyir log byas pa/ gza' tshes dge bar tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po dang gdung rus gcig pa/ sde pa lha gshongs pa'i sar rdzong
bda' byas/ sde dge dbon po phyir 'byon lam du dpal mgon zhal gyi rjes gnang rnams gsan par pheb pa bstan pa la phan phyir/ zhabs drung dbon rin po che dang lhan du chos
srung rnams kyi rjes gnang zur bka' zab pa las kyang ches zab pa rdo rje 'chang tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po yab sras kyi ring lugs drin chen rdo rje 'chang pha bla ma
rin chen bsod nams mchog grub kyi bka' drin las nos pa rnams dang / gzhan yang dbang / rjes gnang / lung sogs ches mang ba zhig phul/ pheb rdzong la rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas
kyi gser sku shin tu legs pa zhig dang byin rten/ na bza'/ snam bu sogs shin tu rgyas par phul te spyi dang bye brag gi bstan pa la phan pa'i bslab bya dpyis phyin par
byas shing / mdzod pa sogs pheb skyel du rdzong bda' byas/ gong sa chen po'i bka' shog gtan tshigs rin po che shin tu legs par yang zhus te bskur/ ston khri 'du nas 'bul
dpon bla ma chos mdzad dpon slob 'khor bcas byon zhing gzhis len gzabs rgyas byas/ gser/ me mda'/ rta/ dre'u/

mdzo/ g.yag /ja/ gzhan yang thab chas/ mgo g.yab sogs sgar gzhis la mkho ba ci rigs bcas rtsis sprod shin tu rgyas par mdzad cing / khri 'dur 'bul sdud sogs 'gro mi sa bdag
byas chog pa'i khang pa gsar bzo mdzad pa dang / sgar gzhis bca' lag sogs 'phral phugs la phan slebs che bar mdzad 'dug pa'i rtsis khra'i tho sogs kyang 'bul bar mdzad/
'dus tshogs la stong rtsa nyin gsum gyi ring 'dzugs pa mdzad song ba'i gang ci'i bkod pa dang / tshogs dbur nged khu dbon la byang rten 'bul ba rgyas pa dang / tshogs par
ja 'gyed bcas tshogs gsog rgya che bar byang bu dang / 'khor gsum yongs dag gi bsngo smon dpyis phyin par byas/ zhag shas nas nged khu dbon la rten 'byung rgyas par mdzad
par ban tshang rnams kyi tshe sbyin yid bzhin 'khor lo'i cho ga bcas rten 'brel legs tshogs che bar mdzad/ sde dge dbon chen gyis 'bul skyel du gnyer pa phrin las rdzong
bda' mdzad par 'byor/ phyag bris nang ltar gser/ rta/ ja/ dre'u sogs bskur ma dpangs mtho bar 'dug pa dang / dbon po ngag dbang grongs pa'i bsngo rten dre'u sogs kyang
byung zhing / bsngo smon yang dag byas/ pho brang du phyag mjal la rdzong bda' byas/ gzhan yang khams/ byang / dbus/ gtsang sogs nas chos don gnyer la byon pa rnams la so
so'i thugs 'dod ltar dbang / rig gtad/ rab byung / bsnyen rdzogs sogs dang / byang bu/ bsngo smon smin rgyas byas/ dgun chos sde chen po'i dus chen khag rnams byed skabs
gzhung sa chen po nas dpal ldan rtser sku rim bskang gsor ban tshang zhal grangs nyi shu rtsa gsum gyis zhag nyer lnga'i ring

gur zhal beg tse sogs kyi bskang ba'i zhabs phyir 'gro dgos tshul sbyi bor pheb pa ltar zhus shing / dgos cha phog yon sogs gzhan dang mi 'dra ba bka' drin bskyangs/ dus chen
khag rnams grub nas/ sa sbug pa rnams kyis kyang dgos tshul nan gyis byung ba nas/ nged khu dbon dpon slob mang ba rta kha bskyod/ zhag bcu skor bsdad par/ gnyer tshang
skor gyis gsol chas kyi mthun rkyen yang dag byung zhing / zhen pa bzhi bral gyi chos ra dang / dbang / rjes gnang gi rigs mang bar byas/ de'i ring rgyal nang / sgrub phu
mda'/ brgya grong rag ma/ sbu tshab/ grub rgyal/ mkhar sdong sogs de skor yon bdag rnams kyis nas sran/ sha mar/ dar ras sogs ster cha byed mi dang / 'phrad mi shin tu
mang bas dus 'da' bar gyur cing / tshes bcu'i dbang lung dang bsnyen gnas kyi sdom pa 'bogs pa/ ma Ni'i bzlas lung sogs 'dod chos ci rigs kyis so so'i thugs dam bskangs/
sa sbug tu snga sor tshes bcu las cho ga gzhan med gshis grong chog la stabs mi bde zhing / ma Ni'i skabs kyang gso sbyong tsam med pas thabs chag pa zhig 'dug par/ spyan
ras gzigs kyi cho ga zhig tshugs na bsam me glang mkhar bsdongs nas zhing sogs mthun rkyen sprod pa sogs grwa sgrig gi bkod pa gnang dgos tshul zhus pa ltar/ dbon rin po
che nas mthun rkyen sogs gang spyi'i bkod pa 'phral phugs su phan slebs che bar mdzad de/ 'phags pa 'jig rten dbang phyug gi cho ga gong ma mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang
pos bka' brtsams gnang ba de 'dzugs par mdzad 'dug pa/ lag len gtsang

khyad bcas sgom khang nas dbu mdzad ma kun dga' chos 'dzoms dang / phrin las dbang mo gnyis bos te gdangs dang phyag len sgom khang sor gnas gong ma'i gsung rgyun ltar bslabs
te/ sa ga zla ba'i ma Ni'i dus kyang dkar phyogs ltar dang / zla ba byung ngo cog gi tshes brgyad la bsnyen gnas sogs gsar sgrig shin tu phan yon che bar btsugs 'dug pa
bcas blo dang mthun par byung 'dug cing / gzhan yang chos spyod kyi skor sogs dang po'i rgyun gyi 'don cha tshang ma phyis su ma nyams shing grwa 'grigs par 'dug pas/ nged
rang nas kyang snam bu/ dar ras sogs kyi ster cha'i gtang rag byas/ dar ras/ nas sran/ snam bu/ dkar yol sogs spyi sger so sos 'bul ba rgyas par byung zhing / phyogs
'dus bcas khrom shin tu che bar tshe dbang byas/ btsun ma rnams dang grub rgyal ldebs kyi grwa rigs yon bdag sogs ci rigs la byin rten/ bsngags mdud sprad cing / gzhis su
bskyod par thab skyel la rtse bar byas shing ster cha'ang sprad/ mkhar sdong du zhag gnyis bsdad/ mkhas grub du ma'i bzhugs gnas rgyun gyi dbang por 'byor/ rin sdings su
chos mdzad ma gnyis dang btsun ma rnams kyis chos skal dgos tshul byung ba ltar phyin te tshem bu lugs kyi dmar khrid smin rgyas dang / rjes gnang sogs 'dod chos rnams byas
shing / btsun ma rnams kyis gzhis len shin tu gzabs pa dang / brtan bzhugs sogs la 'bul ba dar ras/ snam bu/ 'bru cha bcas tshang mas che 'byor chung 'byor lta bu shin
tu rgyas pa dang / chos mdzad ma gnyis kyis kyang rten 'byung sogs gang

legs mdzad/ bar skabs dang mi 'dra ba'i grwa rigs gsar pa mang zhing 'don cha sogs grwa 'grigs par 'dug pas byin rten/ phyag mdud kyang sprad/ bla brang du 'byor nas lo mjug
gi rim gro sogs byas/ /lcags 'brug lor lo gsar dang / srid gsum dbang phyug ma mchod cing zla shas mtshams la bsdad/ zhabs drung dbon rin po ches lam 'bras zhig mdzad pa
snang gsum grub nas rgyu dbang skabs yon bdag zhig gi sar mchod dbur pheb pas sku grib zhig gis bslangs pa lta bu'i bad kan gyi bsnyung ro langs par sku rim 'phrod bsten
sogs byas pas dwangs 'phral rgyud gsum tshugs par gegs med du grub skabs/ ded rang nad ro langs te re grul byung bar 'phrod bsten rim gro sogs byas pas zla gcig nas sangs
drag tu gyur/ 'bog gong nas tsha mo bkra shis dpon g.yog byon pa dang 'phrad cing gang spyi'i 'phros gleng zhib par byung / rten 'byung sogs rgyas par mdzad song zhing
/ rta shin tu legs pa bcas ster cha dang gzhis len gzabs par byas/ gzhis su zla shas bar bzhugs song bar/ yang yang 'phrad par byung zhing / 'byon khar gang spyi'i bslab
bya dang ja sogs kyi ster sbyin kyang byas/ zhol khang gi tshong dpon yab sras rnams nged rang la dad 'dun shin tu che ba yin pa nas/ skabs su dbang dang rab gnas sogs la
'gro dgos yod gshis/ zla ba brgyad pa'i nang du sangs rgyas kyi sku bzhengs pa'i rab gnas dang dbang la phyin par bsnyen bkur dang ster chas rgyas par byung zhing / khong
pa'i a khu bla ma de nged rang la dad pa thun mong ma yin pa zhig yin pa/ shing khyi

lo nang du tshe dus las 'das par skyabs 'gro byang bu sogs byas pas khong rang gi nang bu'i skye ba blangs pa zhig byung song / ston klong nag sangs rgyas rin chen gyi sku
skye lcags phag lo ngor nas mkhan chen dpal mchog rgyal mtshan gyis lung bstan pa bzhin byon byung bar/ lam 'bras sogs thugs bzhed kyi chos rnams byas te phyir pheb par 'brug
lor byon par/ lam 'bras sbyong rgyud sogs chos gang dgos byas shing / grwa rgyun dkor pa sogs 'jags gnas kyi gong sa chen po'i bka' shog rin po che dgos gsung pa ltar
zhus nas phyir byon pas/ khong rang gi yul nas bka' shog rin po che yod pa'i phrag dog gis bla ma dpon khag sogs kha shas kyis bka' 'gong byas 'dug par/ mtsho khar gnam
sa'i dbang phyug dA la'i hod tha'i ji'i sku zhabs su byon te gong sa chen po'i bka' shog spyan 'bebs dang gong spyi'i gnas tshul zhus 'dug pas bka' shog rin po che'i dgongs
don bzhin/ lugs gnyis gang sar sngar babs byas chog pa dang cho lo gnang ba sogs bdag rkyen gzhan dang mi 'dra ba bka' drin bskyangs 'dug pas kun gyi 'gran med lta bur
byung 'dug cing / khong rang gi gnas su byon nas phyogs der bstan pa rgyas par mdzad de/ 'di lo dpon slob shin tu mang bar byon pa dang / nged rang gi 'bul dpon bla ma/
ma yum sprul sku'i grogs dan lo sngon ma gnas tshul skyel mi dbon po mkhyen bzang can la bkod pa song don ltar/ rta/ dre'u phon che ba/ ja/ mdzo sogs dgos byed shin tu rgyas
par phul nas bka' 'gyur rin po che legs par grub pa dang / nged rang gi 'bul sdud bla ma kre bo mchog legs bcas 'grul pa tshan che

ba'ang yod tshul gyi bang phyin byung bar chag la'i bar bsu mi rdzong bda' byas shing / pheb nyin bka' 'gyur rin po cher chibs bsu dang / dge 'dun rnams kyis ser phreng bcas
spyan drangs te nges gsang chos 'khor bskor ba'i gtsug lag khang 'du khang gsang sngags pho brang du mchod pa du ma'i dbus su bzhugs su gsol/ sku mdun dpon slob/ nged rang
gi bla ma gnyis sogs 'grul pa rnams la zhal gro'i ston mo zhus/ phyi nyin nas bzung sku mdun tshang gis nyin gsum par tshogs chen la stong chog mdzad song bar nged khu
dbon tshogs dbur phyin zhing / so so nas byang bu/ bsngo smon sogs byas/ grol nyin rta mang ba/ dre'u/ mdzo g.yag sogs du ma dang / ja nag po 'khor drug sogs ja phon che
ba/ khrab/ gos dar sogs ster sbyin rgya cher mdzad par zab pa chos kyi dbyings dang / rgya che ba sems can gyi don du rgyas btab/ yakShi dge legs sogs 'grul bsdebs rnams
kyis kyang / rta/ mdzo g.yag /dar ras sogs kyi bsngo rten byung ba rnams kyang mchog gsum dam pa rnams la gsol ba btab ste dmigs yul rnams la skyabs 'jug byas/ bla ma mchog
legs kyi tshogs su stong chog mdzad par phyin pa/ rta/ ja phon che ba byung bar dmigs med 'khor gsum yang dag gi bsngo smon byas/ rtse gdong nas bdag chen rin po che
pho brang du gong sa chen po yas phyin gyi mjal khar pheb par dgon gnas su pheb dgos tshul gyi zhu yig phul zhing / rim gyis chos sdings nas chibs kha bsgyur bar zhabs drung
dbon rin po che sogs chos sde chen po'i bla khag las tshan lnga bcu

skor gyis chibs bsu dang / dge 'dun bzhi brgya skor gyis ser phreng rgyas par zhus te/ gzims khang du pheb 'phral nged kyis phyin/ gang spyi'i bka' 'phros kyi 'byams klas/
phyi nyin bco brgyad du gdan 'dren zhus/ gzhis len rgyas pa'i thog chibs/ chib rol/ ja/ dar ras/ snam bu sogs kyi 'bul ba rgya chair phul zhing / lha khang rnams la phyag
nas rgyas par bka' drin bskyangs/ gnang sbyin gya nom pa stsal/ zhag shas bzhugs ring / khams tshan rnams kyis gdan 'dren zhu ba sogs so so nas 'bul ba zhabs tog shin tu
rgyas par zhus song zhing / 'grul pa rnams kyis kyang 'bul dpangs mtho bar byas song / pheb nyin dbon rin po ches dbus las tshan mang bar bcas chibs skyel la pheb/ chos
gter gling nas sprul sku rin po che dpon slob chibs kha bsgyur bar chibs bsu ser phreng sogs rgyas par zhus te/ mjal 'phrad zhus skabs lugs gnyis kyi bka' 'phros zhib par
byung / nged khu dbon la gos chas cha tshang sogs rten 'byung gi gnang sbyin dpangs mtho bar gnang zhing / gzhis len rgyas par zhus/ dbon rin po che bsnyung gzhi'i stabs
dus chen gyi sku mtshams mchod dbur pheb pa sogs 'phral dgos rnams sprul sku rin po che nas gnang / tshong dpon gnyis dga' lags kyis tsandan dmar po'i sdong po gnyis byung
thog /'di ga'i tshong pa ngag dbang gis kyang ngag bkod ltar tsandan dmar po phon che bar byung ba dang / me byi lo nang du sgom sde spo ri bla mas jo bo chen po dpal
ldan a ti sha'i sku tshigs dang po la rnam rgyal ma'i sku rang byon du byon pa ring bsrel du mas spras pa zhig byin byung ba bzhugs gnas su rnam rgyal mchod rten rgyug

mtho lnga pa zhig mon grong nas shing bzo pa dbu mdzad a dang spun dang / brag dbar byang pa bcas gsum bos te zla shas bar legs par bsgrubs par phog yon ston mo sogs shin tu
rgyas par byas/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos kyi rgyal po'i rnam thar thang sku re la grub pa mang ba zhig 'dug kyang / 'phags mchog 'jam dpal dbyangs nas mkhyen rab
chos kyi rgyal po nyid kyi bar 'khrungs rabs thang sku re bcas byung na rang nyid kyi tshogs gsag dang bstan rgyun la phan par 'ong 'dug bsam/ bsam sdings sprul sku ba mkhyen
rab lhun grub dpal bzang gis so so'i rnam thar nas mdzad pa rnams ri mor bri bar mdzad par gzhan pa dpe sogs med gshis de rigs 'ong bar dka' yang / sprul sku ba 'di
shes bya'i rig pa gzhan dang mi 'dra ba zhig 'dug gshis khyad par du 'phags pa byung 'dug cing / der bstun gong ma khu dbon gyi 'khrungs rab thang sku kha shas kyang bkod
par byas te sa stag lo nang du skya ris rnams grub par sprul sku lhun grub dang / a dang spun gyis yos lo dang / 'di lo bcas par mkhyen rab chos kyi rgyal po'i 'khrungs
rabs dgu po legs par grub pa gong sham/ zhal khebs/ tog sogs khyad par du 'phags pa bsgrigs shing / sprul sku ba rnams la phog shin tu bzang ba/ ston mo ster sbyin/ yon du
rta dre'u/ nag po 'khor drug kha shas sogs ja mang ba/ dar ras sogs kyis mnyes par byas shing / tsandan mchod rten la'ang nang gzhug dkar chag tu gsal ba ltar grub pa dang
/ bsam pa lhun grub ma dang / gu ru mtshan brgyad sogs tsandan las grub pa'i sku spar lnga bcu skor btab pa/ ma yum sku skye'i grogs dan gyi bka'

'gyur sogs sku gsung thugs rten du mar hor zla bcu gcig pa'i nyer gnyis res gza' nyin mor byed pa dang / rgyu skar me bzhi dgyes rgur spyod pa'i 'grub sbyor bzang po'i nyin
nged khu dbon/ mchog sprul rin po che/ mtshungs med rngog ston chen po sogs dpon slob bzhi bcu skor gyis/ khyab bdag rnam snang chen po'i cho ga la brten pa'i rab tu gnas
pa legs par byas thog rgyan drung la yon bdag bsgos/ der bstun tshogs chen la'ang zhabs tog shin tu rgyas par bcas cho ga nyin gang ma zhig zhus/ sde dge'i gnyer pa chos
'phel/ tsha ba rab gsal bla ma/ dbu mdzad a khu sogs khams 'grul ba mang bar 'byor pas/ rta/ ja sogs kyi ster sbyin rgya cher byung bar bsngo smon gyi rgyas 'debs yang
dag byas/ 'grul pa don gnyer kha shas la mkha' spyod gtso mo'i khrid cig byas shing / lo mjug gi rim gro sogs sngar rgyun ltar byas/ dgon khag gi chos ra dang gzhung sa chen
po'i mjal kha sogs dbon nas mdzad/ lcags sbrul lo gsar tshes kyi lo gsar dang / tshe sgrub/ mkha' spyod gtso mo'i bsnyen pa zla gcig byas/ nad ro langs pa dang dbon rin
po che'ang gzhis nas cung zhig sku ltem pa bcas kyis mang ja/ grwa ja/ chos sgrogs/ bskang ba sogs byas/ khams gsum chos kyi rgyal po lnga pa chen po de nyid kyis gsung
ngag rin po che 'di nyid nyams len phyogs re tsam ma yin par bstan pa yongs rdzogs kyi nyams len mdo rgyud thams cad kyi don gyi bcud phyung ba lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i
gdams ngag zab mo yin pa nas tshogs bshad 'di 'chad nyan 'phel bar 'dug kyang / slob bshad thun mong ma yin pa

'di chad du nye bar 'dug pas dar rgyas che ba zhig byung na bstan rgyun la phan par 'dug gi dgongs pa gtad cing / phran bur yang 'chad nyan 'phel bar byed dgos tshul gyi bslab
ston brtse ba chen pos bskyangs pa dang / rang nyid kyang chos 'di'i bstan pa la phan pa zhig byung na bsam pa'i lhag bsam 'bral med du yod gshis snga sor mi grangs drug
cu skor la bka' rgya grol nas byas kyang 'chad nyan gnang thub rigs byung ma song zhing / de rjes rtse gdong zhabs drung sku mched la phul skabs sku gzhon pa/ bsnyun
gzhi'i stabs dang / 'phen yul ba sogs mjal kha zhu mi mang ba'i thugs brel che gshis khyug tsam las bsam pa dang mthun pa'i bka' rdzogs lung rdzogs zhig ma grub pa nas/ da
lam nged rang gi dbon 'di rje dbon gong ma'i sku'i rnam sprul thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gi thugs kyi 'od zer 'phros pa zhig yin pas bstan rgyun la
phan pa zhig e 'ong bsam gong sa'i 'jal khar byon pa dang bstun gong sa skyabs mgon chen po drug par mi grangs sogs kyi snyan 'bul zhus par dbon rang gis gtsos sum cu skor
la byas chog gi bka' grol ba dang / nub gcig nged rang gi rmi lam du gzims chung nyi 'od tu dgyes mdzad rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor zhig bzhengs 'dug pa'i phyogs shar du mar
me sum cu skor spar 'dug par/ gsal ba bzhi lnga tsam 'dug pa ni bshad sgrub kyi bstan pa la phan pa de tsam 'ong 'dra bsam pa bcas/ na so rgas shing lus gcong ba sogs gang
spyi'i stabs 'chad bde ba zhig mi 'dug kyang / chos 'di nyid yongs su rdzogs pa zhig grub na lnga pa chen po'i dgongs pa

rdzogs shing / rang re yang 'dun pa tshim pa zhig 'ong 'dug bsam u tshugs kyi 'dun pa yod thog /zhabs drung dbon dang / chos rje rin po che sogs snod ldan kha shas kyis yang
yang bskul nas lo mang tsam song ba dang / nye char nan gyis gsung nan che ba bcas nag pa zla ba'i gza' tshes legs par/ zhabs drung dbon rin po che ngag dbang mkhyen brtse
rab brtan/ nyan po nas mkhas shing grub pa'i dbang phyug chos rje rin po che sku mched/ mkhas dbang dam pa gzims 'og slob dpon pa kun dga' nor bu/ rim gnyis mthar phyin
o thog bla ma cha dkar ho thog thu sogs bla khag bco lnga gtsor gyur gyi snon ldan gyi slob ma sum cu rtsa gsum la/ rje btsun mthu stobs dbang phyug bi rU par bdag med
lha mo bco lngas mkha' 'gro'i zhal rlangs ma yal bar gnang ba'i man ngag /gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i gdams pa/ kha ba'i ljongs 'dir thams cad mkhyen
pa 'brog mi lo tsA bas paN chen gha ya dha ra las gsan te rim par 'phel ba/ shing rta'i srol 'byed rje btsun sa skya ba yab sras kyi dar zhing rgyas par mdzad pa/ thun
mong du ngor rdzong gong dkar phyogs su mang na'ang / ji skad du/ tshar chen rdo rje 'chang chen pos/ nga dal 'byor rdo rje'i lus mchog thob/ /pha mtshan ldan bla mas rjes
su bzung / /lam tshad ma snyan brgyud bzhi ldan thob/ /da gang ltar byas kyang e ma ho/ /zhes dang / kun mkhyen mkhyen brtses/ dus da res dam chos sgor zhugs kyang/ /chos
tshogs bshad sbun pas g.yeng ba'i tshe/ /da khyed kyi thugs kyi rgya mtsho las/ /lam zab mo snyan brgyud rin chen stsal/ /da khyed

kyi byin rlabs kho na yis/ /bdag rtse gcig dam chos sgrub 'dod shar/ /tshe 'di phyir skyid pa'i brtan brling khel/ /chos zab zab gzhan la sems ma shor/ /don snyan brgyud gdams
pa'i bdud rtsis myos/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / khams gsum 'gro ba'i skyabs mgon ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtshos/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gis gtad pa'i bstan/ /'dzin mkhas
kun spangs chos rje'i thugs kyi sras/ /blo gsal rgya mtsho'i rjes 'brang ma gtogs par/ /sa rdzus phal gyis rtogs pa'i skal ba phra/ /zhes gsung pa ltar/ thun mong ma
yin pa bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gis yab 'jam dbyangs chen po dang / /mkhan chen dkon mchog bzang po/ /ngor chen rdo rje 'chang gi thugs sras mus chen 'khor lo sdom pa dkon
mchog rgyal mtshan rnams las gsan pa rje btsun kun spangs chos rje dang / tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po yab sras la bka' babs pa gsang ba las kyang ches gsang ba gsung
ngag rin po che zab mo slob bshad kyi skor rnams kun mkhyen mkhyen brtse'i zin bris bzhin smin rgyas su byas shing / dpon slob rnams kyis gser gyi maNDal/ rten gsum/ gser/
dngul/ bla bre/ gos/ dar/ ja/ mdzo/ snam ras/ khrab/ rung mthun gyi gos mang ba sogs dngos po rgyu bzang la dpangs mtho bar mchod sprin spros te tshar lugs thun mong ma
yin pa'i phyag len gyis brgyan pa/ snang gsum gyi ring lung la/ brgyud 'debs dngos grub char 'bebs sogs bla ma brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs kyi rigs/ gsung ngag rin po che lam
'bras bu dang bcas pa'i zin bris gsang

chen bstan pa rgyas byed ces bya ba las gsung ngag byon tshul kha'u brag rdzong pa'i bzhed pa ma nor ba dang / byung ba'i chos la bshad sgrub bya tshul gnyis mkhyen brtses
mdzad pa/ sa skya pa chen po'i rnam thar nas ngor chen yab sras kyi bar dang / de nas bdag chen rdo rje 'chang nas nged rang gi rtogs brjod kyi bar yongs su rdzogs par byas
shing / thun mong ma yin pa'i maNDal dang / sdom gzung gi tshigs bcad gnyis ka la brten pa rgyas pa'i lugs gnyis kyi sems bskyed legs par byas/ phyi dro slob ma rjes 'dzin
dang / gsag sbyong gi dmigs pa zhib tu phog ste so sor nan tan tu bsgom dgos pa'i bslab bya yang dag byas/ nged bsnyen pa kha gso dang bum chu nus ldan du sgrub pa grol
nas/ sum ldan rdo rje 'dzin pa dge slong rin po che 'dam nas chibs kha bsgyur bar/ mdzod pa sogs pheb bsur btang ste/ bla brang du spyan drangs/ gzhis len shin tu gzabs
pa dang / gser/ ja/ dar/ ras/ rta/ mdzo mo sogs rgyas par phul/ chibs kha bsgyur bar chibs skyel zhus/ de nas dpon slob rnams la mus chen gyi mngon dkyil la tshar chen
gyi lhan thabs dang / snying po bsdus pa sbyar te mkhan chen de nyid kyi gsung rgyun ltar dpal kye rdo rje'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor la brten pa'i rgyu dus kyi dbang
/ dbang lha spyan 'dren gyi dus gzhal yas khang dang lha snam gsum gyi steng gdan gsum tshang ba'i lha tshogs bkod pa dang / slob dpon gyi dbang gi dus slob ma dbang stegs
kyi steng du 'jog pa sogs tshar lugs kyi phyag len 'khrul med byas/ dbang dus su thob pa'i dam tshig dang sdom pa mi nyams shing bsrung ba'i phyir rdo rje theg pa'i rtsa
ba dang yan lag gi ltung ba rgya cher

bshad pa'i rnam bshad 'khrul spong rab gsal bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa sogs yi ge mang po'i lung / dbang gi ye shes la log par rtog pa dgag cing lta ba skyon med
du bsgrub pa'i phyir lta ba 'khor 'das dbyer med kyi dmigs khrid shin tu zhib pa/ bskyed rim gyi dmigs khrid sems 'dzin dang bcas pa shin tu zhib par rdzogs 'phral/ lam
dus kyi dbang bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gi yig cha'i thog nas phul/ bum dbang gi nang bskyed rim dang / 'pho ba bar do'i bar thams cad mkhyen brtse'i zin bris bzhin dang /
bum dbang gi rmi lam/ bar do/ /dbang gong ma gsum gyi khrid rigs brgya'i khyab bdag khams gsum chos kyi rgyal po lnga pa chen pos mdzad pa ltar bdag byin rlabs rlung gtum
mo drod rtags kyi khrid/ pho nya'i lam zhes pa 'dus pa bar pa dkyil 'khor 'khor lo 'byung bzhi lugs 'byung lugs ldog tu bsgom pa/ khams 'dus pa tha ma skyon med gnyug ma
ye shes kyi khrid dam/ rba rlabs gsum gyi khrid dang bcas pa'i dbang bzhi re re la'ang lam/ lta ba/ grub mtha'/ 'da' kha ma/ bar do/ rmi lam/ sgyu lus dang bcas pa dbang
po rab 'bring tha ma'i lam tshang ba sla bcos dang bshad yams su ma song ba'i myong khrid du phul zhing / de dag gi cha lag tu/ bdag med ma'i byin rlabs/ lam sbas bshad/
lam zab phyi nang / bir srung phyi nang / rnam 'joms bir lugs/ brda chig brgyud/ brda don gsal ba/ sgrub pa lung byin/ bla ma rin 'byung / tshar gsum khug pa/ gsang bcu'i
rgyas gdab kyi bar yongs su rdzogs pa rje btsun gong ma dang 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i yi ge las ji

ltar byung ba bzhin du phul/ rgyab skyor lung la jo lcags ma gtso bor gyur pa'i lam 'bras glegs bam kha skong dang bcas pa/ rje btsun gong ma rnams kyi yi ge mang po'i lung
/ bla ma lnga bcu pa'i 'grel pa dngos grub sgo 'byed sogs tshar chen yab sras kyis mdzad pa'i yi ge mang po/ /gong gi khrid yig rnams yongs su rdzogs pa'i lung / bskyed
rdzogs kyi rnam bshad tshar chen gyis mdzad pa/ gsung gi bkra shis tshar chen chos kyi rgyal pos mdzad pa sogs mdor na mkhan chen de nyid kyis nged rang la gsung ngag slob
bshad kyi chos skor gnang ba rnams gcig kyang ma lus par phul zhing / lnga pa chen pos mkhan chen de nyid la gnang ba'i phyag dpe rnams nged rang la bsngags brjod bcas
bka' drin bskyangs byung ba'ang chos bdag por sbrod pa'i tshul gyis sa skya pa'i bstan pa spyi dang / bye brag zab mo slob bshad pa'i bstan pa gong sa lnga pa chen po'i bslab
ston ltar slob bshad kyi bstan pa gsal bar mdzad dgos pa'i snyan 'bul bcas phyag dpe rnams kyang zhabs drung dbon rin po cher phul lo/ /bdag med mkha' 'gro'i zhal drod
dza hu'i rgyun/ /rnal 'byor dbang phyug thugs kyi rgya mtshor 'khyil/ /de las rjes 'brang chu klung bye ba brgyas/ /'phags bod 'dzin ma'i khyon kun dog por byas/ /'jigs
bral stogs bcu'i bdag nyid bi rU'i zhabs/ /byang phyogs kha ba ri pa'i dpung gnyen du/ /legs byon sa skya'i 'jam mgon rjes 'brang gis/ /tshul 'di nyi zla lta bur gsal bar
mdzad/ /thun mong gtam gyi ba tshwa'i rdzing bu'i khrod/ /tshogs bshad 'dam skyes gzhon nu ches mang yang / /gsang chen slob bshad u dumWara'i bcud/ /blo gsal rgya mtsho
rjes 'brang bcas las su/ /khyab bdag sku bzhi'i bdag nyid

he ru ka /ngur smrig bla gos 'dzin pa zhwa lu pa'i/ drin las thub bstan yongs rdzogs nyams len 'di/ /bum pa gang byor thob pa kho bo tsam/ /da lam thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen
brtse'i zhabs/ /rang bstan spel phyir bsam bzhin sprul pa'i gar/ /legs bsgyur rigs dbon mkhyen brtse rab brtan la/ /zab chos yongs rdzogs bdag po nyid la sprad/ /a ho skal
bzang snod ldan blo gsal rnams/ /yongs rdzogs gdams pa'i snying po bstan zin gyi/ /'di snang tshe 'di'i bya bas ma g.yengs par/ /rtse gcig nyams su long zhig snying gi
bu/ /rang bzo'i bshad yams bsgrigs pa'i zla zer gyis/ /snod ldan yid kyi 'dab ma ci zhig bzhad/ /slob bshad nyin byed snang ba 'di shar tshe/ /blo gsal snying gi pad dkar
rang dbang ci/ /gsung ngag gi chos ra zhag lnga drug tsam nas tshugs rtsis nas/ zla gcig lhag tsam gyi ring nad ro ldang ba ya mar babs pa'i sems mi bde ba sogs lhongs
che bar byung skabs/ nyan po nas grub pa'i dbang phyug chos rje rin po che bzhugs yod pas tshe dbang brgya rtsa/ rta mgrin/ phyag rdor/ 'byung 'dul/ rnam 'joms byab khrus
gnang zhing / dbon rin po ches mdzod pa dang / gnyer pa ngag dbang la bslab ston gnang sde bka' 'gyur sogs chos sgrogs/ bskang ba brgya rtsa kha shas/ brgya bzhi/ gtor
chen sogs rim gro'i rigs dang / 'tsho mdzad don grub chos zhu bar yod gshis sman gyi 'phrod bsten mdzad pa dang / rin sdings nas tsha mo chos mdzad ma gnyis kyis gtsos btsun
ma rnams kyis rten 'byung byas pas rim bder song / mthong snang la

gzims chung nyi 'od du bande rigs mi gcig pa du ma 'tshang ba dang / g.yas g.yon du rgyug pa sogs byung skabs dpal ldan lha mo'i dre'u rgyun du rgyug cing / skabs 'gar lha
mo nyid sku mdog sngo nag rgyan phyag mtshan yongs rdzogs dang / chu srin ma'ang khrag mdog lta bur mthong zhing / dam can pu tra nyid ha la nag po ltar ral gri dang zhags
pa thogs pa mngon sum du mthong bas rim gyis drag tu song skabs/ nub gcig rmi lam du gzims chung gi gung na khri mtho ba zhig gi steng du rje btsun chen po rdo rje dang
dril bu bsnams shing / sku'i g.yas g.yon du dge bsnyen gyi tshul gnyis bzhugs 'dug pa/ gcig zhu byas yin 'dug cing / gcig zangs tsha e yin bsam pa byung / mos gus kyis langs
te gsol ba rtse gcig tu 'debs pa zhig byung ba ni snod ldan gyi slob mar slob bshad phul bas mnyes shing bar chad zhi ba'i phyir byin rlabs gnang bar mngon/ dpon slob
rnams kyis tshe sbyin yid bzhin 'khor lo la brten pa'i rten 'byung dang / dngos po'i maNDal rgyas par gnang ste ring por sdod dgos pa'i gsung nan che bar mdzad par nged
rang so skyer song bas khas len ga la zhu nus kyang de kha'i 'dun pa tsam zhu ba'i khas blangs/ chos gegs med du grub pa'i gtang rag tu bstan srung rgya mtshor rten rdzas
sogs yid 'gul ba bshams te gtang rag gi bskang ba rgyas par phul/ mkha' 'gro lnga mnyes par byed pa'i tshogs kyi 'khor lo rgya chen po bskor ba'i zhabs tog mdzod pa lhun
grub kyis rgya che zhing dpangs mtho ba shin tu bzabs par zhus/ ma nas mdzod pa 'di lo bcu gcig nas 'khris su bcar ba'i g.yog 'grus pa byas shing / lhag par mdzod pa dang
/ nad g.yog /sger

nas zas kyi 'phrod bsten/ dbyar dgun gyi mal cha/ rten bzhengs che ba byed skabs rgyu cha dang ston mo dpangs mtho ba/ rim gro dang rten 'byung sogs rgyun mar bsgrubs pas bla
ma rnams kyi nye gnas gyi mig ltos la phan pa zhig yin/ dpon slob tshang mas de ltar bsgrubs pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba pha ma rigs drug gis bsdus pa'i sems can thams cad kyi
don du bsngo ba dang / bstan 'gro la phan bde 'byung ba'i phyir smon lam bkra shis kyis mtha' brgyan par byas/ 'di skabs sgo mo bla ma yon tan gyis gsung ngag bod du 'gyur
mdzad kyi paNDi ta chen po ga ya dha ra dang / thams cad mkhyen pa 'brog mi lo tsA ba/ shing rta'i srol 'byed rdo rje 'chang bla chen sa skya pa sogs kyi sku khyad mtshar
de khar mkho 'ong 'dra zer bslur btang byung ba ni/ rigs brgya'i khyab bdag lnga pa chen pos/ gsung ngag slob bshad nyin byed dkyil 'khor rgyas/ /gangs can rmongs pa'i
smag rum nyer sangs nas/ /snyan brgyud bshad sgrub snang ba 'od po che/ /thub bstan mi nub de srid dar gyur cig /ces gsungs pa ltar dar zhing rgyas pa'i rten 'brel du
sems/ chos ra grol nas klong nag sku skye bla ma mchog legs/ /che ba bla ma mkhyen rab dang / mkhyen rab phun tshogs sogs 'grul pa mang tsam phyir log par byin rten dang
/ gos snam sogs ster cha dang / bstan pa'i zhabs 'degs la brtson pa dgos tshul gyi bkod pa bcas brdzongs/ sgom khang nas tsha bo chos mdzad mched kyis grwa bsgrigs mdzad
de/ grwa rigs rnams rten 'byung du byung bar ngos 'phrad dang rjes gnang sogs byas shing / mgon

khang du spyan gzigs la mi lpags kyis g.yogs pa'i bdud kyi klad pa 'gems pa'i rngam brjid che bar phul/ khyung 'bum gyi bla ma'i gdan sar 'bul dpon bla ma rig 'dzin dpon slob
la rta khal bla chas rgyas par sprad cing / sgar gzhis khams rang la yod pas mkho ba'i yo byad rnams sprad nas bkra shis kyi nas gtor/ bla brang bla ma phyir log pa dang
/ nged rang gi 'bul sdud tsha ba bla ma bstan 'dzin sogs la gos rgyug dang / byin rten gang legs sprad cing / gang spyi'i bkod pa bcas rdzong bda' byas/ tsha bo tshong
dpon gnyis dga' yab sras tshong nas 'khor ba dang phrad cig gang spyi'i 'phros gling rgyas par byung / dgon lags sbug nas kyang grwa rigs rnams ngos 'phrad dang rten 'byung
du byung bar rdo rje phag mo'i rjes gnang dang / bsnyen gnas dang / ma Ni'i lung byas/ dbus gtsang khams sog /a mdo rnams nas bla khag grwa rigs/ dpon khag /yon bdag
rnams kyis byin pa'i dngos po rnams/ ster mi de dag gtso bor gyur pa'i pha ma rigs drug gi sems can rnams kyi tshogs gsag sgrib sbyang gi sems bskyed kyis bla ma dang / dge
'dun gyi sde la bsnyen bkur/ sku gsung thugs kyi rten bzhengs pa/ mchod rdzas bskrun pa/ chos sde'i 'dzin skyong du gtong ba sogs/ bdag gzhan gyi rim gro/ dge rtsa/ tha
na slong mo ba rnams la'ang ci nus byin zhing / dge sbyor gyi dus 'od zer spro bsdu/ bsngo smon gyi rgyas 'debs mkha' khyab kyi sems can la 'dun pa dang ma bral bar byed
pa las rang don du kha zas dang gos sogs kyang gang byung tsam la longs spyod pa las don du mi gnyer ba shes ldan rnams kyi gzigs pa 'di kha phyi nang med pa yin

zhing / bya ba'i gtso bor ni dus gsum rgyal ba'i spyi gzugs khams gsum chos kyi rgyal po rigs brgya'i khyab bdag lnga pa chen po dang / byang chub bar kyi skyabs mgon dkyil
'khor rgya mtsho'i dbang phyug mtshan brjod par dka' ba mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po khu dbon/ khyab bdag dgyes mdzad rdo rje zhwa lu ba/ rdo rje 'chang 'jam mgon chos
kyi rgyal po sa skya pa sku mched yab sras rnams gtso bor gyur pa'i yongs 'dzin dam pa nyi shu rtsa lnga las dam pa'i chos kyi bdud rtsi thob pa rnams rang nyid kyis ci
